Compounding is normally performed in the following sequence:

  • Solvent, usually water, is metered into the compounding tank, to a pre-determined level that is less than the final batch size.
  • Excipients and API in powder or liquid form are charged into the compounding tank in a specified sequence.
  • The solution is mixed to make a homogenous solution.
  • Additional solvent is added, if necessary, to achieve the desired concentration and final batch size.

Additional steps such as temperature adjustment, pH adjustment, or oxygen displacement may be required during formulation. Sample collection should be performed only as required for in-process measurements or testing, to minimize risk of contamination of the bulk solution. Equipment for sampling should be easily cleaned.

Compounding Area Design Considerations

  • Powder handling may create airborne particulates. Airflows should be carefully managed to reduce the risk of cross-contamination and harmful exposure to operators. Use of Computational Fluid Dynamic (CFD) simulation(s) may be of benefit for optimizing airflow patterns.
  • Biologically active substances should not be vented to the atmosphere.
  • The compounding area should be easy to clean.
  • If tanks are to be sterilized, vents on tanks should be fitted with gas/vent filters of sterilizing grade that are arranged to facilitate integrity testing.

Use of flammable solvents in the formulation process requires specialized design activities to ensure personnel and facility safety.

導讀與實務解析

配製：將原料變成可充填藥液

配製（Compounding）是將 API、賦形劑和溶劑按配方混合的步驟。從簡單的溶解到複雜的乳化或脂質體製備都屬於此範圍。

核心概念：配製用水的選擇

  • 注射用水（WFI）：大多數水性無菌產品的標準溶劑 — 內毒素限值最嚴格
  • 低內毒素純化水：僅用於某些眼科和鼻腔產品 — 這是例外而非常規

選擇依據：最終產品的給藥途徑決定用水等級。注射劑 = WFI，眼科/鼻腔用 = 可考慮低內毒素純化水。

核心概念：產品接觸面的「先清後滅」原則

所有產品接觸面（product contact surface）— 包括容器、殼體、製程管路 — 必須在使用前清潔。如果後續是無菌製程，還必須經過驗證過的滅菌循環處理，且從滅菌完成到製程結束，必須維持無菌邊界的完整性。

這就是 CIP（就地清洗）和 SIP（就地滅菌）的核心應用場景。

重點提示：不可過濾產品的特殊配製要求

當產品因物理特性（如懸浮液、脂質體）無法進行除菌過濾時，原料投入（charging）必須在 ISO 5/Grade A 環境下進行，最好使用 RABS 或封閉式隔離器。

粉末處理的氣流速度陷阱：處理細粉時，隔離器內的氣流速度可能需要低於 0.45 m/s。這違背了一般「氣流越快越乾淨」的直覺 — 因為過快的氣流會將粉末吹散，反而增加汙染風險且影響投料精度。

比喻：配製像精密的烘焙程序

配製的標準順序就像做蛋糕：先加水（溶劑）到預定量 → 按順序加入粉料（賦形劑和 API）→ 攪拌均勻 → 最後補水到目標總量。不能把所有材料一股腦倒進去 — 投料順序影響溶解效率和產品品質。

核心概念：配製區設計的四大考量

  1. 粉塵管理：粉末處理會產生空氣微粒，需要 CFD（計算流體力學）模擬來優化氣流模式
  2. 生物活性物質排放：不可排放到大氣中 — 需要密閉系統或適當的廢氣處理
  3. 可清潔性：配製區必須易於清潔 — 設計時就要考慮，不能事後補救
  4. 槽體通氣過濾器：需滅菌的槽體上的通氣口必須裝設滅菌級氣體過濾器，且便於完整性測試

重點提示：取樣的風險平衡

取樣是製程中控（IPC）的必要操作，但每次取樣都是一次汙染風險。ISPE 建議：

  • 僅在必要時取樣（in-process measurement or testing）
  • 取樣設備必須易於清潔
  • 取樣點的設計應最小化對藥液的汙染風險

關鍵參數：配製過程中可能需要調整的項目

  • 溫度調整：某些 API 需要特定溫度才能溶解
  • pH 調整：使用酸/鹼溶液調整到目標 pH 範圍
  • 氧氣置換：對氧敏感產品需用氮氣置換瓶頭空間和溶液中溶解氧
  • 濃度調整：最終補加溶劑至目標批量和濃度

思考練習

  • 為什麼配製區的 HEPA 過濾器最好安裝在槽體人孔（manway）正上方？這與一般的房間層流送風有何不同？
  • 使用易燃溶劑進行配製時，除了防爆設計，還需要考慮哪些安全面向？
  • 如果您正在配製一個脂質奈米粒（LNP）產品，為什麼不能使用除菌過濾？配製環境需要如何調整？

CDMO 應用觀點

  • 配製槽的彈性設計：CDMO 需要不同大小的配製槽來應對不同批量需求（從數十升到數千升），可移動式配製槽或模組化設計提高靈活性
  • CIP/SIP 驗證的規模效應：每個新客戶產品可能需要針對其特定配方驗證 CIP 循環 — 殘留限值因產品而異
  • 一次性配製系統的機會：對小批量或臨床試驗階段產品，單次使用混合袋（single-use mixer bag）可免除 CIP/SIP 驗證，加速從接單到生產的時間
  • 複雜配方的能力建設：隨著 mRNA 疫苗和 LNP 等複雜產品需求增加，CDMO 需要投資乳化、微流體混合等專業配製設備
S

Section Summary / 本節總結

Key Takeaways from Sections 3.1–3.2.3

Key Takeaways

Equipment Selection Framework

ISPE Vol.3 Chapter 3 establishes a seven-dimension framework for process equipment selection: Performance, Functionality, Construction, Instrumentation, Air Quality, Layout, and Services. Each dimension must be evaluated against the URS.

Process Flow Understanding

The typical sterile dosage form process involves 18+ discrete stages from dispensing through secondary packaging. Advanced technologies (BFS, RTU components, closed systems) can combine or eliminate steps to improve sterility assurance.

Environmental Requirements

Aseptic processing requires ISO 5/Grade A at the point of fill; terminal sterilization requires ISO 8/Grade C minimum. Bioburden control is critical for both approaches, with five key risk-elevating conditions identified.

Dispensing Strategies

Centralized vs. decentralized dispensing each have advantages depending on product type and facility design. Cross-contamination prevention requires a multi-layered approach including dedicated HVAC, physical separation, and procedural controls.

Post-Sterilization Control

The chain of sterile custody from sterilizer to point of use is maintained through pass-through sterilizers, barrier-protected carts, multi-layer wrapping strategies, and validated surface disinfection procedures.

Compounding Design

Equipment surfaces must be cleaned and sterilized (CIP/SIP). Products that cannot be sterile filtered require ISO 5/Grade A compounding with barrier technology. Airflow speed may need reduction for powder handling.

重點回顧

設備選型架構

ISPE Vol.3 第三章建立了製程設備選型的七維評估架構：性能、功能、結構、儀器、空氣品質、佈局、服務。URS 是一切的起點。

製程流程全貌

典型無菌劑型製程包含 18 個以上的離散步驟。BFS、RTU 元件、密閉系統等先進技術可合併或省略步驟，提升無菌保證水準。

環境等級邏輯

無菌製程充填點需 ISO 5/Grade A；最終滅菌最低需 ISO 8/Grade C。微生物負荷控制對兩種方式都至關重要。

秤量策略選擇

集中式適合多產品設施的固體原料；分散式適合液體和高毒性物料。交叉汙染防控需要多層防線的系統性方法。

滅菌後無菌鏈維護

穿越式滅菌器、屏障保護推車、多層包覆、驗證過的表面消毒 — 四道機制確保物料從滅菌到使用的無菌完整性。

配製區設計

CIP/SIP 是產品接觸面準備的基礎。不可過濾產品須在 ISO 5 + RABS/隔離器中配製。粉末處理時的氣流速度需特別評估。

下一節預告

Section 3.2.4 起將進入除菌過濾、充填、加塞、凍乾等核心無菌操作步驟的設備考量 — 這些是無菌製造的「黃金地帶」，設備設計直接決定產品的無菌保證水準。

Chapter 2b: 3b. Process Equipment (3.2.4–3.2.6)

製程設備（中上） | p50-p61

ISPE Baseline® Guide Vol. 3: Sterile Product Manufacturing Facilities (3rd Ed. 2018) | p46 – p63

Learning Objectives / 本章學習目標

  • Understand sterile filtration system configurations (aseptically assembled, SIP multi-use, single-use) and their facility design implications / 理解無菌過濾系統的三種組態（無菌組裝式、SIP 多用式、單次使用式）及其對設施設計的影響
  • Know the critical design considerations for sterile filtration including redundant filtration, filter integrity testing, and bulk product holding / 掌握無菌過濾的關鍵設計考量：冗餘過濾、濾膜完整性測試、散裝產品靜置保存
  • Describe container preparation processes: washing machines, depyrogenation tunnels, and ready-to-use container systems / 說明容器準備流程：洗瓶機、去熱原隧道，以及即用型容器系統
  • Explain closure preparation requirements and the importance of endotoxin control / 解釋膠塞準備要求及內毒素控制的重要性
  • Master the design principles for aseptic filling machines, including RABS/isolator integration, UAF protection, and IPC considerations / 掌握無菌充填機的設計原則，包括 RABS/隔離器整合、單向氣流保護、製程中管制
  • Understand BFS (Blow-Fill-Seal) technology: process steps, advantages, limitations, and facility design considerations / 了解 BFS（吹瓶-充填-密封）技術：製程步驟、優缺點及設施設計考量
  • Describe lyophilization equipment selection, loading/unloading systems, CIP/SIP requirements, and production capacity planning / 說明凍乾設備選型、進出料系統、CIP/SIP 要求及產能規劃
  • Know container closure system types, CCI lifecycle approach, and CCIT methods / 了解容器密封系統類型、CCI 生命週期方法及完整性測試方法
  • Understand vial capping/crimping operations, PAT applications, and particulate control / 理解鋁蓋壓封作業、PAT 應用及微粒控制

Section Navigation / 章節導覽

3.2.4 Sterile Filtration Bulk Product Holding Container Preparation Closure Preparation Filling & Sealing BFS Technology 3.2.5 Lyophilization 3.2.6 Container Closure Systems CCIT Methods Vial Capping/Crimping Section Summary
3.2.4 Sterile Filtration 3.2.4 無菌過濾

Original Text

Sterile filtration is a mode of sterilization for solutions that can be used when the solution cannot be subjected to terminal sterilization in its final container/closure system. The process provides a defined reduction in the microbiological load of the feed solution and is intended to render the solution sterile. Sterile filtration has a limited effect on endotoxin reduction, so it is necessary to ensure that the upstream solution has a low bioburden to minimize the formation of endotoxins.

Solutions sterilized by filtration are subsequently processed aseptically by formulation and/or filling operations. The final filtration should occur as close as possible to the point of formulation or filling.

Any aqueous solution destined for terminal sterilization should also be pre-filtered, preferably through a sterilizing grade filter, prior to the terminal sterilization step to remove both bioburden and particulate.

The filtration train and associated vessels and piping network can be prepared in three ways:

  • Aseptically Assembled Multi-Use Systems: Associated with older facilities. Components are cleaned, rinsed, autoclaved, and carefully assembled within ISO 5/Grade A environment using full aseptic handling techniques. Can be closed (no exposure) or open (limited exposure). Declining use as older equipment is replaced.
  • Sterilize-in-Place (SIP) Multi-Use Systems: Usually preferred over aseptically assembled systems, often applied to larger scale operations. Vessels, pipes, and components are cleaned and assembled under clean conditions (ISO 7/Grade B), then the closed system is SIP using clean/pure steam. Alternatively, systems can be CIP and SIP in ISO 8/Grade C.
  • Pre-Sterilized Single-Use Systems: Assembled under clean conditions, placed in protective barrier (e.g., double bagged), sterilized via gamma irradiation. Transferred to ISO 5/Grade A filling area when needed. Equipped with proprietary aseptic connection devices. Benefits include elimination of cleaning/cleaning validation, elimination of SIP, advantages for potent compounds, and ability to stockpile inventory.

In general, reusable product contacting equipment should be product dedicated to reduce cross-contamination risk. If not possible, multi-product contact equipment should be supported by risk assessment and a robust cleaning validation program.

Key design considerations for sterile filtration systems:

  • Sterile filtration should be used only when terminal sterilization cannot be applied.
  • Interaction between sterilizing filter and product should be evaluated (extractables/leachables, chemical compatibility, adsorption).
  • A sterilizing filter should be validated for microbial retention using appropriate challenge microorganisms under worst case processing conditions.
  • Filtration through two sterilizing grade filters in series (redundant filtration) may be appropriate to reduce chance of batch sterilization failure.
  • Integrity of sterilizing filter membrane should be confirmed both prior to and following use by validated test methods (bubble point, diffusion/forward flow, or water intrusion).
  • Sterile vent filters should be checked for integrity post-use and, as a risk mitigation step, pre-use.
  • For pressure rated systems, a pressure hold/decay test should be applied to the assembled system prior to sterilization.
  • Where drain lines are connected, barrier arrangements including valves and air breaks should be provided to minimize back siphoning risk.
Note: The risk assessment for pre-use integrity testing should include whether testing is performed prior to or following sterilization of the filter. EU Annex 1 recommends testing prior to sterilization to avoid non-detection of a compromised filter element. However, this operation has the potential to compromise sterility of the downstream product pathway. Proper system design with redundant filter elements and pre-sterilization integrity testing can minimize both risks.

導師解析

核心概念：無菌過濾的三大系統組態

製藥產業中，無菌過濾系統可分為三大類：

  1. 無菌組裝式多用系統（舊式）：各元件分別清洗、滅菌後，在 ISO 5/Grade A 環境下手動組裝。風險高，正逐步淘汰。
  2. SIP 多用系統（主流）：組裝後封閉系統直接通入純蒸汽進行就地滅菌，無需打開連接點，大幅降低人為污染風險。
  3. 預滅菌單次使用系統（趨勢）：免洗免 SIP，伽馬射線滅菌後直接使用。特別適合高效藥物（potent compounds）及 CDMO 多品項切換。

選擇依據：生產規模、產品數量、廠房新舊及法規市場要求。

重點提示：冗餘過濾與完整性測試

冗餘過濾（Redundant Filtration）是在過濾路徑中串聯兩個滅菌級濾膜，當其中一個膜失效時，另一個仍能提供無菌保障。這是無菌製程的安全網。

濾膜完整性測試是法規強制要求：

  • 使用前測試（Pre-use）：確認濾膜安裝正確且無瑕疵
  • 使用後測試（Post-use）：確認過濾過程中濾膜未受損
  • 測試方法：泡點測試（Bubble Point）、擴散流（Forward Flow）、水侵入（Water Intrusion）

EU Annex 1 建議在滅菌前進行完整性測試，但這可能破壞下游無菌路徑的滅菌狀態——因此需要透過冗餘設計來兼顧兩個風險。

比喻說明：無菌過濾如同淨水系統

想像家用淨水器有三種安裝方式：(1) 每次使用前拆開清洗再組裝；(2) 安裝好後用蒸汽消毒，不用拆開；(3) 直接買全新密封的濾芯插上去用完即丟。

製藥無菌過濾的三種系統也是相同邏輯——從費工高風險的手動組裝，到免洗免消毒的一次性系統，技術演進方向就是「減少人為操作、降低污染風險」。

CDMO 實務觀點

CDMO 需處理多種不同產品，單次使用系統的優勢特別明顯：

  • 免除跨產品清潔驗證的巨大負擔
  • 消除殘留交叉污染風險
  • 可預先建立庫存，縮短換線時間
  • 特別適合小批量、高價值的生物製劑生產
Bulk Product Holding / 散裝產品靜置保存

Original Text

Following compounding, and prior to any filtration process, a solution should be held under conditions designed to protect the solution from contamination from the surrounding environment. The maximum time that a solution can be held under these conditions without risk of increased bioburden should be validated. It is recommended that solutions proceed through a filtration step as soon as possible following compounding to minimize contamination risk. Sustained validated hold periods should only be used by exception. Bioburden sampling of the unfiltered bulk should occur after any holding period, prior to filtration, as a process control step.

In some circumstances, it is necessary to sterilize a solution by filtration into a holding tank, hold it as sterile bulk, and then feed the filling machine from the holding tank without further filtration. If product is held in this way, it should be verified that product integrity is not compromised during the maximum holding time. The holding tank should be maintained at an overpressure with continuous monitoring to ensure that no ingress from the surrounding environment is possible, unless there are safety or product stability considerations which prevent this. This approach may also be used as a pre-filtration or bioburden reduction step where the product is filtered a second time during the filling process.

導師解析

重點提示：Hold Time 驗證是法規稽查重點

散裝藥液的「保存時間限制」是製程驗證中經常被稽查員關注的項目：

  • 過濾前保存（Pre-filtration hold）：驗證在最長保存時間內，生物負載不會超過可接受限度
  • 過濾後無菌保存（Post-filtration sterile hold）：持續正壓監控，確保外部微生物無法進入
  • 生物負載取樣必須在保存期結束後、過濾前進行——這是製程控制步驟

原則是「儘快過濾」，延長保存只能作為例外情況使用。

比喻說明：正壓保護如同氣球防塵

無菌散裝儲罐維持正壓，就像一個充飽氣的氣球——因為內部壓力大於外部，空氣只會從裡面往外跑，灰塵和細菌無法「逆流」進入。一旦正壓消失，就像氣球洩了氣，外部污染物就能輕易侵入。

Container Preparation / 容器準備

Original Text

Container preparation involves the cleaning, sterilization, and depyrogenation (applicable for parenteral products) of the empty product containers. There are four forms of contamination which container preparation processes should control:

  • Bioburden: Viable microbiological counts, as quantified in Colony Forming Units (CFU)
  • Endotoxin: Pyrogenic cell wall material resulting from growth and degradation of gram negative microorganisms
  • Extraneous Particulates: Solid particulate matter, sometimes resulting from container manufacturing, packing, and staging processes (e.g., glass fragments)
  • Extraneous Chemicals: Contamination with chemicals that are not part of the product formulation

Washing and rinsing processes should be designed to effectively remove extraneous particulates and chemicals. Such processes should also be capable of significantly reducing any bioburden or endotoxin contamination. Any remaining bioburden is then inactivated and endotoxins degraded by subjecting the containers to dry heat depyrogenation. For containers that cannot be depyrogenated (e.g., plastic), endotoxin reduction is dependent upon the washing and rinsing process.

Washing Machine Design Considerations:

  • Alarms for low/high pressure and low/high temperature
  • Use of WFI for the final wash step
  • Easy draining, cleaning, and drying of equipment and pipes, with appropriate gradients and drains
  • Whether the washing machine is equipped with an ultrasonic bath
  • Post-wash drying with air passed through a sterilizing grade filter
  • Protection of washed components prior to depyrogenation phase
  • Sampling points to aid in qualification/validation
  • Air breaks at washer drain to prevent back flow

Depyrogenation Tunnel Design:

Modern depyrogenation tunnels are designed with UAF and should be provided with heat-up, dwell, and cool-down zones. The combination of residence time and set point temperature, commonly 250°C (482°F) to 350°C (662°F), in the dwell zone should achieve the required degree of depyrogenation. Residence time is typically controlled by belt speed.

Containers should exit the tunnel via a cooling zone to reach a sufficiently low temperature to avoid affecting either the product when filled, or adversely deflecting the protecting UAF over the exit conveyor.

Depyrogenation tunnel design considerations:

  • Filter quality and construction of gaskets for high temperature air filters (non-shedding at higher than expected use temperatures)
  • Alarms and data recording for critical measurements (temperature, air speed, belt speed, pressure between cooling zone and surrounding area)
  • Design of building HVAC system to accommodate sensible heat emission to surrounding cleanroom
  • Sterilization and performance needs of the cooling zone
  • ISO 5/Grade A environment in the cooling zone
  • Integration with upstream and downstream equipment

Ready-to-Use Containers: Pre-sterilized and pre-depyrogenated containers reduce complexity of facility design. Advantageous for small batch/low volume operations. Supplied in wrapped tub/nest configuration interfacing with loading/unwrapping system. Each batch accompanied by Certificate of Conformance/Analysis.

導師解析

核心概念：容器準備的四大污染控制

注射劑容器在使用前必須控制四類污染：

  1. 生物負載（Bioburden）：活的微生物，以 CFU 計量
  2. 內毒素（Endotoxin）：革蘭氏陰性菌的細胞壁碎片，即使細菌死了，內毒素仍會引發發熱反應
  3. 外來微粒（Particulates）：玻璃碎片、纖維等固體微粒
  4. 外來化學物質（Chemicals）：非產品配方的化學殘留

清洗去除微粒和化學物質，去熱原隧道用高溫破壞內毒素並滅菌——兩步缺一不可。

重點提示：去熱原隧道的三區設計

去熱原隧道分為三個功能區域：

  • 升溫區（Heat-up Zone）：容器從室溫逐漸加熱
  • 恆溫區（Dwell Zone）：維持 250–350°C，停留足夠時間以達到至少 3-log 內毒素降低
  • 冷卻區（Cool-down Zone）：必須是 ISO 5/Grade A 環境，冷卻至不影響產品的溫度

隧道的壓差平衡至關重要——必須在充填室（ISO 5）和洗瓶室（ISO 8）之間維持正確的壓差梯度。

比喻說明：去熱原隧道像烤箱輸送帶

想像一條連續式烤箱輸送帶：玻璃瓶從一端進入，先經過預熱段，然後在超高溫段被「烤」到 250–350°C（這個溫度足以摧毀所有內毒素），最後通過冷卻段降溫。整個過程全自動、連續運行，瓶子排隊通過就像生產線上的產品一樣。

CDMO 實務：即用型容器 (RTU) 的趨勢

預洗預滅菌的即用型容器（RTU, Ready-to-Use）正在迅速改變 CDMO 設施設計：

  • 免除洗瓶機和去熱原隧道的資本投資
  • 大幅減少潔淨室面積需求
  • 降低公用工程（WFI、壓縮空氣、HVAC 散熱）的負荷
  • 特別適合小批量、高價值產品及臨床試驗階段

但需注意：必須稽核供應商的品質系統，每批需附合格證明（Certificate of Conformance）。

練習思考

  1. 為什麼塑膠容器無法使用去熱原隧道？這對內毒素控制策略有何影響？
  2. 去熱原隧道冷卻區失壓時，為什麼需要對冷卻區表面進行乾熱滅菌？
Closure Preparation / 膠塞準備

Original Text

As the closure (e.g., stopper) will be in direct contact with the product at some time during storage/handling/use, it should be sterile, free from foreign contaminants, and essentially free of endotoxins.

Manufacturers should determine the nature and extent of contaminants normally found on closures when received from a supplier. The washing process should be qualified to remove these contaminants, including endotoxins, to an acceptable level.

Washers should use hydraulic or mechanical agitation to dislodge attached particulate matter and to remove such debris without re-deposition onto another portion of the load. WFI should be used for rinsing closures. A cleaning agent or detergent wash may be used for endotoxin load reduction. Use of a cleaning agent or detergent may impact stopper machineability. Siliconization may also be required, in limited instances, for machineability.

Washing should be followed by sterilization and drying. This should be achieved by minimizing the time that closures are held in the wet condition, so that they can be sterilized and dried in a nominal time period, without intermediate handling. For lyophilized products, the final moisture content of the stoppers should be considered when designing and validating a sterilization process.

Ready-to-use (e.g., pre-sterilized) or ready-to-sterilize (e.g., pre-washed) closures may be used with the same benefits and considerations discussed for containers.

導師解析

核心概念：膠塞處理的完整流程

膠塞（Stopper）直接接觸產品，品質要求極高：

  1. 清洗：以水力或機械攪動去除微粒，避免再沉積（re-deposition）
  2. 最終沖洗：必須使用 WFI（注射用水）
  3. 滅菌與乾燥：清洗後儘快完成，避免濕態長時間保存滋生微生物

重點提示：凍乾產品的膠塞水分控制

對於凍乾產品，膠塞的殘留水分至關重要。滅菌後膠塞中殘留的水分可能在凍乾過程中釋放，影響產品的最終含水量和穩定性。因此，膠塞滅菌製程的設計必須同時考慮滅菌效力和乾燥效果。

這是凍乾產品特有的驗證挑戰：需要證明膠塞水分不會影響產品 CQA（關鍵品質屬性）。

即用型膠塞（RTU Closures）

與即用型容器相同的趨勢，預洗預滅菌的膠塞正在被廣泛採用：

  • Ready-to-Sterilize（預洗型）：供應商完成清洗，用戶只需滅菌
  • Ready-to-Use（即用型）：供應商完成清洗和滅菌，用戶直接使用

對 CDMO 而言，這進一步簡化了設施需求並縮短了換線時間。

Filling and Sealing / 充填與密封

Original Text

During filling, the product is dosed into containers and then sealed. For aseptically processed products, the containers, closures, and product should be sterile prior to filling. Filling is a critical operation, particularly for an aseptically filled product, as it often is the only operation following sterile filtration in which the product and product contact surfaces are exposed to an open environment. Aseptic filling should be performed within an ISO 5/Grade A environment.

Liquid filling is usually achieved by one of three methods:

  • Fixed volume stroke piston pumps (e.g., liquid sealed and rolling diaphragm)
  • Time-pressure system: Controlled overpressure applied to a pilot filling vessel, opened to filling needles for a fixed time. Combination of opening time and overpressure control the fill volume.
  • Peristaltic pumps with flexible tubing

A system with automatic adjustment of the filling volume via feedback from a statistical or 100% (non-destructive) in-process check-weighing system is recommended.

After filling, the vial headspace may be purged with sterile nitrogen or other qualified non-reactive gas to displace atmospheric gases to pre-defined limits. This technique is commonly used for products sensitive to oxygen.

Design considerations for aseptic filling machines:

  • The machine should be sited within an ISO 5/Grade A RABS or isolator to minimize operator contact with product, product contact surfaces, and containers/closures.
  • Container closure contact surfaces should be constructed of stainless steel, of suitable design and finish to withstand cleaning and sterilization.
  • Design should allow introduction of sterile container-closure components into the critical zone without compromising sterile integrity.
  • Design should permit easy access for cleaning and disinfection with absence of crevices or niches where contamination may accumulate. Threaded fittings should be avoided.
  • Equipment should be suitable for delivering product into the container with fill accuracy assurance.
  • Moving parts and lubricating fluids within ISO 5/Grade A should be minimized. Lubricants should be evaluated and purchased sterile or sterilized (e.g., gamma irradiation).
  • Design for easy changeover between batches and container/closure configurations.
  • IPC samples should be removable or testable (check-weigh) without interrupting line operation.
  • Critical area should support optimal UAF pattern to prevent contamination.
  • RABS doors and machine guards should prevent particulate contamination when manipulated. Access doors should be interlocked to automatically shut down filling operations when opened.
  • Equipment should be installed to allow inherent intervention and maintenance from outside critical zones.
  • Design with consideration to operator ergonomics for line setup and corrective intervention.
  • Design for ease of setup (tool-less), to minimize post-sterilization assembly activities and eliminate manual contacting of sterile processing contact surfaces.
  • Operator interface should be restricted, preferably using glove port access.
  • Stopper hoppers should be designed to prevent particulate contamination. 316L stainless steel or non-shedding, robust materials recommended.
  • Stopper bowls and delivery chutes that cannot be SIP should be easily demountable for autoclaving. If closed isolator technology is used with VHP decontamination, this can also decontaminate indirect product contact parts. A thorough cleaning step should be applied to remove potential silicone layers from vibrating siliconized stoppers.
  • Barrier enclosure should permit transfer of sterilized components while maintaining ISO 5/Grade A continuity.
  • Transport belts or cassette/tray loading systems should be protected under ISO 5/Grade A UAF until vials are loaded in the lyophilizer.
  • Filling and sealing of potent/hazardous compounds may require special air exhaust or particulate capture systems for operator safety.

For lyophilized products, stoppers are not fully seated to enable solvent escape during sublimation and desorption. The stoppering tool height should be pre-adjusted for consistent stopper positioning.

Glass ampoules should be sealed by application of heat (gas flame jet or laser) under ISO 5/Grade A conditions. Note: Sealing of ampoules generates high levels of particulates, removed via active exhaust/vacuum utilities with non-return systems.

導師解析

核心概念：充填是無菌製程的最高風險環節

充填是產品在無菌過濾後唯一暴露在開放環境中的操作。這就是為什麼：

  • 必須在 ISO 5/Grade A 環境下進行
  • 必須使用 RABS 或隔離器
  • 必須最大限度減少人員介入
  • 任何中斷（intervention）都必須被記錄和評估

設計要點清單：充填機的 16 項關鍵考量

本節列出的充填機設計要求可歸納為五大原則：

  1. 隔離原則：RABS/隔離器隔離人員、手套埠操作、門互鎖
  2. 可清潔原則：無縫隙、無螺紋連接、316L 不鏽鋼、可拆卸高壓滅菌
  3. 單向氣流原則：最佳 UAF 氣流模式、微粒排出設計
  4. 快速換線原則：免工具設計、最少組裝步驟、預滅菌組件
  5. 製程控制原則：IPC 取樣不中斷、秤重系統、氮氣置換

比喻說明：充填機像手術室中的手術台

充填機所在的 ISO 5 環境就像手術室裡的無菌區：手術刀（充填針）、手術台（充填工位）和所有接觸組織的器械（產品接觸面）都必須滅菌。外科醫生透過手套操作（glove port），護士從外部傳遞器械（barrier transfer），整個過程中空調系統維持正壓和單向氣流以排除微粒。

凍乾產品的膠塞半插設計

凍乾產品的膠塞在充填後不會完全壓入瓶口，而是「半插」（partially seated）。這是因為凍乾過程中，溶劑需要從瓶口逸出（昇華和解吸階段）。凍乾完成後，凍乾機的層板下壓將膠塞完全壓入瓶中。

從充填機到凍乾機之間，這些半插膠塞的瓶子必須全程在 ISO 5/Grade A 環境下受保護——這是設施佈局設計的關鍵考量。

重點提示：三種充填方式的比較

無論哪種方式，都建議配備自動秤重反饋系統（check-weighing），實現充填量的即時監控和調整。

Blow, Fill, and Seal (BFS) Technology / 吹瓶-充填-密封技術

Original Text

An alternative technique to filling in a pre-formed container is to use BFS technology. BFS technology is the integration of plastic blow molding and aseptic filling on a single machine where the container is created by the machine just prior to filling. Use of a BFS process generally replaces the steps for container and stopper preparation.

The BFS process consists of the following steps:

  1. Dry heat extrusion of plastic into a parison (i.e., molten tube)
  2. Forming of the container in the mold
  3. Filling the container with product
  4. Insertion of a pre-sterilized component, if applicable
  5. Sealing the container
  6. Trimming the container and conveyance to the inspection area

Advantages of BFS:

  • Exposure of container to environment is very short compared to conventional filling
  • Capable of continuously filling for extended durations (>120 hours) for large batch sizes
  • Reduced requirements for adjacent manufacturing support space
  • Fully automated with restricted access design, minimizing operator presence
  • Wide variety of container designs and sizes (0.25 mL to 1 L or larger)

Limitations and special considerations:

  • May not be compatible with heat or oxygen sensitive products. Plastic extrusion temperatures generally exceed 150°C and most plastics are gas permeable.
  • Requires special operator training.
  • Output speed slower than conventional fill lines.
  • Risk of leachables from plastic and/or secondary packaging materials.

Two machine design types:

  • Open Parison (Shuttle Type): Molds move between parison formation zone and aseptic fill zone. Hot or ultrasonic knife cuts parison each cycle. More flexible for product changeover, suited for smaller batches, only type capable of component insertion.
  • Closed Parison (Rotary/Reciprocating): Molds indexed beneath parison formation zone. Filling nozzles integrated with parison head. Higher output capacity. Larger footprint. Significantly reduced plastic waste stream.

Facility design considerations for BFS:

  • Ventilation must cope with particles generated by the filling machine and heat load from extrusion area. A grey side/white side approach may improve mechanical access and heat distribution.
  • Multiple plastic types available (low/high density polyethylene, polypropylene). Polypropylene and special grades of polyethylene amenable to terminal sterilization.
  • Extrusion process should be evaluated for sterilizing polymer and reducing endotoxin.
  • Best suited for high volume products with large batch sizes and long filling durations.
  • Continuous waste stream of plastic needs to be transferred out of manufacturing space.
  • Storage space for raw plastic granulate should be allocated.
  • Care should be taken to ensure upstream process does not promote microbiological growth in bulk product, as fill duration is usually longer than ordinary filling machines.
  • Sealed containers should be leak tested following deflashing (removal of excess plastic). Typical technology: vacuum decay and high voltage. Some markets require 100% testing.
  • Consideration for downstream processing needs (ampoule separation, overwrapping).

導師解析

核心概念：BFS 一體成型的革命性設計

BFS 技術將三個傳統上分離的步驟整合在一台機器上：

  1. 吹瓶（Blow）：塑膠粒經高溫擠出成為管狀（parison），再吹模成型為容器
  2. 充填（Fill）：成型後立即充填產品
  3. 密封（Seal）：充填後立即熱封密封

整個過程中，容器暴露在環境中的時間極短，大幅降低污染風險。

比喻說明：BFS 像自動包裝冰棒的機器

傳統充填像是先買好空瓶、洗瓶、消毒、再灌裝液體、再蓋蓋子——每一步都有污染風險。BFS 就像自動冰棒包裝機：塑膠管加熱融化、吹成容器形狀、立刻灌入液體、瞬間熱封——從無到有一氣呵成，容器幾乎沒有機會接觸外界環境。

設施設計挑戰：BFS 的「灰區/白區」概念

BFS 機器的擠出區產生大量熱量和塑膠微粒。解決方案是將機器分為兩側：

  • 白區（White Side）：充填和成型區域，維持潔淨環境
  • 灰區（Grey Side）：機械系統區域，便於維護和散熱

這種設計透過實體牆將兩個區域分隔，既保護了無菌充填區，又方便了設備維護。HVAC 系統必須能夠應對擠出區產生的巨大熱負荷。

CDMO 實務：BFS 的定位

BFS 最適合大批量、長時間連續充填的產品（如眼藥水、吸入劑、小容量注射液）。對 CDMO 而言：

  • 高初期投資但營運成本低
  • 免除容器和膠塞準備的整條生產線
  • 需要注意可萃取物/浸出物（E&L）的評估
  • 不適合需要凍乾的產品或對溫度/氧氣極敏感的生物製劑
3.2.5 Lyophilization / 凍乾（冷凍乾燥）

Original Text

The lyophilization process, also known as freeze drying, is completed to enhance product stability in the dry state.

Lyophilization consists of three distinct phases:

  1. Freezing
  2. Sublimation or primary drying
  3. Desorption or secondary drying

The total sequence of operations (15 steps):

  1. Pre-use cleaning of chamber
  2. Sterilization of chamber
  3. Shelf cooling
  4. System leak testing
  5. Loading
  6. Freezing
  7. Sublimation/primary drying
  8. Desorption/secondary drying
  9. Backfill
  10. Stoppering
  11. Aeration
  12. Unloading
  13. Defrosting
  14. Post-use cleaning/CIP
  15. Filter integrity testing

Loading Systems: Systems vary from manual tray-by-tray loading, through semi-automatic loading, to fully automatic loading (with simultaneous insertion of pre-loaded group of trays or sequential layer-by-layer loading with automatic tray lifter). Automated loading devices represent the method of choice. The system should ensure that the ISO 5/Grade A environment where partially stoppered vials are exposed is fully protected from the surrounding cleanroom. Barrier technology should be considered for operator segregation during loading.

Selection of loading/unloading method should consider:

  • Type of barrier technology selected
  • Lyophilizer/batch size
  • Lyophilizer configuration (single side load/unload or pass-through type)
  • Number of lyophilizers to be installed
  • Loading with frames or frameless loading

Lyophilizer specification data requirements:

  • Ability to effectively clean and sterilize the chamber and condenser on a routine basis
  • Detailed process cycle for each product: product type, density, eutectic/glass transition point, time and temperatures for all phases, vacuum level, chamber stoppering pressure, and vapor flux
  • Product container data (size, filling quantity)
  • Maximum ice load/condenser capacity, temperature, and surface area
  • Freezing rate of the product
  • System leak rate (typically validated via aseptic process simulation studies)
  • Batch size

A lyophilizer may be the bottleneck of the production chain, due to the extended time required for freeze drying. Selection of lyophilizer size, based on batch sizes, product mix, and expected line usage, is fundamental to overall production yield. Two or more freeze dryers may be required to fully utilize the capacity of a filling line.

Care should be taken to optimize the lyophilization cycle early in the development process, due to the large impact on facility production capacity.

Additional specification data:

  • Type of refrigeration system (compressors or liquid nitrogen)
  • Process control system and parameters to be controlled/monitored
  • Number and type of doors (single or pass-through)
  • Door closing system
  • Cleaning and sterilization requirements
  • Use of a capper dedicated to lyophilizer products, to avoid impact on processing of liquid products

Cleaning and Sterilization: Required between each batch. Most common medium is moist heat.

Advantages of moist heat: easily available, easy to monitor, highly penetrating, easy to distribute uniformly, non-hazardous if traces remain.

Disadvantages of moist heat: need to reach high temperatures and pressures with saturated steam, time required for cooling, potential thermo-mechanical stress on system leak rate, potential effect of residual moisture on leak testing.

VHP for lyophilizer decontamination has been applied and validated for small and commercial scale units. Particularly suitable for laboratory scale units or retrofit to older commercial units not pressure rated. To date, VHP decontamination has seen limited commercial scale application.

All moving parts should be correctly sterilized with sterility maintained during all process steps (e.g., sterile bellows enclosing stoppering pistons), including effective sterilization of shelf support columns, rams, gas lines, condenser, and the system used to seal containers.

The lyophilizer construction will be in a state of mechanical stress due to the wide range of temperatures and pressures during operation. This may increase the risk of leakage over time, emphasizing the importance of an effective preventative maintenance and equipment inspection program.

導師解析

核心概念：凍乾的三階段與 15 步操作序列

凍乾的核心目的是提高產品在乾燥狀態下的穩定性。三個關鍵階段：

  1. 冷凍（Freezing）：將產品降溫至共熔點/玻璃轉化溫度以下，使水分結冰
  2. 昇華/初級乾燥（Primary Drying）：在真空條件下，冰直接昇華為水蒸氣，被冷凝器捕捉
  3. 解吸/二級乾燥（Secondary Drying）：移除結合水，進一步降低含水量至目標值

但完整的操作序列遠不止這三步——從清洗、滅菌、冷卻、洩漏測試到裝載、凍乾、出料、除霜、清洗，共 15 個步驟。

重點提示：凍乾機是產線瓶頸

凍乾是整條無菌充填線中最耗時的環節，一個凍乾週期可能需要 24–72 小時甚至更長。因此：

  • 凍乾機大小的選擇直接決定整條產線的產出效率
  • 通常需要 2 台或更多凍乾機來匹配一條充填線的產能
  • 計算產能時必須考慮完整週期時間（含清洗、滅菌、除霜、維護保養）
  • 凍乾製程優化應在開發早期完成，因為對產能影響巨大

比喻說明：凍乾機像太空級冷凍乾燥機

想像一台巨型太空食品乾燥機：先將食物急速冷凍，然後在極低壓的真空中，冰晶不經過液態直接「蒸發」（昇華）。最後的產品像是一塊海綿狀的乾燥餅，加水後可以恢復原狀。不同的是，製藥用凍乾機必須在無菌條件下操作，而且每批之間必須完全清洗和滅菌。

進出料系統：從手動到全自動的演進

凍乾機的裝載（loading）和卸載（unloading）是無菌製程中的高風險環節：

  • 手動裝載：操作員逐盤放入，風險最高
  • 半自動裝載：部分自動化，減少人為操作
  • 全自動裝載：自動托盤預裝 + 同步送入，或逐層堆疊 + 自動升降器

全自動系統是首選，尤其當同一套自動化系統能服務多台凍乾機時，產能利用率最高。

重點提示：凍乾機的清洗與滅菌挑戰

濕熱滅菌（蒸汽）是最常用的方法，但有其挑戰：

  • 需要達到高溫高壓——凍乾機的設計必須能承受壓力容器等級
  • 冷卻耗時——增加了批間轉換時間
  • 熱膨脹-收縮的機械應力可能導致密封墊劣化，增加洩漏風險
  • 殘留水分可能影響後續的洩漏率測試

VHP 除污是新興替代方案，特別適合無法承受壓力的舊式設備或小型實驗室設備，但商業規模應用仍然有限。

CDMO 實務：凍乾機是最昂貴的單一設備

對 CDMO 而言，凍乾機的投資決策是最具策略性的設備選擇之一：

  • 一台商業級凍乾機的成本可達數百萬美元
  • 配置錯誤（太大或太小）直接影響數年的營收
  • Pass-through 設計（穿透式）可分隔裝載側和卸載側的潔淨等級
  • 自動裝卸系統的投資回收期通常在 2–3 年內
  • 凍乾週期優化對產能影響極大——縮短 10% 的週期時間可能增加 10% 以上的年產能

練習思考

  1. 一條充填線的充填速度是每小時 10,000 瓶，凍乾週期需要 48 小時，每台凍乾機可裝載 50,000 瓶。若要維持充填線不停機，至少需要幾台凍乾機？
  2. 為什麼 ISPE 建議在開發早期就優化凍乾製程？這與設施設計有什麼關係？
  3. VHP 除污為什麼特別適合舊式凍乾機？它的限制是什麼？

凍乾機規格選定的關鍵參數

正確規格化凍乾機需要的製程數據包括：

3.2.6 Container Closure Systems / 容器密封系統

Original Text

There are various container closure systems routinely used for small volume parenteral drugs and biologics, including ampoules, BFS containers, vials, syringes and cartridges. These containers are sealed either by fusion (ampoules and BFS containers) or through use of an elastomeric closure (syringes, cartridges, and vials). In the case of vials or cartridges, the elastomeric seal may be combined with an aluminum or plastic cap/crimp seal for final package sealing.

The objective of any container/closure system is to maintain product quality attributes of sterility and physiochemical stability through expiry. Container closure systems should be fully validated to ensure that these objectives are met; that is, the container closure system has the necessary Container Closure Integrity (CCI).

Development and subsequent production of primary packaging having adequate CCI requires a lifecycle approach that includes the following phases:

  • Package development, package processing and assembly validation
  • Product manufacturing
  • Commercial product shelf life stability assessments

Package development includes selection of appropriate and compatible primary packaging components that, when assembled or sealed under defined operating conditions, provide the necessary CCI. CPPs, as required to ensure CCI, should be defined.

In the product manufacturing phase, CPPs are measured and controlled to ensure consistent product quality. Several test methods are suitable for in-process (statistical) or 100% basis inspection.

In the final lifecycle phase, commercial product shelf life stability assessments are performed to monitor package performance over the shelf life of the product.

Note: Each specific container/closure system behaves differently and should be validated separately. For example, independent testing should be performed for each combination of two different stoppers (different formulation and/or configuration) with a single vial.

Containers closed by fusion (ampoules and BFS containers) comprise less complex packaging systems since a single material is used to form and seal the container.

Regulatory requirements for inspection:

  • EU Annex 1: "Containers closed by fusion, e.g., glass or plastic ampoules should be subject to 100% integrity testing. Samples of other containers should be checked for integrity according to appropriate procedures." Also: "Containers sealed under vacuum should be tested for maintenance of that vacuum after an appropriate, pre-determined period."
  • US FDA: "A container closure system that permits penetration of microorganisms is unsuitable for a sterile product. Any damaged or defective units should be detected, and removed, during inspection of the final sealed product."

導師解析

核心概念：容器密封完整性（CCI）生命週期

CCI 不是一次性的測試，而是一個貫穿產品生命週期的驗證體系：

  1. 開發階段：選擇相容的容器/膠塞/鋁蓋組合，定義 CPP，進行初始 CCI 測試
  2. 生產階段：監控和控制 CPP（如壓蓋力、膠塞壓縮量），進行統計取樣或 100% 檢查
  3. 安定性階段：長期穩定性試驗中監控密封完整性是否隨時間劣化

每一種容器/膠塞組合都需要獨立驗證——不同的膠塞配方或規格搭配同一種瓶子，CCI 表現可能完全不同。

重點提示：密封方式的兩大類別

  • 熔合密封（Fusion）：安瓿瓶和 BFS 容器——單一材料成型密封，系統較簡單，但 EU Annex 1 要求 100% 完整性檢查
  • 彈性體密封（Elastomeric）：西林瓶、預填充注射器、卡式瓶——使用膠塞 + 鋁蓋壓封，涉及多個組件的介面，系統較複雜

美國 FDA 和歐盟 EMA 均認為：西林瓶在鋁蓋壓封完成前，密封系統不算完整。這一立場直接影響了壓蓋區的環境等級要求。

比喻說明：CCI 如同保溫瓶的密封

容器密封完整性就像保溫瓶的蓋子——不管保溫瓶做得多好，如果蓋子沒蓋緊，熱量就會散失（無菌性喪失）。CCI 的生命週期方法就是確保：蓋子選得對（開發）、每次都蓋好（生產）、放久了也不會鬆（穩定性）。

Container Closure Integrity Test Methods / 容器密封完整性測試方法

Original Text

A variety of tests are available to measure container closure integrity. Table 3.1 shows these tests and general applicability:

[ND] = Non-Destructive, [D] = Destructive

Selection considerations:

  • HVLD may not be suitable for products with very low conductivity (e.g., WFI).
  • RSF monitoring is specific to vials with elastomeric seals and caps.
  • Product CQAs may include maintenance of headspace conditions (inert gassing or vacuum). In such cases, in-process headspace gas analyzer or 100% laser-based HSA may be appropriate.
  • Selection should consider PAT to monitor and control CPPs in conjunction with appropriate inspection methods.
  • Following a risk-based approach, use of PAT may eliminate or reduce inspection requirements.

導師解析

核心概念：CCIT 方法的三層應用

CCI 測試方法按應用場景分為三層：

  1. 開發階段測試：所有方法都適用——建立密封完整性的基線數據和接受標準
  2. 製程中測試：只有非破壞性方法（RSF 例外）適用——取樣監控
  3. 100% 在線檢查：僅少數非破壞性方法（HVLD、HSA、真空/壓力衰減、氣體電離）適用——全數檢查

實務選擇指南

選擇 CCIT 方法時需考慮：

  • 容器類型（安瓿、西林瓶、預充填注射器各適合不同方法）
  • 產品特性（導電性、頂空要求、穩定性）
  • 設備通量（是否需要匹配充填線速度）
  • 法規市場要求（部分市場要求 100% 檢查）
  • 洩漏偵測靈敏度（不同方法的偵測下限不同）

重點提示：關鍵 CCIT 方法解析

PAT（製程分析技術）的應用趨勢：透過持續監控 CPP 來降低或取消抽樣檢查需求。

Vial Capping/Crimping / 西林瓶壓蓋/壓封

Original Text

For vials, two cases frequently arise where transfer of the container and final sealing is performed:

  • Liquid vials: Aseptically filled and fully stoppered in ISO 5/Grade A environment, subsequently transferred out of aseptic zone for capping.
  • Lyophilized vials: Aseptically filled and partially stoppered on filling equipment, transferred to lyophilizer and loaded onto shelves. After lyophilization, containers are fully stoppered by collapsing shelves, then unloaded for capping.

Application of the crimp seal can be performed in the aseptic zone using sterilized caps or as a clean operation outside the aseptic core.

The US FDA and EMA do not consider the container closure system to be fully integral until the application of the crimp seal is complete. EU Annex 1 states: "The container closure system for aseptically filled vials is not fully integral until the aluminum cap has been crimped into place on the stoppered vial."

Therefore, additional measures to safeguard product sterility are required if capping is performed outside the aseptic zone:

  • Use of LP/GAAS (Laminar Protection / Grade A Air Supply) to safeguard the product from exit of aseptic zone until crimp seal is complete.
  • Use of raised/missing stopper detection systems for inspection prior to crimp seal. Non-conforming containers should be rejected prior to capping.

Raised/missing stopper detection systems: Can be laser or camera-based. Should detect skewed stoppers and evenly lifted stoppers by inspecting from at least 2 directions (typically 90° apart). Maximum allowable gap should be determined for each container/closure combination using suitable method (e.g., helium leak testing, HSA). More sensitive systems detect and measure the gap between container neck flange and bottom of stopper with 0.1mm resolution.

Recent PAT developments for capping:

  • Pneumatic application of pre-capping compression (centrally adjustable, continuous monitoring and alarming)
  • Compressive force confirmation via strain gauge
  • Monitoring of container rotation during capping (to detect slip)
  • Residual seal force testing (destructive for flip-off type seals)
  • Visual crimp inspection via camera-based systems (real-time quality monitoring)

Aluminum seal application steps:

  1. Seal placement on container by neck draw-off (cap chute) or pick-and-place mechanism
  2. Pre-sealing stopper compression via pneumatic or spring-loaded spindle
  3. Roll bottom edge of seal under container neck flange to maintain compressive force

Crimping mechanisms:

  • Jaw type crimping (smaller seals, lower speed)
  • Container rotation against fixed outer rail or inner disk
  • Container rotation about fixed idle roller(s)

For multi-head capping machines, controls should detect consecutive faults on a per-spindle basis. Sample sets should correspond to a defined capping spindle sequence.

During capping, mechanical working of the seal generates particulates. Proper airflow design should provide unidirectional flow to sweep particles away from critical zones. Particle generation may also cause cap discoloration, particularly with white flip seals.

導師解析

核心概念：壓蓋前的密封完整性風險

法規立場非常明確：西林瓶在鋁蓋壓封完成前，不被視為密封完整。這意味著：

  • 從充填區到壓蓋區之間的轉運過程中，產品處於「未完全密封」狀態
  • 必須使用 LP/GAAS（層流保護/Grade A 空氣供應）保護產品
  • 必須在壓蓋前進行膠塞偵測（raised/missing stopper detection）
  • 不合格品必須在壓蓋前被剔除

重點提示：膠塞偵測系統的精度要求

膠塞偵測系統必須能夠偵測：

  • 歪斜膠塞（Skewed stopper）：一側有縫隙、另一側正常
  • 整體上浮膠塞（Evenly lifted stopper）：膠塞均勻抬高
  • 必須從至少 2 個方向（通常 90° 夾角）進行檢查
  • 最靈敏的系統可偵測到 0.1mm 的間隙

每種容器/膠塞組合的「最大允許間隙」都必須透過適當方法（如氦氣洩漏測試、HSA）獨立確定。

壓蓋 PAT 技術五大進展

  1. 氣動預壓縮：取代彈簧，可集中調整、持續監控和警報
  2. 應變計確認：壓蓋過程中即時確認壓縮力
  3. 旋轉監測：偵測壓封時容器是否打滑（導致密封不良）
  4. 殘留密封力（RSF）測試：監控壓封後的殘餘壓縮力
  5. 視覺壓封檢查：攝像機即時檢查壓封外觀品質

這些 PAT 應用正在將壓蓋從「事後檢查」轉變為「即時控制」的製程。

重點提示：多頭壓蓋機的按主軸監控

多頭壓蓋機中，每個壓蓋頭（spindle）可能產生不同的缺陷模式。因此：

  • 控制系統必須能夠按單個主軸追蹤連續缺陷（如主軸 #1 連續出現 3 次缺陷）
  • 取樣組必須對應定義的主軸順序（如 1–12 號頭依序取樣）
  • 這與充填機按單個充填頭取樣的邏輯相同

比喻說明：壓蓋如同開瓶的逆向操作

想像用開瓶器開啤酒——壓蓋就是這個動作的逆向過程。鋁蓋被放在膠塞上方，先施加向下壓力確保膠塞緊貼瓶口，然後滾輪將鋁蓋邊緣捲入瓶頸凸緣下方鎖定。如果壓蓋時瓶子打滑（rotation），就像用開瓶器時瓶蓋歪了——密封就會失敗。

微粒管理：壓蓋區的特殊挑戰

壓蓋過程中金屬碾壓會產生大量微粒。如果壓蓋在 ISO 5/Grade A 環境內進行，微粒管理尤為重要：

  • 單向氣流設計必須將微粒從關鍵區域吹走
  • 需要調整風速、回風口位置，可能使用 RABS/隔離器內部隔板
  • 白色翻蓋特別容易因微粒而變色——需考慮蓋子顏色選擇和分選碗清潔頻率

練習思考

  1. 為什麼 EU Annex 1 認為西林瓶在壓蓋完成前不算「密封完整」？如果膠塞已經完全壓入，為什麼還不夠？
  2. 一台 12 頭壓蓋機中，3 號和 7 號頭各出現了 2 次連續缺陷。根據「按主軸監控」原則，你會採取什麼行動？
  3. 比較在無菌區內壓蓋和在無菌區外壓蓋的優缺點——各需要哪些額外措施？

Section Summary / 本章重點回顧

  • Sterile Filtration Systems (3.2.4): Three system configurations (aseptically assembled, SIP multi-use, pre-sterilized single-use) with a clear industry trend toward single-use systems. Redundant filtration and pre/post-use filter integrity testing are regulatory essentials. / 無菌過濾系統：三種組態從手動組裝到單次使用演進，冗餘過濾與完整性測試為法規基本要求。
  • Bulk Product Holding: Hold time validation is critical. Post-filtration sterile hold requires continuous overpressure monitoring. Minimize hold time; sustained holds are exceptions. / 散裝產品保存：保存時間驗證為稽查重點，無菌保存需持續正壓監控，原則上儘快過濾。
  • Container Preparation: Four contamination types to control (bioburden, endotoxin, particulates, chemicals). Washing + depyrogenation tunnel (250-350 deg C) for glass; RTU containers are an emerging CDMO trend. / 容器準備：控制四類污染，洗瓶 + 去熱原隧道為傳統方案，即用型容器為 CDMO 新趨勢。
  • Closure Preparation: WFI rinse mandatory, stopper moisture content critical for lyophilized products. RTU/RTS closures increasingly adopted. / 膠塞準備：WFI 沖洗為必要條件，凍乾產品特別注意膠塞含水量。
  • Filling and Sealing: Highest-risk step in aseptic processing. Three filling methods (piston, time-pressure, peristaltic). 16 key design considerations for filling machines centered on isolation, cleanability, UAF, quick changeover, and process control. / 充填與密封：無菌製程最高風險環節，充填機設計以隔離、可清潔、氣流、快換線、製程控制為五大原則。
  • BFS Technology: Integrates container forming, filling, and sealing in one machine. Two designs (shuttle vs. rotary). Best for high-volume continuous production; not suitable for lyophilized or heat-sensitive biologics. / BFS 技術：一體成型降低污染風險，適合大批量連續生產，不適用凍乾或熱敏生物製劑。
  • Lyophilization (3.2.5): Three-phase process (freezing, sublimation, desorption) with 15-step operational sequence. Lyophilizer is the production bottleneck and one of the most expensive equipment investments. Loading/unloading automation, CIP/SIP between batches, and cycle optimization are key design drivers. / 凍乾：三階段 15 步操作，凍乾機是產線瓶頸且為最昂貴設備投資，自動進出料和週期優化是設計核心。
  • Container Closure Systems (3.2.6): CCI requires lifecycle approach (development, manufacturing, stability). 10 CCIT methods with different applicability for development, in-process, and 100% inspection. / 容器密封系統：CCI 需生命週期驗證，10 種 CCIT 方法按場景分層應用。
  • Vial Capping/Crimping: Container not considered fully integral until crimp seal is complete (FDA/EMA). LP/GAAS and stopper detection required. Five PAT developments transforming capping from post-check to real-time control. / 壓蓋/壓封：法規認定壓蓋前密封不完整，需 LP/GAAS 和膠塞偵測，五項 PAT 進展推動即時控制。
2c

Chapter 2c: 3c. Process Equipment (3.2.7–3.2.9)

製程設備（中下） | p62-p72

ISPE Baseline Guide Vol. 3 (3rd Ed.) | p62 – p72

Learning Objectives / 學習目標

  • Understand the principles, process factors, and equipment types for terminal sterilization (moist heat, irradiation) / 了解最終滅菌的原理、製程因素及設備類型（濕熱、輻射等）
  • Distinguish overkill versus adjunct sterilization processes and their impact on facility design / 區分過度殺滅與輔助滅菌製程及其對設施設計的影響
  • Describe the regulatory basis and methods for visual inspection (manual, semi-automated, fully automated) / 說明目視檢查的法規基礎及各類方法（手動、半自動、全自動）
  • Explain the Knapp methodology and operator qualification requirements for inspection processes / 解釋 Knapp 方法學及檢查人員資格要求
  • Identify facility design considerations for inspection equipment, secondary packaging, and serialization / 確認檢查設備、二次包裝及序列化的設施設計考量

3.2.7 Terminal Sterilization / 最終滅菌

Original Text — ISPE Baseline Guide

3.2.7 Terminal Sterilization

Terminal sterilization refers to a process within which the product, filled and sealed in its final primary package, is sterilized via moist heat, irradiation, or other suitable method. It is a well-accepted principle that sterile drugs should be manufactured using aseptic processing only when terminal sterilization is not feasible due to instability in the drug formulation.

Design and qualification of terminal sterilization processes is a complex topic. For additional information, refer to USP <1229.2>.

Terminal sterilization can be undertaken as a full overkill process (F0 ≥ 15), or as an adjunct process (F0 ≥ 8) for products that cannot tolerate full overkill exposure. The endpoint objective of both processes is the same — to produce product having a Probability of a Non-Sterile Unit (PNSU) of ≥ 1 in 106. Pre-sterilization bioburden is reduced using validated methods and routinely monitored, in order to achieve this level of sterility assurance for the adjunct process.

Design Factors for Terminal Sterilization

Several factors should be considered when designing a terminal sterilization process:

  • D-value of target organisms: Many products exhibit a protective effect on challenge organisms, increasing the required target F0. This is particularly important for adjunct processes, due to their sub-overkill lethality.
  • Range of F0 for the process: Container type and nominal size, fill volume, autoclave size, autoclave type, and product load pattern all have significant influence on the range of F0 delivered throughout the load. F0 is accumulated during heat up, cool down, and the soak interval at and above 121°C.
  • Maximum allowable pre-sterilization hold time: The time between completion of filling and start of sterilization should be defined, in order to ensure control of pre-sterilization bioburden. The allowable hold times directly impact staging area size requirements and material flow.

For products that are not heat-labile, stability samples may be subjected to single and double terminal sterilization cycles (worst case). Data is generated during stability testing to support additional processing as may be required.

教學解說 — 繁體中文

最終滅菌概述

最終滅菌（Terminal Sterilization）是將產品在已完成充填與密封的最終包裝狀態下進行滅菌的製程。常用方法包括濕熱（蒸汽滅菌鍋）、輻射照射及其他適當方法。

核心原則：最終滅菌優先

國際法規共識：只有當藥品配方無法承受最終滅菌條件（如蛋白質藥物熱不穩定）時，才應採用無菌製程（Aseptic Processing）。這反映了「能最終滅菌就不該用無菌製程」的基本邏輯。

F0 值與滅菌策略

F0 值代表在 121°C 下的等效滅菌時間：

  • 過度殺滅（Overkill）：F0 ≥ 15 — 不需了解產品中的生物負荷，純靠高 F0 保證滅菌
  • 輔助製程（Adjunct）：F0 ≥ 8 — 適用於不耐高溫產品，但需搭配嚴格的滅菌前生物負荷監控

兩者目標相同：達到 PNSU ≥ 10-6（每一百萬單位中不超過一個非無菌單位）。

比喻：全熟牛排 vs. 三分熟牛排

Overkill 像全熟牛排 — 不管肉的品質如何，高溫長時間一定熟透。Adjunct 像三分熟牛排 — 必須確認肉源品質優良（低生物負荷），才能用較短的加熱時間達到安全。

設計關鍵：D 值與 F0 分佈

產品溶液可能「保護」微生物（如高黏度或高蛋白含量），導致需要更高的 F0。此外，滅菌鍋中不同位置的 F0 會有差異 — 加熱與冷卻階段都會累積 F0，但速率因位置而異。製程設計必須確保「最冷點」也達到要求。

Facility Impact of Terminal Sterilization

Terminal sterilization also has a significant impact on facility layout/space requirements, process sequence, material flow and equipment flow. Factors for consideration include:

  • Products are often loaded into specialized trays and racks to promote good temperature uniformity, drainage during the cycle, and post-sterilization drying. After completion, they should be transferred into alternate trays or totes for inspection and secondary processing.
  • Terminal sterilization of syringes requires inversion during processing to avoid condensate accumulation in the syringe barrel, and may require de-nesting/re-nesting equipment.
  • Material flow and facility arrangement should be designed to segregate non-sterile and sterile material, such as via pass-through type autoclaves and segregated staging/drying areas.
  • Automated loading and unloading systems can be employed, especially for large volume containers or IV bags. Space requirements can be considerable.
  • Following sterilization, space should be provided for material draining and drying. HVAC equipment should be configured to control latent and sensible heat loads.
  • Container inspection for particulate matter, cosmetic defects, and container integrity should be performed after terminal sterilization, since the process may impact these attributes.
  • Utility requirements for large scale terminal sterilization operations are significant and should be carefully considered during facility design.

設施設計影響

最終滅菌對設施佈局有深遠影響，不僅是放一台滅菌鍋那麼簡單。

關鍵設施考量

  • 非無菌/無菌物料隔離：使用貫穿式（pass-through）滅菌鍋，物料從非無菌側進、無菌側出，確保清潔區隔
  • 專用托盤與回流：滅菌用托盤需回收到加工區重複使用，形成設備逆向物流
  • 注射器特殊處理：滅菌時需倒置以避免冷凝水累積在針筒內
  • 乾燥與暫存空間：滅菌後的產品需要排水和乾燥區，HVAC 系統需處理蒸汽帶來的顯熱與潛熱負載
  • 公用設施負荷：大規模滅菌操作的蒸汽、冷卻水、壓縮空氣需求極為可觀

CDMO 實務觀點

對代工廠而言，最終滅菌產品的設施需求遠大於純無菌充填線。需要額外的暫存區、專用托盤庫存、乾燥間及大容量公用設施。在產能規劃時，滅菌鍋的周轉時間（含裝載、滅菌、冷卻、卸載）往往是產線瓶頸。

Air Over-Pressure and Container Integrity

During the sterilization of liquid-filled containers, differential pressures between the interior of the containers and the sterilization chamber may potentially impact container integrity. Air over-pressure (air ballasting) is used to minimize the pressure differential between the container and the sterilizer to protect the integrity of the container, especially pre-filled syringes and plastic containers.

The amount of internal overpressure in the container is proportional to the internal temperature and does not remain constant throughout the process. The overpressure component should therefore be adjusted during the course of the cycle.

Autoclave Types

Among the sterilization methods available, moist heat autoclaving is the most widely used. There are several autoclave designs:

  • Air steam mix autoclaves: Clean steam is injected directly into the chamber along with sterile filtered air for overpressure control. Suitable means (fans or air ejector nozzles) are employed for good temperature uniformity. Steam must be of compendial quality. Usually used for small volume materials; load is drier upon unloading.
  • Superheated water shower type units: Water is heated/cooled indirectly using external heat exchangers. A recirculating pumping system sprays water over the product load via nozzle arrays for uniform heating and cooling. Water used as heating medium should be of known quality (e.g., distilled or USP purified water). Usually used for larger volume materials, achieving faster heating/cooling rates and better temperature uniformity.

空氣加壓與容器完整性

液體充填容器在高溫滅菌時，內部壓力會隨溫度升高而增加。如果滅菌鍋腔體壓力低於容器內壓，容器可能膨脹破裂或密封失效。因此使用空氣加壓（Air Ballasting）來平衡壓差。

比喻：蒸爐 vs. 水浴鍋

空氣蒸汽混合型像蒸爐 — 蒸汽直接包圍產品，適合小東西但大物件受熱不均。過熱水淋浴型像水浴鍋 — 水的熱傳導效率高，適合大容量產品，但卸載後會比較濕。

3.2.8 Inspection / 檢查

Original Text — ISPE Baseline Guide

3.2.8 Inspection

Products intended for parenteral administration in humans are subjected to various regulatory and compendial requirements for visual inspection. USP <790> establishes the expectation that each finished unit is inspected to ensure absence of particulate matter, as well as absence of any container or seal defect that could compromise sterility.

Requirements for final post-manufacture inspection vary depending on the product itself (e.g., lyophilized, liquid, suspension) as well as the primary package type.

The inspection process typically includes:

  • Foreign matter in solution
  • Fill volume
  • Ampoule and BFS container integrity
  • Vial cap/crimp and stopper (presence, color, visible defects)
  • Black spots at the seal of the ampoule
  • Cake appearance (for lyophilized products)

Inspection Process Design

The design of an inspection process should include which inspections to perform and how/when to perform them. A documented product risk profile/assessment should be developed.

In general, inspection operations can be implemented as:

  • In-process test (statistical sampling at defined intervals) during production
  • 100% in-line inspection (semi-automated or automated)
  • Finished product inspection only, 100%
  • Finished product inspection only, AQL basis
教學解說 — 繁體中文

檢查概述

所有供人體注射的產品都必須通過目視檢查（Visual Inspection），以確保無微粒污染（Particulate Matter）且容器密封完整。USP <790> 是目視檢查的核心法規依據。

常見檢查項目

  • 異物/微粒：溶液中的外來物質
  • 充填量：確認符合標示裝量
  • 容器完整性：安瓿密封、BFS 容器完整
  • 瓶蓋/壓蓋：膠塞存在性、顏色、壓蓋品質
  • 安瓿封口黑點：熔封不良的指標
  • 凍乾餅外觀：是否有塌餅（meltback）

檢查策略選擇

檢查可以在不同階段、以不同方式實施：

  • 製程中抽樣：統計取樣（成本低但覆蓋率有限）
  • 100% 線上檢查：即時全檢但影響產線效率
  • 成品 100% 全檢：離線全檢，需額外空間和人力
  • 成品 AQL 抽樣：依可接受品質限度抽樣

CDMO 實務觀點：檢查是產能瓶頸

在代工廠中，檢查往往是整條產線最大的瓶頸。充填機可能每分鐘產出 300-600 瓶，但手動檢查只能處理數十瓶/分鐘。自動化檢查設備的投資報酬率在高產量產品上非常顯著，但對多品項小批量的 CDMO 而言，設備轉換（changeover）時間也是關鍵考量。

Factors for Inspection Process Design

Several factors should be considered:

  • Capital cost of inspection equipment
  • Space requirements for inspection equipment (in-line versus decoupled)
  • Impact of product investigations on in-process material flows and reinspection requirements
  • Staffing requirements for automated/high tech equipment, especially for off-shift operations
  • Decreased overall line efficiency for in-line inspections
  • Increased material handling requirements for decoupled inspections
  • Use of PAT to reduce/eliminate inspection for certain attributes (e.g., fill weight)

The specific product and package type dictates which inspections are required. For example, some liquid products are susceptible to bubble formation during filling and require an off-line "relaxation time" or use of a pre-spin system prior to particulate inspection.

For high value products, additional inspection steps and PAT may be justified based on decreased product reject rates. For low value products, finished product inspection(s) may be more cost effective.

Emerging Inspection Technologies

  • X-ray analysis of lyophilized cakes for particulate matter
  • Near Infrared (NIR) analysis of lyophilized cakes for moisture content
  • Headspace Analysis (HSA) for products sealed under vacuum or inert gas

設計因素與成本效益

線上 vs. 離線檢查的取捨

  • 線上（In-line）：減少物料搬運，但降低產線整體效率（OEE）
  • 離線（Decoupled）：不影響產線速度，但需要暫存空間（WIP）和額外搬運人力

選擇取決於產品價值、批量大小及設施空間限制。

PAT（製程分析技術）可以即時監控某些屬性（如充填重量），減少或消除對這些項目的離線檢查需求。

新興檢查技術

  • X 射線分析：檢測凍乾餅中的不可見微粒
  • 近紅外光（NIR）：非破壞性測量凍乾餅水分含量
  • 頂空分析（HSA）：確認真空或惰性氣體密封的容器密封完整性（CCI）

這些技術需逐案評估是否納入檢查流程。

比喻：氣泡 vs. 微粒

某些液體產品在充填後會產生氣泡，這些氣泡在自動檢查時會被誤判為微粒。就像剛倒好的汽水 — 需要等氣泡消散（relaxation time）或先旋轉（pre-spin）讓氣泡浮出，才能準確檢測真正的異物。

3.2.8.1 Visual Inspection / 目視檢查

3.2.8.1 Visual Inspection

Many inspection criteria for products are visual; for example, "essentially free of visible particulate matter" or criteria based on product appearance/color or lyophilized cake appearance. Therefore, establishing a manual inspection baseline and challenge sets is important for training/qualification of human inspectors and for adjustment/qualification of automated equipment.

Manual inspection capability is also required when investigating production anomalies or high reject rates from automated equipment. A manual inspection capability should be developed and maintained.

Defect Library

Establishing and maintaining a defect library is required for construction and maintenance of challenge sets. Considerations include:

  • The library should consist of actual defects as well as defect photos or videos. Clear, written descriptions of defect types should be provided.
  • The library should include examples of each type of defect, with a focus on critical defects. Where possible, examples should be obtained from actual production rejects.
  • The quality of defects degrades over time due to repeated handling, so the library should be continuously refreshed with new reject material. This is particularly important for lyophilized products.

Factors Influencing Inspection

  • Human capabilities
  • Process and environmental conditions
  • Defect type and characteristics (particle size, color, shape, movement)
  • Product characteristics and package type

The Knapp methodology classifies containers based on their Probability of Rejection (PR):

  • Reject: 0.7071 < PR < 1.0
  • Gray Zone: 0.30 < PR < 0.7071
  • Accept: 0 < PR < 0.30

The security of rejecting "must-reject" containers is the Reject Zone Efficiency (RZE). Manual and automatic inspection processes should be qualified to ensure adequate removal of reject containers (high RZE) and acceptably low false reject rates.

目視檢查方法

許多檢查標準本質上是視覺性的 — 如「基本上無可見微粒」或凍乾餅外觀。因此建立人工檢查基線（Manual Inspection Baseline）和挑戰組（Challenge Sets）極為重要。

缺陷庫（Defect Library）

缺陷庫是檢查系統的基礎設施：

  • 包含實際缺陷樣品、照片/影片及書面描述
  • 重點收集關鍵缺陷（Critical Defects）的範例
  • 樣品會因反覆操作而劣化，需持續更新 — 尤其凍乾產品的缺陷樣品更易變質

重點：RZE 與假拒絕率的平衡

檢查系統需同時滿足兩個目標：(1) 足夠高的 RZE 確保真正缺陷品被剔除；(2) 足夠低的假拒絕率避免浪費合格品。可透過二次檢查（reinspection of 1x rejects）策略來降低假拒絕率，前提是合併後的 RZE 仍然達標。

Knapp 方法學：容器分類

拒絕區效率（RZE）衡量的是：必須被剔除的缺陷容器，實際被成功剔除的比例。

3.2.8.2 Operator Qualification / 操作人員資格

3.2.8.2 Operator Qualification

Operator qualification and training programs are required for manual and semi-automated inspection processes. Considerations include:

  • Inspectors should be qualified using a manual test set having a known proportion of defect containers. RZE (or POD) and false reject rates are calculated against acceptance criteria.
  • For new inspectors, multiple successful inspections are required for qualification.
  • Operators should be requalified annually, at a minimum.
  • Qualified shift times should be established.

Operators should be tested initially and at regular intervals for near vision acuity and color perception.

Operator fatigue is an important factor. Environmental conditions (ambient light, background noise, activity) and ergonomics should be optimized. Operators performing inspection should take routine breaks (e.g., once per hour) to reduce risk of eye fatigue.

檢查員資格與訓練

檢查員資格要求

  • 初始資格：使用已知缺陷比例的測試組進行多次成功檢查
  • 年度再確認：至少每年一次重新驗證
  • 視力測試：近視力敏銳度 + 色彩辨識能力（初始及定期）
  • 合格班次時間：建立每人每日可執行檢查的最長時間

疲勞管理

目視檢查極度依賴眼力，操作員疲勞是品質風險的主要來源。ISPE 建議：

  • 每小時強制休息一次
  • 優化環境照明、背景噪音及人體工學
  • 建立輪班機制，避免長時間連續檢查

比喻：航空管制員的輪班制度

目視檢查員的疲勞管理類似航空管制員 — 高度專注的工作不能連續太久。管制員每工作 1.5-2 小時就必須休息，目視檢查員同理。忽視疲勞管理等於接受檢查品質隨時間下降的風險。

3.2.8.3 Visual Inspection Methods and Equipment / 目視檢查方法與設備

Manual Visual Inspection (MVI)

Sealed, filled containers are inspected by qualified inspectors under controlled conditions. Critical Process Parameters (CPPs) for MVI include:

  • Light wavelength and intensity
  • Background and contrast
  • Inspection rate (pace)
  • Container handling and movement

Magnification can be employed; however, it can increase eye strain and may not improve overall detection rates. It is therefore not recommended for routine inspection.

Throughputs for MVI are low compared to semi-automated or automated equipment. For this reason, MVI is generally performed off-line.

Visual Inspection with Semi-Automatic Machines

A semi-automatic inspection machine transports and rotates the product while being inspected by an operator. Adjustable factors include: light, angle of product, angle of mirrors, background, and container rotation speed.

During inspection, the operator marks containers to be rejected; these are discarded automatically by the machine.

Throughput rates are higher than for manual inspection, but are often overestimated in the process design stage. Semi-automated systems can be designed for sequential or parallel inspection to increase throughput.

手動目視檢查 (MVI)

MVI 是最基礎的檢查方式：操作員在受控條件下逐瓶檢視。關鍵製程參數（CPP）包括光源波長/強度、背景對比、檢查速率及容器操作方式。

MVI 限制

  • 產出速度最低，通常離線進行
  • 放大鏡可用但不建議例行使用 — 增加眼睛疲勞且不一定提升檢出率
  • 仍是異常調查和自動設備高拒絕率時的必要能力

半自動檢查機

機器負責傳送與旋轉產品，操作員負責判斷。可調整光源、產品角度、鏡面角度、背景及旋轉速度來強化缺陷可見性。

比喻：壽司迴轉台 + 品管員

半自動檢查機就像壽司迴轉台 — 產品自動旋轉送到眼前，檢查員只需專心看（不用拿取和放回），大幅提升效率。但設計階段常高估實際產出速率，應以「最差情況產出率」進行產能分析。

Fully Automatic Inspection Machines

A fully automatic inspection machine consists of an automated material handling/transport system, outfitted with one or more camera stations and/or other instruments designed to inspect product for various defects.

Automated inspection systems may not be suitable for some container types, such as flexible containers. In these cases, a mix of automated, semi-automated, and manual operations may be employed.

Automated equipment is capable of high output rates and is suitable for in-line or off-line (decoupled) installations. In-line installations reduce material handling but impact line efficiencies. For off-line systems, material handling and WIP storage should be considered.

Examples of inspection capabilities include:

  • Particulates in solution
  • Fill level
  • Flip seal presence and color
  • Ampoule banding color
  • Crimp quality (absence of dents/wrinkles)
  • Cracks in tip, neck, shoulder, sidewall, or heel
  • Plunger placement (syringes and cartridges)
  • Needle shield presence
  • Lyophilized cake appearance

Improvements in image capture, processing rates, vision tools, and lighting systems allow capture and analysis of multiple images of each container in real time. Machines can capture and store large numbers of images; these video libraries are helpful during investigations and machine setup. Using video libraries, virtual inspection of container sets is possible, optimizing machine parameters while avoiding degradation of sample sets.

Inspection systems may have unique requirements impacting facility design, such as control of ambient lighting conditions or shielding for X-ray systems.

全自動檢查機

全自動系統使用自動化物料傳輸搭配一個或多個相機站及其他檢測儀器（如 X 射線、雷射頂空分析）。

自動化檢查能力一覽

  • 溶液中微粒
  • 充填液位
  • 翻蓋存在性與顏色
  • 安瓿環帶顏色
  • 壓蓋品質（無凹痕/皺褶）
  • 玻璃裂紋（瓶尖、頸、肩、壁、底）
  • 柱塞位置（注射器/卡匣）
  • 針頭護套存在性
  • 凍乾餅外觀

影像庫的價值

現代自動檢查機可擷取並儲存大量影像，形成「影像庫」。用途包括：

  • 調查異常拒絕率時回溯分析
  • 設備調機時使用影像進行「虛擬檢查」，避免反覆操作實體樣品導致劣化
  • 優化機器參數而不消耗挑戰組樣品

思考題：選擇檢查策略

一家 CDMO 同時生產高價值生物製劑（年產 10 批，每批 5,000 瓶）和低價值小分子注射劑（年產 50 批，每批 50,000 瓶）。

  • 高價值產品應採用何種檢查策略？為什麼？
  • 低價值高產量產品呢？
  • 如何在共用設施中平衡兩者的檢查需求？

設施設計提醒

自動檢查設備可能有特殊設施需求：X 射線系統需要屏蔽、光學系統需要環境光控制。這些需求應在設施設計階段就納入考量，避免事後改裝的高成本。

3.2.9 Secondary Packaging / 二次包裝

Original Text — ISPE Baseline Guide

3.2.9 Secondary Packaging

The same general principles used for packaging of non-sterile products apply to sterile products. For further information, refer to the ISPE Good Practice Guide: Packaging, Labeling and Warehousing Facilities.

Note: Many regulatory markets are in the process of, or are considering, implementing product serialization requirements as an anti-counterfeiting measure. This involves application of a unique identifier code to the product (unit of use) during packaging that can be checked and verified throughout the distribution channel. Appropriate expertise should be sought during line design to accommodate future equipment and technology requirements in this area.

教學解說 — 繁體中文

二次包裝

無菌產品的二次包裝原則與一般產品相同，包括標示（Labeling）、裝盒、裝箱等。ISPE 另有專門的包裝、標示及倉儲設施指南可參考。

序列化（Serialization）趨勢

全球多個法規市場正在推動或已實施產品序列化要求：

  • 目的：防偽 — 每個單位產品都有唯一識別碼
  • 技術：在包裝過程中貼附唯一編碼（如 2D barcode），可在整個配送鏈中查驗
  • 設施影響：需要在包裝線上預留空間和介面，供序列化設備（印碼機、相機驗證系統、資料管理系統）使用

設計前瞻性

即使目前市場尚未強制要求序列化，新建或改建包裝線時應預留空間和公用設施介面，以便未來加裝序列化設備。改裝成本遠高於預留空間的成本。

CDMO 實務：序列化的挑戰

對 CDMO 而言，序列化帶來額外複雜度：不同客戶可能需要不同的序列化格式和標準（EU FMD、US DSCSA、中國追溯碼等）。包裝線需要靈活的軟體配置能力和快速切換能力。這是選擇包裝設備供應商時的關鍵評估項目。

Section Summary / 本節摘要

  • Terminal Sterilization (3.2.7) / 最終滅菌： Products sealed in final packaging are sterilized via moist heat or irradiation. Overkill (F0 ≥ 15) and adjunct (F0 ≥ 8) processes both target PNSU ≥ 10-6. Facility design must address non-sterile/sterile segregation, specialized trays, drying areas, and significant utility loads. / 最終包裝產品透過濕熱或輻射滅菌。過度殺滅與輔助製程目標相同。設施需考量物料隔離、專用托盤、乾燥區及大量公用設施需求。
  • Autoclave Types / 滅菌鍋類型： Air steam mix units (small volumes, drier load) vs. superheated water shower units (large volumes, faster heating/cooling, better uniformity). Air ballasting protects container integrity during sterilization. / 空氣蒸汽混合型（小容量、較乾）vs. 過熱水淋浴型（大容量、加熱冷卻快、均勻性佳）。空氣加壓保護容器完整性。
  • Inspection (3.2.8) / 檢查： USP <790> requires visual inspection of all parenteral units. The Knapp methodology (RZE, PR zones) provides a scientific framework for qualifying both manual and automated inspection. Operator qualification, fatigue management, and defect libraries are essential. / USP <790> 要求所有注射劑目視檢查。Knapp 方法提供科學化的資格確認框架。操作員資格、疲勞管理與缺陷庫不可或缺。
  • Inspection Methods (3.2.8.3) / 檢查方法： MVI (lowest throughput, off-line), semi-automatic (operator + machine, higher throughput), and fully automatic (camera-based, highest throughput, real-time image analysis). Emerging technologies include X-ray, NIR, and HSA. / MVI（最低產出、離線）、半自動（操作員+機器）、全自動（相機、最高產出、即時影像分析）。新興技術包括 X 射線、NIR 及頂空分析。
  • Secondary Packaging (3.2.9) / 二次包裝： Same principles as non-sterile products. Product serialization for anti-counterfeiting is an emerging requirement; line design should accommodate future serialization equipment. / 原則同非無菌產品。序列化防偽是新興要求，產線設計應預留未來設備空間。
2d

Chapter 2d: 3d. Process Equipment (3.2.10–end)

製程設備（下） | p73-p78

ISPE Baseline Guide Vol. 3 (3rd Ed.) | p73 – p78

Learning Objectives / 學習目標

  1. Understand the requirements for cleaning, disinfection, and sterilization of facility surfaces and equipment in sterile manufacturing. / 理解無菌製造設施與設備的清潔、消毒與滅菌要求。
  2. Distinguish between cleaning of critical parts (product-contact) and facility surfaces (non-product-contact). / 區分關鍵部件（產品接觸面）與設施表面（非產品接觸面）的清潔差異。
  3. Evaluate the advantages, limitations, and implementation considerations of single-use systems. / 評估一次性系統的優勢、限制及導入考量。
  4. Design effective equipment flow and cleaning equipment strategies (CIP, parts washers, ultrasonic). / 設計有效的設備流向與清潔設備策略（CIP、部件清洗機、超音波）。
  5. Apply steam sterilization (autoclave and SIP) design principles including air removal, condensate drainage, and qualification. / 應用蒸汽滅菌（高壓蒸汽鍋與SIP）設計原則，包括排氣、冷凝水排放與確效。
  6. Understand considerations for other sterilization methods (VHP, gamma irradiation, EtO) and their facility impact. / 理解其他滅菌方法（VHP、伽瑪射線、環氧乙烷）及其對設施的影響。

3.2.10 Cleaning, Disinfection and Sterilization 3.2.10 清潔、消毒與滅菌

Cleaning and Disinfection of Facility and Stationary Equipment

Cleaning, disinfection and sterilization are critical processes in a sterile facility as they have the potential to adversely impact critical quality attributes of finished product.

Note: The terms disinfection and sanitization are often used interchangeably, which can lead to confusion about the efficacy of the process. Regulated companies should ensure that their in-house terminology is well defined.

Facility space and stationary equipment surfaces (non-product contact) should be cleaned and disinfected on a routine basis to maintain a state of environmental control as demonstrated by environmental monitoring data.

Written procedures for cleaning and disinfection should contain information on:

  • Frequency
  • Approved cleaning/disinfecting solutions
  • Equipment/utensils/consumables
  • Methodology
  • Operator protection requirements

Solutions used for cleaning and disinfecting should be qualified as effective against a broad range of microorganisms on prevalent surface materials in use in the facility. Multiple agents should be rotated, where appropriate. Surface material compatibility with cleaning/disinfecting solutions should be evaluated during the selection process.

To prevent introduction of contamination, disinfectants should be:

  • Sterile
  • Handled appropriately in suitable (e.g., sterile) containers
  • Labeled and expiry dated
  • Used for no longer than the predefined period specified by written procedures

Critical areas (ISO 5/Grade A) likely require cleaning on a more frequent basis than less critical areas (ISO 8/Grade C), due to higher environmental standards.

解讀與應用

清潔與消毒的核心定位

清潔、消毒與滅菌是無菌製造設施的三道核心防線。ISPE Vol.3 把這些流程與製程設備章節放在一起討論，強調設備設計必須從一開始就考慮「如何清潔」與「如何滅菌」。

術語混淆警告：消毒 vs. 殺菌

Disinfection（消毒）與 Sanitization（殺菌）在行業中經常混用。FDA 使用 disinfection 作為標準用語。藥廠應在內部文件中明確定義並統一使用，避免稽核時產生疑慮。

比喻：餐廳廚房的清潔層次

想像一家高級餐廳：廚房地板每天擦洗（設施表面清潔），砤板與刀具每次用後徹底消毒（關鍵部件清潔），而整棟廚房定期大掃除（深層滅菌）。這與無菌製造的三層清潔策略完全對應。

消毒劑管理四要素

  • 無菌（Sterile）：消毒劑本身不能是污染源
  • 適當容器：避免轉移過程中引入微生物
  • 標籤與效期：追溯性與有效性的基礎
  • 使用時限：開封後的消毒劑不是永遠有效

CDMO 實戰：多產品線消毒策略標準化

在 CDMO 環境中，操作多條產線時，建議建立「消毒劑矮陣」——統一核准的消毒劑清單與輪替計畫，適用於所有生產套件，減少每條產線各自驗證的重複成本。

Cleaning of Critical Parts

Critical parts, which are defined as parts either in direct contact with product or have the possibility to contaminate the product, should be subjected to a qualified cleaning process a short period after use to remove product residue.

Critical parts should be identified via a documented risk assessment. Clean hold times for parts should be established; when these clean hold times expire, the parts should be cleaned again prior to next use.

Chemical cleaning agents may be necessary to remove residual product from product contacting surfaces. Selection of an appropriate agent should be based on the type of soil and cleaning process (e.g., ultrasonic, high impingement) and may be undertaken in conjunction with the cleaning agent vendors.

When cleaning agents are used, the cleaning process should include qualified rinse steps to demonstrate removal of these agents to a safe level.

Note: Endotoxins are not appreciably retained by most sterilizing grade filters, nor are they appreciably reduced by moist heat sterilization. Control of endotoxins, therefore, requires a comprehensive approach including bioburden control, cleaning, dry heat depyrogenation, and filtration processes.

解讀與應用

關鍵部件清潔的時間壓力

關鍵部件必須在使用後「短時間內」清潔，這是因為產品殘留物會隨時間乾燥固化，大幅增加清潔難度。建立 Dirty Hold Time（臟污保留時間）與 Clean Hold Time（潔淨保留時間）是清潔驗證的基礎。

內毒素控制：綜合策略

內毒素（Endotoxin）不能被過濾器挡住，也不能被蒸汽滅菌消除。唯一可靠的去除方法是乾熱除熱原（通常 250°C 以上）。這就是為什麼玻璃瓶與安瓶通常需經過除熱原通道處理。

思考練習：風險評估實作

假設你的 CDMO 生產線有一台配液槽、過濾管路與填充平台三個站點：

  • 哪些部件屬於「關鍵部件」？
  • 各站點的 Dirty Hold Time 應設定為多久？
  • 如何透過風險評估確定清潔流程的優先順序？

Single-Use Systems 一次性使用系統

Single-Use Systems

Implementation of single-use disposable technology and single-use systems is an increasing practice. Single-use disposable systems are available for a variety of fill/finish unit operations, including formulation, material addition, buffer prep, filtration, product transfer, and product filling.

Single-use systems offer several advantages such as:

  • Elimination of cleaning steps
  • Reduced operator exposure to high potent or toxic materials during cleaning
  • Elimination of cleaning validation
  • Reduced risk of cross-contamination
  • Flexible scalability
  • Reduction of capital costs

Single-use systems are not suitable for all product types. For example, temperature limits on the film may exclude products requiring heating for formulation/filtration/filling.

Implementation of single-use systems requires a cross-functional corporate effort in areas such as:

  • Primary and secondary film/vendor selection (includes quality audits and supplier agreements)
  • Single-use system design (includes film selection, component selection, tubing selection, packaging, sterilization, etc.)
  • Testing for extractables, leachables and particulates (primary and backup systems)
  • Integrity testing of single-use assemblies, including filters (pre and/or post-use)
  • Batch record modifications

Single-use systems entail higher operating costs (consumables) than traditional systems. A careful financial analysis is required to evaluate costs versus potential savings. The timeframe associated with completion of these activities is quite lengthy, and is in fact much longer than the typical timeframe for facility conceptual and detailed design.

解讀與應用

一次性系統的關鍵優勢

一次性系統最大的價值在於「消除清潔驗證」與「降低交叉污染風險」。對於 CDMO 而言，這代表更快的產品切換速度與更低的每批次驗證負擔。

比喻：免洗餐具 vs. 磁器餐具

一次性系統就像用免洗餐具開派對——不用洗碟，用完即丢，操作簡單；但每次都要買新的，累積起來成本不低。傳統不鏽鋼系統就像高級磁器餐具——一次買貴，但洗復使用，長期成本較低。

導入時程警告

ISPE 特別提醒：一次性系統的導入時程「遠比設施設計本身還長」。這包括薄膜選擇、供應商稽核、E&L測試、完整性測試驗證等。CDMO 應在設施設計階段即啟動這些活動，不要等到設施落成才開始。

CDMO 實戰：混合策略

多數 CDMO 採用混合策略：對於高價值小批量產品（如細胞治療）使用一次性系統，對於大規模量產產品繼續使用不鏽鋼固定設備。關鍵是在設施規劃時就預留足夠的柔性空間。

Equipment Flow

Careful consideration of equipment flow during cleaning, preparation and staging operations is required to effectively mitigate risk of cross-contamination. This cross-contamination can be either batch to batch for Product A, or from Product A to Product B.

Use of pass-through type washers and autoclaves and unidirectional equipment flows are recommended to ensure that clean parts do not come in close proximity to dirty parts.

Segregated staging areas of sufficient size should be provided for soiled, cleaned, and sterilized equipment. Segregation of pre and post-use filter integrity testing should also be considered.

解讀與應用

單向流原則

設備流向與人員流向、物料流向一樣重要。核心原則是：臟污設備與潔淨設備絕對不能在同一區域交會。通過式清洗機和高壓滅菌鍋的使用，確保設備從「臟側」進入、從「潔側」取出。

比喻：大樓的貨梯與客梯

這就像高級飯店的動線設計：垃圾走貨梯，客人走客梯，絕不交叉。無菌製造設施的臟污設備與潔淨設備也必須走不同的路徑。

多產品設施的額外挑戰

對於 CDMO 的多產品設施，交叉污染風險不僅是 batch-to-batch，還包括 Product A 到 Product B 的污染。因此需要更嚴格的設備分區儲放和流向管理。

Cleaning Equipment 清潔設備

Semi-Automated and Automated Cleaning Systems

Semi-automated and automated cleaning systems can provide an enhanced level of process control and reliability. Use of such systems is recommended over manual cleaning processes.

Examples of semi-automated cleaning systems include ultrasonic baths and parts (cabinet) washers. These systems are useful for components and equipment that require disassembly for effective cleaning. Load mapping of items in automated and semi-automated cleaners is required to ensure reproducibility.

Some equipment, such as formulation vessels and filling line process pathways, lend themselves to fully automated CIP systems. The advantage of automated CIP is its potential to configure both the CIP system and the component for cleaning, execute the cycle, and return the component to service or subsequent sterilization without disassembly/assembly.

CIP systems should be designed from the beginning for cleanability and proper CIP to avoid potential issues with product contamination. Considerations include:

  • Elimination of dead legs
  • Adequate flow rates (to ensure turbulent flow in piping systems)
  • Complete drainability
  • Cleaning of piping high and low points
  • System drying
  • Material surface finishes

Modern cleaning devices and CIP equipment include electronic controls that allow for programming, monitoring/alarming, and recording of critical parameters such as cycle time, water temperature, water pressure, flow rate/totalized flow, and detergent addition (volume/weight).

Design considerations for CIP systems include:

  • Single versus multi-tank
  • High impingement dynamic spray devices versus static spray balls/nozzles (or combination)
  • Recirculating or once through

解讀與應用

自動化清潔的三個層次

  • 半自動（超音波浴、部件清洗機）：適合需要拆卸的部件，例如填充泵
  • 全自動 CIP：適合配液槽、管路等固定設備，不需拆卸
  • 手動清潔：應儘量避免，因為可重複性差，但某些特殊部件仍無可避免

CIP 設計六大要素

  • 消除死角（Dead Legs）：管路中清潔液流不到的地方
  • 充足流速：確保紐流（Turbulent Flow）以徹底清除殘留
  • 完全可排水性：管路不能有積水點
  • 高低點清潔：管路的最高與最低點都要能被清潔到
  • 系統乾燥：殘留水分會促進微生物生長
  • 表面粗糙度（Ra 值）：表面越光滑越容易清潔

噴淋裝置的機械故障風險

動態噴淋裝置和靜態噴淋球都可能因機械故障或堵塞而失效。必須透過流程控制或儀表監控（如流量計、轉速感測器）來確保清潔效果的一致性。

比喻：家用洗碗機 vs. 工業級 CIP

家用洗碗機有固定的噴水臂和溫度設定，但你不會把鍋子直接接在洗碗機上。CIP 就是讓清潔液「流進鍋子裡面」，直接在設備內部循環清洗，不需拆卸。

CDMO 實戰：標準化清潔設備配置

在多套件生產設施中，建議每條產線採用相同型號的部件清洗機和 CIP 系統。這樣不僅減少驗證成本，還能讓操作員在不同產線之間無縫調動。

Cleaning Equipment Location and Selection

Cleaning equipment should be located to minimize impact of mechanical systems and maintenance activities on the cleanroom environment. For example, a pass-through type parts washer can be installed to allow access to the mechanical sections from CNC or mechanical space. Drains should be located in a mechanical area, when possible, due to their high moisture levels and potential to introduce contamination.

Specific considerations for selection of cleaning equipment include:

  • Types of equipment and components that require cleaning
  • Product characteristics/unique cleaning requirements
  • Cycle times and impact on capacity
  • Demand on water systems as well as heating and cooling systems
  • Location in facility
  • Use of and need for detergents
  • Local requirements for capture and treatment of rinse water

解讀與應用

潔淨室與機械區的分隔

清潔設備的放置位置是設施設計的重要決策。核心原則：把產生噪音、濕氣和維護需求的機械部分放在潔淨室外面，只讓潔淨操作面面向潔淨區。

排水口的污染風險

排水口是潔淨室中已知的污染風險點，因為高濕度環境利於微生物生長。ISPE 建議將排水口放在機械區而非潔淨區內，這與 EU GMP Annex 1 對 Grade A/B 區域禁止設置排水口的要求一致。

Steam Sterilization 蒸汽滅菌

Steam Sterilization

Critical parts in an aseptic process, which are defined as parts, equipment, tools and utensils either in direct contact with sterile product or having the possibility to contaminate the product, should be subjected to a qualified sterilization process within a defined period prior to use.

Use of sterile articles, components, or equipment in aseptic fill/finish operations requires:

  1. Effective sterilization of the article
  2. Protection of the article from contamination during staging and transfer to the aseptic zone
  3. Transfer into the aseptic zone

Several sterilization methods are available:

  • Gamma irradiation
  • E-beam irradiation
  • Ethylene Oxide (EtO)
  • Dry heat
  • Moist heat
