The two available methods for moist heat (or steam) sterilization are autoclaving or SIP. These cycles are generally qualified according to the overkill approach, requiring a minimum F0 of 12 minutes.

When qualifying a steam sterilization process, the following should be verified:

  • Steam quality at point of delivery (dryness, superheat, non-condensable gases)
  • Preparation/wrapping of articles to be sterilized (autoclave only)
  • Effective removal of air from porous loads or wrapped articles (autoclave) or from all points in the system (SIP)
  • Effective removal of condensate from the system during the cycle
  • Appropriate design of the sterilizing cycle (pre-vacuum pulses, F0 requirements, post-vacuum drying)
  • Temperature mapping (minimum F0 delivered at all locations)
  • Orientation/equipment configuration
  • Minimum and maximum loads (autoclave only) and load mapping
  • Determination of worst case conditions
  • Ability to inactivate biological challenge (Geobacillus stearothermophilus, 1.0 x 106 minimum population)

解讀與應用

滅菌三步驟：滅菌 → 保護 → 轉移

滅菌不只是「放進滅菌鍋」這麼簡單。完整的滅菌流程包括三個階段：有效滅菌、防污染儲放、安全轉移到無菌區。任何一個環節失敗，都等於整個滅菌無效。

F0 值的意義

F0 是衡量濕熱滅菌效果的標準單位，表示在 121.1°C 下的等價滅菌時間（分鐘）。Overkill 方法要求最小 F0 為 12 分鐘，確保即使在最差情況下也能完全滅菌。

蒸汽品質：常被忽略的關鍵因素

蒸汽的乾燥度、過熱和不凝縮氣體含量直接影響滅菌效果。濕蒸汽含有太多水分會導致裝載濕潤，過熱蒸汽則減少熱傳遞效率。建議定期測試蒸汽品質，特別是新設施或蒸汽系統變更後。

比喻：烤箱與滅菌鍋

高壓滅菌鍋就像烤箱：你需要確保溫度均勻（溫度記錄）、食物放對位置（裝載圖）、預熱足夠（排氣），而且要用溫度計確認熬到位（生物指示劑）。

思考練習：滅菌確效規劃

您的 CDMO 要為一台新的雙門高壓滅菌鍋進行確效，請列出：

  • 需要驗證的裝載類型（至少三種）
  • 每種裝載的最大與最小配置
  • 如何確定溫度最差點位置

Autoclave Process Design

Effective removal of air from wrapped articles and porous loads is required for good sterilization efficacy. Autoclaves should be properly maintained and checked at regular intervals for vacuum integrity (leak rate). Use of an air removal test (e.g., Bowie-Dick, DART, Lantor Cube) at a regular interval is also recommended.

Autoclave sterilization process design should consider the packaging/wrapping of articles:

  • Packaging/wrapping should be designed to promote effective air removal, steam penetration, and condensate removal during sterilization.
  • Packaging and wrapping may be a manual operation; effective training is required to ensure consistent and reproducible preparation of articles.
  • Packaging/wrapping materials should provide an effective microbiological barrier to maintain sterility during cool down and staging.
  • The packaging/wrapping should allow for successive improvement steps during transfer of the articles to areas of higher cleanliness.
  • Permeability of the packaging/wrapping as required for sterilization may impact selection of subsequent improvement steps.

Sterilized articles should be securely staged and transferred to the aseptic processing zone. Considerations for secure transfer include:

  • Technologies such as Rapid Transfer Ports (RTPs) or automated VHP airlocks for secure transfer across the RABS/isolator boundary
  • For isolator-based facilities, autoclaves may be unloaded into an ISO 8/Grade C area
  • In RABS-based facilities, autoclaves are generally unloaded into an ISO 5/Grade A area

The number and size of autoclaves should be designed to support production operations, considering types of equipment, number of cycles, cycle time, and impact of routine testing on availability.

解讀與應用

排氣測試的重要性

空氣是蒸汽滅菌的最大敵人。空氣的導熱係數遠低於飽和蒸汽，如果裝載中殘留空氣，該區域的溫度將無法達到滅菌要求。Bowie-Dick 測試或 DART 測試是驗證空氣去除效果的日常工具。

包裝設計：滅菌 vs. 無菌保護的平衡

包裝必須同時滿足兩個矛盾需求：滅菌時要讓蒸汽穿透（透氣性），滅菌後又要阻擋微生物（屏障性）。多層包裝設計（如雙層 breather bag）讓操作員在轉移過程中逐層去除外層。

RTP vs. VHP 氣閉 — 轉移技術選擇

  • RTP（快速轉移埠）：適用於隔離器技術，通過機械密封實現無菌轉移
  • VHP 氣閉：使用過氧化氫滅菌的自動氣閉，適合 RABS 和隔離器

兩者均優於傳統的手動消毒液噴灑方法。

CDMO 實戰：高壓滅菌鍋產能規劃

高壓滅菌鍋往往是無菌製造的產能瓶頸。建議在設計階段充分評估：每天所需滅菌循環數量、每個循環時間（含升溫、保溫、乾燥）、日常測試占用時間，確保不會成為生產瓶頸。

Sterilize-In-Place (SIP) 定位蒸汽滅菌 (SIP)

Sterilize-In-Place (SIP)

The term SIP is commonly used to refer to both:

  • Sterilization of large scale fixed holding vessels and fill line process piping
  • Sterilization of smaller portable vessels at a dedicated SIP (or CIP/SIP) process station

Product compounding/filtration/transfer/holding systems can be designed as completely closed systems, due to advances in aseptic fluid transfer and material addition technologies (e.g., tubing welders, aseptic connectors, closed addition devices). This allows installation in areas of lower cleanliness (e.g., ISO 8/Grade C, Grade D or CNC zones).

When installed in aseptic areas, systems should be designed to minimize impact of mechanical and control elements and steam/condensate release in the process area. This may be accomplished via use of "half-wall" or split systems that segregate the process side of the equipment from the mechanical side.

Design considerations for effective SIP include:

  • Air removal: Pre-vacuum steps or gravity displacement; leak rate assessment on regular basis; proper steam trap design; multiple steam injection points for large systems
  • Sterilization of vent filters: Avoid compromising filter integrity at elevated temperatures; limit flow across filters; use multiple steam injection points for large systems
  • Condensate drainage: System should drain condensate quickly from all portions; use steam traps and orifices; avoid group trapping of drain legs
  • Drying and cool down: Use 0.2 µm sterile filtered air or nitrogen; avoid exceeding differential pressure rating of filters at elevated temperatures; maintain overpressure until time of use

Calibrated temperature sensors (RTD, thermocouples) and pressure sensors are required for system control and monitoring. Temperature sensors should be installed at potential cold spot locations. Comparison of system pressure and temperature can verify presence of saturated steam.

解讀與應用

SIP 的兩種應用場景

  • 固定系統 SIP：大型儲槽、產線管路直接通蒸汽滅菌，不需拆卸
  • 可移動式 SIP（Steam Out of Place）：將小型容器送到專用 CIP/SIP 站進行滅菌

封閉系統的革命性意義

隨著焊接管器、無菌連接器和封閉添加裝置的成熟，製程系統可以設計為完全封閉系統。這意味著即使安裝在 ISO 8 或 CNC 區域也能保持無菌，大幅降低對高等級潔淨室的依賴。

比喻：半牆 — 位前台與後台的分隔

「半牆」或分體式設計就像餐廳的廚房窗口：你只看到乾淨的出餐面，而爐灶、管線、熱水器都藏在後面。SIP 系統的蒸汽閤、冷凝水排放和控制元件都放在機械側，潔淨側只有無菌製程路徑。

SIP 四大設計挑戰

  1. 排氣：管路系統比高壓滅菌鍋容易排氣（沒有多孔載荷），但大型系統需要多點注汽與門序列控制
  2. 通氣過濾器保護：高溫時過濾器耐壓能力大幅下降，必須限制跨過濾器的流量
  3. 冷凝水排放：避免群組捕水器（Group Trapping），否則會導致不均勻的冷凝水排放
  4. 乾燥與冷卻：使用 0.2 µm 無菌過濾空氣或氮氣，維持正壓直到使用

思考練習：溫度感測器佈局

您要為一套包含配液槽、兩條過濾管路和填充槽的 SIP 系統規劃溫度感測器佈局：

  • 潛在冷點在哪裡？（提示：獨立流路末端）
  • 哪些位置需要感測器來偵測蒸汽捕水器故障？
  • 如何用壓力與溫度的對比來確認飽和蒸汽的存在？

Other Sterilization Methods 其他滅菌方法

Other Sterilization Methods

The use of fumigants—for example, hydrogen peroxide (H2O2), chlorine dioxide (ClO2), and nitrogen dioxide (NO2)—for room and equipment surface decontamination should consider that, in order to be effective, they need to be able to directly contact target surfaces in adequate concentrations.

Fumigation is generally not required to maintain aseptic conditions in a facility; however, in some cases it can provide a useful add-on process. Considerations include:

  • VHP: Usually used to decontaminate the interior of barrier isolators.
  • Gamma irradiation: Usually used for sterilization of single-use technology, as well as selected ready-to-use elastomeric components such as syringe plungers. Cycles should be validated and under routine dose auditing.
  • Ethylene oxide (EtO): Usually used for sterilization of ready-to-fill pre-nested components such as syringes, vials, and cartridges and ophthalmic containers.

解讀與應用

薰蒸滅菌的限制

薰蒸劑必須能「直接接觸」目標表面且達到足夠濃度才能有效。這意味著被遮擋的表面（如裝載堆疊的內側）可能無法被充分薰蒸。這也是為什麼薰蒸不能取代常規的清潔與消毒程序。

CDMO 實戰：委外滅菌的供應鏈管理

由於伽瑪射線和 EtO 滅菌通常委外處理，CDMO 需要關注：滅菌後組件的儲存條件與位置、有效期管理（通常兩年）、供應商的劑量稽核計畫。這些都應納入定期供應商管理流程。

Section Summary — Chapter 3d: Process Equipment (3.2.10–end)

Key Concepts

  • Cleaning, disinfection, and sterilization form the three-layer defense for sterile manufacturing facilities and equipment
  • Disinfectants must be sterile, properly labeled, expiry-dated, and rotated; terminology (disinfection vs. sanitization) must be standardized
  • Critical parts require documented risk assessment, dirty hold times, clean hold times, and qualified cleaning processes
  • Single-use systems eliminate cleaning validation and cross-contamination risk, but require lengthy implementation timelines and cross-functional effort
  • Unidirectional equipment flow with pass-through washers/autoclaves prevents clean/dirty cross-contamination
  • CIP design requires elimination of dead legs, adequate flow rates, complete drainability, and appropriate surface finishes (Ra values)
  • Steam sterilization (autoclave and SIP) requires effective air removal, condensate drainage, temperature mapping, and F0 ≥ 12 min (overkill approach)
  • SIP systems benefit from closed system design and half-wall installation to segregate process from mechanical areas
  • VHP, gamma irradiation, and EtO serve specific niches; fumigation supplements but does not replace routine cleaning/disinfection

核心重點摘要

  • 清潔、消毒與滅菌是無菌製造的三道防線，設備設計必須從一開始就考慮這三個面向
  • 關鍵部件（產品接觸面）需要風險評估、臟污/潔淨保留時間管理及清潔驗證
  • 一次性系統是 CDMO 的利器，但導入時程長於設施設計，需提前啟動
  • 設備流向必須單向，臟污與潔淨絕對分離，對 CDMO 多產品設施尤其重要
  • CIP 設計關鍵：消除死角、充足流速、完全可排水、適當表面粗糙度
  • 蒸汽滅菌（高壓鍋 + SIP）的 F0 ≥ 12 分鐘，需驗證排氣、冷凝水排放、溫度記錄與生物指示劑
  • 大型 SIP 系統採用封閉設計與半牆安裝，減少對潔淨室的影響
  • VHP、伽瑪射線、EtO 各有專屬應用場景，CDMO 需管好委外滅菌的供應鏈與有效期
3a

Chapter 3a: 4a. Architecture (4.1–4.3)

建築佈局（上） | p79-p91

ISPE Baseline Guide Vol. 3 (3rd Ed.) | p79 – p91

Learning Objectives / 學習目標

  1. Understand the three fundamental facility design approaches for product protection: spatial separation, procedural means, and time separation (campaigning)
  2. Differentiate between open processing (with and without barrier technology) and closed processing for aseptic production
  3. Identify the key process & operational considerations that drive facility layout decisions
  4. Explain the programming process for layout design: goals, block flow diagrams, zoning diagrams, and space planning
  5. Describe the principles of unidirectional material and personnel flows and their impact on contamination control
  6. Recognize additional layout considerations including fire protection, cost optimization, and service distribution

Section Contents / 章節目錄

4.1 Introduction 4.1.1 Facility Design Approaches 4.1.2 Design Approach Implementation 4.1.3 Concurrent Production 4.2 General Design Criteria 4.2.1 Process & Operational 4.2.2 Site & Building 4.2.3 Facility Fit 4.3 Layout Considerations 4.3.7 Material/Personnel Flows 4.3.8 Additional Layout Issues 4.3.9 Cost & Fire Protection

4.1 Introduction 4.1 簡介

4.1 Introduction

This chapter addresses the importance of integrated design and examines considerations for facility layout, together with the architectural detailing and finish requirements. The key concept emphasized in this chapter is risk assessment and how it integrates into facility design.

A risk assessment should appropriately evaluate where the product is at risk and to address and mitigate the potential for product chemical or bio-contamination by using facility design approaches.

The facility design approaches addressed in this chapter are:

  • Product protection by spatial (physical) separation
  • Product protection by procedural means
  • Product protection using time separation (also referred to as "campaigning" or "temporal segregation")

Implementation of these approaches is determined by three basic categories for aseptic production:

  • Open processing aseptic production: e.g., filling of open vials in an isolator where product is exposed to the environment within the isolator
  • Closed processing aseptic production: e.g., direct connections of formulation charging containers to formulation vessels via aseptic transfer valves
  • Open processing non-aseptic production for terminally sterilized products: measures should minimize bioburden prior to sterilization

Note: The term "product protection" as used in this chapter includes protecting the product, product contact sterile processing surfaces, and protecting the prepared primary components and containers for filling.

第四章 引言

本章探討整合設計的重要性，並檢視設施佈局、建築細部與飾面要求。本章的核心概念是風險評估及其如何融入設施設計。

風險評估應適當評估產品面臨風險的環節，並透過設施設計方法來因應與降低潛在的化學或生物污染。

三大設計方法

  1. 空間（物理）分隔 — 透過實體屏障將潔淨區與非潔淨區隔離
  2. 程序手段 — 透過 SOP、操作培訓與工作指令進行控制
  3. 時間分隔（戰役式生產） — 不同產品或操作在不同時段進行，中間施以清潔與換氣

比喻：醫院手術室的無菌保護

想像一間手術室：物理分隔就像無菌門與玄關；程序手段就像洗手與穿手術衣流程；時間分隔就像在兩台手術之間進行手術室消毒。三者都是為了保護病人（產品）免受污染。

三類基本無菌生產模式：

  • 開放式無菌生產：產品暴露於環境（如隔離器內的裝填操作）
  • 密閉式無菌生產：產品在密封管路與容器內流轉
  • 開放式非無菌生產：最終滅菌產品，仍需控制生物負荷

4.1.1 Facility Design Approaches 4.1.1 廠房設計方法

4.1.1 Facility Design Approaches

Facility design approaches for product protection have traditionally been achieved by procedural segregation, spatial segregation, by campaigning (segregation by time), or by a combination of all three. This Guide recommends the use of spatial separation, where practical, to maintain protection of the ISO 5/Grade A environment.

Examples of product protection by spatial (or physical) separation include:

  • An open process placed within either an isolator or RABS:
    • In an isolator setup, the surrounding room environment does not come in contact with the product. The level of finish and HVAC classification of the surrounding room can be reduced.
    • In a RABS setup, most interactions occur through integral glove ports. The surrounding environment should meet ISO 7/Grade B specifications. The space next to the RABS into which doors open should meet LP/GAAS conditions.
  • Closed process systems where the product is processed within closed or sealed process equipment
  • Dedicated gowning rooms for ingress (entering) and egress (exiting) to prevent contamination from egress garments reaching ingress garments

An example of product protection using time separation:

  • Shared gowning room for bidirectional traffic, but with non-concurrent gowning and de-gowning, with a suitable air exchange clean-up period

The use of separate routes for personnel ingress and egress into aseptic areas of classification ISO 7/Grade B and cleaner is recommended, where possible.

4.1.1 設施設計方法

本指南推薦在可行情況下優先使用空間分隔來維護 ISO 5/Grade A 環境的保護。

重點：隔離器 vs. RABS 對周圍環境的影響

  • 隔離器：周圍房間與產品完全隔離，房間等級可降低（ISO 8/Grade C 或更低）
  • RABS：偶爾需開門，周圍環境仍需維持 ISO 7/Grade B，門開啟側需滿足 LP/GAAS 條件

空間分隔的典型應用：

  • 開放製程置於隔離器或 RABS 內
  • 密閉製程系統（密封管路運送產品）
  • 專用穿衣室：進入與離開分開，防止脫衣污染影響穿衣區

比喻：分隔方式的選擇

想像一家餐廳的廚房動線：進料口與出菜口分開（空間分隔）是最佳方案；但小餐廳可能只能用同一個門但錯開時間（時間分隔）。廠房規模與風險決定了哪種方法最適合。

4.1.2 Design Approach Implementation 4.1.2 設計方法實施

4.1.2 Design Approach Implementation

There are three basic facility types related to open processing sterile product manufacturing:

  • Open processing aseptic production in the absence of barrier technology
  • Open processing aseptic production utilizing barrier technology
  • Open processing non-aseptic production for terminally sterilized products

4.1.2.1 Open Processing Without Barrier Technology: Where open aseptic production occurs without barrier technology, operations should be conducted within a laminar flow cabinet. ISO 5/Grade A conditions should be met within the cabinet. The surrounding room should meet ISO 7/Grade B requirements.

Design measures include:

  • Room air classification, zoning, directional airflow, and monitoring to protect the product
  • Personnel gowning areas and material airlocks providing step-up transitions to cleaner classifications
  • Coved corners at floor, wall, and ceiling intersections to facilitate room cleaning
  • Flush detailing to minimize horizontal surfaces and difficult-to-clean areas
  • Low wall HVAC exhaust points designed for easy cleaning; vertically mounted louvered grills should be avoided

4.1.2.2 RABS: The aseptic critical zone is separated from the surrounding environment via barrier walls and ISO 5/Grade A air overspill. Most intrusions use glove ports; however, occasional door openings may be needed, requiring ISO 7/Grade B surrounding environment.

4.1.2.3 Isolators: Isolators provide a fully enclosed and segregated aseptic environment. The critical zone is reduced to the volume of air inside the isolator. Key reductions may include: room classification, gowning requirements, number of airlocks, extent of room cleaning, and room finishes (still meeting ISO 8/Grade C minimum).

4.1.2.4 Non-Aseptic Processing (Terminal Sterilization): The process should occur within RABS protected by LP/GAAS. The local environment should not add particulates or bioburden that the terminal sterilization process cannot remove.

4.1.2.5 Closed System Aseptic Processing: Defined with examples in Section 2.8.2.

4.1.2 設計方法實施

開放式無菌製造有三種基本設施類型：

重點：隔離器技術的節省效果

使用隔離器時，可能減少的項目：

  • 房間空氣分級與監測要求
  • 穿衣等級要求
  • 氣閘與穿衣室數量
  • 清潔範圍與頻率
  • 房間飾面與細部要求（但仍需滿足最低標準）

注意：物料流仍需控制

即使使用隔離器，物料、製程、人員、廢棄物和設備的移動路徑仍需適當分離，以防止混淆和交叉污染。風險評估應確定分離要求，特別是在多產品併行製造時。

4.1.3 Concurrent Production 4.1.3 同步生產

4.1.3 Concurrent Production

Although concurrent production of multiple products (each in its own fully segregated system in the same area) is technically feasible, the practical application can generate many concerns regarding the potential for mix-ups.

Such a facility would have to rely heavily on procedures and automation to control the status of all containers, equipment, and components associated with different lots and stages of production.

In accordance with GMPs, it is generally recommended to provide physical barriers and adequate space to control materials rather than to rely on procedures. Concurrent multi-product facilities, which place different products in separate rooms, provide a robust engineering solution for prevention of lot mix-up and errors.

4.1.3 併行生產

多產品併行生產在技術上可行，但實際操作中混淆風險很高。

GMP 原則：工程手段優於程序手段

GMP 規範一致推薦使用物理屏障與足夠空間來控制物料，而非僱仍依靠程序控制。將不同產品放在獨立房間是最穩健的工程解決方案。

比喻：廚房的食材分隔

就像食品工廠不會在同一工作台上同時處理花生和不含花生產品一樣，藥品工廠應將不同產品放在獨立房間，用物理屏障防止混淆。

4.2 General Design Criteria 4.2 一般設計準則

4.2 General Design Criteria

A facility should be designed to help protect the product. It should also protect operators from hazardous product exposure. Protection begins with a thorough knowledge of the product(s) to be produced. This knowledge sets the direction for facility design.

One of the first major decisions in the project should be to determine which of the three basic approaches (spatial, procedural, or time-based) will apply to the facility design.

The general design criteria are grouped into two major categories:

  • Process and operational
  • Facility (site and building)

4.2 一般設計準則

設施設計的雙重目標：保護產品免受污染，同時保護操作人員免受有害產品暴露。設計的起點是充分理解製造的產品。

設計準則兩大類別

  1. 製程與操作：產品類型、產量、設備、流向
  2. 設施：場址、建築、整合配合

4.2.1 Process & Operational Considerations 4.2.1 製程與營運考量

4.2.1 Process and Operational Considerations

The operating philosophy can determine how a facility is organized and how layouts are developed. Key points to consider include:

  • Types of products and desired throughput per year
  • Potential product hazards and containment requirements
  • Whether products are aseptically produced, non-aseptically produced, or a combination
  • Product final form: liquid, lyophilized powder, or sterile API powder
  • Clinical fills vs. commercial fills (no facility difference, but barrier technology should be utilized)
  • Governing regulatory agencies
  • Product volume scaling up or down
  • Production schedules and rate of product movement through the facility
  • Material handling approaches (high volume lines need high quantities of primary containers)
  • Batch versus continuous processes
  • Use of ready-to-use components (e.g., syringes, vials, stoppers, caps/seals)
  • Use of single-use disposable systems and impact on storage
  • Multi-product campaigned or concurrent production
  • Level of technology: manual fills are high risk and not recommended
  • Level of automation
  • Line integration: primary fill with secondary packaging
  • Open vs. closed processes (RABS require individual rooms; isolators can share rooms)
  • Equipment layout footprints, operational and maintenance access clearances
  • Material staging and access for each process area
  • Movement of used equipment parts to cleaning rooms
  • Environmental room classification for each room or area
  • Number of personnel and gowning philosophy
  • Routing of utilities (central or localized)
  • Waste disposal/treatment
  • Personnel support areas

4.2.1 製程與操作考量

操作哲學決定了設施的組織方式與佈局開發。以下是關鍵考量點的分類整理：

產品與製程定義

  • 產品類型、產量與產能目標
  • 危害性與控制需求
  • 無菌 vs. 非無菌製程
  • 最終劑型：液體、凍乾粉末、無菌 API 粉末
  • 臨床試驗 vs. 商業生產

設備與技術決策

  • 批次 vs. 連續製程（如批次洗瓶+烘箱 vs. 連續隧道）
  • 即用型組件（RTU 針筒、西林瓶、膠塞、封蓋）
  • 一次性系統對倉儲的影響
  • 自動化程度（手動裝填為高風險，不建議）

RABS vs. 隔離器對佈局的影響

開放製程使用 RABS 時，每個開放製程步驟應佔用獨立房間，需要更多樓地面積與更多潔淨 HVAC 分區。隔離器保護的製程則可與其他隔離器製程共用房間。

4.2.2 Site & Building Considerations 4.2.2 廠址與建築考量

4.2.2 Site and Building Considerations

Few projects begin as a "green field" site with unlimited building area. Most projects and sites have limitations from both internal and external sources. The key is to understand the limitations and make reasonable decisions in fitting the process and operational criteria into the project site.

Site and building limitations or opportunities to consider:

  • Site planning ordinances or construction code requirements (building height, total area)
  • Environmental protection codes
  • Operator protection codes
  • Site access/traffic including shipping and receiving vehicles (truck traffic patterns are key for air intake locations)
  • Existing site infrastructure
  • Constructing within an existing building with physical limitations
  • Retrofitting an existing filling suite
  • Project construction phasing, schedule, funding, and approvals

4.2.2 場址與建築考量

大多數專案都有場址限制。關鍵在於理解這些限制，並合理地將製程與操作需求整合到場址中。

特別注意：車輛與進氣位置

卡車與大型車輛的交通動線對決定 HVAC 與製程壓縮空氣系統的進氣位置至關重要。進氣口應遠離排氣、車輛廢氣與飾塵源。

常見專案場景

  • 新建（Green Field）：最大設計自由度
  • 既有建築改造：受結構、樓高、柱距限制
  • 既有裝填套件改裝：最嚴格的限制，需在原有框架內最佳化

4.2.3 Facility Fit Considerations 4.2.3 設施適配性考量

4.2.3 Facility Fit Considerations

Fitting or integrating the process and operational requirements into a project site is considered essential for a successful project. Although the project focus tends to be on the production areas, designers should also consider equipment, engineering, and operational requirements.

This process is called facility modeling. Consideration should be given to facility systems and support areas to ensure that the entire project scope can be accommodated.

4.2.3 設施適配考量

將製程與操作需求整合到專案場址是專案成功的關鍵。這個過程稱為設施建模（Facility Modeling）。

除了生產區域外，設計者還應考慮：

  • 設備維護空間
  • 工程技術區域（機械夹層、管道通道）
  • 操作支援區域（清潔室、倉庫、人員支援）

4.3 Layout Considerations 4.3 配置考量

4.3 Layout Considerations

Designers should go through a programming process consisting of the following steps:

  1. Define goals and objectives that support the business case for the project
  2. Understand product and process requirements and use this information to generate block flow diagrams and a specific project program
  3. Create a zoning and transition diagram which defines transition requirements between different area classifications and identifies directional airflows. This establishes the "rules" the layout should follow.
  4. Develop conceptual layout based on the program, equipment arrangements, and requirements of the zoning and transition diagram

The process specialist, architect, layout engineer, HVAC engineer, and QA representative should collaborate to ensure a successful integrated design.

4.3.1 Project Goals and Objectives: Goals are the "what" — expected outcomes. Objectives are the "how" — statements of action that should be clear, realistic, specific, measurable, and time-limited.

4.3.2 Block Flow Diagram: Used to define production steps, identify major processing areas, area classifications, key adjacencies, segregation, and flows. They document inputs and outputs for given activities.

4.3.3 Facility Program: A list of all rooms with special requirements and designated area classifications. An initial program should be developed based on known requirements and updated as the design develops. (See Table 4.1 for example.)

4.3 佈局考量

設計師應遵循四步驟規劃流程：

佈局設計四步驟

  1. 定義目標與目的 — 支持專案商業案例
  2. 理解產品與製程 — 產生方塊流程圖與專案程式書
  3. 建立分區與轉換圖 — 定義區域分級轉換與氣流方向
  4. 發展概念佈局 — 整合設備配置與分區規則

比喻：佈局設計如城市規劃

佈局設計如同規劃一座城市：先確定功能分區（住宅、商業、工業），再規劃交通動線（物料流與人員流），最後布置具體建築（設備配置）。分區圖就是城市的都市計畫法，確保各區域間的轉換合理。

設施程式書（Facility Program）範例：

4.3.4 Transition and Zoning Diagram

The transition and zoning diagram identifies all areas that can affect or influence the required space or unit operations, defines their interrelationships, and establishes the flow pattern that best represents the process GMP and operator requirements.

These diagrams establish the "rules" of the facility and serve as the basis from which the layout is developed. Personnel, product, and material flows should be fully understood prior to development of the layout.

Area classifications and directional airflows should be defined to ensure proper airlock schemes at transitions and where containment is required.

4.3.5 Space Planning: The designer should develop a series of functional room layouts which graphically illustrate the area requirements to support operations. A conceptual layout is developed by combining all functional room layouts in an arrangement meeting transition and zoning requirements.

4.3.6 Equipment Arrangements: Equipment arrangements help determine room sizes, structural grids, and access routes. They are generally developed to optimize production, but facility restrictions may impact arrangements, requiring collaborative effort between architects, engineers, and equipment vendors.

4.3.4 轉換與分區圖

轉換與分區圖識別所有影響單元操作的區域，定義其相互關係，並建立最能符合 GMP 和操作員需求的流動模式。

分區圖的關鍵要素

  • 區域分級：每個房間的潔淨等級
  • 氣流方向：從高潔淨區流向低潔淨區（壓力梯度）
  • 氣閘配置：每個區域轉換點的氣閘設計
  • 人員與物料路徑：清楚定義的動線

空間規劃：設計師應開發功能房間佈局，圖解支援操作所需的面積。團隊應評估未來技術或產能擴充對空間的影響。

設備配置：設備配置協助確定房間大小、結構柱距和通道路線。需要建築師、工程師與設備供應商共同協作。

4.3.7 Material/Personnel Flows 4.3.7 物料/人員動線

4.3.7 Material/Personnel Flows

The design of personnel and material flows should minimize or prevent the introduction of contaminants into the clean area. This is significant in open system aseptic processing rooms where container closures and product are exposed to the room.

Product, material, and equipment flows should address:

  • Layout should prevent product cross-contamination and environmental contamination
  • One-way flows should be considered for suites where open aseptic processing occurs without barrier technology or with RABS
  • Simultaneous two-way flows through a common area should be prohibited by using door interlocks, indicator lights, alarms, or similar means
  • Process waste should be removed from the aseptic area without contaminating the product
  • In-process storage should be provided
  • Logical flow of product components to prevent mix-ups

Personnel flow into and within the clean area should address:

  • Compliance with gowning requirements
  • Sufficient space for personnel movement with clearly defined instructions
  • Compliance with GMP and HVAC zones
  • No non-emergency personnel ingress/egress except through controlled gowning change area
  • Design of airlocks, step-over benches, gowning areas, time delay alarms, and door interlocks
  • One-way personnel flow for areas where product is exposed to the room environment
  • Minimizing interventions into the critical zone

Note: Changing rooms requiring crossover benches for GMP should not be placed in the path of egress as the benches could be viewed as tripping hazards.

4.3.7 物料流與人員流

人員與物料流的設計應最大程度降低污染物進入潔淨區的風險。

物料流設計原則

  • 單向流：開放製程區域應採用單向流動
  • 禁止雙向同步流：透過門聯鎖、指示燈、警報防止
  • 廢棄物路徑：不得經過產品暴露區
  • 製程中暫存：應提供適當空間
  • 避免混淆：組件流動路徑應合理明確

人員流設計原則

  • 穿衣合規：每次進入必須經過控制的穿衣區
  • 氣閘與跨越式更衣椅：門聯鎖防止同時雙向通行
  • 單向人員流：產品暴露區域必須單向
  • 最小化干預：減少對臨界區的人員介入

安全注意：跨越椅 vs. 逃生路徑

GMP 要求的跨越式更衣椅不應放在緊急逃生路徑上，因為它們可能被視為絆倒危險。應考慮使用物料氣閘或獨立緊急門作為逃生路徑。

4.3.8 Additional Layout Considerations 4.3.8 其他配置考量

4.3.8 Additional Layout Considerations

In addition to flow considerations, the layout should address:

  • Adoption of barrier or isolator technology can significantly impact material flow and personnel movement compared with traditional open aseptic processing
  • A risk assessment should determine the extent of unidirectional flows, considering cleanliness levels, product type, extent of closed processing, and concurrent multi-product production
  • Where room integrity is critical, equipment interfaces with building fabric/finishes should be minimized; where unavoidable, clear access all around should be provided
  • Services penetrating clean areas can be grouped together to allow manifold plates
  • Service distribution and pipework should be located outside the cleanroom in a separate manifold room, where possible
  • Cleanrooms ISO 8/Grade C or cleaner should not be placed directly adjacent to exterior walls (moisture infiltration, pest infiltration, wind influence on room pressure)
  • Equipment interchangeability and long-term maintenance/replacement access should be incorporated
  • General piping and services distribution should be addressed by allocating horizontal and vertical distribution zones
  • HVAC airflow patterns should be compared to equipment layout to avoid turbulence or dead spots in critical zones
  • Horizontal surfaces should be avoided to prevent UAF disruption and particle accumulation
  • Open sinks and drains are not permitted in aseptic processing areas (ISO 7/Grade B and ISO 5/Grade A)
  • Properly designed HEPA filtered portable vacuums are acceptable. Central vacuum systems should have back flow preventers installed.

4.3.8 附加佈局考量

除了流動設計外，佈局還應處理以下問題：

關鍵規則：潔淨室與外牆

ISO 8/Grade C 或更高等級的潔淨室不應直接緊鄰外牆。原因包括：

  • 濕氣滲透/凝結風險
  • 害蟲入侵風險
  • 風力對房間壓力的影響

管路與服務配置原則

  • 穿越潔淨區的管路應集中配置，使用歧管板
  • 管路與服務配置盡量放在潔淨室外的獨立管道室
  • 分配水平與垂直管道區域

無菌區域嚴禁事項

  • ISO 7/Grade B 和 ISO 5/Grade A 區域禁止開放式水槽與排水口
  • 水平面應盡量減少，防止微粒積累與干擾單向氣流（UAF）
  • 真空系統的主機不得放在 ISO 5 或 ISO 7 區域內

4.3.9–4.3.10 Cost Optimization & Fire Protection 4.3.9–4.3.10 成本最佳化與消防

4.3.9 Planning Layouts to Minimize Cost

External Building Shape: The layout configuration affects cost by influencing materials, labor, and running costs. External walls and insulation are high cost items. Simple plan shapes are most economical. Minimum perimeter length results from a square plan shape.

Building Height: Average cost per square meter increases with the number of stories due to:

  • Increase in perimeter wall for any given total floor area
  • Effect of increased load on the structure
  • Additional hoisting of materials and extra time for operators to reach higher floors

Foundation: Foundation costs vary with load and height. Cost of structure per square meter increases rapidly above four stories.

Internal Layouts: The overall cost of the aseptic area (including HVAC services) is significantly higher than any other part of the facility. This area should be kept as small as possible without affecting efficient operation.

Modular wall and ceiling systems or prefabricated systems reduce construction time and may provide flexibility to expand, rearrange, or relocate.

4.3.10 Fire Protection and Means of Escape

Issues become more onerous as building size grows:

  • Specific time periods of fire resistance for design elements
  • Compartmentalization of the building to isolate fire within specific areas
  • Emergency escape routes for personnel
  • Provision of suitable separation to prevent fire, hot gases, and smoke spreading via circulation routes

4.3.9 成本最佳化佈局

外部建築形狀：簡單的平面形狀最經濟。正方形平面在相同面積下週長最小，外牆成本最低。

建築高度與成本關係

  • 樓層增加 → 每平方米平均成本上升
  • 超過四層時結構成本急劇增加
  • 環境與服務隨建築複雜度與高度增加而變得更貴

關鍵成本原則：無菌區面積最小化

無菌區域（含 HVAC 服務）的整體成本顯著高於設施其他部分。在不影響製造效率的前提下，應盡量縮小無菌區面積。

模組化牆體與天花板系統可縮短施工時間，並提供未來擴建、重新配置或搬遷的彈性。

4.3.10 消防與逃生

  • 建築設計元件的耐火時限要求
  • 建築分艘化：將火災隔離在特定區域
  • 人員緊急逃生路徑
  • 防止火焰、高溫氣體與煙霧透過水平/垂直通路擴散
3b

Chapter 3b: 4b. Architecture (4.4–4.6)

建築佈局（中） | p92-p100

ISPE Baseline Guide Vol. 3 (3rd Ed.) | p92 – p100

Learning Objectives / 本節學習目標

  1. Identify the five general functional categories of facility areas and their roles in sterile manufacturing. / 辨識設施區域的五大功能分類及其在無菌製造中的角色。
  2. Explain the design requirements for changing rooms, including gowning philosophy and ingress/egress control. / 說明更衣室的設計要求，包括更衣策略與進出動線控制。
  3. Describe how surface finishes and materials of construction vary by area classification (Grade D through Grade A). / 描述不同區域等級（D 級至 A 級）的表面處理與建材要求差異。
  4. Compare airlock types (PAL, MAL, pass-through) and their design philosophies for contamination control. / 比較各類氣閘（人員氣閘、物料氣閘、傳遞窗）及其污染控制設計策略。
  5. Apply the concept of "improvement step" and sequential transitions to design compliant transfer zone procedures. / 將「改善步驟」與逐級轉換概念應用於傳遞區程序的合規設計。

Section Navigator / 章節導覽

4.4 Room Function 4.4.2 Changing Rooms 4.4.3 Bulk Storage 4.5 Surface Finishes Table 4.2 4.5.2 Room Finishes 4.6 Transfer Zones 4.6.1 Improvement Step 4.6.2 Sequential Transitions 4.6.3 Airlock Design 4.6.4 Pass Boxes
4.4

4.4 Room Function

房間功能分類  |  p. 92–93

4.4.1 Room Function

Facility areas are divided into five general functional categories:

  • Areas for aseptic processing of product or components
  • Areas immediately adjacent to the above, comprised of material/personnel airlocks
  • Preparation areas closely related to the aseptic processing area
  • Areas immediately adjacent to the above, comprising material airlocks, personnel clean change, inspection, and other associated areas ("pharmaceutical" areas)
  • General ancillary/support functions, including warehousing, offices, plant utilities, and circulation areas with no protection requirements other than, perhaps, a factory change/uniform for unclassified areas

房間功能五大分類

ISPE 將無菌設施分成五個層級，從最核心的無菌製程區到最外圈的一般支援區，層層遞進。理解這五層結構是設計潔淨室布局的基礎。

核心概念：由內到外五圈防護

  • 第一圈：無菌製程核心（Grade A/B）— 產品直接暴露區
  • 第二圈：緊鄰氣閘與人員/物料轉換區
  • 第三圈：準備區（配液、清洗、組裝）
  • 第四圈：製藥區（檢驗、乾淨更衣、物料暫存）
  • 第五圈：一般輔助區（倉庫、辦公室、公用工程）

比喻：洋蔥式防護

想像整個設施是一顆洋蔥 — 每一層都是一道屏障。越靠近中心（無菌核心），環境控制越嚴格；每跨越一層，都必須經過一個「轉換站」（氣閘或更衣室）。這就是為什麼設施布局必須從核心向外規劃。

4.4

4.4.2 Changing Rooms

更衣室設計  |  p. 93

4.4.2 Changing Rooms

Changing rooms should be designed to accommodate the gowning philosophy and changing regimes determined by process operations. They should be arranged to support procedures which prevent the ingress of outside environmental contaminant. Personnel should pass from facility changing rooms (where street clothes are replaced with facility uniforms) to clean environment or aseptic changing rooms in a logical progression.

Changing rooms into open process aseptic areas (including RABS) should, where possible, have separate ingress/egress routes to prevent chemical or bio-contamination of clean garments. Clean and aseptic processing change areas can be sequential and in separate rooms. HVAC and personnel movements should be controlled.

Changing facilities can range from CNC or Grade D to ISO 7/Grade B or higher, so the changing area standards and finishes should be appropriate for the highest cleanliness processing area into which it opens. The flow and storage of gowning materials should also be considered in the design.

Personal showering and toilet facilities should not be directly connected to classified cleanroom locker room or gowning areas.

更衣室設計要點

更衣室設計四大原則

  • 邏輯遞進：人員從一般更衣室（換廠服）逐步進入潔淨更衣室（穿無塵衣），分階段完成。
  • 進出分離：進入無菌區（含 RABS）的更衣室應盡可能設計獨立的進入與離開路線，避免乾淨衣物被汙染。
  • 等級匹配：更衣室的環境控制標準應匹配它所通往的最高潔淨等級。
  • 隔離廁所：淋浴間與廁所不得直接連通分級潔淨室或更衣區。

實務提醒

更衣室的「進出分離」原則在稽核中是常見缺失項。許多舊廠因空間限制，進出共用同一條走廊。若無法實體分離，至少需要有 SOP 規定同時只允許單向通行（gowning 或 de-gowning），並以 HVAC 正壓流向作為補償措施。

4.4

4.4.3 Bulk Storage Areas

散裝儲存區  |  p. 93

4.4.3 Bulk Storage Areas

Bulk storage areas within warehouses are generally remote from the clean core. Some intermediate, product, and components storage may be required within the preparation and aseptic processing areas. Storage within these areas should have dedicated floor space and may need special HVAC provisions.

散裝儲存區設計

大宗物料倉儲區通常遠離潔淨核心。但某些中間產品、成品或零組件可能需要暫存於準備區或無菌製程區內。此類暫存區需有專屬空間並可能需要特殊的 HVAC 設計（如溫濕度控制）。

比喻：廚房的食材暫存

大倉庫像是餐廳後方的冷藏庫（遠離料理區），但廚房內通常還需要一個小型工作台冰箱來暫放即將使用的食材。潔淨室內的暫存區就是這個「工作台冰箱」— 空間小、控管嚴、只放即將投入製程的物料。

4.5

4.5 Surface Finishes and Materials of Construction

表面處理與建材  |  p. 93–94

4.5.1 Architectural Detailing

In detailing the architectural aspects of cleanrooms, key factors which should be addressed include:

  • The principal function of the room is to provide an enclosure to contain the defined activity and its associated equipment.
  • Finish materials should be non-shedding, non-porous, and resistant to sustaining microbial growth.
  • Surfaces should be smooth and easy to clean, with minimal ledges and joints. Corners at walls, ceilings, and floors should be coved with a sufficient radius to facilitate cleaning and minimize areas that are difficult to access, particularly near the product and process equipment.
  • Finishes should be able to withstand repeated cleaning and sanitization with various chemicals and resist surface oxidization.
  • Attention should be given to these issues when detailing any interface between the facility and the equipment and services.
  • Wall protection and guarding to prevent mechanical failure should be considered to maintain the integrity of the finishes and minimize damage or premature wearing.

Door hardware should be carefully considered for ease of cleaning. "Hands off" proximity sensors and openers should be installed, where possible. Normally, doors should swing towards higher room pressures, to assist in maintaining differential pressurization. Fire regulations governing escape in an emergency, however, usually take precedence, requiring door closers of sufficient force to overcome the pressure. Door interlocks should have emergency override features in case of fire.

A risk assessment should be made when doors swing into ISO 7/Grade B or higher areas as these doors may contaminate the aseptic area, having been exposed to lower classified areas.

The goal of architectural detailing is to help protect the product by providing finishes which can withstand cleaning and sanitization requirements, providing details which minimize horizontal ledges and provide tight seals at penetration points or where different systems are integrated.

Higher quality, robust finishes can evoke an environment of cleanliness and control, where lesser finishes which do not hold up as well to use and cleaning can make a facility look dated and in need of repair. Higher quality finishes demonstrate a dedication to quality to inspectors.

建築細節設計

潔淨室表面處理六大原則

  • 不脫落（Non-shedding）：材料不會釋出微粒
  • 不滲透（Non-porous）：表面不吸收液體或微生物
  • 抗微生物：不利於微生物在表面附著生長
  • 易清潔：表面光滑、接縫最少、牆角圓弧化（Coved）
  • 耐化學品：能承受反覆清潔消毒，不氧化腐蝕
  • 耐衝擊：需考慮防撞設施，尤其是高流量區域

門的設計 — 壓差與消防的兩難

門應朝壓力較高的一側開啟，以維持壓差。但消防法規要求門朝逃生方向開啟。這兩個需求常互相衝突，尤其在 Grade B 以上區域。解決方案通常是加裝足夠力量的門弓器（Door Closer）來克服壓差，並且設置緊急開門覆蓋功能。

比喻：表面處理像選「防水手機殼」

潔淨室的表面處理就像選手機保護殼一樣 — 你需要它防水（不滲透）、防摔（耐衝擊）、好擦拭（易清潔），而且不能掉漆（不脫落）。越高等級的潔淨室，就像越昂貴的手機，需要越高規格的保護。

稽核觀點：外觀即品質

ISPE 特別指出：高品質的表面處理可以向稽核員傳達對品質的承諾。反之，老舊脫落的牆面或生鏽的門框會讓稽核員對整個設施的管理水準產生懷疑。這不只是美觀問題，更是 GMP 文化的展現。

T4.2

Table 4.2: Architectural Materials and Finishes Guide

建材與表面處理指引表  |  p. 94–97

Table 4.2 — Floors

Table 4.2 — Interior Walls

Table 4.2 — Ceilings

Table 4.2 — Junctions, Doors, Hardware, Lighting, Sprinklers, Penetrations

Table 4.2 關鍵解讀

建材等級速查邏輯

隨著區域等級從「未分級」升至 Grade A，建材要求呈現明確的階梯式升級：

  • 地板：密封混凝土 → 環氧樹脂/乙烯基 → 焊縫乙烯基+圓弧踢腳板 → 禁止排水口
  • 牆壁：乳膠漆石膏板 → 金屬面板/釉面磚 → 化學抗性塗料 → 無縫隙、圓角、抗腐蝕
  • 天花板：懸吊式天花 → FRP/金屬面板 → 密封齊平安裝 → HEPA 過濾器陣列（UAF）
  • 門：標準五金 → 環氧塗裝金屬 → 全不鏽鋼 + 免接觸感應器

Grade A 的獨特要求

  • 禁止排水口和水槽（Floor drains and sinks are not permitted）
  • 天花板由 HEPA/ULPA 過濾器陣列組成，提供單向氣流（UAF）
  • 消防噴頭必須為不擾動 UAF 的特殊設計
  • 所有門把五金為凹入式、免接觸致動器

比喻：從一般廚房到手術室

未分級區就像家裡的廚房 — 用瓷磚地板、塗漆牆壁就足夠了。Grade C/D 像是餐廳後廚 — 需要不鏽鋼檯面和可沖洗地板。Grade A 則像手術室 — 天花板就是層流出風口、牆角全部圓弧化、地上不能有一個排水孔。每升一級，就更接近「零死角、零藏污」的極致標準。

常見稽核缺失：石膏板發霉

Table 4.2 的 Note 2 特別警告：石膏板（Gypsum Board）在高濕度或頻繁清潔消毒區域有發霉風險。若必須使用，應選擇玻璃面或抗菌石膏板。這是新廠設計時最容易忽略、舊廠最常出問題的建材議題。

4.5

4.5.2 Room Finishes

房間表面規格  |  p. 98

4.5.2 Room Finishes

While specifying room finishes for cleanrooms, key factors which should be addressed include:

  • The nature of the process performed in the room should be considered. Manufacturing or preparation activity in an ISO 8/Grade C room places more demands on housekeeping, cleaning, disinfection, and environmental monitoring than if an aseptic processing isolator were placed in the same room.
  • The balance of installation costs against maintainability and ease with which repair or replacement can be performed.
  • Finishes should allow for the ease of installation of building services, grilles, controls/switches, and piped penetrations.
  • Finishes should accommodate integration of fixtures such as CCTV, intercom panels, key pads, telephones, sprinkler heads and covers, and emergency showers.
  • Wall or floor mounted wall protection is recommended in high traffic areas.
  • Fire protection aspects should be accommodated: surface flame spread, fire resistant construction (doors and vision panels), detectors, sprinkler heads, and alarm sounders.
  • Air tightness of room fabric, particularly around door openings and sprinkler heads, and the choice of finish materials that are not adversely affected by sanitizing chemicals.
  • All wall penetrations (electrical outlets, data ports, fire extinguisher cabinets, etc.) should be sealed to maintain air pressure control and prevent pest infiltration.
  • Electrically conductive and grounded flooring should be considered in areas where explosion control is required.
  • Method and frequency of cleaning, cleaning agents, and details such as equipment surface fixings and floor drains should be considered. Floor drains are not permitted inside the aseptic processing area. In other areas, floor drains should be minimized with concave, minimum 2" air break on process drain lines. Back flow preventers and trap controllers should be utilized.

房間表面規格選擇要點

表面規格選擇的決策因素

  • 製程需求：同一等級房間內，開放式製程 vs. 隔離器操作，對表面要求天差地別
  • 安裝 vs. 維護成本：選材時需平衡初始安裝成本與長期維護/更換的便利性
  • 系統整合：牆面必須容納 CCTV、對講機、門禁、消防噴頭等多種設備
  • 氣密性：門框、噴頭、穿管等所有開口都必須密封，維持壓差控制
  • 防爆：有溶劑的區域需考慮防靜電導電地板

排水口管控 — 微生物風險熱點

排水口是潔淨室微生物汙染的高風險點。ISPE 的立場非常明確：

  • 無菌製程區（Aseptic Area）：完全禁止排水口
  • 準備區等其他區域：排水口應最小化，且必須使用凹面設計、至少 2 吋空氣斷口、逆流防止器與存水彎控制器

排水口的微生物回溯汙染（Backsplash/Backflow）是導致無菌測試失敗與批次報廢的常見原因之一。

思考練習

你的 Grade C 準備區目前使用環氧樹脂地板搭配排水口，用於清洗作業排水。最近連續兩次環境監測發現排水口附近的微生物計數偏高。你會考慮哪些改善措施？

  • 增加排水口的清潔消毒頻率
  • 安裝逆流防止器與存水彎監控器
  • 評估是否能減少排水口數量或重新配置位置
  • 在排水口上加裝密封蓋，僅在排水時打開
4.6

4.6 Transfer Zones

傳遞區（氣閘系統）  |  p. 98–99

4.6 Transfer Zones

Transfer zones and airlocks into and out of cleanroom areas should provide suitable transition for materials, personnel, equipment and waste. Airlocks are used to maintain pressure differentials between areas of differing classifications and to provide a controlled environment for the transfer of materials or the transition/gowning of personnel between classified areas.

Personnel and material (including components, raw materials, equipment and waste) require airlocks to enter and exit areas of different classifications. The staging and movement of personnel and materials should be designed to minimize errors, maintain gowning room hygiene, and minimize the risk of cross-contamination. Airlocks should be appropriately sized and environmentally controlled depending upon the activity occurring within the airlock.

傳遞區總論

氣閘（Airlock）的三大功能

  • 維持壓差：作為不同等級區域之間的緩衝空間，防止一開門就破壞壓差梯度
  • 提供轉換環境：人員更衣、物料清潔消毒等「改善步驟」在此完成
  • 降低交叉污染風險：通過門互鎖、單向流動等機制，確保低等級空氣不進入高等級區域

比喻：潛水艇的壓力艙

氣閘就像潛水艇上的壓力艙（Airlock）— 你不能直接從海水中走進潛艇內部，必須先進入壓力艙、關閉外門、調整壓力、再打開內門。潔淨室的氣閘也是一樣的概念：關門 → 執行清潔/更衣 → 等待壓差恢復 → 再開另一扇門。兩扇門永遠不能同時打開。

4.6

4.6.1 Improvement Step

改善步驟  |  p. 99

4.6.1 Improvement Step

There is an expectation that when personnel and materials transition from a lower area classification to a higher area classification that an improvement step occurs.

For materials, the improvement step can be a cleaning and/or sanitization activity:

  • Depending on the cleanliness of the intended area, it can consist of removing an outer cover or wrapping, a manual wipe down, or fumigation/decontamination.
  • A transition line is recommended for airlocks moving into ISO 8/Grade C and higher areas. Materials should be transferred over the line after they have been cleaned/sanitized.
  • For materials going into a CNC or Grade D space, cleaning can take place outside of the Grade D airlock.

For personnel, the improvement step can include putting on an additional layer of protective clothing.

改善步驟 — 每次跨級都要「升級」

「改善步驟」核心規則

從低等級區域進入高等級區域時，必須執行一項能提升清潔度的具體行動（Improvement Step）：

  • 物料：拆除外包裝 / 擦拭消毒 / 燻蒸除汙
  • 人員：加穿一層防護衣物

轉換線（Transition Line）

氣閘內應設置視覺明確的「轉換線」— 物料必須在清潔消毒完成後才能跨越此線。這是一個簡單但極為有效的防汙染措施。在 ISO 8/Grade C 及更高等級的氣閘中，ISPE 明確建議設置轉換線。

實務上，轉換線可以是地板上一條醒目的彩色膠帶或嵌入式標線。有些設施甚至使用不同顏色的地板來區分「髒側」和「乾淨側」。

比喻：機場安檢線

就像過機場安檢一樣 — 行李（物料）要過 X 光機（消毒），人要脫外套過金屬探測門（換穿防護衣）。安檢線前後是不同管制等級的區域，你不能帶著未經檢查的東西越過那條線。

4.6

4.6.2 Sequential Transitions

逐級轉換  |  p. 99

4.6.2 Sequential Transitions

Airlock transitions should occur one grade at a time when transitioning from lower to higher (cleaner) classifications, for both personnel and materials. When exiting, it is often acceptable to step down in classification. Although, when exiting from an ISO 7/Grade B production room, an ISO 7/Grade B exit airlock is preferred to protect the critical area.

An airlock should be provided for transitioning from an unclassified environment into CNC or Grade D.

ISO 5/Grade A environments may only be accessed from ISO 7/Grade B environments. Airlocks are generally not provided between ISO 5/Grade A and ISO 7/Grade B; however, clear visual indications and physical barriers should be provided so that the boundary between these environments can be seen and understood by personnel.

ISO 7/Grade B environments should be accessed from ISO 8/Grade C, through airlocks. There should be separate entry airlocks for personnel and materials for entry to ISO 7/Grade B from ISO 8/Grade C rooms. The entry airlock into an ISO 7/Grade B aseptic area should demonstrate ISO 7 "at rest" conditions in the location where the final stages of gowning occurs.

Regular access to mechanical rooms should be from unclassified areas, or provisions should be made to accommodate required airlocks and gowning.

逐級轉換的關鍵規則

等級轉換路徑圖

進入時必須逐級升級：

未分級 → CNC/Grade D → ISO 8/Grade C → ISO 7/Grade B → ISO 5/Grade A

  • 每一個「→」都代表一個氣閘轉換
  • 不可跳級（例如不可從 Grade D 直接進入 Grade B）
  • 退出時可以跳級，但 Grade B 出口仍建議設 Grade B 氣閘以保護核心區

Grade A 與 Grade B 的特殊關係

Grade A 與 Grade B 之間通常不設氣閘（因為 Grade A 本身就在 Grade B 環境內），但必須有：

  • 清晰的視覺指示（如地板標線、顏色區分）
  • 物理屏障（如 RABS 擋板、懸掛式隔簾）

Grade C 進入 Grade B 時，必須設置人員與物料分離的獨立氣閘。Grade B 人員氣閘中最後階段更衣處需達到 ISO 7「靜態」條件。

快速自測

一名技術人員需要從倉庫（未分級）進入 Grade B 無菌充填室。請列出他需要經過的所有氣閘和更衣步驟：

  1. 未分級 → Grade D 氣閘（換廠服）
  2. Grade D → Grade C 人員氣閘（穿第一層無塵衣）
  3. Grade C → Grade B 人員氣閘（穿完整無菌衣 + 手套 + 護目鏡，最後更衣處達 ISO 7 靜態）
  4. Grade B → Grade A：無氣閘，但有視覺標示與物理屏障
4.6

4.6.3 Airlock Design Philosophies

氣閘設計策略  |  p. 99–101

4.6.3 Airlock Design Philosophies

Airflow direction is generally from higher grade to lower grade. A higher grade room or airlock should be positive to a lower grade room or airlock. Airlock doors should be interlocked or alarmed to prevent both sets of doors from being opened simultaneously, to control the ingress of potential contaminates to the cleaner zones.

Alternate airlock pressurization schemes are often required for containment or the mitigation of cross-contamination between different products. A risk assessment should be performed on such airlocks to evaluate the risk of product contamination versus the potential for cross-contamination or the requirements for containment.

氣閘設計基本原則

氣閘壓差與門互鎖

  • 氣流方向：從高等級流向低等級（正壓向外推）
  • 壓差維持：氣閘本身應對低等級側保持正壓
  • 門互鎖（Interlock）：兩扇門不得同時打開，可用機械互鎖或電子連鎖+警報

密閉 vs. 防護 — 壓差方向的例外

當需要「防護」（Containment）時，壓差方向可能反轉 — 例如處理高活性或高毒性產品時，氣閘需要對產品區保持負壓，防止有害物質外洩。此時需要風險評估來權衡：

  • 產品汙染風險（外界進入）
  • 交叉汙染風險（產品間）
  • 操作人員安全（有害物質外洩）

4.6.3.1 Personnel Airlocks (PAL) 4.6.3.1 人員氣閘 (PAL)

4.6.3.1 Personnel Airlocks (PAL) from Lower Grade to Higher Grade

Unidirectional flow is suggested for ISO 8/Grade C and higher personnel airlocks (i.e., personnel should not gown and de-gown in the same PAL). If a single airlock is provided, procedures should be established to prevent simultaneous gowning and de-gowning.

PAL considerations include:

  • PALs should have clearly defined changing areas, adequate garment storage, dressing mirrors, and access control.
  • Step-over benches should be used in ISO 8/Grade C and ISO 7/Grade B PALs to put on shoe covers, boot covers, etc.
  • Toilet rooms should not be directly accessed from locker rooms or transfer zones where personnel will change for entry into ISO 8/Grade C or higher areas.
  • Hand washing sinks should be limited to CNC or Grade D areas.
  • Hand sanitizing gels and solutions should be used in higher (cleaner) classifications.

人員氣閘（PAL）設計

PAL 設計五要素

  • 單向流動：進入與離開應使用不同路線（Grade C 以上）
  • 跨越板凳（Step-over Bench）：Grade C 與 Grade B 的 PAL 中用於穿鞋套，劃分乾淨側與髒側
  • 更衣鏡：讓人員自我檢查更衣完整性
  • 門禁控制：確保只有經過更衣訓練的人員進入
  • 洗手設施：洗手水槽僅限 Grade D 以下；Grade C 以上使用乾洗手液

為什麼高等級區不能有水槽？

水槽是微生物的溫床 — 水、有機物、溫度三者結合，是理想的微生物培養環境。排水管線更可能藏匿 Pseudomonas 等水源性微生物。因此 ISPE 規定 Grade C 以上區域以乾洗手液取代水洗。這也呼應了 4.5.2 中「無菌區禁止排水口」的原則。

比喻：Step-over Bench 就像鞋店的試穿凳

跨越板凳的功能就像鞋店的試穿凳 — 你坐下來，把街上穿的鞋脫掉放在凳子的「髒側」，腳跨過凳子到「乾淨側」穿上無塵鞋套。這個簡單的物理隔離確保地板上的汙染物不會被鞋底帶進潔淨區。

4.6.3.2 Material Airlocks (MAL) 4.6.3.2 物料氣閘 (MAL)

4.6.3.2 Material Airlocks (MAL) from Lower Grade to Higher Grade

Airlocks should be sized appropriately to allow materials to be staged in the airlocks during disinfectant dwell times and to allow personnel adequate space for movement without compromising the materials or airflows.

Personnel gowning is allowed in a material airlock exclusively to allow personnel access to higher grade airlocks to support the movement of material. Personnel may not enter the production suite through this path.

A transition line should be established when an improvement step takes place within the airlock. Transition across the line requires an improvement activity, either unwrapping or wiping of all materials.

For sequential, adjacent MALs, personnel on the entry side of a MAL may pass through the MAL to the entry side of the higher grade MAL for the purpose of facilitating material movement. For example, CNC or Grade D personnel can go to the entry side of the ISO 8/Grade C MAL (without crossing the transition line).

Note: Manual transfers into ISO 7/Grade B are often inferior to automated sterilization systems or decontamination chambers; these should be used where practical. Decontamination should allow for the required dwell time to assure the effectiveness of disinfection for manual transfers.

物料氣閘（MAL）設計

MAL 的獨特設計要求

  • 空間尺寸：必須能容納物料在消毒劑停留時間（Dwell Time）內暫存，同時讓人員有足夠操作空間
  • 轉換線：MAL 內設置轉換線，物料必須經過擦拭或拆除外包裝後才能越線
  • 人員限制：人員可以在 MAL 內更衣（僅為協助物料移動），但不可經由 MAL 路線進入生產區
  • 逐級通行：低等級人員可進入 MAL 的入口側（髒側），但不可跨越轉換線

自動化 vs. 手動傳遞

ISPE 明確指出：手動將物料傳入 Grade B 的方式，通常不如自動滅菌系統或除汙腔室可靠。建議在可行情況下使用自動化方案（如 VHP 除汙傳遞艙、隧道式烘箱）。若仍需手動傳遞，必須確保消毒劑有足夠的接觸停留時間（Dwell Time），以達到有效的消毒效果。

4.6.3.3 & 4.6.3.4 Same Grade / Exit Airlocks 4.6.3.3 & 4.6.3.4 同級/出口氣閘

4.6.3.3 PAL or MAL within the Same Grade

No additional gowning is required when moving between areas of the same grade, except where required for personnel protection or material containment.

4.6.3.4 Exit Airlocks from Higher Grade to Lower Grade

Generally, personnel and materials can share exit airlocks. Separate personnel and material exit airlocks are preferred at higher classifications where the de-gowning activity is substantial and in areas of high material movement activity.

Separate airlocks must be provided when there is a dwell time associated with material decontamination using chemical disinfectants.

同級通行與出口氣閘

同級通行

在相同等級區域之間移動，不需要額外更衣。但如果涉及人員防護（如高活性藥物）或物料防護（防止交叉汙染），仍需額外措施。

出口氣閘設計原則

  • 原則上，人員與物料可共用出口氣閘
  • 高等級區域建議分開 — 因為脫衣程序繁複且物料流量大
  • 當物料需要化學消毒且有停留時間要求時，必須分設獨立氣閘

出口設計常被忽略

許多設施在設計時把重點放在「入口」，卻忽略了「出口」的汙染控制。其實出口也是風險點 — 脫衣過程中釋放的微粒、廢棄物料的處理、以及開門時的氣流擾動，都可能影響高等級區域的環境完整性。

4.6

4.6.4 Pass Boxes

傳遞窗  |  p. 100–101

4.6.4 Pass Boxes

Pass boxes (also known as pass-through boxes or transfer hatches) may be used in lieu of material airlocks for smaller materials, equipment, product containers, waste, samples, etc.

The materials and construction should be compatible with the cleaning regime and consistent with the standards of the room(s) they are located in.

For detailed information about pass boxes, refer to Chapters 5 and 11.

傳遞窗（Pass Box）

傳遞窗 vs. 物料氣閘

  • 傳遞窗（Pass Box / Pass-Through）：用於小型物品（樣品、容器、廢棄物等），體積較小，通常嵌入牆壁
  • 物料氣閘（MAL）：用於大型設備、整批物料，需要人員進入操作
  • 兩者都必須具備門互鎖功能，兩扇門不得同時開啟
  • 傳遞窗的建材與表面處理必須符合其所在房間的等級要求

比喻：銀行的氣動傳遞筒

傳遞窗就像銀行得來速（Drive-through）的氣動傳遞筒 — 你把文件放進去、關上你這邊的門、銀行行員打開另一邊取出。兩端的門永遠不會同時打開，物品在密閉通道中完成轉移。差別在於潔淨室的傳遞窗還可能內建 UV 燈或 HEPA 過濾器來進一步降低汙染風險。

綜合練習：設計一個 Grade C 到 Grade B 的傳遞方案

你的設施需要將以下三類物品從 Grade C 傳入 Grade B 無菌充填室。請為每類物品選擇適當的傳遞方式：

  1. 環境監測培養皿（小型） — 適合使用傳遞窗（Pass Box），內部可擦拭消毒
  2. 不鏽鋼充填零件（中型，需滅菌） — 建議使用自動除汙傳遞艙或隧道式乾熱滅菌爐
  3. 整托盤的玻璃瓶（大型批量） — 需使用物料氣閘（MAL），搭配轉換線與擦拭消毒程序

Section Summary / 本節重點摘要

  • Five functional zones: Sterile facilities are organized from the aseptic core outward through preparation, pharmaceutical, and support zones, each requiring progressively less stringent controls. / 五大功能區：無菌設施從核心無菌區向外依序為準備區、製藥區、支援區，環境控制逐步遞減。
  • Changing room design: Ingress/egress separation, logical gowning progression, grade-matched finishes, and isolation from toilet facilities are essential. / 更衣室設計：進出分離、邏輯更衣動線、等級匹配的表面處理、與廁所隔離為四大要件。
  • Surface finishes escalate by grade: From standard construction (unclassified) to seamless, non-porous, coved, stainless steel finishes (Grade A), with no drains permitted in aseptic areas. / 表面處理隨等級升級：從標準建材到無縫、不滲透、圓弧化、不鏽鋼處理，無菌區禁止排水口。
  • Transfer zones maintain contamination barriers: Airlocks use pressure differentials, door interlocks, and improvement steps (cleaning/gowning) to prevent contamination ingress. / 傳遞區維持汙染屏障：氣閘利用壓差、門互鎖、改善步驟來防止汙染侵入。
  • Sequential one-grade-at-a-time transitions: Entry must progress one classification step at a time; Grade A is accessed only from Grade B without a separate airlock but with clear visual/physical barriers. / 逐級轉換：進入必須逐級升級；Grade A 只能從 Grade B 進入，無獨立氣閘但需明確視覺/物理屏障。
  • PAL vs. MAL vs. Pass Box: Personnel and material airlocks serve different functions; pass boxes replace MALs for smaller items; all require door interlocks and grade-appropriate construction. / 人員氣閘、物料氣閘與傳遞窗各有適用場景，均需門互鎖與等級匹配建材。
3c

Chapter 3c: 4c. Architecture (4.7–4.8)

建築佈局（下） | p101-p106

ISPE Baseline Guide Vol. 3 (3rd Ed.) | p101 – p106

Learning Objectives / 本節學習目標

  • Understand the design principles for support areas (gowning rooms, equipment prep, parts washing, buffer preparation, component staging) and their role in maintaining cleanroom integrity / 了解輔助區域的設計原則及其對潔淨室完整性的重要性
  • Explain why technical support areas should remain separate and unclassified, and how service chases minimize contamination risk / 說明為何技術輔助區域應保持分離與非分級，以及服務通道如何降低污染風險
  • Interpret five concept diagrams (Figures 4.4–4.8) showing functional adjacencies for different manufacturing configurations: small/large scale, RABS/isolator, aseptic/terminally sterilized / 解讀五種不同製造配置的概念圖
  • Apply the unidirectional flow principle to material and personnel movement in facility layout / 將單向流動原則應用於物料與人員動線設計
  • Differentiate between segregation by physical barrier, procedural control, and time separation / 區分物理屏障隔離、程序控制隔離與時間隔離三種方式
4.7 Support Areas 4.7 支援區域

Original Text

Technical support areas for the cleanrooms should be proximal to minimize service runs, but kept separate in unclassified areas.

Process support areas should be isolated from the aseptic area. If necessary, they can be adjacent, with vision panels and transfer hatches, and should generally be unclassified. Access would normally be provided by the facility corridor.

Services to equipment, such as autoclaves, may be provided by using a service chase (ideally accessed from outside the production areas).

Autoclaves, tunnels, and washers with access from two sides may have mechanical support rooms accessible from clean areas. Access should be from the less clean of the two areas, with tight seals on the critical side. Such service areas should be kept at pressures negative to the areas to which they connect.

The location of clean utility and CIP/SIP systems should consider the proximity to utility users and serviceability from unclassified areas. Locating these systems above or below the production area may be desirable.

Walkable ceilings can be an optimal solution for the overhead maintenance of cleanrooms. Regulated companies may prohibit access above processing areas during production, as traffic can dislodge particles.

導師解析

核心概念：輔助區域的定位

輔助區域是潔淨室的「後勤供應鏈」。ISPE 將其分為兩類：

  • 技術輔助區域（Technical Support）：機電維修、設備後端服務，應保持非分級（Unclassified）並與潔淨室分離
  • 製程輔助區域（Process Support）：緩衝液配製、零件清洗、組件暫存等，可與無菌區相鄰但須隔離

關鍵原則：靠近但隔離——縮短管路與搬運距離，同時防止污染回流。

比喻說明：醫院手術室的配套空間

想像一間醫院手術室：手術房本身是最高等級潔淨區域，但它周圍還需要：器械消毒間（零件清洗）、藥品準備區（緩衝液配製）、更衣區（更衣室）、以及設備維修通道。

這些空間都不需要與手術房同等級的空氣品質，但必須緊鄰手術房以便快速支援，同時隔離以防止外界污染進入。藥廠的輔助區域邏輯完全一樣。

重點提示：雙面設備的壓差策略

滅菌鍋（Autoclave）、隧道烘箱（Tunnel）、清洗機（Washer）這類橫跨兩個區域的設備，其維修側必須遵守兩條規則：

  1. 從較低等級側進入——避免維修人員穿越高等級區域
  2. 維修側壓差為負壓——確保氣流方向是「從潔淨到非潔淨」，微粒不會從維修通道回流到生產區

這是 Annex 1 壓差階梯（Pressure Cascade）原則在設備層級的直接應用。

可行走天花板（Walkable Ceiling）

可行走天花板讓維修人員從上方進入潔淨室的 HEPA 過濾器、燈具和感測器，而不必進入潔淨室本身。

限制條件：生產期間禁止進入——行走產生的振動可能使微粒穿透天花板密封件落入潔淨室。這就是為何許多公司將天花板維修排在批次之間或停機期間進行。

4.7 Support Areas — Design Summary Table 4.7 支援區域 — 設計摘要表

Original Text — Summary

The overarching principle: support areas should be close enough to serve the cleanroom efficiently, but separated enough to prevent contamination. Physical barriers, pressure differentials, and procedural controls are the three tools to achieve this balance.

導師解析

比喻說明：餐廳的前場與後場

任何高檔餐廳都有嚴格的前場（用餐區）與後場（廚房、洗碗間、儲藏室）分區。後場要離前場近（上菜速度），但絕對不能讓油煙、噪音或髒碗回流到用餐區。

藥廠的輔助區域就是潔淨室的「後場」：

  • 零件清洗區 = 洗碗間
  • 緩衝液配製 = 備料區
  • 服務通道 = 員工動線
  • 可行走天花板 = 屋頂維修通道

練習思考

  1. Your facility has an autoclave that spans between a Grade C filling support room and an unclassified maintenance corridor. Which side should maintenance personnel access it from, and what pressure differential should the maintenance side maintain relative to Grade C?
  2. A CIP skid is currently located inside the Grade D production area. Based on Section 4.7 guidance, would you recommend relocating it? What are the pros and cons?

實務應用：輔助區域佈局查核清單

  • 所有雙面設備（滅菌鍋、清洗機）維修側是否保持負壓？
  • 服務通道（Service Chase）是否可從生產區外部進入？
  • CIP/SIP 系統是否可從非分級區域進行維修？
  • 潔淨室天花板上方維修是否排除在生產時間之外？
  • 製程輔助區域是否使用視窗（Vision Panel）和傳遞窗（Transfer Hatch）與無菌區通訊？
4.8 Concept Diagrams — Overview 4.8 概念圖 — 概述

Original Text

Figure 4.4, Figure 4.5, Figure 4.6, Figure 4.7, and Figure 4.8 provide a graphic approach to the concepts discussed in this chapter. These figures are an approach to functional adjacencies and are not layouts or floor plans.

The five concept diagrams cover the following configurations:

  • Figure 4.4 — Small Scale Open System Aseptic Fill with RABS
  • Figure 4.5 — Small Scale Open System Aseptic Fill with Isolators
  • Figure 4.6 — Large Scale Open System Aseptic Fill with RABS
  • Figure 4.7 — Large Scale Open System Aseptic Fill with Isolators
  • Figure 4.8 — Large Scale Open Filling for Terminally Sterilized Product with RABS

導師解析

核心概念：概念圖 vs. 平面圖

ISPE 特別強調這些是功能鄰接關係圖，不是實際平面圖。它們回答的問題是「哪些房間應該彼此相鄰？」而不是「房間尺寸是多少？」

這種方法的價值在於：先確定功能邏輯（物料流、人員流、隔離需求），再進入具體的建築設計。許多設施設計失敗的根源就是跳過功能鄰接分析，直接畫平面圖。

重點提示：五張圖的分類邏輯

ISPE 用兩個維度將無菌製造設施分成五種典型配置：

理解這三個維度，就能快速判斷你的設施最接近哪個概念圖，再依此為基礎進行細部設計。

Figure 4.4: Small Scale Open System Aseptic Fill with RABS Figure 4.4: 小規模開放式無菌充填搭配 RABS

Original Text

Notes for Figure 4.4:

  • All processes are open. Compounding is not prepared aseptically. Product is sterile filtered to the filling area. LP/GAAS is used to minimize bioburden.
  • The Parts Wash and Compounding rooms contain open processes with product exposure and should be segregated from other areas. Separate PAL In and PAL Out rooms are provided for the Compounding room, to prevent contamination of clean gowning supplies during de-gowning.
  • The airlocks into the Compounding room can also prevent the transportation of residual product into the corridor and allow for concurrent formulation and filling of multiple products.
  • Dirty parts and utensils are transferred to the Pre-Wash room through the Process Corridor. The Pre-Wash room can be a CNC or Grade D area, provided the final wash/rinse occurs within the pass-through washer which can be unloaded in an ISO 8/Grade C area.
  • The Process Corridor is a shared concurrent path for all non-product exposed items and personnel.
  • If waste cannot be considered closed, then it is an open system and segregation can be provided by procedural means or by transporting waste across the Process Corridor during "off hours" — this is segregation achieved by time separation.

Component transport notes:

  • Transportation of components shall be within RTP canisters or other closed transfer devices which can be docked with the RABS barrier system.

導師解析

小規模 RABS 設施的關鍵特徵

這是最基礎的無菌充填配置，適合小型 CDMO 或臨床試驗生產。核心特徵：

  • 全開放製程——產品在非封閉環境下暴露，因此環境控制至關重要
  • 非無菌配製——配製室不需無菌等級，但需要隔離以防止交叉污染
  • 無菌過濾作為關鍵控制點——產品在進入充填區前經過除菌過濾
  • RTP 密閉容器轉運——組件通過密封容器進入 RABS

重點提示：時間隔離（Time Separation）

當物理隔離不可行（例如廢棄物必須通過製程走廊），ISPE 允許「時間隔離」——在非生產時段（off hours）搬運開放性廢棄物。這並非理想方案，但在空間受限的小型設施中是實用的折衷。

如果廢棄物污染了走廊，則必須在恢復生產前完成清潔。這意味著需要經過驗證的清潔程序和放行標準。

比喻說明：共用走廊的管理

Process Corridor 就像醫院的公共走廊——醫護人員、訪客、推車都使用同一條路。但手術器械會放在密封推車裡運送，醫療廢棄物則在特定時段由專人清運。

藥廠的 Process Corridor 採用相同邏輯：非暴露品共用，暴露品密封運送，廢棄物時間隔離。

Figure 4.5: Small Scale Open System Aseptic Fill with Isolators Figure 4.5: 小規模開放式無菌充填搭配隔離器

Original Text

Notes for Figure 4.5:

  • Open aseptic processes occur within isolators.
  • The Parts Wash room contains an open process with product exposure and should be a separate room.
  • A Compounding room directly connected to the Filling Suite is for a single product or campaign basis. Compounding of one product and filling for another product cannot be performed simultaneously.
  • The Process Corridor is a shared concurrent path for all non-product exposed items and personnel. It is primarily used to connect personnel from the locker rooms to the ISO 8/Grade C production suite and to transfer materials into the same suite.
  • Having the corridor eliminates the complicated procedures frequently involved with multiple in-line airlocks and allows for proper transitioning through areas of increasing cleanliness.
  • Product containers, stoppers, and caps are either pre-sterilized and ready-to-use, or are batch processed within RTP containers. Pre-wrapped ready-to-use components can be transferred into the isolator via VHP decontamination airlocks built into the isolator.
  • This figure shows the capping process inside the ISO 5/Grade A isolator. Therefore, caps should be sterilized.

導師解析

重點提示：製程走廊消除了多級氣閘

ISPE 指出，Process Corridor 的一個重要好處是取代串聯式氣閘（in-line airlocks）。傳統設計中，人員從更衣區到生產區可能需要通過三到四個氣閘，每個都有壓差控制和程序要求。

一條設計良好的 Process Corridor 能讓人員在「逐漸增加潔淨度」的空間中自然過渡，既簡化程序又降低人為錯誤風險。

比喻說明：campaign 生產的限制

「配製室直接連接充填套間」的設計，就像餐廳只有一個備料區。如果今天備料做牛排，就不能同時備料做海鮮——否則交叉污染。你必須「一個產品做完、清潔完、再做下一個」，這就是 Campaign 生產。

隔離器配置 vs. RABS 配置的關鍵差異

比較 Figure 4.4（RABS）和 Figure 4.5（Isolator）：

隔離器提供更高的產品保護，但犧牲了操作靈活性。

Figure 4.6: Large Scale Open System Aseptic Fill with RABS Figure 4.6: 大規模開放式無菌充填搭配 RABS

Original Text

Notes for Figure 4.6:

  • All processes are open and, therefore, unidirectional flows are provided for the exposed product areas. Compounding is not performed aseptically. Product is sterile filtered to the filling area and aseptic connectors are used.
  • RABS barrier technology is used along with RTP containers for material transfers to minimize manual handling of exposed and sterilized components and reduce the ISO 5/Grade A zones.
  • Automated loading and unloading of the lyophilizer (LYO) eliminates manual handling of filled, partially stoppered vials.
  • The Parts Wash and Compounding rooms contain open processes with product exposure and should be segregated. Separate PAL In and PAL Out rooms are provided for the Compounding room.
  • Dirty parts and utensils are transferred to the Pre-Wash room through the Process Corridor. The Pre-Wash can be a CNC or Grade D area, provided the final wash/rinse occurs within the pass-through washer.
  • This figure assumes the use of ready-to-sterilize stoppers which are sterilized in the pass-through autoclave.
  • The VHP chamber should be utilized to bring items that cannot be autoclaved into the ISO 7/Grade B areas.

導師解析

大規模 RABS 的升級設計

從 Figure 4.4（小規模）升級到 Figure 4.6（大規模），ISPE 增加了幾項關鍵設計：

  • 單向流動（Unidirectional Flow）——所有產品暴露區域的物料和人員流動方向一致，不允許回流
  • 無菌連接器（Aseptic Connectors）——取代開放式管路連接，減少暴露風險
  • 自動化冷凍乾燥裝載——消除人工搬運半加塞小瓶的風險
  • VHP 傳遞艙——處理無法高壓滅菌的物品

重點提示：為何大規模設施必須單向流動？

小規模設施可以用 Process Corridor 共用路徑，因為人流物流量小，可透過程序控制管理。但大規模設施的交通量高，共用雙向路徑的交叉污染風險急劇增加。

因此 ISPE 在大規模配置中明確要求單向流動：乾淨物料只往高等級方向走，髒污物料只往低等級方向走。這就是「物料流」和「人員流」分離的具體實踐。

練習思考

  1. Figure 4.6 mentions the use of "ready-to-sterilize stoppers" that are sterilized in a pass-through autoclave. What would change in the facility layout if you switched to pre-sterilized ready-to-use (RTU) stoppers instead?
  2. Why does ISPE recommend automated LYO loading/unloading for large-scale facilities but not necessarily for small-scale? What risk does manual handling introduce?
Figure 4.7: Large Scale Open System Aseptic Fill with Isolators Figure 4.7: 大規模開放式無菌充填搭配隔離器

Original Text

Notes for Figure 4.7:

  • All processes are closed except for Parts Wash. Filling and stoppering are performed in isolators.
  • The Parts Wash room contains an open process with product exposure and should be segregated from other areas. The bidirectional entry airlock to the Pre-Wash room is provided to allow personnel to over-gown upon entering and de-gown upon exiting to prevent the transportation of exposed product into the Process Corridor.
  • The Process Corridor is a shared concurrent path for all non-product exposed items and personnel.
  • If waste cannot be considered closed, segregation can be provided by temporal means or by transporting waste during "off hours" to the MAL Out.
  • The product transitions from the ISO 5/Grade A isolator to crimping under LP/GAAS. Capping can occur within a RABS within the ISO 8/Grade C environment and the caps do not need to be sterile.
  • Particulates generated by crimping are prevented from entering the isolator by the positive pressure of the isolator and the exiting airflow at the mousehole.
  • This figure shows the option of having capping inside the filling room instead of outside in a Grade D room.

導師解析

隔離器 + 大規模：最高保護等級

Figure 4.7 代表了無菌充填的最高保護配置。關鍵特徵：

  • 幾乎全封閉製程——只有零件清洗是開放製程
  • 隔離器正壓保護——即使加蓋產生微粒，隔離器內的正壓和出口氣流（mousehole）防止微粒回流
  • 加蓋在 ISO 8/Grade C 環境中的 RABS 內進行——因為此時小瓶已完全加塞，瓶蓋不需無菌

比喻說明：Mousehole 的概念

Mousehole（鼠洞）是隔離器與外部環境之間的小開口，讓產品容器通過。想像一棟建築的通風口——總是有氣流向外吹出，所以灰塵不會從外面吹進來。

隔離器的 mousehole 利用同樣原理：隔離器內部正壓使空氣持續從 mousehole 向外流出，阻止加蓋區的微粒進入無菌充填區域。

重點提示：雙向氣閘（Bidirectional Airlock）

Pre-Wash 區的雙向氣閘設計精妙：人員進入時加穿防護衣（over-gown），離開時脫掉。目的是確保接觸過暴露產品的防護衣不會被帶入 Process Corridor，避免殘留產品交叉污染。

這是「人員流」管理中的重要細節——不只是控制人往哪走，還要控制人身上帶了什麼。

Figure 4.8: Large Scale Open Filling for Terminally Sterilized Product with RABS Figure 4.8: 大規模開放式終端滅菌產品充填搭配 RABS

Original Text

Notes for Figure 4.8:

  • All processes are open. Filling is performed within a RABS under LP/GAAS. Compounding is not produced aseptically or sterile filtered.
  • The Parts Wash and Compounding rooms contain open processes with product exposure and should be segregated. The bidirectional entry airlock into the Pre-Wash room prevents the transportation of exposed product into the Production Hallway.
  • Only one product can be made at a time.
  • The Process Corridor is a common concurrent path for all non-product exposed items and personnel.
  • If waste cannot be considered closed, segregation by temporal means or transport during "off hours" to the MAL Out.
  • Gowning into the ISO 8/Grade C area is unidirectional so the personnel exiting the area do not contaminate the gowning supplies of those who enter the production areas.

導師解析

重點提示：終端滅菌不代表可以放鬆環境控制

雖然終端滅菌提供了額外的安全網，ISPE 仍然要求：

  • 充填在 RABS + LP/GAAS 下進行
  • 開放製程區域需要隔離
  • 更衣流程單向設計
  • 同一時間只能生產一個產品

這反映了現代法規趨勢：即使是終端滅菌產品，也應盡可能降低充填前的微生物負荷（bioburden），以確保滅菌保證水準（SAL）。

比喻說明：更衣流程的單向設計

想像游泳池的更衣室：進入泳池前走淋浴通道（穿上泳衣、淋浴），離開泳池後走另一條出口（沖洗、換回便服）。如果進出走同一條路，濕淋淋的泳客會弄髒準備進場的乾淨區域。

藥廠更衣室的單向設計原理完全一樣——進入的人不會與離開的人在更衣區交會，確保潔淨更衣用品不被污染。

終端滅菌 vs. 無菌充填：設施設計的根本差異

Figure 4.8 是唯一的終端滅菌（Terminally Sterilized）配置，與前四張圖的無菌充填有本質差異：

Cross-Diagram Comparison — Five Configurations at a Glance 跨圖比較 — 五種配置一覽

Original Text — Synthesis

Common themes across all five diagrams:

  • Parts Wash rooms with open product exposure must always be segregated
  • Process Corridor serves as shared concurrent path for non-exposed items
  • Waste handling requires either closed containment or time separation
  • RTP canisters or closed transfer devices are required for all component transport
  • PAL In/Out separation prevents gowning contamination

導師解析

五張圖的共通設計原則

無論選擇哪種配置，ISPE 強調的核心設計原則始終不變：

  1. 隔離開放製程——任何產品暴露的房間都需要獨立隔離
  2. 密封轉運——所有組件在潔淨區間的移動都必須在密閉容器中進行
  3. 更衣分流——進入與離開的更衣路徑分開，避免污染潔淨更衣用品
  4. 廢棄物管理——密封或時間隔離，二擇一
  5. Process Corridor 共用——但僅限非暴露品與人員

實務應用：選擇你的設施配置

你正在規劃一座新的無菌充填設施。請根據以下場景，判斷最適合的概念圖：

  1. 年產量 500 萬瓶注射劑，產品熱穩定，可承受終端滅菌 → ?
  2. 年產量 10 萬瓶生物製劑，不耐熱，需無菌充填，預算有限 → ?
  3. 年產量 2,000 萬瓶大輸液，需冷凍乾燥，要求最高產品保護等級 → ?

（提示：考慮規模、產品特性、屏障技術選擇三個維度）

練習思考

  1. Why does using isolators allow a lower background classification (ISO 8/Grade C) compared to RABS (ISO 7/Grade B)? What risk trade-off is being made?
  2. All five diagrams mention the Process Corridor as a "shared concurrent path." Under what circumstances would you need to abandon the shared corridor concept and implement fully segregated corridors?
  3. Figure 4.8 (terminally sterilized) is the only configuration that explicitly states "only one product can be made at a time." Why is concurrent production feasible in aseptic configurations (Figs 4.4, 4.6) but not here?
Section Summary / 本節總結

Key Takeaways

Section 4.7 — Support Areas

  • Technical support areas should be proximal to cleanrooms but unclassified and separated
  • Process support areas (compounding, parts wash, buffer prep) should be isolated from aseptic areas, with vision panels and transfer hatches if adjacent
  • Dual-access equipment (autoclaves, washers, tunnels) should be serviced from the less clean side, with the service area at negative pressure
  • Clean utility and CIP/SIP systems should be serviceable from unclassified areas
  • Walkable ceilings enable overhead maintenance without entering cleanrooms, but access must be prohibited during production

Section 4.8 — Concept Diagrams

  • Five concept diagrams illustrate functional adjacencies (not floor plans) for small/large scale facilities using RABS or isolators for aseptic or terminally sterilized products
  • All configurations share common principles: segregation of open processes, closed material transfer, unidirectional gowning, and waste management by containment or time separation
  • Isolators permit lower background classification than RABS due to superior barrier integrity
  • Large-scale facilities require unidirectional flow for product-exposed areas
  • The Process Corridor concept reduces airlock complexity while maintaining contamination control

重點回顧

4.7 輔助區域 — 核心要點

  • 技術輔助區域（機電維修）應靠近潔淨室但保持非分級與物理分離
  • 製程輔助區域（配製、零件清洗、緩衝液配製）必須與無菌區隔離
  • 雙面設備從較低等級側維修，維修側保持負壓
  • CIP/SIP 系統宜設於生產區上方或下方，可從非分級區域維修
  • 可行走天花板在生產期間禁止進入

4.8 概念圖 — 核心要點

  • 五張概念圖涵蓋小/大規模 + RABS/隔離器 + 無菌充填/終端滅菌的典型配置
  • 所有配置共享：開放製程隔離、密閉轉運、單向更衣、廢棄物密封或時間隔離
  • 隔離器因屏障完整性高，允許較低的背景環境等級
  • 大規模設施必須實施單向流動
  • Process Corridor 概念簡化了傳統多級氣閘設計
4a

Chapter 4a: 5a. HVAC (5.1–5.4)

HVAC（上） | p107-p122

ISPE Baseline Guide Vol. 3 (3rd Ed.) | p107 – p122

Learning Objectives / 學習目標

  • Understand the scope and role of HVAC in sterile product manufacturing / 理解 HVAC 在無菌製造中的範疇與角色
  • Explain how HEPA/ULPA filtration controls airborne particulates / 說明 HEPA/ULPA 過濾如何控制空氣微粒
  • Differentiate occupancy states: in operation, at rest, and as-built / 區分操作狀態：運行中、靜止態與空置態
  • Apply risk assessment methods (HACCP, FMEA) to HVAC systems / 將風險評估方法應用於HVAC系統
  • Describe Local Protection (LP) and Grade A Air Supply (GAAS) applications / 描述局部保護與A級空氣供應應用
  • Identify capital and operating cost drivers for HVAC systems / 識別HVAC資本與營運成本驅動因素
  • Recognize internal and external sources of particulate contamination / 認識內部與外部微粒污染來源

Section Contents / 章節目錄

5.1 Introduction 5.1.2 Role of HVAC 5.1.3 Particulate Control 5.1.4 Maintaining Classification 5.1.5 Occupancy States 5.1.5.1 Recovery 5.1.5.2 Risk Assessment 5.1.6 LP/GAAS 5.2 Cost Considerations 5.3 Contamination Sources 5.4 Environmental Requirements Section Summary
5.1

Introduction — Scope & Role of HVAC

Pages 107–108

5.1.1 Scope

This chapter deals with creating a suitable environment for the processing of sterile products, including sterile bulks and terminally sterilized products. Biopharmaceutical bulk facilities are covered in the ISPE Baseline Guide: Biopharmaceutical Manufacturing Facilities (Second Edition), but further HVAC details for classified manufacturing space are considered in this Guide.

ISPE has chosen a new harmonized nomenclature for space classification that bridges the differing cleanliness classifications, focusing on the US FDA guidance, EU Annex 1, ISO 14644-1, and ISPE legacy grading systems (see Table 5.3).

For further information, refer to the ISPE Good Practice Guide: Heating, Ventilation, and Air Conditioning, ISPE Baseline Guide: Biopharmaceutical Manufacturing Facilities (Second Edition), and Chapter 11 of this Guide.

5.1.1 範疇

本章探討如何為無菌產品（包括無菌原料藥與最終滅菌產品）的製造創建適當環境。生物製藥原料藥設施已在ISPE生物製藥設施指南中涵蓋，但有關分級製造空間的HVAC細節在本指南中進一步討論。

Key Point / 重點

ISPE採用新的協調命名法來統一各地潔淨室分級：結合美國FDA指南、歐盟Annex 1、ISO 14644-1以及ISPE舊版分級系統（詳見Table 5.3）。

詳細資訊請參閱ISPE HVAC良好實務指南、ISPE生物製藥設施指南以及本指南第11章。

5.1.2 The Role of HVAC

The role of HVAC in sterile product facilities is primarily to ensure that the processing environment does not negatively impact product quality. The product and process should be understood, to assess the level of environmental control necessary to reliably make product. The environmental control provided by HVAC typically impacts a very limited number of Critical Process Parameters (CPPs). The critical environmental parameters associated with sterile product quality can include:

  • Airborne particulates (both viable and non-viable, which may contaminate the product)
  • Temperature (which may affect product stability and operator comfort/cleanliness)
  • Humidity (which impacts microbial growth, operator comfort and cleanliness, static electricity, and may impact some products)
  • Relative pressurization (which may impact the ingress and egress of airborne gases and particles)
  • Gaseous contaminants and oxygen concentration (which may impact operator health/safety)
  • Airborne product aerosols (which may impact operator health/safety and cross-contamination risk)

The control of airborne particulates is usually associated with HVAC for sterile manufacturing. HVAC can also indirectly affect surface contamination by limiting the deposition of airborne particulates, but it has limited use in removing deposited (surface) contaminants, due to the high velocities typically required to overcome surface attractions.

Advanced aseptic processing techniques (such as isolators, BFS, single-use technologies, etc.) have influenced the importance of airborne particulate control required in facilities. These advanced technologies are intended to provide enhanced separation of the processing environment from the room environment (and personnel). This separation improves sterility assurance and decreases the impact of room conditions on product quality. Therefore, lower space classifications and HVAC environmental controls may be required, depending on the level of separation provided.

5.1.2 HVAC的角色

HVAC（暖通空調）在無菌製藥設施中的主要角色是確保製造環境不會對產品品質產生負面影響。必須充分理解產品與製程，以評估可靠製造所需的環境控制等級。HVAC提供的環境控制通常僅影響少數關鍵製程參數（CPPs）。

Six Critical Environmental Parameters / 六大關鍵環境參數

  • 空氣微粒（活性與非活性，可能污染產品）
  • 溫度（影響產品穩定性與操作員舒適度）
  • 濕度（影響微生物生長、靜電與部分產品）
  • 相對壓力（影響空氣與微粒的進出）
  • 氣態污染物與氧濃度（影響操作員健康）
  • 產品氣溶（影響健康與交叉污染風險）

Analogy / 比喻說明

想像HVAC系統如同潔淨室的「呼吸系統」——它持續供應潔淨空氣並排出污染物，維持室內環境的「健康」。但HVAC無法清除表面污染，因為需要極高風速（3,000-5,000 ft/min）才能克服表面附著力。

Advanced Technology Impact / 先進技術影響

隔離器、BFS、一次性技術等先進無菌製程技術可提供製程環境與房間環境的增強隔離。此隔離提升無菌保證並降低房間條件對產品的影響，因此可能允許較低的空間分級與HVAC控制要求。

Temperature & Humidity Impact on Product

The temperature and humidity of the room can impact the product in four ways:

  • The comfort of operators present in the room can be affected, and therefore impact the number of particles (viable) shed by them. A high degree of protective gowning is usually employed to minimize contamination from operators, but cooler room temperatures and lower relative humidity may be needed to keep operators comfortable with this added gowning.
  • Heat sensitive products (especially large molecules) may need to be processed or stored at temperatures well below those required for comfort.
  • Hygroscopic (or moisture reactive) products may need to be processed at lower relative humidity than is required for health and safety.
  • The temperature and relative humidity of a space significantly impact the growth of microorganisms and can impact the hygiene of a facility.

溫濕度對產品的四種影響

Four Impact Pathways / 四大影響路徑

  • 操作員舒適度：溫度過高會增加操作員釋放的微粒數量。較低溫度與濕度可幫助穿著厚重防護服的人員保持舒適。
  • 熱敏感產品：特別是大分子藥物，可能需要在遠低於舒適溫度的條件下製造或儲存。
  • 吸濕性產品：可能需要在低於健康與安全要求的相對濕度下製造。
  • 微生物控制：溫度與相對濕度顯著影響微生物生長與設施衛生。
5.1.3

HVAC and Particulate Control for Product Quality

Pages 109–111

5.1.3 HVAC and Particulate Control for Product Quality

HVAC systems control particulates by applying filtration of varying efficiencies to incoming and recirculating airstreams. For the most critical environments (ISO 5/Grade A, ISO 6, ISO 7/Grade B, ISO 8/Grade C), FDA guidance suggests that one layer of HEPA filtration of at least 99.97% efficiency at 0.3 μm particle diameter should be applied (similar to EU filter designation H13). While not required, HEPA filters with 99.99% efficiency (similar to EU filter designation H14) or Ultra Low Penetration Air (ULPA) filters may also be applied to provide enhanced particulate matter control and to comply with integrity testing to a limit of 0.01% penetration as suggested by the FDA.

This filter is typically fitted at the boundary to the room (terminal) to separate the HVAC system from the critical environment, although it is not stipulated in regulations.

EU filter designation F9/MERV 14-15 filtration may achieve ISO 8/Grade C classification at particle sizes ≥ 0.5 μm (depending on room internal particle generation), making this level of filtration suitable for lower class environments (such as Grade D or CNC) or for pre-filtration of air prior to final HEPA filtration.

Regulated companies may employ two or more HEPA filters in series in the most critical environments. This practice may be justified in cases where highly potent products may be present in recirculated air.

Exhaust and return grilles are generally not fitted with filters, but these may be added to protect ductwork and the outside environment where an aerosol of a highly potent or sensitizing product is present or for biosafety level (BSL) above BSL-2.

5.1.3 HVAC與微粒控制

HEPA Filtration Hierarchy / HEPA過濾層級

  • HEPA 99.97%（H13）：FDA建議的最低要求，適用於ISO 5至ISO 8等級
  • HEPA 99.99%（H14）：提供增強微粒控制，符合0.01%穿透率的完整性測試要求
  • ULPA過濾器：用於需要更高潔淨度的關鍵應用
  • F9/MERV 14-15：可達到ISO 8（≥ 0.5 μm），適用於較低分級或預過濾

Terminal Filter Placement / 終端過濾器位置

HEPA過濾器通常安裝在房間邊界（終端位置），將HVAC系統與關鍵環境分隔。雖然法規未強制要求此配置，但終端過濾器被強烈建議用於ISO 7/Grade B及更高等級，並常見於ISO 8/Grade C系統。

Dual HEPA in Series / 雙重HEPA串聯
