在最關鍵環境中可採用兩個或更多HEPA過濾器串聯，特別是當高效產品可能存在於回風中時。但ISPE HVAC指南建議使用MERV 13/14作為替代方案。

Particles in the Critical Area

Particles generated inside the critical area, where sterile product or materials are exposed, may be composed of:

  • The product itself
  • Particles from the process equipment
  • Particles from containers/closures
  • Particles from operators

The difference between particles from these different sources should be understood. Particles of product are not a contaminant and steps should be taken to exclude these during space qualification or environmental monitoring. Particles generated by equipment, materials, or personnel are of concern.

The HVAC system can control particulates within the critical area by providing a flow of clean, nearly particle free air to displace these potential contaminants and sweep them out of the critical area. This unidirectional flow of air from the source, through the critical zone, to a less clean area, and without recirculation back into the critical zone should maintain ISO 5/Grade A conditions and establish LP/GAAS zones.

Particles generated outside the critical zone (i.e., in the room) should be kept out of the critical zone, especially viable particles from operators. This is generally accomplished by use of displacing unidirectional flow and physical barriers. The concentration of particulate within areas outside the critical zone is typically controlled by dilution of airborne particulate with a flow of clean, nearly particle free air.

關鍵區域內的微粒

Four Particle Sources / 四大微粒來源

  • 產品本身：不被視為污染物，應在監測時排除
  • 製程設備：需關注的污染來源
  • 容器/密封件：需關注的污染來源
  • 操作員：最大微粒污染來源

Two Control Strategies / 兩大控制策略

策略一：單向氣流置換——在關鍵區域（ISO 5/Grade A）內，使用單向氣流（UAF）從HEPA過濾器經過關鍵區域掃向較不潔淨的區域，將污染物掀出。

策略二：稀釋混合——在關鍵區域外（ISO 7/Grade B、ISO 8/Grade C），通過大量潔淨空氣稀釋微粒濃度。稀釋計算應以微粒產生率（「源強度」）為基礎。

Air Change Rate (ACR)

Traditionally, the industry has used the Air Change Rate (ACR), expressed in Air Changes per Hour (ACH) to specify the desired diluting airflow. The target ACR has historically been correlated to a specific cleanliness level; however, industry standards such as ISO 14664-4 and IEST-RP-CC012 no longer provide minimum ACH tables and are shifting towards a scientific evaluation utilizing dilution calculations and computer modeling.

While FDA guidance states that a value of 20 ACH is typically acceptable for ISO 8 (0.5 μm, "in operation"), this Guide recommends using ACH as a planning tool and suggests using the following parameters as acceptance criteria for cleanrooms: room particulate, viable concentration, or other empirical measures of room performance (such as recovery, as outlined in ISO 14644-3).

換氣次數（ACR / ACH）

Industry Shift / 行業轉變

傳統作法是以換氣次數（ACH）來規定稀釋氣流，並將其與特定潔淨等級關聯。但ISO 14644-4及IEST-RP-CC012等標準已不再提供最低ACH表格，轉向基於科學的稀釋計算與電腦建模。

Recommended Approach / 建議作法

FDA建議ISO 8採用20 ACH作為參考值，但本指南建議將ACH僅作為規劃工具，實際驗收標準應採用：

  • 房間微粒計數
  • 活性微生物濃度
  • 其他經驗性性能指標（如恢復測試）
5.1.4

Maintaining Environmental Classification

Pages 110–111

5.1.4 Maintaining Environmental Classification

The airborne particulate concentration in a room is the result of a balance of competing factors:

Particles entering the room:

  • Internal activities (particle generation into the space from personnel and processes)
  • Particles entering at the interfaces to outside spaces
  • Particles entering through the HVAC system

Particles retained within the room:

  • Containment devices
  • Adhesion or deposition of airborne particles on surfaces

Particles leaving the room:

  • Returns
  • Effectiveness of airflow patterns in the room and/or unidirectional flow
  • Exhaust of particles from their source

Quantity of air diluting the particles

A good design should include specific controls to address all of these factors:

  • Equipment should be designed for minimal particulate release into the cleanroom. Particle generating components should be fully enclosed and provided with filtered ventilation or remotely mounted outside the clean space.
  • Personnel should be properly gowned in a properly ventilated gowning room.
  • Particles entering at the interfaces should be controlled by air pressure differences, mass flow across openings, or airlocks and pass-through boxes.
  • Particles entering through HVAC should be appropriately filtered.
  • Wherever possible, ensure that generated particles cannot be disseminated through the room by use of containment barriers and exhaust.
  • Ensure rapid removal of particles from the room via evenly distributed low returns, effective airflow patterns, exhaust at source, and adequate dilution air quantity.

In ISO 7/Grade B and ISO 8/Grade C rooms, dilution of airborne particles using high airflow rates of clean supply air is common. Within these rooms, areas of unidirectional flow (e.g., UFH) can be used to create conventional ISO 5/Grade A areas or areas of LP/GAAS.

Historically, unidirectional air has been introduced at nominally 0.45 m/s (90 ft/min) ± 20%, although other velocities (as low as 0.20 m/s / 40 ft/min) may create more favorable airflow patterns. The velocity employed should be periodically verified as consistent with velocities found at the time of airflow visualization.

5.1.4 維持環境分級

Particle Balance Model / 微粒平衡模型

房間內的微粒濃度是多個競爭因素平衡的結果：

  • 進入：人員與製程產生、外部界面滲透、HVAC送風
  • 滞留：容納装置、表面沉積與附著
  • 離開：回風口、氣流模式效率、源頭排氣
  • 稀釋：空氣量的稀釋效果

Design Control Principles / 設計控制原則

  • 設備應將微粒產生部件完全封閉或配置過濾通風
  • 人員應在適當通風的更衣室正確穿著
  • 界面控制採用壓差、質量流或氣閘/傳遞箱
  • HVAC送風適當過濾
  • 使用容納屏障與排氣防止微粒擴散
  • 均勻分佈的回風口、有效氣流模式、充足稀釋空氣量

UAF Velocity / 單向氣流速度

歷史上單向氣流速度為 0.45 m/s（90 ft/min）± 20%，但較低速度（低至0.20 m/s / 40 ft/min）可能產生更佳的氣流模式。速度應定期驗證，通常與過濾器完整性測試（FIT）同步進行。

5.1.5

Environmental Classification and Monitoring: Occupancy States

Pages 111–113

"In Operation" State

Both the US FDA and EU require that sterile manufacturing cleanrooms should be designed and tested to ensure proper cleanliness while "in operation". Operational, or "in operation", is defined in ISO 14644-1, Section 3.3 as "agreed condition where the cleanroom or clean zone is functioning in the specified manner, with equipment operating and with the specified number of personnel present".

It is recommended that pharmaceutical "in operation" (also referred to as "dynamic") complies with this ISO definition, with HVAC in operation, including local protection devices, with product or simulated product present, with process equipment running, and the specified number of operating and support personnel performing appropriate tasks.

Regulations require that monitoring of the "in operation" particle counts be continuous during aseptic operations. EU regulations require that this be undertaken with a fixed system within Grade A space. The FDA prefers this approach for ISO 5, but allows for portable equipment. The ISO 7/Grade B space surrounding ISO 5/Grade A space should also be monitored "in operation".

「運行中」狀態

"In Operation" Definition / 「運行中」定義

依據ISO 14644-1第3.3節，「運行中」是指潔淨室或潔淨區在規定方式下運作，設備運轉中，且規定人數在場。

製藥「運行中」建議包含：HVAC運行、局部保護裝置啟用、產品或模擬產品在場、製程設備運轉、操作與支援人員執行適當任務。

Monitoring Requirements / 監測要求

  • EU：Grade A空間需採用固定系統連續監測「運行中」微粒計數
  • FDA：ISO 5優先固定系統，但允許使用攜帶式設備
  • ISO 7/Grade B周圍空間也應在「運行中」進行監測

"At Rest" State

In addition to designing for "in operation" conditions, design should account for an "at rest" datum condition to meet EU requirements. "At rest" is defined in ISO 14644-1, Section 3.3 as "condition where the cleanroom or clean zone is complete with equipment installed and operating in a manner agreed upon, but with no personnel present".

Pharmaceutical "at rest" (also referred to as "static") is monitored with HVAC in operation, including local protection devices where these impact room cleanliness, with no product or personnel present, and with process equipment not running.

The FDA 2004 guidance suggests that "as-built" conditions be measured initially as reference data, and it is considered good practice to periodically verify these conditions (e.g., at any major change to HVAC or room configuration, or annually to biennially).

Where "at rest" testing is undertaken, it is important that a "clean up" (also called a "purge") be allowed after the sampling personnel leave the space, before samples are collected. A period of at least 5 minutes should be allowed, with a delay of up to 15–20 minutes being fully appropriate.

「靜止態」狀態

Purge Time / 淨化時間

進行「靜止態」測試時，採樣人員離開後必須等待「淨化」期：至少5分鐘，最長15-20分鐘均為適當。此期間HVAC持續運行以掃除人員產生的微粒。

5.1.5.1 Recovery

EU Annex 1 specifies airborne particulate limits for rooms in both the "in operation" and "at rest" states. Recovery testing for classified spaces is needed to prove that this requirement has been satisfied. The speed with which the airborne particle concentration of a classified space (ISO 7/Grade B or ISO 8/Grade C) recovers from "in use" concentration to "at rest" concentration depends on the effectiveness of ventilation (dilution efficiency) and on the air changes.

There are two approaches to the measurement of recovery:

Method 1 — In-operation monitoring transition:

  • Once equilibrium is achieved, operations are ceased and the room is vacated while counting remains ongoing.
  • The recovery time is recorded as the time required to get from "in operation" particulate concentration to the appropriate "at rest" limit.
  • This method does not ensure the facility can recover from elevated particulate concentrations and does not test HVAC performance alone.

Method 2 — ISO 14644-3 recovery test:

  • The particulate concentration is raised to, or above, the "in operation" limit, often using a challenge agent.
  • The injection is ceased and the room is allowed to recover as much as 3-log.
  • Target recovery: 1-log for Grade C, 2-log for Grade B.
  • This method provides more data, covers a broader range of concentrations, and challenges HVAC at upset levels.

The term "recovery" and "air change" do not apply to UAF spaces (usually ISO 5/Grade A) where unidirectional airflow naturally creates extremely large air change rates and very rapid removal of particles.

5.1.5.1 恢復測試

UAF Exception / UAF例外

「恢復」與「換氣次數」的概念不適用於單向氣流（UAF）空間（通常為ISO 5/Grade A）。UAF天生創造極大的換氣次數與極快的微粒去除速度，無需單獨測試恢復。

5.1.5.2 HVAC Risk Assessment

Before an HVAC risk assessment can be performed, process and product parameters should be defined. A successful risk assessment exercise should reduce high risks to an acceptable level through redesign or, if necessary, through procedures.

Generally, the risks to be considered when specifying area classifications include: the risk inherent in the product being produced (sterile products are high risk) and the risk that the background environment can impact the product quality or patient health.

Two approaches to risk assessment are very well suited to HVAC and environmental control:

  • Hazard Analysis and Critical Control Points (HACCP): This seven-step process focuses on the critical parameters and the monitoring of control points. In the case of HVAC, these control points are typically room temperature, room humidity, room DP, room filter integrity, room airflow, and room airborne contamination (viable and non-viable).
  • Failure Modes and Effects Analysis (FMEA): This approach provides a score for risks and allows easy assessment of the impact of failures. A fixed taxonomy (HAZOP) can easily be used as HVAC can only impact temperature, humidity, pressure and airborne particulate.

Risk assessment should address expected failure and transitional states (e.g., loss of power, loss of controls, shut down, restart, etc.). The expected conditions for pressurization, cleanliness and other critical parameters should be planned and tested.

5.1.5.2 HVAC風險評估

Two Risk Assessment Methods / 兩大風險評估方法

  • HACCP（危害分析與關鍵控制點）：七步驟法，專注於關鍵參數與控制點監測。HVAC的控制點通常為溫度、濕度、壓差、過濾器完整性、氣流與微粒監測。
  • FMEA（失效模式與效應分析）：提供風險評分，易於評估失效影響。可配合HAZOP固定分類法使用，因HVAC僅影響溫度、濕度、壓力與微粒四項參數。

Failure & Transitional States / 失效與過渡狀態

風險評估必須涵蓋預期的失效與過渡狀態，例如斷電、控制失效、關機、重啟等。應規劃並測試各狀態下的壓差、潔淨度與其他關鍵參數。

Critical Control Points in HVAC Risk Assessment

Typical critical parameter/control points where a risk assessment might indicate that drug product quality could be affected include:

  • Room temperature monitoring system
  • Room humidity monitoring system
  • Room DP monitoring system
  • Environmental monitoring for total and viable airborne particulate
  • Continuous airborne particulate monitoring system (expected for ISO 5/Grade A, optional for lower grades). Note: Automated continuous particle monitoring systems provide extensive relevant data and are generally more reliable than manual monitoring.
  • Periodic final HEPA filter integrity (as proven by regular scheduled filter integrity testing)
  • Periodic verification of airflow and/or the airflow monitoring system
  • Periodic verification of ISO 5/Grade A filter face velocity and air velocity proximate to work height. Note: velocity near work height will not be the same as velocity near the filter face.
  • Periodic verification of airflow patterns in ISO 5/Grade A (unidirectional) and general room airflow patterns in ISO 7/Grade B or at interfaces, airlocks, pass-throughs, etc.

Items which only indirectly affect the process environment — and therefore have no direct patient safety and product quality impact — usually include AHU pre-filters, fans, coils, humidifiers, dehumidifiers, ductwork, chilled water, and steam.

HVAC風險評估的關鍵控制點

Nine Critical Control Points / 九大關鍵控制點

  1. 房間溫度監測系統
  2. 房間濕度監測系統
  3. 房間壓差（DP）監測系統
  4. 總微粒與活性微粒環境監測
  5. 連續微粒監測系統（ISO 5/Grade A必要）
  6. 定期HEPA過濾器完整性測試
  7. 定期驗證氣流與監測系統
  8. 定期驗證過濾器表面速度與工作高度風速
  9. 定期驗證氣流模式（ISO 5單向流與房間氣流）

Direct vs. Indirect Impact / 直接與間接影響

僅間接影響製程環境的項目（無直接安全/品質影響）通常包括：AHU預過濾器、風扇、盤管、加濕器、除濕器、風管、冷凍水與蒸汽。這些列為GEP範疇而非關鍵控制點。

5.1.6

Local Protection and Grade A Air Supply (LP/GAAS)

Pages 114–118

Background and Definition

The terms "Local Protection" and "Grade A Air Supply" have appeared in several regulatory documents. In 2004, the FDA guidance introduced the terms "Local Class 100 (ISO 5) protection" and "local protection". In 2008, the EU GMP Annex 1 introduced "Grade A air supply". In 2010, PIC/S provided a definition and noted that Grade A air supply is one of the most significant changes in Annex 1.

The terms Local Protection (LP) and Grade A Air Supply (GAAS) should be considered as equivalent, and are used to indicate any instance where a localized HEPA filtered air supply is used to reduce the risk of total or viable particulate contamination of critical surfaces within a specified working zone.

LP/GAAS is generally configured with terminal HEPA filtration proximate to the work zone (above or to one side, as appropriate to the risks) in order to ensure ISO 5 particulate levels. This engineering control can be applied to reduce risk in any background classification (including Grade D, ISO 8/Grade C, and ISO 7/Grade B cleanroom areas).

A well-designed LP/GAAS involves proper configuration of the extract to ensure a flushing flow of clean air through the area of concern. In certain cases, additional engineering controls (such as enclosures or RABS with glove ports) can be reasonably employed to enhance the air quality within the work zone.

背景與定義

LP/GAAS Definition / LP/GAAS定義

局部保護（LP）與A級空氣供應（GAAS）應視為等價，指任何使用局部HEPA過濾空氣供應來降低指定工作區域內關鍵表面微粒污染風險的情況。

配置要點：

  • 終端HEPA過濾器靠近工作區（上方或側方）
  • 確保ISO 5微粒等級
  • 適用於任何背景分級（Grade D至ISO 7/Grade B）
  • 適當配置回風口以確保潔淨空氣沖洗流

Analogy / 比喻

LP/GAAS如同手術室中的局部無菌燈光——即使整個房間不是最高等級，但在關鍵操作區域提供最潔淨的空氣保護。

Table 5.1: Examples of LP/GAAS Applications

表5.1：LP/GAAS應用實例

Application Summary / 應用總結

LP/GAAS可應用於多種場景，從Grade D到ISO 7/Grade B的背景分級：

  • 去包裝站：保護預滅菌注射器盒的內袋
  • 製程罐體：保護敞開的產品接觸表面
  • 加蓋操作：符合EU Annex 1及FDA要求
  • 隔離器鼠洞：降低渦流造成的空氣入侵風險
  • RABS門擇區：保護手套與門表面
  • 高壓釜/烘箱卸貨：已滿菌物品冷卻時防污染
  • 零件準備：包裝與滅菌準備時保護潔淨表面
  • 清洗機卸貨：減少卸貨與轉運時的微粒污染

Environmental Monitoring for LP/GAAS

Application of LP/GAAS is straightforward from an HVAC design perspective. However, establishing target "at rest" or "in operation" limits for these areas is often overlooked during facility design, which can cause considerable difficulty and delays during qualification.

LP/GAAS zones should be differentiated from ISO 5/Grade A zones or conditions, as these limits may not be applicable.

Principles for establishing LP/GAAS EM limits:

  • Monitoring/testing should include measurement of total and viable particulates proximate to the work zone.
  • "At rest" monitoring/testing is primarily useful as a pre-check of overall system performance.
  • LP/GAAS air supply should generally meet ISO 5 requirements for 0.5 μm and 5.0 μm particles, when measured 100–150 mm below the filter face, under all conditions.
  • A well-designed LP/GAAS should achieve a 1-log reduction in total particulates below the "in operation" background limit.
  • Care should be taken for viable limits where LP/GAAS is used in classified areas below ISO 7/Grade B.
  • For initial qualification, viable particulate limits 1/2 to 1/3 of background environment limits are recommended.

LP/GAAS環境監測

Common Pitfall / 常見陷阱

LP/GAAS區域的「靜止態」或「運行中」限值經常在設施設計階段被忽略，導致確認時出現重大困難與延誤。應在設計初期即建立LP/GAAS的EM限值。

EM Limit Principles / EM限值原則

  • LP/GAAS與ISO 5/Grade A應明確區分，限值可能不同
  • 空氣供應應在過濾器面下100-150 mm處滿足ISO 5
  • 良好設計應實現背景「運行中」限值的1-log降低
  • 初始確認時活性微粒限值建議為背景限值的1/2至1/3

Table 5.2: Recommended Initial Qualification Limits for LP/GAAS

表5.2：LP/GAAS初始確認限值建議

Key Observations / 重要觀察

  • 背景越高，限值越嚴格：ISO 7/Grade B背景的活性空氣限值僅5 CFU/m³，而Grade D背景為100 CFU/m³
  • RABS效果：同為ISO 8/Grade C背景，有RABS時活性限值為33，無RABS為50 CFU/m³
  • 總微粒限值：等於背景分級的「運行中」限值，反映1-log降低的目標

Practical Tip / 實務提示

完成初始確認測試後，應回顧歷史EM數據並利用統計分析調整限值。這確保限值既能保護產品品質，又不會造成過多的假陽性逾規。

5.2

Cost Considerations

Pages 118–120

5.2.1 Capital Costs

HVAC systems for sterile manufacturing are expensive and can represent a significant proportion of the total facility cost. The capital cost of a system can vary greatly and is dependent upon the decisions made throughout the design stages. The main factors that influence HVAC cost include:

  • Use of isolators and other microenvironments: The use of isolators may reduce room classification requirements, leading to smaller and lower cost HVAC systems. Other microenvironments (such as RABS and LP/GAAS) can reduce the particulate challenge to critical zones, also reducing HVAC system sizing. Process closure and closed filling have a similar impact.
  • Size of aseptic processing area: This should be optimized, without compromising material flow and product quality. HVAC size may be optimized correspondingly.
  • Redundancy: The need for redundant HVAC equipment is best addressed via a failure mode risk analysis. It is often unnecessary to duplicate all HVAC plant items.
  • Simplicity: Overly elaborate design solutions are more expensive and may have a greater risk of failure.
  • Integration: Process room layouts, gowning room design, material transfers and process equipment design can all impact HVAC design.

5.2.1 資本成本

Five Capital Cost Drivers / 五大資本成本驅動因素

  • 隔離器與微環境：採用隔離器可降低房間分級要求，減小HVAC系統規模與成本。RABS、LP/GAAS、封閉製程同樣有助
  • 無菌區域大小：應在不影響物料流與品質的前提下優化面積
  • 冗餘設計：通過失效模式風險分析決定，通常無需完全複製
  • 簡單性：過度複雜的設計更貴且故障風險更高
  • 整合性：製程布局、更衣室、物料轉運與設備設計都影響HVAC

5.2.2 Operating Costs

The HVAC system design affects the operating costs of the manufacturing facility, particularly as continuous operation of HVAC is normally required. The preceding capital cost considerations may be outweighed by operating costs if a lifecycle approach to costing is undertaken.

Important energy considerations/approaches in the design process include:

  • Optimizing the size and occupancy of classified space to minimize airflow needed
  • Optimizing airflow through modeling and/or dilution calculations
  • Designing room air distribution for the most effective ventilation practical
  • Designing rooms to minimize excess leakage
  • Optimizing temperature and humidity requirements (widest acceptable ranges)
  • Treating outside air separately from recirculated air, especially for humidity control
  • Providing energy recovery on exhaust streams:
    • Enthalpy or heat wheel (low cross-contamination concern)
    • Air to air energy recovery (greater concern)
    • Heat pipes and runaround (serious concern)
  • Optimizing differential pressures
  • Optimizing filtration to minimize total pressure drop and maximize HEPA filter life
  • Recirculation of air (global or primary/secondary systems)
  • Advanced airside control strategies:
    • Airflow setback during idle periods
    • Occupancy sensing airflow setback
    • AHU supply static pressure setback
    • Discharge air temperature setback
    • Tracking VAV control of primary airflow
    • Adaptive airflow control (monitoring particulate and adjusting airflow)
  • Commissioning according to GEP
  • Utilizing common sized HEPA filters to reduce spares inventory
  • Design for ease of maintenance and testing

5.2.2 營運成本

Lifecycle Cost Perspective / 生命週期成本觀點

HVAC需要持續運行以維持潔淨度。資本成本的節省可能被運營成本抵消，因此應採用生命週期成本法進行總體評估。

Energy Optimization Strategies / 能源優化策略

  • 空間優化：最小化分級區域面積與人員數量
  • 氣流建模：以科學計算取代固定ACH標準
  • 熱回收：依交叉污染風險選擇轉輪、空對空或熱管方案
  • 壓差優化：避免過度壓差與過大流量差
  • 過濾優化：最小化總壓降，最大化HEPA壽命
  • 先進控制：閒置氣流調降、在場感應、VAV控制、自適應氣流控制

Warning: HVAC Shutdown / 警告：HVAC關機

強烈不建議為節能而定期關閉HVAC系統，因為這可能導致環境控制喪失並增加產品污染風險。數小時或數天的關機通常需要大量清潔、消毒與監測工作才能恢復生產。

5.3

Sources of Particulate Contamination

Pages 120–122

5.3.1 Internal Sources

Non-viable (microbiologically inert) particles may be dust, smoke, plastic, and metal debris from process or HVAC equipment, synthetic clothing fibers, makeup, hair, skin flakes, etc. Non-viable particles may also be active product from another area within a multi-product facility, which is a cross-contamination concern. Among and upon non-viable particles, there can be viable (living) organisms, such as spores, bacteria, and viruses. HEPA (and optional higher quality ULPA) filters can effectively remove more than 99.97% of these particles from the HVAC air supply.

Typical sources from inside the classified space include:

  • Personnel
  • Process equipment
  • Contamination entering through gaps in construction and cycling of doors
  • Contamination on items entering the space
  • Shedding from surfaces and cleaning materials or agent residue
  • Contamination from facility systems and HVAC ductwork downstream of final HEPA filters
  • Product particulate contamination from air returning from other product processing areas

Personnel: People are the greatest source of particle contamination, and the level of contamination they add depends on gowning and how they perform their tasks. Interventions (people inserting themselves into the aseptic process) are a common source of risk. The number and activity level of personnel, coupled with their gowning, is one of the most significant factors challenging the cleanroom environment.

The impact of gowning is often much greater than the impact of increasing dilution airflow (air change rate). The use of barrier technology (RABS or isolators) minimizes or eliminates interventions into the ISO 5/Grade A environment.

Process and Equipment: Contaminants released from equipment are mostly non-viable if equipment was properly cleaned and stored. Cleaning activities may release large quantities of particles. Single-use equipment can reduce the particulate associated with cleaning. Airborne product itself may become a cross-contaminant of another product.

Particles generated within the HVAC system should be virtually eliminated by HEPA filters. Terminal filters (located at the point where air enters the room) are preferable, and are strongly recommended for rooms classified ISO 7/Grade B or higher and commonly applied in ISO 8/Grade C.

5.3.1 內部來源

Internal Contamination Sources / 內部污染來源

  • 人員：最大的微粒污染來源。或為非活性（皮屑、衣物纖維）或活性（細菌、霉菌）
  • 製程設備：如正確清潔儲存，主要釋放非活性微粒
  • 建築縫隙與門循環：外部污染的入侵途徑
  • 進入物品上的污染：物料與零件攜帶的微粒
  • 表面脫落與清潔殘留：清潔活動可能釋放大量微粒
  • HEPA過濾器下游的風管：終端過濾器後的污染來源
  • 其他製程區域的回風：交叉污染風險

Personnel = #1 Risk / 人員＝首要風險

人員是最大的微粒污染來源。穿著的影響通常遠大於增加換氣次數（稀釋氣流）的效果。使用屏障技術（RABS或隔離器）可最大程度減少或消除人員對ISO 5/Grade A環境的干預。

Single-Use Advantage / 一次性優勢

一次性設備可減少與清潔相關的微粒，因為清潔活動本身會釋放大量微粒。這是一次性技術除了避免交叉污染外的另一項優勢。

5.3.2 External Sources

A positive room differential pressure relative to surrounding areas helps to exclude external contaminants, reducing infiltration from more contaminated spaces through cracks in the room fabric and doors. Where rooms of different air quality classifications are joined by a doorway, an airlock should be used to ensure that at least one door in the potential contamination path is closed, thus maintaining DP between the spaces.

In tightly constructed envelopes (e.g., panelized or modular wall systems), the airflow necessary to generate differential pressure across the envelope may be very small. By contrast, some stick-built walls and suspended ceiling systems may consume significant airflow to maintain pressurization.

A negative room differential pressure may be required to help contain highly potent or sensitizing compounds, live pathogen, or other high-risk materials. In these cases, surrounding positive pressurized clean spaces are most preferable, commonly achieved using airlocks and clean corridors.

Where isolators are employed to provide both a barrier and containment of potent/pathogenic compounds, "bubble" or "sink" airlock zones may be employed as part of the isolator design.

Particles entering the HVAC system, such as from outdoor (fresh) air used for room pressurization and operator health, are usually removed in the HVAC air filtration system, with the location and performance of the final HEPA filter being important to assuring removal.

5.3.2 外部來源

Pressure Cascade / 壓力梯度

正壓差可防止外部污染物透過縫隙與門長射入。不同分級區域之間應使用氣閘，確保污染路徑中至少一道門關閉。

Construction Type Matters / 建築類型影響

  • 模組化牆板系統：緊密建造，產生壓差所需氣流極小
  • 傳統建造與懸吊天花板：可能消耗大量氣流來維持加壓，並可能成為顯著的微粒來源

Negative Pressure Cases / 負壓案例

處理高效藥物、致敏化合物或活性病原體時，可能需要負壓房間以防止泄漏。此時周圍空間應為正壓潔淨區域，通常通過氣閘與潔淨走廊實現。隔離器可採用「泡泡」或「沉陷」式氣閘區設計。

5.4

Environmental Requirements — Pharmaceutical Cleanroom Standards

Pages 122–123

5.4.1 Table 5.3: Harmonized Airborne Environmental Requirements

This table bridges the differing cleanliness classifications used by major regulators (US FDA, EU/PIC/S) and international standards (ISO 14644-1) under the ISPE harmonized nomenclature.

US FDA Classification (In Operation)

EU/PIC/S Classification (In Operation)

EU/PIC/S Classification (At Rest)

Microbiological Action Limits (In Operation)

5.4.1 表5.3：協調空氣環境要求

Key Regulatory Differences / 關鍵法規差異

  • FDA：僅規定「運行中」條件，無「靜止態」值；未定義Grade D
  • EU/PIC/S：同時規定「運行中」與「靜止態」；Grade B在「靜止態」需達ISO 5
  • ISO 6：FDA認可，EU未定義（EU體系中無對應等級）
  • CNC：控制非分級區域，限值由業主決定，通常比外部空氣潔淨

Important Notes / 重要註解

  • ISO 5/Grade A條件應在產品、接觸部件與開口容器1英尺內測量
  • ISO 5/Grade A採用單向氣流（UAF），速度應視情況調整並証明
  • 微生物限值中，Grade A的< 1 CFU/m³表示復現率比計數本身更有意義
  • 監測位置應在氣流上游以避免計入產品氣溶
S

Section Summary / 章節總結

Key Takeaways from Sections 5.1–5.4

Summary of Key Concepts

5.1 Introduction

  • HVAC is the backbone of environmental control in sterile manufacturing facilities, primarily controlling airborne particulates, temperature, humidity, and pressure differentials.
  • Advanced aseptic technologies (isolators, BFS, single-use) can reduce room classification requirements by providing enhanced separation.
  • HEPA filtration (99.97% at 0.3 μm minimum) is the primary tool for airborne particulate control; ULPA filters may be used for enhanced performance.
  • Air Change Rate (ACH) should be used as a planning tool, not an acceptance criterion; empirical measures (particle counts, recovery tests) are preferred.

5.1.4–5.1.6 Classification, Risk, and LP/GAAS

  • Room particulate concentration is a balance of particles entering, retained within, and leaving the room, diluted by clean air supply.
  • Three occupancy states: "In Operation" (dynamic), "At Rest" (static), and "As-Built".
  • Recovery testing proves the transition from "in operation" to "at rest" conditions; two methods available (operational transition vs. ISO 14644-3 challenge).
  • HACCP and FMEA are the recommended risk assessment approaches for HVAC systems.
  • LP/GAAS provides localized HEPA-filtered air protection in any background classification, from Grade D to ISO 7/Grade B.

5.2–5.4 Cost, Contamination, and Standards

  • HVAC capital costs are driven by isolator use, area sizing, redundancy, simplicity, and integration with other facility systems.
  • Operating costs can be optimized through energy recovery, airflow modeling, pressure optimization, advanced control strategies, and lifecycle costing.
  • Personnel are the greatest internal source of particulate contamination; gowning impact exceeds dilution airflow impact.
  • Positive pressure differentials exclude external contaminants; airlocks preserve classification between differing zones.
  • Table 5.3 provides a globally harmonized classification bridging US FDA, EU/PIC/S, and ISO 14644-1 nomenclatures.

關鍵概念總結

5.1 導論

  • HVAC是無菌製造設施環境控制的骨幹，主要控制微粒、溫度、濕度與壓差
  • 先進無菌技術可降低房間分級要求
  • HEPA過濾（0.3 μm處至少99.97%效率）為主要微粒控制工具
  • ACH應作為規劃工具而非驗收標準

5.1.4–5.1.6 分級、風險與LP/GAAS

  • 微粒濃度是進入、滞留、離開與稀釋的平衡結果
  • 三種占用狀態：運行中、靜止態、空置態
  • HACCP與FMEA為HVAC推薦風險評估方法
  • LP/GAAS可在任何背景分級下提供局部HEPA過濾保護

5.2–5.4 成本、污染與標準

  • 資本成本受隔離器使用、區域大小、冗餘、簡單性與整合性驅動
  • 營運成本可通過熱回收、氣流建模、壓差優化與先進控制策略優化
  • 人員是最大微粒來源，穿著影響超過稀釋氣流
  • 正壓差排除外部污染，氣閘維持區域間分級
  • 表5.3提供美國FDA、EU/PIC/S與ISO的全球協調分級表

Reflection Questions / 反思問題

  1. 如果您的設施採用隔離器填充，HVAC設計可以如何簡化？
  2. 您的設施是否仍使用固定ACH作為驗收標準？是否應轉向基於科學的稀釋計算？
  3. 您的LP/GAAS區域是否已建立明確的EM限值，還是直接套用ISO 5/Grade A限值？
  4. 您的HVAC系統是否已進行過HACCP或FMEA風險評估？
4b

Chapter 4b: 5b. HVAC (5.5–5.7)

HVAC（中） | p123-p136

ISPE Baseline Guide Vol. 3 (3rd Ed.) | p123 – p136

Learning Objectives

  1. Understand the environmental Critical Parameters (temperature, humidity, particulates) and their acceptable ranges for sterile manufacturing.
  2. Explain how facility layout drives Pressure Cascade design and the role of airlocks in maintaining differential pressure.
  3. Describe the principles of cascade, bubble, and sink pressurization arrangements and when each is applied.
  4. Articulate how process knowledge (product form, barrier technology choice, equipment type) shapes HVAC system design.
  5. Identify supply and extract point design considerations that affect room air distribution and particulate control.
  6. Compare UAF approaches (horizontal vs. vertical) and their suitability for different process scenarios.
5.5

Environmental Critical Parameters

Temperature, Humidity, Contaminants, and Other HVAC Parameters

5.5.1 Temperature 5.5.1 溫度

Higher room temperature may affect the comfort of operators in the room, causing them to release more viable particles (perspiration and respiration), especially during more strenuous activities. A renovated or new facility should find technical solutions to eliminate the need for strenuous manual activities. Heavier gowning also would require lower room temperatures for comfort.

Generally, a room temperature in the lower end of the typical comfort range, around 18–22°C (64.4–71.6°F), can be easily maintained at reasonable cost.

Product temperature limits may differ from room temperatures for operator comfort. For prolonged residence of product with no special temperature requirements, USP <659> suggests temperature limits for “controlled room temperature” and other storage conditions. Room temperature limits of 15–25°C (59–77°F) are common.

溫度控制要點

無菌製造的溫度控制需同時考量兩個面向：

  • 操作員舒適度：過高溫度會增加操作員流汗與呼吸釋放，產生更多活性微粒子。穿著較重的無菌服時，建議降低室溫。
  • 產品需求：產品可能有獨立的溫度限制，不一定與人員舒適範圍相同。

實務提醒

一般無菌區建議 18–22°C，儲存區則可放寬至 15–25°C。CDMO 的不同客戶產品可能有不同溫度範圍要求，HVAC 系統設計應保留彈性。

5.5.2 Relative Humidity 5.5.2 相對濕度

Because product may be exposed to the surrounding environment for a relatively short time, usually during formulation and filling, the influence of the room’s humidity is minimal. Hydrophilic liquids and products in powder form, however, may be significantly affected by moisture in the surrounding air, and should be processed in low Relative Humidity (RH) rooms or enclosures.

Low humidity environments may create their own problems, such as static electricity and powder flow problems.

Room RH above 70% can, over time, lead to mold growth in some areas. It has been good practice to hold the room environment to below 60% RH (as growth of yeast and fungi are not observed below 0.60 AW or 60% RH, per USP <1112>). Studies have shown that some mold spores can germinate when exposed to >70% RH and can propagate on common building materials as RH approaches and exceeds 80%.

Unless product requirements dictate otherwise, a comfort humidity of 30–60% RH is recommended. RH values as low as 20–25% may be used as a lower limit in dry or cold climates, but these values are at the lower end of the range suggested for human health and may result in elevated levels of static electricity. RH below 25% is not recommended.

相對濕度的雙向影響

濕度過高的風險

  • RH > 70%：可能導致黴菌生長
  • RH > 80%：在石膏、紙張、水泥等建材上大量繁殖
  • 操作員釋放更多活性污染物
  • 金屬設備腐蝕風險增加

濕度過低的風險

  • 靜電積累——微粒子附著於非導電表面，擾動時大量釋放
  • 操作員呼吸道問題（另一個活性微粒子來源）
  • 粉末產品流動性問題

建議範圍

一般建議 30–60% RH，不建議低於 25%。對於粉末產品或親水性液體，可能需要更低的濕度環境，但需充分評估靜電和操作員健康風險。

5.5.3 Environmental Contaminants 5.5.3 環境污染物

Airborne particulate contaminant levels depend on:

  • Grade and integrity of final air supply filters — affecting quality of air delivered to the space
  • Quantity of airborne contaminants entering the space from within the room (from personnel, equipment, and materials) and from sources external to it (particle generation rate). Note: Leakage of unfiltered air from HVAC equipment can also be a source of particles.
  • Airflow introduced to the space:
    • Cleanliness and flow rate sufficient to dilute airborne particles to acceptable levels
    • Air change rate may be used as an indirect measure of dilution airflow, which affects the time for the room to recover from “in use” to “at rest” conditions
  • Differential pressure regime (including cascade, bubble, and sink arrangements)
  • Airlocks and anterooms (providing transition zones for cleaning of incoming materials and personnel as well as a buffer to intercept airborne particulate)
  • Airflow patterns within the cleanroom:
    • Particulate removal efficiency (ventilation efficiency) for non-unidirectional cleanrooms
    • Airflow visualization to demonstrate satisfactory patterns, per ISO 14644-3

粒子污染的多層次防禦

空氣中的微粒子控制是多層因素的結果，並非單一措施能達成：

比喻：洋蔥模型

想像粒子控制是一個洋蔥：

  • 最外層：過濾器等級與完整性（送風品質）
  • 中間層：壓差制度（壓力梯度）+ 氣鎖（緩衝區）
  • 核心層：換氣次數、氣流型態、粒子稀釋效率

恢復時間 (Room Recovery)

換氣次數越高，從「使用中」回到「靜態」的恢復時間越短。這是評估 HVAC 系統效能的重要指標。

5.5.4 Other Potential HVAC Critical Parameters 5.5.4 其他潛在暖通空調關鍵參數

  • Airflow patterns within the room to ensure sufficient mixing in turbulent cleanroom design, especially if air change rates are below 20 ACH in an ISO 8/Grade C space, or if local sites of high airborne particles are observed.
  • Recovery period from “in use” to “at rest” (common in EU facilities), which is a good indicator of the air system’s overall effectiveness (“robustness”):
    • The recovery time is measured from the time when room activity ceases
    • The EU GMPs suggest 15 to 20 minutes as an acceptable recovery time
  • Noise and vibration levels (rarely product requirements, but may be driven by operator health requirements)
  • Occupational (operator) product exposure levels

其他關鍵參數

恢復時間的意義

EU GMP 要求恢復時間應在 15–20 分鐘以內。這個指標反映的是 HVAC 系統的「強健性」——即系統從擾動中恢復的能力。

對於 CDMO，不同產品的生產過程粒子生成率不同，建議在設計階段以最差情境作為基準。

常見過失

噪音和振動往往被忽略，但對操作員健康有直接影響，特別是長時間暴露於高換氣次數的潔淨室環境中。

5.6

Facility Layout and HVAC Design

Pressure Cascades, Airlocks, Containment, and Hazardous Products

5.6.1 Manufacturing Environment and Cleanliness Cascades 5.6.1 製造環境與潔淨度級聯

Critical areas are locations where sterile product, container/closures, product contact surfaces, or filled (partially stoppered) containers are exposed or unprotected. Examples include:

  • Point of fill
  • Sterilized vials/caps entering the sterile processing area
  • Product containers opened in the aseptic processing area
  • Connections made to product containers
  • Holding of sterilized container/closures and machine contact surfaces
  • Transfer of partially stoppered containers for lyophilization
  • Cooling of sterilized container/closures following heat sterilization
  • Connecting, opening, or assembling of process sterilizing filters
  • Storage and assembly of sterilized equipment
  • Transfer or holding of stoppered, uncapped vials
  • Capping of filled vials

Once critical areas are identified, appropriate environmental standards can be assigned.

The guide defines three pressurization principles:

  • Cascade Principle (Figure 5.1A): Air flows from highest pressure to lowest pressure area.
  • Sink Principle (Figure 5.1B): Commonly applied to high containment products. The transition zone is at lowest pressure; air flows from the cleanroom and corridor.
  • Bubble Principle (Figure 5.1C): Commonly applied to high aerosol producing products. The transition zone is at highest pressure; air flows to the cleanroom and corridor.

潔淨度階梯與三種壓力原則

首先識別所有「關鍵區域」（產品暴露點），再指定環境分級。HVAC 設計必須服務於這個分級架構。

比喻：水壢與水流

壓力階梯就像水壢——水永遠從高處往低處流。Cascade 是正常流向（潔淨→不潔淨），Sink 是在中間放一個「排水孔」收集有害物質，Bubble 則是在中間放一個「噪泉」向外推握氣溶膠。

5.6.2 Differential Pressures 5.6.2 壓差

An airflow cascade should be set up using a differential pressure (DP) cascade. Key considerations:

  • Minimum suggested DP is 10–15 Pa (0.04–0.06" wg) between air classes with doors closed. Typical design pressure: 12.5 ± 2.5 Pa per step.
  • Rooms of differing criticality within an air class may be separated by less pressure, as long as DP can be reliably maintained and monitored.
  • Minimum suggested DP value is 5 Pa between areas of like classification.
  • Where DP less than zero (pressure reversal) is possible, DP sensors should be capable of sensing negative pressures and triggering alarms.
  • Excessive compounded pressure may create problems with the fabric of the highest pressure room, materials transferred across boundaries, or doors. Typical maximum room pressure is usually less than 45 Pa relative to the building.
  • There is no mandate to maintain pressurization between spaces while the door between them is open; attempting to do this generally results in oversized mechanical systems and unstable control.
  • An overall flow of air in the desired direction when door(s) are open should be maintained.
  • Pressure stabilizers (barometric dampers) are preferred over open ports and fixed dampers for maintaining velocity across open doors.
  • Temperature differences between spaces should not induce convection currents that overcome the intended direction of flow.
  • Highly potent, radiological, live microorganism, sensitizing, cytotoxic, hormonal, or biosafety hazards should be contained, possibly requiring bubble and sink arrangements.

A risk assessment is recommended to review all concerns and potential failure states in the determination of the final pressure regime.

壓力階梯設計實務

開門與關門的差異

開門時不要求維持壓差，但必須維持正確方向的氣流。試圖在開門時維持壓差會導致過大的機械系統和不穩定的控制。

壓力穩定器 (Pressure Stabilizer)

氣壓擋板（barometric damper）在門關閉時開啟，提供替代洩漏路徑，確保開門時有足夠的氣流速度。優於固定孔口或固定擋板，因為更容易清潔且不會壓縮工作區域的分險。

Pressurization Scheme Examples 加壓方案範例

Table 5.4: Scheme #1 — Tighter Control Range, Larger Step Spacing

Increment: 12.5 Pa | Range: ±2.5 Pa | Min DP Step: 7.5 Pa | Max DP Step: 17.5 Pa

Table 5.5: Scheme #2 — Less Stringent Control Range, Tighter Spacing

Increment: 12.5 Pa | Range: ±5.0 Pa | Min DP Step: 12.0 Pa | Max DP Step: 32.0 Pa

兩種壓力方案對比

選擇建議

方案一適合控制系統精度高、層數較少的設施；方案二適合控制精度有限、需要更大容許範圍的設施。但方案二的累積壓力更高，可能導致門的開關困難。

5.6.3 Airlocks 5.6.3 氣閘

Airlocks preserve some DP between rooms of different air classification; if there is no airlock, the DP between two rooms would drop to nearly zero when the door is opened.

Airlocks are usually small and should be highly ventilated rooms (for quick recovery), with doors interlocked and/or alarmed to prevent more than one being opened at a time. Local alarms should be employed if:

  • A door remains open for more than a preset period
  • Both doors are opened simultaneously
  • The DP across an airlock goes to zero

Airlocks between classified areas interpose multiple doors between areas of differing classification. Regardless of the airlock classification, there is no need to design for 10–15 Pa per door; it is more appropriate to divide the target pressurization across the number of doors present.

Material pass-throughs (transfer hatches) for higher risk transfers should incorporate ventilated hatches (actively supplied with filtered air or passively ventilated). Best practice is to use pass-through hatches capable of automated sanitization (e.g., via VHP, pulse UV, NO2).

Airborne particle levels near the door of an airlock, at rest, should meet the same level as the highest classified room served by the airlock.

氣鎖設計要點

氣鎖的三大功能

  • 維持壓差：通過多重門保持區域間的壓力差異
  • 緩衝污染：揔截微粒子從低級別區進入高級別區
  • 快速恢復：高換氣次數確保開門後迅速恢復

壓差分配原則

重要：氣鎖的壓差不是每道門都要 10–15 Pa，而是將總目標壓差均分到所有門上。例如：兩道門的氣鎖，每道門只需 5–7.5 Pa。

傳遞窗最佳實踐

高風險傳遞（跨兩個以上級別）應使用通風型傳遞窗，並具備自動消毒功能（VHP、脈衝 UV、NO2）。

5.6.4 Biological Safety / Bio-Containment 5.6.4 生物安全 / 生物防護

Where products may contain pathogens, viral vectors, or recombinant human DNA, biological safety requirements may modify the pressurization, filtration, and airlocking schemes suggested by the desired space cleanliness classification.

生物安全考量

當產品含有病原體、病毒載體或重組 DNA 時，生物安全要求可能會覆寫標準的壓力、過濾和氣鎖方案。這在細胞與基因治療 (CGT) 製造中特別重要。

5.6.5 Hazardous Products and Operator Protection 5.6.5 危險產品與操作人員防護

For an open process, airflow pattern testing should consider operator protection as well as product protection. Local exhaust ventilation can help control the dissemination of hazardous aerosols to limit operator exposure.

Local pickup of potentially hazardous aerosols for treatment (e.g., filtration) and return to the room is possible for operator protection; however, risk assessment is recommended as failure of the treatment system should be considered. Generally, return of treated room air has a very low risk, while return of treated hazardous exhaust has a high risk.

The use of barrier technologies provides an opportunity to overcome this problem by preventing hazardous aerosols from entering the operator’s environment.

危害產品與操作員保護

雙向保護原則

HVAC 設計必須同時考慮：

  • 產品保護：防止環境污染物進入產品
  • 操作員保護：防止有害氣溶膠進入操作員呼吸空間

屏障技術（隨離器、RABS）是解決這個矛盾的最佳方案。

5.7

Process Knowledge and HVAC Design

Sterilizers, Barrier Technology, Lyophilizers, Capping, and UAF Design

5.7 Process-HVAC Interface Overview 5.7 製程-暖通空調介面概述

Considerations for process knowledge, as it relates to HVAC design, include:

  • Product specific processing limits (e.g., temperature, humidity, particles in air)
  • Occupational (operator) exposure limits
  • Product form (liquid, dry powder, etc.) and other special physical or chemical parameters
  • Degree of separation between the immediate process environment and the general room environment:
    • Very high degree: isolator, closed process, closed RABS
    • High degree: active RABS, well-sealed passive RABS
    • Moderate degree: LP/GAAS, most passive RABS, some machine guarding
    • Low degree: strip curtains, air curtains

製程知識如何影響 HVAC 設計

這是本章的核心觀點：HVAC 不是獨立的工程學科，它必須服務於製程需求。

分離度階層

從隨離器（最高）到條帶簾（最低），分離度越低，對 HVAC 系統的要求越高，因為背景環境必須承擔更多的污染控制責任。

5.7.1.1 Sterilizers 5.7.1.1 滅菌器

A key equipment selection that interacts with HVAC is the “in-feed” sterilizer. There are two basic types:

  • Static equipment (such as autoclaves, dry heat ovens): Has little effect on the HVAC system and environmental balance, although hot air currents liberated on door opening may affect normal airflows. Heat and humidity gains should be considered. These are constant known quantities that can be anticipated.
  • Dynamic equipment (such as integrated sterilizing tunnels with conveyor openings): Have many differing operational and non-operational modes. They take air from or leak it to surrounding areas; these volumes change depending upon air temperature in the tunnel at the time. These changing conditions require careful integration with the HVAC system. There are serious risks of reversing DP and putting product at risk.

Tunnel designs may have a DP control zone at the washed vial entry point to prevent blow-through of hot sterilizing air into the washing room.

滅菌設備與 HVAC 的交互

CDMO 實務提醒

隧道式滅菌器是 HVAC 設計中最具挑戰性的設備之一。其內部溫度變化會導致不同模式下的氣流量變化，必須與 HVAC 系統密切配合，否則有壓差逆轉的風險。

5.7.1.2 Filling Room Equipment & ISO 5/Grade A Environments 5.7.1.2 充填室設備與 ISO 5/A 級環境

Facilities using UAF and machine guarding or strip curtains provide inferior separation of the exposed sterile product from the surrounding environment, especially during operator intrusions.

The advent of personalized therapies (such as cell and gene therapy) has increased the need for small scale aseptic filling, sometimes for a single patient. In these situations, biological safety cabinets or clean workstations may be used to provide an ISO 5/Grade A environment. It is still preferable that these activities take place in an ISO 7/Grade B background.

Open filling operations are best protected by the use of barrier technology. The choice of barrier technology (isolator or RABS) impacts HVAC and controls design.

Isolators exhibit four primary modes of HVAC operation:

  • Outflow: flowing HEPA filtered air over critical areas and out into the room through open doors
  • Decontamination: air tight to room while recirculating gaseous decontamination agent
  • Aeration: flowing HEPA filtered air out through the exhaust
  • Operation: flowing HEPA filtered air into the surrounding room through mouseholes

RABS have only one mode of operation from an HVAC perspective, but come in two types:

  • Passive RABS: utilize air directly from the HVAC system terminal HEPA filters (ceiling-mounted)
  • Active RABS: take in room supply air and circulate it through HEPA filters before releasing back to room below work height

Best practice: all RABS air should be removed from the room via low returns, not from a high inlet on the RABS unit. High inlets can seriously impede proper air patterns. CFD modeling is recommended.

屏障技術與 HVAC 的交互

Passive vs Active RABS

  • Passive RABS：直接使用天花板 HEPA 送風，無獨立風機
  • Active RABS：自帶風機循環，吸入房間空氣再經 HEPA 過濾

RABS 設計警告

  • Active RABS 的高位進氣口會干擾周圍氣流，應避免
  • Passive RABS 面板間的大開口可能導致 Grade B 空氣被吸入 Grade A 內部
  • 建議使用 CFD 模擬驗證氣流型態

5.7.1.3 Lyophilizers 5.7.1.3 凍乾機

Stoppers in vials should be fully seated in an environment that meets ISO 5/Grade A microbial limits. Transfer of partially stoppered vials to lyophilizers should be under ISO 5/Grade A environmental conditions.

Loading the shelves of lyophilizer equipment creates potential for biological contamination of partially stoppered vials, unless ISO 5/Grade A continuity is maintained, preferably by the use of barrier technology. The use of automated loading represents best practice to maintain the sterile integrity of the product during lyophilizer loading.

凍乾機與無菌連續性

關鍵要求

部分壓塞的西林瓶在轉移至凍乾機的過程中，必須始終維持在 ISO 5/Grade A 條件下。自動裝載是最佳實踐，可最大限度降低污染風險。

5.7.1.4 Capping Equipment 5.7.1.4 加蓋設備

Cappers traditionally generate large quantities of particles and are generally located outside filling and lyophilizer rooms. Airborne bioburden should be kept low until the cap has been crimped.

Transfer of stoppered, uncapped vials to capping should be under ISO 5/Grade A conditions until the vial leaves the aseptic environment. Thereafter, the vial transfer and capping environment should be served with LP/GAAS HEPA filtered air. It is acceptable that the actual environment may not meet ISO 5/Grade A “in use” during capping due to the liberation of particulates.

壓蓋設備的特殊考量

壓蓋是粒子生成大戶

壓蓋過程會產生大量金屬微粒子，因此通常設置在填充室外部。在壓蓋前，瓶子必須在 ISO 5/Grade A 條件下轉移；壓蓋區域則可接受 LP/GAAS 級別的 HEPA 過濾空氣。

5.7.2 General Manufacturing Area Environmental Design 5.7.2 一般製造區環境設計

HVAC design based on constant volume supply to the space can minimize potential for DP upsets and low airflow, which could lead to higher particle counts. An airflow monitor should be fitted to indicate and alarm a reduction of airflow (and therefore air changes) to rooms.

5.7.2.1 Operational Issues

Personnel practices can significantly impact contamination. Considerations include:

  • Limiting or eliminating operator intervention into ISO 5/Grade A areas, and reducing operator numbers in ISO 7/Grade B areas
  • Avoiding personnel moving near critical areas such as isolator mouseholes or RABS when doors are opened (movements should be slow to minimize airflow interruption)
  • Understanding where operators are stationed during normal operation
  • Fitting glove ports in lieu of opening RABS during operation
  • Understanding personnel traffic routes to assure particulates are properly flushed from the space

Process considerations include:

  • Where the process generates particles — airflow patterns should direct particles away from critical sites
  • Control of heat from process equipment (ventilation with cool air, exhaust, or enclosure)
  • Controlling vapors from sporicides and other cleaning solutions (may require more outside air than needed for pressurization)

5.7.2.2 Physical Issues

  • Good room and equipment finishes, cleanable to minimize re-entrainment of settled contamination
  • How rooms are sanitized (contact time, how quickly odors should be diluted)
  • Holes through walls (conveyor belts, sprinkler housings, electrical boxes) — potential for pressure leakage
  • Door clearances and tolerances — tighter doors require less exfiltration airflow
  • Door swings, closure force, and effect on room pressure
  • Equipment locations relative to air supply and return openings
  • Physical locations of critical areas in relation to uncontrolled areas
  • Use of active pressure control via automated dampers or use of statically balanced systems

製造區環境設計考量

定風量 (Constant Volume) 的優勢

定風量供氣可最大限度減少壓差波動和低風量導致的粒子數升高。建議安裝風量監控器，在風量下降時發出警報。

比喻：交通規劃

將潔淨室想像成一個封閉的城市：

  • 操作員就像車輛，移動時揚起「灰塵」（微粒子）
  • 交通動線必須設計得遠離「醫院」（關鍵區域）
  • 通風就像道路清掃車，必須有足夠的「掃除頻率」

常見物理洩漏點

牛空帶開口、未密封的灑水頭毼體、電氣箱等都是常見的壓力洩漏點。設計階段必須統計所有穿牆開口並納入洩漏量計算。

5.7.2.3 Supply and Extract Point Locations 5.7.2.3 送風與排風口位置

For ISO 7/Grade B and ISO 8/Grade C rooms, the design and location of air supply outlets are critical to proper performance. The “Contaminant Removal Effectiveness” (ASHRAE) depends on the location and type of both supplies and returns. Considerations include:

  • Air volume supplied to help achieve room design air change rates for recovery and particle dilution or displacement
  • Optimum number of air supply outlets to achieve good air distribution:
    • Uniform distribution of supply points with smallest practical dead zones
    • Utilizing a larger number of terminal HEPA outlets generally produces better results than using the fewest supplies at highest allowable flow
    • The % ceiling coverage technique (ISO 14644-3) can provide good airflow patterns
  • Avoiding airflow through any HEPA or ULPA filter exceeding the manufacturer’s rating
  • Use of airflow distributing screens (polyolefin) for more nearly unidirectional flow
  • Use of non-aspirating diffusers (radial flow) for uniform air distribution
  • Consideration of final equipment location to avoid interference with supply outlets/equipment intakes
  • Standardized terminal HEPA filter sizes to limit replacement and capital costs; using a single size HEPA with different airflow volumes at each location can lead to differential blinding
  • For critical environments (>1 µm): extract/return grilles at low level (to minimize upward airflow) and at multiple locations evenly around the room
  • For high particle count areas (Grade D, CNC) with low risk operations: high level returns may be employed without adverse effect

送風與回風位置設計

送風口設計原則

  • 布局均勻，死區最小化
  • 嬧可多個小風口，不要少個大風口
  • 不要超過 HEPA 過濾器的額定風量
  • 標準化過濾器尺寸，避免差異化堵塞 (Differential Blinding)

差異化堵塞 (Differential Blinding)

當同一尺寸的 HEPA 過濾器在不同位置使用不同風量時，低風量的過濾器會接收更多微粒子（因為停留時間更長），導致不均勻的堵塞和更短的使用壽命。

5.7.3 Unidirectional Airflow (UAF) Design Considerations 5.7.3 單向氣流 (UAF) 設計考量

5.7.3.1 Local Airflow Patterns

The effect of localized air movement on room conditions during operation should be considered. Generally speaking:

  • Airflow patterns that circulate from the floor up to work height are undesirable
  • Areas of very low velocity near critical operations are undesirable
  • Areas of very low velocity where particulate can accumulate are undesirable
  • Areas of closed recirculation (reservoir of particles) are undesirable
  • Airflow from less clean to more clean areas is undesirable

Large thermal loads within the space (e.g., equipment heat gains, items cooling after sterilization) may cause thermal airflow movement that should also be taken into account. Ceiling mounted extract can help minimize recirculation due to high heat.

In principle, UAF protection sweeps air from the cleaner environment (where product is exposed) toward the operator and other potential contamination sources. Room airflow should be verified with airflow visualization (smoke) tests under at rest and simulated operational conditions.

5.7.3.2 Horizontal versus Vertical Unidirectional Airflow

Two approaches to providing unidirectional flow protection:

  • Horizontal airflow — effective when only product protection or only operator protection is of concern
  • Vertical airflow — usually used when both product and operator protection must be considered

Target velocities are suggested as a footnote in the FDA guideline and other regulations. The important principle is protection of the critical area. During qualification, the velocity required to optimize protection during operating conditions should be determined, documented, and used as the basis of ongoing monitoring.

Advanced computer-aided airflow modeling programs (CFD) may assist in initial room and UAF modeling, but fine tuning may still be required during qualification.

單向氣流 (UAF) 設計

五個「不可接受」的氣流型態

  1. 從地板向上到工作高度的氣流
  2. 關鍵操作附近的極低速區
  3. 微粒子積累的低速死區
  4. 封閉迴圈（粒子蓄池）
  5. 從低潔淨區流向高潔淨區的氣流

驗證重點

氣流可視化（煙霧測試）應在靜態和模擬運行條件下進行。CFD 模擬可作為初始設計工具，但實際微調仍需在確認階段完成。

思考練習

您的填充室使用 Passive RABS，發現某個位置的粒子數持續偏高。您會如何調查？

  1. 檢查 RABS 面板間是否有過大的間雙
  2. 確認天花板與 RABS 頂部的密封性
  3. 執行煙霧測試確認是否有向上氣流或封閉迴圈
  4. 檢查附近是否有熱源導致熱對流
S

Section Summary / 章節摘要

Key Takeaways from Sections 5.5–5.7

Key Takeaways

  • Environmental Critical Parameters: Temperature (18–22°C), humidity (30–60% RH), and airborne particulates are the three pillars of cleanroom environmental control. Each must be evaluated through product-specific risk assessment.
  • Pressure Cascades: Design DP of 10–15 Pa between air classes (doors closed), with 5 Pa minimum between like classifications. Maximum room pressure typically <45 Pa relative to building.
  • Three Pressurization Principles: Cascade (standard aseptic), Sink (high containment), and Bubble (high aerosol) address different product/process risk profiles.
  • Airlocks: Distribute target DP across all doors (not 10–15 Pa per door). High ventilation rates for quick recovery. Door interlocks and alarms are essential.
  • Process-HVAC Integration: The choice of barrier technology (isolator vs. RABS), sterilizer type (static vs. dynamic), and product form fundamentally shapes HVAC design requirements.
  • Supply and Return Design: More, smaller supply outlets outperform fewer, larger ones. Low-level returns for critical environments; standardized HEPA sizes to avoid differential blinding.
  • UAF Principles: Sweep air from clean to less clean. Verify with smoke tests. Use vertical UAF when both product and operator protection are needed. CFD modeling recommended.

重點整理

  • 環境關鍵參數：溫度（18–22°C）、濕度（30–60% RH）、空氣微粒子是潔淨室控制的三大支柱。每個參數都必須通過產品風險評估來確定。
  • 壓力階梯：不同級別間 10–15 Pa，相同級別間 ≥ 5 Pa，最大房間壓力通常 <45 Pa。
  • 三種壓力原則：階梯（標準無菌）、沉降（高含毒）、氣泡（高氣溶膠）分別應對不同風險。
  • 氣鎖：將目標壓差均分到所有門，高換氣率確保快速恢復。
  • 製程-HVAC 整合：屏障技術選擇、滅菌器類型和產品形態根本性地決定了 HVAC 設計需求。
  • 送回風設計：多個小風口優於少個大風口；關鍵區域用低位回風；標準化 HEPA 尺寸避免差異化堵塞。
  • UAF 原則：氣流從潔淨區向不潔淨區吹。煙霧測試驗證。雙向保護用垂直氣流。建議 CFD 模擬。
4c

Chapter 4c: 5c. HVAC (5.8–5.10)

HVAC（下） | p137-p142

ISPE Baseline Guide Vol. 3 (3rd Ed.) | p137 – p142

Learning Objectives / 本章學習目標

  • Understand the rationale for continuous vs. periodic monitoring of HVAC parameters (particle counts, differential pressure, temperature, humidity) and how each contributes to sterility assurance / 理解連續監測與定期監測的差異，以及各環境參數（粒子計數、壓差、溫濕度）如何共同保障無菌水準
  • Know the recommended test frequencies for HEPA filter integrity testing, airflow pattern analysis, recovery time testing, and open door testing / 掌握 HEPA 過濾器完整性測試、氣流型態分析、恢復時間測試和開門測試的建議頻率
  • Describe the role of Environmental Monitoring Systems (EMS) and their compliance with 21 CFR Part 11 / 描述環境監測系統（EMS）的角色及其符合 21 CFR Part 11 的要求
  • Explain the IQ/OQ/PQ approach for HVAC qualification, including airflow visualization (smoke studies) and recovery testing / 說明 HVAC 確效的 IQ/OQ/PQ 方法，包括氣流可視化（煙霧測試）和恢復測試
  • Identify critical considerations for differential pressure monitoring: sensor placement, accuracy, reference points, and alarm management / 辨識壓差監測的關鍵考量：感測器位置、精度、參考點及警報管理
  • Understand HVAC cleaning, maintenance philosophy, and HEPA filter integrity testing as ongoing operational requirements / 理解 HVAC 清潔、維護哲學及 HEPA 過濾器完整性測試作為持續營運要求的重要性
5.8 Monitoring — HVAC Monitoring 5.8 監控 — 暖通空調監控

Original Text

It is not possible to assess product sterility on-line. The level of sterility assurance required for sterile products means it is unlikely that random sampling of the finished product will detect any sterility failure resulting from processing.

Such techniques as particle counting (per ISO 14644-2), active and “at rest” air sampling, surface sampling, and personnel sampling provide useful data. Even with this essential and informative data, final product sterility cannot be assured. Hence, aseptic operations rely upon validated procedures carried out in strictly controlled environments for all critical stages to minimize potential product risk.

Certain environmental parameters may be considered critical. These parameters should be monitored and documented, but it is not always possible to do so continuously. Aseptic manufacturing HVAC should have a robust design to minimize potential problems, and a well-considered and qualified monitoring/documenting program.

Parameters that are often continuously or frequently monitored include:

  • Temperature
  • Humidity
  • Differential pressure (DP) between air classes where a contamination path exists
  • Airflow volume rate (volume/time) — continuous monitoring is optional
  • Airborne non-viable particle levels
  • Grade A air supply velocity at 100–150 mm below the filter face — continuous monitoring is optional

Typically, periodic requalification may repeat some tests carried out as part of the original equipment qualification, such as:

  • Integrity testing of terminal HEPA filters
  • Confirming airflow or air change rates
  • Checking ISO 5/Grade A and LP/GAAS velocities at a defined distance proximal to the work surface and below the filter face (typically 300 mm above vial, 100–150 mm below filter)
  • Checking ISO 5/Grade A and LP/GAAS airflow patterns
  • Checking airflow patterns at the interface between ISO 5/Grade A and ISO 7/Grade B as well as between ISO 7/Grade B and surrounding areas
  • Recording room airflow patterns (optional in ISO 7/Grade B and ISO 8/Grade C)
  • Confirming room recovery time
  • Open door testing (confirming how long a door can remain open without need for an alarm)
  • Checking operator product exposure levels
  • Airborne non-viable particle levels (classification)
  • Shut down and restart testing
  • Reduced flow rate testing
  • Verification of impact of loss of HVAC on environmental control (time before triple clean is required)
"Airflow pattern analysis (visualization) outside of the Grade A zone may be undertaken as a qualification activity or as an engineering study."

教學解析

核心概念：為什麼不能只靠產品測試？

無菌產品的無菌保證水準（SAL）通常要求達到 10-6，代表每一百萬個單位中不超過一個非無菌品。這意味著你幾乎不可能透過隨機抽樣在成品中檢測到污染。

因此，整個無菌製造的品質保證邏輯是過程導向而非結果導向：我們監測環境條件來確保製程始終處於受控狀態，而非事後檢驗產品是否無菌。

這就是 HVAC 監測如此重要的根本原因 — 它是過程控制的基石。

連續監測 vs 定期監測

ISPE 將監測分為兩大類：

  • 連續監測（Continuous）：溫度、濕度、壓差、粒子計數 — 這些參數變化快，需要即時偵測異常
  • 定期再確效（Periodic Requalification）：HEPA 完整性測試、氣流型態分析、恢復時間測試 — 這些是較深入的系統性能驗證

連續監測告訴你「現在正常嗎？」，定期再確效告訴你「系統本質上還好嗎？」

比喻說明

健康監測 vs 年度體檢：

連續監測就像你每天戴的智慧手錶 — 持續追蹤心率、血氧、體溫。一旦數值異常，立刻警示。

定期再確效則像每年一次的全面健康檢查 — 包括 X 光、血液檢查、心電圖等深入檢查項目。

你不會因為手錶每天都顯示正常就跳過年度體檢；同樣地，你不會因為壓差每天都在規格內就跳過 HEPA 完整性測試。兩者互補，缺一不可。

重點提示：再確效測試清單

ISPE 列出了 13 項定期再確效測試項目。對於 CDMO 營運而言，最關鍵的幾項：

  • HEPA 過濾器完整性測試 — 一個洩漏的 HEPA 可以污染整個區域
  • 氣流型態分析（煙霧測試） — 確認單向流確實存在且未被干擾
  • 恢復時間測試 — 潔淨室在受到污染事件後多快能回到分類標準
  • 開門測試 — 確認門開啟多久不會觸發環境失控

這些項目直接關係到是否需要啟動偏差調查。

5.8.2 Typical Frequencies for Testing 5.8.2 典型測試頻率

Original Text

The test frequency for each test depends upon plant operating experience, the process/equipment qualification findings, and regulatory expectations. It may also vary from area to area. Considerations for testing frequencies are as follows:

  • Room airborne particles should be checked frequently as established by the EM plan. Use of automated continuous particle monitoring is recommended. Automated particle monitoring systems provide extensive relevant data on the state of the environment and are generally more reliable than manual monitoring.
  • Integrity testing of terminal HEPA filters should typically be performed twice per year in aseptic fill environments and once every year or two in less critical areas. The rationale for the testing frequency should be supported by ongoing data.
  • Checking ISO 5/Grade A and LP/GAAS velocities and uniformity at the filter face should be performed when integrity testing the HEPA filters.
  • Checking room airflow patterns is usually performed at HVAC qualification, but may be justified when room equipment layouts change.
  • The need for retesting ISO 5/Grade A and LP/GAAS patterns should be assessed whenever the process physically changes (such as new or relocated equipment) or when operator procedures change; otherwise, the frequency should be every 3 to 5 years.
  • Determining how long a door may remain open should be performed at qualification and every 3 to 5 years thereafter.
  • Confirmation of recovery time (EU) should be performed at qualification. There is no fixed requirement for re-verification frequency; this should be determined by risk assessment.
  • Parameters such as operator product exposure levels should be tested frequently for reasons other than GMP.

教學解析

HEPA 完整性測試（DOP/PAO）為何如此關鍵？

DOP/PAO 完整性測試（Dioctyl Phthalate / Poly-Alpha Olefin 氣溶膠挑戰測試）是驗證 HEPA 過濾器是否有洩漏的唯一可靠方法。

一個洩漏的 HEPA 不會在壓差監測中顯現異常 — 壓差可能仍然正常，但大量粒子已經穿透。這就是為什麼 ISPE 建議無菌充填區每年測試兩次。

常見洩漏位置：

  • 濾材本身的針孔或破損
  • 濾框與天花板框架之間的密封墊
  • 框架本身的裂縫或變形

任何一處洩漏都可能讓外界粒子直接進入 Grade A 區域，等同於失去最後一道防線。

比喻說明：防彈背心的定期檢查

HEPA 過濾器就像無菌區的「防彈背心」。即使你穿著它感覺很好（壓差正常），你仍然需要定期檢查背心有沒有磨損或裂縫（DOP/PAO 測試）。

一件看起來完好但內部纖維已經劣化的防彈背心，在被子彈（微粒）擊中時可能完全無效。同樣，一個看起來正常但有微小洩漏的 HEPA 過濾器，在面對真實生產環境的微粒挑戰時可能無法保護產品。

5.8.3–5.8.4 Environmental Monitoring Systems & Typical EMS Monitoring 5.8.3–5.8.4 環境監測系統與典型 EMS 監控

Original Text

5.8.3 Environmental Monitoring Systems

From an engineering perspective, automated environmental monitoring should provide feedback on the HVAC system’s overall performance. It should highlight lack of performance in an individual system or room and notify the occupants of the condition.

An automated Environmental Monitoring System (EMS) is recommended to provide a GMP record of critical environmental parameters. Automated monitoring systems should comply with US FDA 21 CFR Part 11 and be subject to validation to assure the accuracy of the readings and records produced by the system.

EU Annex 1 requires that HVAC monitoring systems notify occupants when the HVAC has failed. The monitoring system should notify the occupants when any critical parameter is out of specified range for more than a predetermined period of time. The system should be equipped with colored warning lights to indicate the state of the HVAC system.

5.8.4 Typical EMS Monitoring for Aseptic HVAC

Differential Pressures

All DPs within a sterile area environmental cascade should be continuously measured, indicated, recorded, and alarmed. It may be advisable to select a representative number of particular DP measurements as key indicators of overall HVAC system “health.”

Additional considerations for monitoring of DPs include:

  • Monitor DP across airlocks; DP should not go to zero as long as one door in the contamination path remains closed.
  • DP sensors can be employed to detect door opening and control the time that doors remain open.
  • Only one DP sensor is needed per room, but it should be located to minimize impact of air currents at the sensor.
  • The monitoring system should document the duration of an unexpected loss (reduction) in pressure differential.
  • Reversed direction of airflow across a door is undesirable and should only occur for brief intervals.
  • The accuracy of differential measurement devices is critical. For control to ± 2.5 Pa, an accuracy of 0.25 Pa is desirable.
  • The reference point selected for DP measurements is critical. If measurements are made to a central reference, this reference point should be located in a large stable space.

Airflow to Rooms

While continuous measurement of airflow is not required, assurance of a consistent airflow supply is an indirect indicator of the ability to dilute contaminants and of room environmental control. Airflow monitoring is usually continuous since an airflow volume/velocity monitor is often installed to adjust fan delivery to compensate for air filter loading.

If a variable airflow scheme (such as idle airflow setback) is utilized, room airflow measurement is recommended. These schemes typically are not implemented until 15–20 minutes after cessation of use to allow for recovery.

Temperature and Humidity

Temperature and humidity for rooms with critical operations should be monitored to ensure control of operator comfort, product temperature, humidity requirements, and bioburden. Monitoring and data collection at short intervals (minutes instead of seconds) should provide adequate data without creating data overload.

The accuracy of temperature and humidity instruments is critical. Platinum RTD are preferred for temperature reading and capacitance sensors are preferred for RH.

Airborne Particle Count (Total or Non-viable)

In critical zones (e.g., ISO 5/Grade A and at ISO 5/Grade A to ISO 7/Grade B interface), the use of automated continuous particle monitoring is recommended. Automated particle monitoring systems provide extensive relevant data on the state of the environment and are generally more reliable than manual monitoring.

教學解析

EMS 系統的三大功能

環境監測系統（EMS）不只是「記錄數據」，它扮演三個關鍵角色：

  1. 即時回饋（Real-time Feedback）：持續監控 HVAC 系統整體性能，發現問題立即通知
  2. GMP 記錄（GMP Records）：符合 21 CFR Part 11 的電子記錄要求，包括審計追蹤、電子簽名、資料完整性保護
  3. 警報管理（Alarm Management）：當關鍵參數超出規格時，透過彩色警示燈和聲響通知作業人員

壓差（DP）監測的關鍵細節

壓差是無菌區環境控制中最重要的連續監測參數之一。ISPE 對 DP 監測提出了多項關鍵要求：

  • 精度要求：控制範圍 ±2.5 Pa 時，感測器精度需達 0.25 Pa（即控制範圍的 10%）
  • 參考點選擇：應選擇大型穩定空間作為參考點。室外因風速不穩定是不良參考點；機械室因溫控通風也不適合
  • 氣閘壓差：只要污染路徑上有一扇門保持關閉，壓差就不應降至零
  • 反向氣流：門開啟時可能短暫出現反向氣流，但應僅維持極短時間

比喻說明：壓差就像水壩的水位差

想像無菌區是一座位於高處的水庫，而外界環境是低處的河流。壓差就像水庫和河流之間的水位差 — 只要水位差存在（正壓），水（空氣/微粒）只會從高處流向低處，外界的污染物無法逆流進入無菌區。

如果水位差降到零甚至反轉，河水就會倒灌 — 這就是壓差反轉（reversed airflow）為什麼被視為嚴重事件。

DP 感測器就像水庫上的水位計，必須安裝在不受水流湍動影響的穩定位置，才能提供準確讀數。

溫濕度與粒子監測實務要點

  • 溫度感測器：推薦使用鉑電阻溫度計（Platinum RTD），精度高且穩定
  • 濕度感測器：推薦使用電容式感測器（Capacitance Sensor），回應快且耐用
  • 數據採集頻率：以分鐘為間隔即可（非秒級），避免資料過載同時確保足夠解析度
  • 大型房間：應進行溫度映射（Temperature Mapping）以確定最具代表性的監測位置
  • 粒子監測：關鍵區域（ISO 5/Grade A）強烈建議使用自動連續粒子計數器，比手動監測更可靠
5.8.5 HVAC Controls (Building Automation System / Building Management System) 5.8.5 暖通空調控制（樓宇自動化系統 / 建築管理系統）

Original Text

When considering the HVAC control system, it is important to consider it as another service supporting environmental condition control. Automatic controllers may indirectly affect patient safety and product quality, but performance can be monitored by a qualified EMS. HVAC controls would not need to be qualified; HVAC field devices would only need to be qualified when HVAC control and environmental monitoring are shared.

HVAC automatic controls may be employed to control variables such as temperature and humidity. In more complex designs, other variables may also be controlled:

  • Room DP (especially where airflows to/from rooms are expected to vary)
  • Constant supply and extract fan volume control (to compensate for air filter loading)
  • Filter blinding condition (pressure drop) monitoring
  • Active room pressure control

During design, risk assessment should be performed to assess the positive and negative impacts of an automatic control system. Considerations include:

  • What would happen if constant fan volume control were not employed?
  • What would happen if an active pressure control system failed?
  • Does the system incorporate fail safe features?
  • Does the control design prevent catastrophic failures such as duct collapse and airflow reversals?
  • Are visible and audible alarms included to monitor environmental control changes?

教學解析

BAS/BMS vs EMS — 分清角色

這是一個容易混淆的概念。ISPE 做了明確區分：

  • BAS/BMS（樓宇自動化系統）：負責控制 HVAC — 調節溫度、濕度、風量、壓差。它是執行者。
  • EMS（環境監測系統）：負責監測並記錄環境參數 — 產生 GMP 合規記錄。它是監督者。

關鍵原則：BAS/BMS 本身不需要確效（因為 EMS 可以獨立驗證其性能），但如果 BAS 和 EMS 共用現場設備（如同一個感測器），則該設備需要確效。

這體現了基於風險的方法 — 只確效直接影響 GMP 記錄的部分。

設計階段的風險評估問題

ISPE 列出的五個風險評估問題本質上都在問同一件事：「如果這個控制失效了，最壞會發生什麼？」

最嚴重的兩個失效模式：

  • 風管塌陷（Duct Collapse）：可能由風扇控制失效導致負壓過大引起，會造成整個 HVAC 系統癱瘓
  • 氣流反轉（Airflow Reversals）：污染物從低潔淨度區域流向高潔淨度區域，直接威脅產品無菌性

設計時必須內建故障安全（Fail-safe）機制，例如：風扇故障時自動開啟旁通、壓差過低時自動關閉送風門等。

情境思考

  1. 你的工廠在審計時被問到：「BAS 有沒有做確效？」你會如何回答？依據是什麼？
  2. 如果 BAS 和 EMS 共用同一個壓差感測器，確效範圍會有什麼變化？為什麼？
  3. 一個主動壓力控制系統突然故障，你預期會看到哪些環境參數的變化？應該如何回應？
5.9 Qualification of HVAC Systems 5.9 暖通空調系統確效

Original Text

HVAC systems serving an aseptic manufacturing suite should be considered as a system which may affect patient safety and product quality. Qualification, testing, and commissioning, in line with GEP, should be considered.

For additional information, refer to ISPE Baseline Guide: Commissioning and Qualification [34]. Field qualification procedures are detailed in ISO 14644-3 (Cleanrooms and Associated Environments, Part 3 – Test Methods).

教學解析

HVAC 確效的 IQ/OQ/PQ 架構

雖然 ISPE 在此節僅做概述並引用其他指南，但 HVAC 確效的標準流程值得完整理解：

  • IQ（安裝確效）：驗證 HVAC 系統是否按照設計規格正確安裝。包括：設備型號/序號確認、管線連接檢查、HEPA 過濾器安裝密封性、電氣接線、控制系統配置
  • OQ（操作確效）：驗證系統在設計的操作範圍內能否正確運行。包括：送風量測試、壓差梯度驗證、溫濕度控制測試、警報功能測試、故障模式測試
  • PQ（性能確效）：驗證系統在實際生產條件下的持續性能。包括：氣流可視化（煙霧測試）、恢復時間測試、粒子分類測試、HEPA 完整性測試

煙霧測試（Smoke Study）— 氣流可視化的核心

氣流可視化（Airflow Visualization）是 PQ 階段最具視覺衝擊力的測試。透過在關鍵區域釋放煙霧，可以直接觀察到：

  • Grade A 區域是否真正維持單向流（Unidirectional Flow）
  • 操作人員介入時，氣流是否被擾動
  • Grade A 與 Grade B 交界處的氣流方向
  • 是否存在渦流（Turbulence）或死角（Dead Zone）

煙霧測試的結果通常以影片記錄，作為確效文件的一部分。這是法規查核時最常被要求檢視的文件之一。

恢復測試（Recovery Testing）

恢復時間是指潔淨室在受到污染事件後，回復到其分類標準所需的時間。

EU Annex 1 的要求：

  • Grade A：恢復時間應少於 15 分鐘（從「靜態」到粒子計數達標）
  • Grade B：恢復時間應少於 15-20 分鐘

恢復時間直接反映了 HVAC 系統的換氣能力和過濾效率。恢復時間越短，代表系統越強健，能越快消除異常事件的影響。

在實務中，恢復測試通常以人工產生氣溶膠粒子來模擬污染事件，然後測量粒子計數器回到基線水準所需的時間。

比喻說明：游泳池的自淨能力

恢復時間就像游泳池的自淨能力。如果有人在泳池裡撒了一瓶墨水（污染事件），循環過濾系統需要多久才能把水恢復到清澈透明（達到分類標準）？

一個配備強力循環泵和高效過濾器的泳池（高換氣次數 + HEPA）可能在幾分鐘內就恢復清澈；而一個循環能力不足的泳池可能需要好幾個小時。

這就是為什麼換氣次數（Air Change Rate）和 HEPA 過濾效率是決定恢復時間的兩大關鍵因素。

5.10 Cleaning and Maintenance of HVAC Systems 5.10 暖通空調系統清潔與維護

Original Text

5.10.1 Air System Cleaning and Sanitization

  • Ductwork should be manufactured, inspected, and installed according to GEP.
  • To minimize potential for growth of bioburden within the duct, ductwork should be cleaned internally prior to assembly, and temporarily sealed after installation.
  • Periodic cleaning of duct systems is not normally required due to the performance of pre-filtration.
  • Fumigating production rooms may be desirable for control of microorganisms. The HVAC system should be specially designed to isolate rooms to allow fumigation without circulation of the agent to surrounding spaces. Room pressurization may need to be controlled to prevent migration of sanitizing agent.
  • Fumigating some or all of the system may be desirable where highly potent or pathogenic materials are handled. The system should be designed to allow fumigation through the HVAC system without circulation to surrounding spaces. HVAC system materials should be selected with this procedure in mind.

5.10.2 Maintenance Philosophy

  • As much of the system as possible should be accessible and maintained from outside the aseptic processing area.
  • When replacement of terminal air filters (and lighting) are expected to be more frequent than planned maintenance shutdowns, access to these items from outside the processing area should be considered.
  • Access should not require working directly on ceilings from above.
  • HVAC designers should understand the planned facility maintenance philosophy.
  • An effective and fast-response breakdown maintenance plan can minimize the economic impact of unplanned HVAC shutdowns.
  • HVAC maintenance personnel should be trained on the system and its effect on the product/process.
  • Critical components in systems which affect patient safety and product quality should be under quality change control.
  • Thoroughly investigate the impact of filter leaks to determine patient and product risk. Proper investigation of filter leaks can determine if contamination that penetrates HEPA filters has the potential to jeopardize patient safety.
  • Refer to ISO 14644-3 for suggested commissioning and retesting procedures.

教學解析

風管清潔的實務原則

一個常見的誤解是認為潔淨室的風管需要定期清洗。ISPE 明確指出：由於預過濾的效能，風管系統通常不需要定期清潔。

但這建立在幾個前提上：

  • 風管在安裝前已經過內部清潔
  • 安裝後暫時密封，防止施工灰塵進入
  • 預過濾器（Pre-filter）和中效過濾器（Medium Filter）正常運作，攔截了絕大部分粒子

如果這些前提不成立（例如預過濾器長期未更換），風管內部可能累積灰塵甚至滋生微生物。

燻蒸（Fumigation）的 HVAC 設計考量

燻蒸是控制微生物的有效手段，但對 HVAC 設計提出特殊要求：

  • 房間隔離：HVAC 系統必須能將待燻蒸的房間與其他區域完全隔離，防止燻蒸劑擴散
  • 壓力控制：燻蒸過程中需控制房間壓力，防止燻蒸劑遷移至其他空間
  • 材質相容性：處理高毒性或致病性材料時，HVAC 系統材料必須能承受燻蒸劑（如 VHP/甲醛）的腐蝕

常見燻蒸劑：過氧化氫蒸氣（VHP）、甲醛（Formaldehyde）、二氧化氯（ClO2）。

維護哲學的核心原則

ISPE 提出的維護哲學可歸納為一個核心理念：「盡可能從潔淨區外部進行維護。」

這意味著在設計階段就必須考慮：

  • 走入式天花板（Walk-on Ceiling）：讓維護人員可以從上方夾層更換 HEPA 過濾器和燈具，無需進入潔淨室
  • 維護通道設計：設備的維護側面朝向非潔淨區或技術走廊
  • 更換頻率考量：如果 HEPA 更換頻率高於計畫停機頻率，必須提供外部更換通道

每次進入潔淨區進行維護都會帶來污染風險和停產損失，因此好的設計應該最小化這種需求。

HEPA 過濾器洩漏調查

ISPE 特別強調要「徹底調查過濾器洩漏的影響」。這不是簡單地更換過濾器就了事：

  • 需要判斷洩漏何時開始（回溯至上次合格的 DOP/PAO 測試）
  • 需要評估洩漏期間的所有生產批次是否受到影響
  • 需要分析穿透 HEPA 的污染物是否具有影響病患安全的潛力
  • 需要評估是否需要擴大環境監測數據的回顧範圍

這是為什麼 HEPA 完整性測試的頻率和記錄完整性如此重要 — 它們決定了洩漏調查的時間窗口和影響範圍。

實務應用：HEPA 洩漏的影響評估

假設你的無菌充填區 Grade A HEPA 在半年度 DOP 測試中發現洩漏。以下是你需要執行的關鍵步驟：

  1. 確認上次合格日期：回溯至最近一次通過 DOP/PAO 測試的日期
  2. 列出受影響批次：該時間段內在此區域充填的所有批次
  3. 回顧 EM 數據：檢視該期間的粒子計數和微生物監測是否有異常趨勢
  4. 風險評估：根據洩漏大小、位置和 EM 數據，評估產品風險
  5. CAPA：更換過濾器、分析根本原因（密封墊老化？安裝不當？振動損壞？）、調整測試頻率
Section Summary / 本章總結

Key Takeaways

Core Principles from Sections 5.8–5.10

  1. Sterility cannot be tested into the product. Environmental monitoring through validated HVAC systems is the primary assurance mechanism for aseptic manufacturing.
  2. Continuous monitoring + periodic requalification provide complementary assurance. Key continuous parameters: DP, temperature, humidity, particle counts. Key periodic tests: HEPA integrity (DOP/PAO), airflow visualization (smoke studies), recovery testing.
  3. HEPA filter integrity testing is the most critical periodic test. Recommended frequency: twice per year for aseptic fill areas. A leaking HEPA can compromise an entire zone without triggering DP alarms.
  4. DP monitoring accuracy and reference point selection are engineering decisions with direct GMP impact. Accuracy should be 10% of the control range; reference points must be in stable pressure zones.
  5. EMS must comply with 21 CFR Part 11 and be validated. BAS/BMS does not require qualification unless it shares field devices with EMS.
  6. HVAC maintenance should be performed from outside the aseptic area wherever possible, to minimize contamination risk from maintenance activities.
  7. HEPA filter leaks require thorough investigation — not just replacement, but retrospective assessment of all production batches since the last passing integrity test.

重點回顧

5.8–5.10 節核心要點

  1. 無菌性無法透過成品檢驗來保證。通過經確效的 HVAC 系統進行環境監測，是無菌製造的主要保證機制。
  2. 連續監測 + 定期再確效提供互補的保證。連續監測：壓差、溫度、濕度、粒子。定期測試：HEPA 完整性（DOP/PAO）、氣流可視化（煙霧測試）、恢復測試。
  3. HEPA 過濾器完整性測試是最關鍵的定期測試。無菌充填區建議每年兩次。洩漏的 HEPA 可能在壓差正常的情況下污染整個區域。
  4. 壓差監測的精度和參考點選擇是直接影響 GMP 的工程決策。精度應為控制範圍的 10%；參考點必須位於壓力穩定區域。
  5. EMS 必須符合 21 CFR Part 11並經過驗證。BAS/BMS 不需要確效，除非與 EMS 共用現場設備。
  6. HVAC 維護應盡可能從潔淨區外部執行，以最小化維護活動帶來的污染風險。
  7. HEPA 過濾器洩漏需要徹底調查 — 不僅是更換過濾器，還需回溯評估自上次合格完整性測試以來的所有生產批次。

綜合練習題

  1. 請列出無菌充填區中需要連續監測的四個關鍵 HVAC 參數，並說明每個參數的監測目的。
  2. 解釋為什麼 DOP/PAO 測試能發現壓差監測無法偵測的問題。提供一個具體情境。
  3. 你的工廠正在設計新的無菌區。針對 HEPA 過濾器的更換維護，你會建議採用什麼設計方案？依據是什麼？
  4. 一位品質人員提議將 HEPA 完整性測試頻率從每年兩次降為每年一次，以節省成本。你會如何評估這個提議？需要什麼數據來支持決定？
  5. 說明恢復時間測試（Recovery Testing）的執行方式，以及為什麼它是 HVAC 性能確效的關鍵指標。
5

Chapter 5: 6. Utility Systems

公用工程系統 | p143-p150

ISPE Baseline Guide Vol. 3 (3rd Ed.) | p143 – p150

Learning Objectives / 學習目標

  1. Distinguish between Process Systems and Process Support Systems and understand the criteria for classification / 區分製程系統與製程支援系統，理解分類標準
  2. Understand the critical quality attributes of WFI, clean steam, and process gases in sterile manufacturing / 了解注射用水、潔淨蒸汽與製程氣體在無菌製造中的關鍵品質屬性
  3. Identify key design considerations for utility distribution, filtration, and point-of-use requirements / 辨識公用工程分配、過濾及使用點需求的關鍵設計考量
  4. Recognize the importance of risk-based approaches to utility system qualification and sterile boundary definition / 認識風險基礎方法在公用工程系統確效與無菌邊界定義中的重要性
  5. Apply CDMO-relevant principles: utility capacity planning for multi-product facilities / 應用CDMO相關原則：多產品設施的公用工程產能規劃
6.1 Introduction / 導論

6.1 Introduction

Utility systems used in sterile facility operations may be categorized as either Process Systems or Process Support Systems. The sterile product manufacturer should review the various systems within the facility and determine their respective categories. This provides the basis for determining the design, construction, commissioning, verification, and documentation requirements for the system.

Process Systems are systems that:

  • Contact the product (as defined by the ASME BPE Standard as a surface that contacts raw materials, process materials, and/or product)
  • Contact materials or components which ultimately become part of the product
    • Process components include piping, fittings, valves, gaskets, vessels, pumps, filter housings, and instruments
  • Control contamination of surfaces that contact the product
  • Could otherwise directly affect product quality as determined through risk assessment (e.g., systems that prepare components and equipment for production)

Process Support Systems are systems that:

  • Do not contact the product or materials which ultimately become part of the product
  • Are generally site or building systems that are not specifically tailored to sterile manufacturing operations
  • Deal with an ancillary manufacturing process (e.g., waste disposal)
  • Do not explicitly affect product quality as determined through risk assessment

Examples of system categorization:

  • Purified water (depending on use), WFI, and clean steam are normally categorized as Process Systems.
  • Airflow of a depyrogenation tunnel or barrier isolator is generally a Process System since air contacts product contact components.
  • Compressed air and inert gases may be either Process or Process Support Systems, depending on use.
    • Sterile compressed air for post-SIP sterilization or pressure transfer of product to filling = Process System.
