    • Compressed air used as instrument air without product contact = Process Support System.
  • Breathing air, chilled water, instrument air, potable water, and floor drains are normally Process Support Systems.

Systems should be defined with clear system boundaries, indicating the scope of the sections that are subject to more stringent testing and commissioning activities.

6.1 導論解析

核心概念：製程系統 vs. 製程支援系統

本章將無菌設施中的公用工程分為兩大類：

  • 製程系統（Process Systems）：直接接觸產品或影響產品品質的系統，需要嚴格的設計、建造、調試與確效。
  • 製程支援系統（Process Support Systems）：不接觸產品的輔助系統，依照良好工程規範（GEP）設計即可。

分類的關鍵問題：該系統是否會接觸產品？是否會影響產品品質？

生活比喻：餐廳的水源分類

想像一間餐廳：

  • 製程系統好比廚房用的純淨水——直接用於料理食材，必須符合飲用水標準。
  • 製程支援系統好比沖洗地板的自來水——不直接接觸食物，清潔用途即可。

但如果自來水意外濺到食材上，就會造成污染風險。同理，製程支援系統若設計不當（例如儀器空氣排入ISO 5區域），也可能影響產品。

重點提示：系統邊界定義

ISPE強調必須為每個系統定義清楚的系統邊界（system boundaries）。這決定了：

  • 哪些部分需要嚴格的調試與確效（commissioning & qualification）
  • 哪些部分只需遵循GEP
  • 文件化要求的範圍

在CDMO環境中，同一條壓縮空氣管路可能同時服務製程用途和儀器用途——必須在系統邊界處清楚劃分。

6.2 Descriptions / 系統描述

6.2.1 Process Systems

Process Systems are considered to affect patient safety and product quality, and therefore, should be designed, constructed, commissioned, and verified to provide a service that meets a defined specification (considering product quality requirements) and prevents product contamination accordingly.

Design considerations for Process Systems:

  • Appropriate materials of construction for process contact surfaces that allow systems to be cleaned, sterilized if required, operated, and maintained
  • Appropriate materials of construction for non-product contact surfaces that could affect the particulate count within the cleanroom
  • Exposure to cleaning materials of the room
  • Access for removal or maintenance
  • Particulates generated from rotating parts of equipment exhausts which could affect the particulate count of the cleanroom
  • Control of the system in service, out of service, and returned to service cases
  • Functional use and operator interaction
  • Ergonomic functionality

For material selection, refer to the ASME BPE Standard. Selection of materials for fluid storage and distribution systems should consider the nature of the fluid being conveyed. For non-corrosive liquids and gases (such as nitrogen), typical materials include copper, plastics, and stainless steel.

Regulated companies should consider the type of cleaning agents and sterilants to be used and how those chemicals affect the surface of the equipment contacting the process. Each piping component and connection should be reviewed to determine how the system should be sterilized and whether the materials of construction are appropriate.

Service components and piping should be located outside the aseptic area, where possible. Surfaces inside the cleanroom should be sanitized or sterilized to meet or exceed allowable limits for bioburden.

Single-use systems should be designed to protect product integrity and prevent contamination from interrupted connections. Single-use systems and connections should be designed for routine operator interaction and functionality.

6.2.1 製程系統設計考量

核心概念：製程系統設計八大考量

設計製程系統時，需系統性地檢視以下面向：

  1. 接觸面材質——可清洗、可滅菌、耐操作與維護
  2. 非接觸面材質——不會增加潔淨室微粒數
  3. 耐清潔劑——能承受潔淨室清潔化學品
  4. 維護可及性——方便拆卸或維修
  5. 微粒控制——旋轉零件排氣不影響潔淨度
  6. 服務狀態管理——運行中、停機中、恢復使用三種狀態
  7. 操作員互動——功能性與人因工程
  8. 人因設計——符合人體工學原則

重點提示：材質選擇原則

  • 接觸產品面：依ASME BPE標準選擇，通常為316L不銹鋼
  • 非腐蝕性流體（如氮氣）：可用銅、塑膠或不銹鋼
  • 必須考慮清潔劑和滅菌劑對表面的影響
  • 管路與元件盡可能設於無菌區域之外

CDMO觀點：單次使用系統

對CDMO而言，單次使用系統（Single-Use Systems）是多產品製造的重要策略：

  • 減少交叉污染風險——無需產品轉換間的清潔確效
  • 降低設備共用的複雜度
  • 但必須確保連接完整性——中斷的連接是污染的主要來源

6.2.2 Process Support Systems

Process Support Systems generally do not affect patient safety and product quality, and should be designed and constructed in compliance with GEP and applicable codes and standards. Such systems typically are not located within a cleanroom; therefore, the materials of construction depend upon service requirements.

If these services or their points-of-use need to be located in the aseptic area, the materials of construction should be:

  • Non-additive
  • Non-reactive
  • Non-absorptive
  • Able to withstand repeated sanitation with harsh chemicals

Care should also be taken to prevent accidental spills and possible contaminant release into the area (e.g., point of use or vent filters for an instrument air supply line where instrument air may vent into an ISO 5/Grade A critical zone).

Preventative maintenance and equipment integrity should be established at locations where the process can be impacted (e.g., process heat exchanger integrity, piping integrity, equipment seals between process and process support systems).

6.2.2 製程支援系統

核心概念：支援系統的材質要求

製程支援系統通常依GEP設計即可，但若其使用點位於無菌區域內，材質必須符合四項要求：

  • 不添加（Non-additive）——不會釋出物質到環境中
  • 不反應（Non-reactive）——不與清潔劑或環境發生化學反應
  • 不吸附（Non-absorptive）——不會吸收液體或微生物
  • 耐消毒——能承受反覆的強效化學消毒

重點提示：意外洩漏防護

即使是「非製程」系統，也可能因設計不良而造成污染。典型風險場景：

  • 儀器空氣排放到ISO 5/Grade A區域——必須加裝使用點過濾器
  • 熱交換器洩漏——製程與支援系統之間的密封完整性
  • 管路接頭鬆脫——支援流體進入製程區域

預防性維護（PM）計畫必須涵蓋所有可能影響製程的交界點。

6.2.3 Common System Classifications

Table 6.1 provides general guidance on typical system classifications. A risk-based approach should be used to define the critical aspects of each system to determine the GMP importance and requirements for documentation, commissioning, and sterile boundary conditions.

Note: Poor design of sanitary plumbing drains and process drains or poor procedures can lead to contamination of cleanrooms due to back flow of liquids or vapors that lead to microbial ingress.

6.2.3 常見系統分類解析

核心概念：分類表的實務應用

此表是設施設計的起點，但實際分類必須透過風險評估確定。關鍵觀察：

  • WFI、潔淨蒸汽、製程氣體——永遠是製程系統（P），需要完整確效
  • 純化水——依使用目的而定（最終沖洗用 = P；一般沖洗 = PS）
  • 壓縮空氣——可能是P或PS，取決於是否接觸產品
  • 排水——雖標記為PS，但設計不良會導致潔淨室微生物污染

重點提示：過濾器要求

製程氣體的過濾要求是本表最嚴格的部分：

  • 預過濾：5 μm——控制微粒
  • 使用點過濾：0.2 μm——確保無菌
  • 兩道過濾缺一不可：第一道保護系統，第二道保護產品

CDMO觀點：多重分類的經濟決策

壓縮空氣系統常見的CDMO決策：

  • 多條製造線：可能值得建設獨立的製程級壓縮空氣系統
  • 少數製造用途：使用支援系統 + 使用點過濾器 + 不銹鋼管路更經濟
  • 決策取決於：製造用點數量、產品敏感度、設施規模

6.2.4 Multiple Categorization

The design of systems that can be multi-categorized should be considered with regard to the cost/benefit derived from installing separate utility systems or distribution networks versus special treatment at points of use. Filters, with break tanks or non-return valves, are widespread applications.

For example, an oil-free compressed air system may be used as both a Process and a Process Support system. If there are many manufacturing uses, there may be economical justification for running separate compressed air systems throughout the facility. If there are only a few manufacturing uses, utilizing a Process Support system (with point of use filters and stainless steel piping after the filter at the manufacturing use points) may be the more economical design.

Due consideration should be given to the upstream piping materials to ensure the air quality is not compromised.

6.2.4 多重分類決策

生活比喻：自來水 vs. 淨水器

就像家中的用水：

  • 可以裝設全屋淨水系統（獨立製程級系統）——成本高但管理簡單
  • 或在廚房水龍頭加裝淨水器（使用點過濾）——成本低但需逐點管理

選擇取決於「使用點數量」和「品質要求」。無菌製造也是同樣邏輯。

思考練習：您的設施需要幾套壓縮空氣系統？

假設您的CDMO設施有以下壓縮空氣用途：

  1. 充填線乾燥——製程用途
  2. 滅菌器真空破壞——製程用途
  3. 門驅動氣缸——儀器用途
  4. 控制閥驅動——儀器用途
  5. 產品壓力轉移——製程用途

考量因素：3個製程用途是否足以支持獨立系統？使用點方案的管理負擔如何？

6.3 Specific Service Considerations / 特定服務考量

6.3.1 Purified Water and Water for Injection (WFI)

Water used in the manufacture of sterile pharmaceutical parenteral products should meet USP WFI grade requirements or relevant pharmacopeia standard. Water used for cleaning product contact surfaces should be from a controlled source and meet WFI standards during the final rinse or rinses.

Water used to clean non-product contact surfaces should not increase the background flora within the facility.

For further information, refer to ISPE Baseline Guide: Water and Steam Systems (Second Edition) and ISPE Good Practice Guide: Approaches to Commissioning and Qualification of Pharmaceutical Water and Steam Systems (Second Edition).

6.3.1 純化水與注射用水

核心概念：WFI——最關鍵的公用工程

注射用水（WFI）是無菌製造中最關鍵的公用工程，因為它：

  • 直接用於產品配方
  • 用於清洗產品接觸表面的最終沖洗
  • 必須在使用點保持無菌

水的使用層級：

  • 產品製造 → 必須符合USP WFI標準
  • 產品接觸面清洗 → 最終沖洗必須達WFI標準
  • 非產品接觸面清洗 → 不得增加設施內的背景菌量

重點提示：WFI系統的CDMO挑戰

CDMO面對的WFI挑戰：

  • 需求波動——不同產品的WFI用量差異大
  • 儲存與分配——系統必須維持循環以防止微生物生長
  • 死角管理——每個使用點的死管（dead leg）長度必須最小化
  • 溫度控制——通常維持在80°C以上循環或定期消毒

6.3.2 Pure Steam or Clean Steam

Pure steam (also referred to as clean steam) is predominantly used for sterilization. Pure steam should be free of boiler additives and have no impurities beyond that of the purified water used in production. The condensed steam should meet WFI specifications and clean/pure steam should be made from a controlled source feed.

Design practices (such as sloping lines and minimizing steam traps) should eliminate potential microbial growth in condensate within the system. Process steam for sterilization should contain minimal superheat entering the autoclave.

Non-Condensable Gases (NCG) should be controlled by preheat/pretreatment of feed water or vented from the system, preferably at the steam generator. The values for NCGs, dryness fraction, and superheating of the steam supply should be periodically tested and controlled within specified limits where the steam is used for the direct sterilization of product contact equipment and components.

6.3.2 潔淨蒸汽

核心概念：潔淨蒸汽的品質要求

潔淨蒸汽（Clean Steam）主要用於SIP（就地滅菌），其品質要求：

  • 不含鍋爐添加劑
  • 冷凝水必須符合WFI規格
  • 來源水必須受控
  • 進入滅菌器時應含最少的過熱度（superheat）

重點提示：三大品質參數

潔淨蒸汽用於直接滅菌產品接觸設備時，必須定期測試並控制：

  1. 非凝結氣體（NCG）——形成氣袋阻礙蒸汽穿透
  2. 乾燥度（Dryness Fraction）——水分過多降低滅菌效率
  3. 過熱度（Superheat）——過熱蒸汽無法有效傳遞潛熱

NCG可透過進水預處理或在蒸汽產生器處排放來控制。

生活比喻：蒸汽就像「熱的清潔劑」

想像用蒸汽清潔衣物：

  • 蒸汽必須是純淨的（不能含有化學添加物）
  • 必須是濕熱的（乾蒸汽殺菌效果差）
  • 必須能均勻穿透（不能有氣泡阻擋）

NCG就像衣服裡的氣泡——蒸汽到不了被氣泡隔開的地方，那裡就無法被滅菌。

6.3.3 Nitrogen and Other Process Gases

If process gas is to be used in an aseptic or sterile process, it should be sterile filtered at the point of use. The filter and downstream components need sterilization or sanitization, as well as in situ or off-line integrity testing on a regular basis. If the service is not used in an aseptic process, but is a Process Support utility, standard materials of construction may be used.

Process gas system design considerations:

  • Process gas quality should meet product requirements.
  • Filtration may be used for several reasons: particulate control, environmental protection, or microbial control. For pre-filtration, 5 μm or better is recommended. For aseptic or sterile applications, 0.2 μm filtration is required at point of use.
  • One 0.2 μm filter can be used at the system boundary for particulate control, and a second 0.2 μm filter at the process system boundary for microbial control.
  • The gas distribution system design should include sampling points. Sterile filtered points of use should also permit downstream aseptic sampling for physical and biological quality.
  • Back flow from other systems into process gas systems should be prevented.

6.3.3 氮氣與製程氣體

核心概念：雙重過濾策略

製程氣體的過濾採用兩道防線：

  • 第一道 0.2 μm 過濾器——設於系統邊界，用於微粒控制與取樣
  • 第二道 0.2 μm 過濾器——設於製程系統邊界（使用點），用於微生物控制

過濾器及其下游元件必須：

  • 定期滅菌或消毒
  • 定期進行完整性測試（就地或離線）

重點提示：防止逆流（Backflow Prevention）

必須防止其他系統的物質逆流進入製程氣體系統。實務做法：

  • 安裝逆止閥（non-return valves）
  • 維持正壓差
  • 使用斷流槽（break tanks）

在CDMO中，多產品共用氣體系統時，逆流防護尤為重要——避免產品交叉污染。

實務檢查清單：製程氣體系統

  • 使用點是否配置0.2 μm無菌過濾器？
  • 過濾器完整性測試頻率是否已定義？
  • 是否設有下游無菌取樣點？
  • 是否安裝逆流防止裝置？
  • 預過濾（5 μm）是否就位？
  • 氣體品質規格是否符合產品要求？

6.3.4 Compressed Air

Process Compressed Air

Compressed air (such as used for drying or transferring product, for vacuum break, or for inlets into sterilizers) should be treated as a process gas.

For determination of compressed air attributes, refer to ISO 8573-1, ICH Q8, ICH Q9, and site-specific guidelines. The site location of the system should support maintaining these attributes. Air intake should not be located near traffic, shipping/receiving lanes, or emission-producing equipment. Hydrocarbon contamination should be prevented and monitored.

Instrument Air

Properly designed and maintained systems should prevent instrument air from coming into contact with product; therefore, these systems may be designed in accordance with GEP. Instrument air should be vented away from ISO 5/Grade A areas, to preserve low particulate and microbial levels.

Breathing Air

Breathing air is a Process Support system important to operator safety. It should be labeled and easily identifiable. Maximum contaminant levels per OSHA and CSA standards:

6.3.4 壓縮空氣系統

重點提示：空氣進氣口位置

壓縮空氣品質始於進氣口。必須遠離：

  • 交通區域（車輛廢氣）
  • 裝卸貨區（粉塵）
  • 其他排放設備（化學物質）

碳氫化合物污染必須被預防和監測。在設施選址時，進氣口位置是關鍵的設計決策。

生活比喻：三種空氣如同三種水

  • 製程壓縮空氣好比瓶裝礦泉水——直接接觸「食物」，品質最高
  • 儀器空氣好比洗手用水——不入口，但品質仍需控管
  • 呼吸空氣好比空調過濾——保護人員安全

核心概念：壓縮空氣的三種用途

壓縮空氣在無菌設施中有三種截然不同的用途，分類也不同：

6.3.5 Vents

Nitrogen, compressed air, instrument air, and other gases are vented at several locations during operation (e.g., pneumatically operated parts on filling lines). In the case where these gases are vented during an aseptic process, vents should be released to a non-critical area outside of the equipment. A risk assessment should be performed to assess venting locations.

6.3.5 排氣設計

重點提示：排氣位置的風險評估

氣動元件（如充填線的氣動閥門）在運作中會排出氣體。若此排氣發生在無菌製程中：

  • 排氣口必須導向非關鍵區域，遠離設備內部
  • 必須進行風險評估以確認排氣位置是否適當
  • 避免排氣直接進入ISO 5/Grade A區域

許多充填線的偏差事件可追溯至排氣位置不當，導致微粒或微生物進入關鍵區域。

6.3.6 Heating and Cooling Systems

Heating and cooling systems (including cooling and chilled water, glycol systems, and heat transfer fluid systems) should not contact the product. It is usually a Process Support utility, but can directly affect the product.

Equipment used for indirect heat transfer should not leak into the atmosphere or the product. Selection of the heat transfer medium should consider the potential risk of leakage. Provisions should be made to monitor such system leakage through pressure testing and level monitoring.

Designers should consider that a heat transfer fluid that would leak from a tank jacket into a batch of formulated product would contaminate the batch, regardless of the properties of the fluid, so jacket integrity should be assured.

For temperature-sensitive products, the temperature of the heating/cooling medium may be a critical parameter if it is not possible to monitor the product temperature at the heat transfer surface.

6.3.6 加熱與冷卻系統

核心概念：間接接觸的風險

加熱/冷卻系統雖然不應接觸產品，但它們可能：

  • 控制去熱原隧道的空氣溫度
  • 控制製程槽內的產品溫度
  • 因夾套洩漏直接污染整批產品

因此必須建立洩漏監控機制：壓力測試與液位監控。

重點提示：夾套完整性

ISPE明確指出：無論熱傳介質的性質如何，從夾套洩漏到配方產品中都會污染整批。這意味著：

  • 即使使用「食品級」熱傳介質，洩漏仍是批次報廢的原因
  • 夾套完整性測試是預防性維護的關鍵項目
  • 管路位置應避免架設於無菌加工區域上方

6.3.7 Facility Steam and Hot Water Systems

Facility steam and hot water systems should not be used in applications where there is exposure to the product. These systems should be designed using GEP.

Care should be taken in the selection of boiler additives, especially when facility steam is used for HVAC humidification. The location of condensate and pressure controlling systems should be in facility areas, not within cleanrooms. These devices should not be located above aseptic areas, in case of leakage.

6.3.8 Process Vacuum Systems

If a single vacuum source is used for a mixture of process uses, the contamination risk increases. Steps should be taken to prevent pressure reversals or reverse flow (e.g., non-return valves or fail-safe vacuum pump/pressure arrangements) and to prevent material dropping from the system into the process.

Sanitization or sterilization is recommended for points of use upstream (nearer to the process) of the local vacuum isolation valve. Appropriate steps should be designed to prevent possible cross-contamination.

6.3.9 Potable Water

Potable water should be designed with GEP. Proper labeling and identification of these services is required. Potable water should not be used in the aseptic processing area. The chemical and microbiological profiles should exceed drinking water standards. A risk assessment should determine if the local drinking water quality increases risk of chemical and microbial contamination events.

6.3.7–6.3.9 設施蒸汽、真空與飲用水

核心概念：位置配置原則

設施蒸汽與冷凝水系統的配置有一個關鍵原則：

  • 冷凝水排放與壓力控制裝置 → 放在機械區，不在潔淨室內
  • 這些裝置不應位於無菌區域上方——防止洩漏風險
  • 鍋爐添加劑若用於HVAC加濕，須謹慎選擇（避免引入化學污染物）

重點提示：真空系統的交叉污染風險

共用真空源的風險最容易被忽略：

  • 壓力反轉——真空泵停機時可能產生逆流
  • 物料倒流——其他製程的物料可能經真空系統進入
  • 防護措施：逆止閥、故障安全真空泵配置、使用點上游滅菌

在CDMO中，多產品共用真空系統是常見配置，必須有嚴格的交叉污染防護設計。

CDMO觀點：飲用水的標示管理

飲用水系統看似簡單，但在製藥設施中有兩個常見問題：

  • 標示混淆——操作人員可能誤用飲用水進行製程清洗
  • 水質風險——當地自來水品質可能引入化學或微生物風險

正確的管路標示與識別是最基本但最容易被忽略的GEP要求。

6.3.10 Mechanical Seal Fluids

If a pump is used for product transfer, the seal fluid should be of the same quality standards as the product. Double mechanical seals or equivalent are preferred. Typically for aseptic facilities, sterile alcohol, USP purified water, or WFI is used as a seal fluid.

If the pump is not for product transfer (i.e., for a Process Support service), then vendor recommended fluids should be considered.

6.3.11 Drains

There are several types of drains that can be located within process space. The US FDA suggests that drains should not occur within ISO 5/Grade A, ISO 6, or ISO 7/Grade B spaces, but allows exceptions.

Drains within the process spaces should be minimized. Drains within a classified process space should be sealed and capped. Where possible, drains should be located within mechanical spaces instead of within process spaces.

Waste transfer lines should be sloped to gravity flow and should not vent gases into the process space. Cleanouts should be located within mechanical space. Drain points should be designed to prevent capillary action and should be free flowing.

For products produced for use in the EU, Annex 1 requires that any drain connected to a sterile area should have an air gap. For locations where splash or condensate would cause contamination concerns, the drain should be enclosed while maintaining the air gap.

Where drains are placed within maintenance space (usually uncontrolled, non-ventilated), the need for point ventilation or enhanced biological control should be evaluated.

6.3.10–6.3.11 機械密封液與排水系統

核心概念：機械密封液——產品級品質

用於產品轉移的泵浦，其密封液品質標準必須與產品相同：

  • 首選雙機械密封（double mechanical seals）
  • 密封液通常使用：無菌酒精、USP純化水或WFI
  • 非產品用泵浦可使用供應商推薦的密封液

原因：密封液一旦洩漏就會直接接觸產品——這是最後一道防線。

重點提示：排水系統——被低估的污染源

排水系統是潔淨室微生物污染最容易被忽略的來源：

  • FDA建議：ISO 5/Grade A、ISO 6、ISO 7/Grade B區域不應有排水口
  • 必須存在時：排水口應密封加蓋
  • EU Annex 1要求：連接無菌區域的排水必須設有空氣斷流（air gap）
  • 廢液管線必須有坡度、重力流動，不得向製程空間排放氣體

思考練習：排水系統設計審查

在設計審查中，您注意到以下排水配置。哪些需要改善？

  1. ISO 7/Grade B走廊有一個未加蓋的排水口
  2. 隔離器內有一個排水連接，帶空氣斷流
  3. 機械空間的清潔排水口直接排入無菌區域下方的管道
  4. 充填室有一個密封加蓋的地排，每週維護一次

提示：考慮FDA建議、Annex 1要求、以及微生物逆流風險。

Section Summary / 章節總結

Key Takeaways

  1. Dual classification system: Every utility must be classified as Process (P) or Process Support (PS) based on risk assessment, which determines design, qualification, and documentation requirements.
  2. WFI is the most critical utility in sterile manufacturing — it must meet pharmacopeial standards and be sterile at the point of use.
  3. Clean steam quality is defined by three parameters: NCG content, dryness fraction, and superheat — all must be periodically tested.
  4. Process gases require dual filtration: 5 μm pre-filtration plus 0.2 μm sterilizing-grade filtration at the point of use.
  5. System boundaries must be clearly defined to delineate qualification scope from GEP-only scope.
  6. Backflow prevention is essential across all shared utility systems — especially vacuum and compressed gas systems.
  7. Drains are underestimated contamination sources: minimize in classified areas, seal and cap when present, maintain air gaps per Annex 1.
  8. Location matters: condensate systems, pressure devices, and heat transfer piping should not be above aseptic areas.

章節重點回顧

一句話總結

公用工程系統的設計核心是「分類決定標準，風險決定範圍」——透過風險評估將系統分為製程級（P）與支援級（PS），再據此決定設計、確效與文件化的嚴格程度。

CDMO應用重點

  • 產能規劃：多產品製造需考慮WFI、潔淨蒸汽、製程氣體的尖峰需求
  • 交叉污染防護：共用真空與壓縮氣體系統的逆流防護設計
  • 經濟決策：獨立系統 vs. 使用點處理——依據製造線數量決定
  • 單次使用策略：降低公用工程交叉污染風險的有效方法
  • 變更管理：新產品導入可能改變公用工程的分類——必須重新評估

自我檢測：您能回答這些問題嗎？

  1. WFI與純化水在系統分類上的差異是什麼？
  2. 潔淨蒸汽的三大品質參數分別是什麼？
  3. 製程氣體為何需要兩道0.2 μm過濾器？
  4. 為什麼排水口不應出現在ISO 5/Grade A區域？
  5. CDMO在公用工程設計上面對的獨特挑戰是什麼？
6

Chapter 6: 7–8. Electrical & Controls

電氣與儀控 | p151-p166

ISPE Baseline Guide Vol. 3 (3rd Ed.) | p151 – p156

Learning Objectives / 本章學習目標

  • Understand the GMP requirements for electrical equipment in cleanroom environments of different classifications (ISO 5 through ISO 8) / 了解不同潔淨室等級（ISO 5 至 ISO 8）中電氣設備的 GMP 要求
  • Recognize the importance of UPS (Uninterruptible Power Supply) and emergency power for critical control systems / 認識不斷電系統（UPS）與緊急電力對關鍵控制系統的重要性
  • Learn the design principles for cleanroom lighting: flush-mount fixtures, non-shedding materials, and airflow compatibility / 學習潔淨室照明設計原則：嵌入式燈具、不脫落材質、與氣流的相容性
  • Understand door interlock systems for airlocks and their role in maintaining pressure cascades / 了解氣閘門連鎖系統及其在維持壓差級聯中的角色
  • Grasp wiring principles: minimizing wall penetrations, sealing conduits, and preventing contamination pathways / 掌握配線原則：最小化穿牆孔、密封管線、防止污染路徑
  • Know when and why hazardous (ATEX) electrical classifications apply in sterile facilities / 了解在無菌設施中何時及為何需要防爆電氣分類
7.1 Introduction 7.1 簡介

Original Text

This chapter focuses on electrical services that may have GMP implications. It outlines the critical characteristics of systems appropriate to the manufacturing environment.

導師解析

核心概念

電氣服務的 GMP 角色：在無菌製造設施中，電氣系統通常不直接影響產品品質或患者安全。然而，電氣設備的設計與安裝方式會影響潔淨室的可清潔性、密封完整性以及壓差維持能力。

本章的核心問題是：電氣設備如何在不破壞潔淨室完整性的前提下提供必要功能？

比喻說明

手術室的電源插座：想像醫院的手術室 — 你不能隨意在牆上打洞來拉電線，每個插座和開關都必須嵌入式安裝、可清潔消毒、不能有任何藏污納垢的縫隙。潔淨室的電氣設計邏輯完全相同：功能要有，但不能犧牲環境品質。

7.2 General Requirements 7.2 一般要求

Original Text

When designing, selecting, and installing electrical equipment within aseptic processing areas, GMP considerations are limited to ensuring that equipment is cleanable, ledge and crevice free, non-shedding, sealed, and compatible with sanitization agents.

The selection and installation of all electrical equipment and wiring should, at a minimum, be in accordance with applicable local codes. All electrical components and materials should be compatible with the manufacturing process and operations.

Although the criteria for equipment appear to be identical from ISO 5/Grade A to ISO 8/Grade C environments, the degree of these aspects may differ (e.g., equipment in ISO 5/Grade A environments will require a higher standard). Recessed electrical devices may help achieve the standard required in each of these areas.

Sealed components are specified, not only to alleviate the risk of contamination, but also to cope with the different pressure regimes of adjacent rooms. In ISO 5/Grade A environments, the term “sealed” refers to being hermetically sealed, whereas in ISO 8/Grade C environments, the term “sealed” refers to a high degree of protection against the ingress of water and dust.

Electrical equipment within ISO 5/Grade A environments should be kept to an absolute minimum. Any services that can achieve their function by being located in an adjacent room or area should be so located. For example, a light switch for the room could be located outside the access door in the corridor.

Regarding the manufacturing process, electrical services normally do not affect patient safety and product quality; however, for business continuity and ensuring uninterrupted product supply, these systems should be designed in accordance with GEP (Good Engineering Practice).

"Electrical equipment within ISO 5/Grade A environments should be kept to an absolute minimum. Any services that can achieve their function by being located in an adjacent room or area should be so located."

Table 7.1: Typical GMP Requirements for Electrical Systems

導師解析

核心概念：電氣設備的 GMP 五大要求

所有安裝在無菌區域的電氣設備必須滿足五個基本要求：

  • 可清潔（Cleanable） — 表面平滑，可使用標準清潔劑擦拭
  • 無凸緣與縫隙（Ledge & Crevice Free） — 不能有微生物或微粒積聚的死角
  • 不脫落（Non-shedding） — 材質不會釋放微粒到環境中
  • 密封（Sealed） — 防止空氣洩漏影響壓差，並阻止外部污染進入
  • 與消毒劑相容（Compatible with Sanitization Agents） — 能承受 VHP、過氧化氫、酒精等消毒劑

重點提示：「密封」的不同等級

原文特別區分了不同等級的「密封」含義：

  • ISO 5/Grade A — 氣密封（Hermetically Sealed）：完全不透氣，確保單向氣流不受干擾
  • ISO 8/Grade C — 高度防護（High Protection against Ingress）：防水防塵，相當於 IP65 等級以上

這個區別在實務上非常重要 — ISO 5 區域內的每個電氣元件都必須視為潔淨室外殼的一部分。

比喻說明

潛水艇 vs 雨衣：ISO 5 的電氣密封要求就像潛水艇 — 絕對氣密，任何微小的洩漏都不能接受。ISO 8 的密封要求則像一件好的雨衣 — 能擋住水和灰塵，但不需要像潛水艇一樣承受壓力差。

重點提示：最小化原則

ISO 5 區域的「減法思維」：在最高等級的潔淨室中，設計原則不是「如何安裝電氣設備」，而是「如何避免安裝電氣設備」。能放在外面的就放在外面 — 燈的開關放走廊、配電盤放機房、感測器盡可能遠端安裝。

這是 GMP 電氣設計中最常被忽略的原則。許多工程師習慣在需要的地方安裝設備，而不是先問「能不能把這個東西搬到外面去？」

實務應用

GEP 原則：電氣系統雖然不直接影響產品品質，但影響業務連續性。根據 GEP（Good Engineering Practice），設計時需考慮：冗餘供電、緊急發電機、UPS 保護等。停電造成的生產批次損失可能高達數百萬元。

7.3 Control System Power 7.3 控制系統電源

Original Text

The prevalence of digital controls in HVAC and process equipment requires strong consideration of reliable and continuous power to the control units. Considerations should be made with regard to:

  • How multiple power sources affect equipment (e.g., equipment may have multiple power sources, such as line voltage motors, or the control system may operate on Uninterruptible Power Supply (UPS) while the fan motor operates on three phase line voltage)
  • Providing for orderly shutdown or planned restarts on loss of main equipment power
  • Programming of the systems to prevent tripping of main breakers on simultaneous restart of all equipment
  • Power needs for associated instruments

導師解析

核心概念：控制系統電力

UPS（不斷電系統）：現代無菌設施大量依賴數位控制系統（BMS、SCADA、PLC）。這些控制器對電力中斷極為敏感 — 即使短暫的電力閃斷也可能導致：

  • 控制程式遺失或重置
  • HVAC 系統失去控制，房間壓差崩潰
  • 製程參數記錄中斷，造成 GMP 數據完整性問題

因此，關鍵控制系統必須由 UPS 供電，確保斷電時仍能執行有序關機（Orderly Shutdown）或維持監控。

比喻說明

電腦突然關機 vs 正常關機：想像你正在電腦上做一份重要的報告，突然停電 — 所有未存檔的工作全部遺失。UPS 就是給你的電腦裝一個大電池，讓你在停電後有足夠時間儲存檔案並正常關機。在無菌設施中，這個「未存檔的工作」可能是一個價值百萬的生產批次。

重點提示：同時重啟的風險

跳閘保護（Breaker Trip Prevention）：停電恢復後，如果所有設備同時啟動，瞬間湧入電流（Inrush Current）可能超過主斷路器容量，導致再次跳閘。系統必須程式化為依序啟動（Staggered Restart），避免這種「二次災難」。

這在 CDMO 工廠尤其重要 — 多條生產線的 HVAC、冷水機組、充填設備同時啟動的衝擊電流可能是正常運行的 5-8 倍。

7.4 Power Distribution 7.4 配電

Original Text

Both reliability and stability of the power supply are important.

The impact of surges, dips, or total power loss on the overall manufacturing process, HVAC/mechanical services, or individual equipment items, should be studied to determine risk and effects. Generally, the impact is economic (loss of production capacity). If these impacts are considerable, then a standby generator or UPS should be considered.

For HVAC systems, momentary power losses may be significant; impact could be mediated if there are provisions for fan rotation to continue and room pressures are maintained within acceptance criteria for short periods. The impact of any power loss potentially affecting the sterility of the product should be evaluated.

Power for monitoring of DP (differential pressure) is a critical issue, as loss of differential or the ability to monitor differential pressure during outages may result in significant product quality impact.

Consideration for UPS or emergency generators can be considered for critical processes, equipment, and systems that may provide, maintain, or record critical parameters as part of GMP operations.

Power quality is equally important as precision equipment has a narrow bandwidth to operate within. Special consideration should be given to:

  • Power factor correction
  • Phase balance
  • Harmonics from digital equipment

導師解析

核心概念：配電系統的雙重要求

配電系統必須同時滿足兩個面向：

  • 可靠性（Reliability） — 電力不中斷，保證生產連續性
  • 穩定性（Stability） — 電壓、頻率穩定，不出現突波或驟降

壓差監控（DP Monitoring）的特殊地位：原文特別強調差壓監控的電力供應是「關鍵議題」。因為潔淨室的壓差級聯是防止交叉污染的核心屏障 — 如果停電後既失去壓差、又無法監控壓差，就無法證明產品在停電期間未受污染。

重點提示：HVAC 風扇慣性

風扇旋轉續行（Fan Rotation Continue）：短暫停電後，HVAC 風扇的慣性可以讓氣流繼續運行數秒。如果設計得當，這段時間足以維持房間壓差在可接受範圍內。這就是為什麼原文說「impact could be mediated」— 不是所有短暫停電都會導致壓差崩潰。

但這需要經過風險評估來確認：停電多長時間壓差仍可接受？這通常是確效（Qualification）過程中需要測試的項目。

練習思考

  1. If differential pressure monitoring loses power during a production batch, what investigation steps would you initiate? How would you determine if the batch is still acceptable?
  2. Your facility experiences a 3-second power dip. HVAC fans coast for 5 seconds. Is this sufficient to maintain cleanroom integrity? What data would you need to make this determination?
7.5 Lighting 7.5 照明

Original Text

There should be good uniform lighting levels in all manufacturing areas. Minimum levels in the personnel work areas should be no less than 500 lux, one meter from the floor.

Light fixtures in manufacturing areas should:

  • Be designed and selected to be cleanable, non-shedding, ledge free, or sealed, as appropriate for the different classifications of areas
  • Be arranged to prevent accumulation of dust, and be air tight and sealed to ensure no foreign matter is released into the manufacturing environment
  • Be located so they are not directly above the work area when the manufacturing process is open to the room
  • Have sealing properties which can withstand water jet pressure in wash down areas
  • Be constructed of materials that are compatible with room cleaning agents, which may be corrosive (stainless steel or aluminum fixtures may be considered appropriate because they are non-shedding and resistive to corrosive environments)

In ISO 5/Grade A environments, recess mounted or teardrop fixtures may be appropriate. The installation of surface mounted lighting in unidirectional ISO 5/Grade A airflow zones may interfere with airflow patterns and should be avoided.

In ISO 7/Grade B environments, recess mounted fixtures are beneficial because they can be installed through the ceiling, with maintenance access provided from a walkable ceiling or floor (facility room) above.

Lamps or fixtures, maintained from within the room, may be changed on an annual basis to reduce the effects of unplanned disturbances to production due to occasional lamp failures. Considerations for lighting include:

  • Redundant lighting units
  • Upgraded light types (e.g., T-5 fluorescent or Light Emitting Diode (LED)) which allow for longer life and reduced maintenance intervention
  • Adjustable lighting (adjusted in lux output) for night time operation, as increased light levels have demonstrated to improve night time work performance — if increasing light output, consideration for product impact (photo stability) should be evaluated

If color rendition and intensity of lighting equipment used for inspection, cleaning, etc., is considered critical, appropriate provisions should be made.

Emergency lighting should be provided in accordance with applicable local codes. Combining emergency fixtures with normal fixtures helps to limit the amount of electrical equipment on ceilings or walls.

Since priority needs to be given to the HVAC systems (e.g., air supply diffusers) and services to process equipment, lighting fixtures cannot always be positioned to achieve ideal lighting distribution. Therefore, careful coordination of ceiling services should be considered at the design stage.

導師解析

核心概念：潔淨室照明設計原則

潔淨室照明設計必須平衡三個目標：

  • 足夠亮度 — 最低 500 lux（工作區域），確保人員操作安全與準確
  • 不破壞潔淨度 — 燈具本身不能成為微粒或微生物的污染源
  • 不干擾氣流 — 特別在 ISO 5 單向氣流區域，表面安裝燈具會擾亂層流

核心概念：嵌入式 vs 表面式燈具

嵌入式燈具（Recess Mounted / Flush-Mount Fixture）：

  • 燈具嵌入天花板，表面與天花板齊平
  • 不產生凸出面，不干擾氣流
  • 維護可從天花板上方的技術夾層進行，不進入潔淨室
  • ISO 5 和 ISO 7 區域的首選方案

淚滴式燈具（Teardrop Fixture）：

  • 流線型設計，減少對氣流的干擾
  • 適用於 ISO 5 區域中無法嵌入安裝的位置

比喻說明

天花板是寸土寸金的「不動產」：潔淨室的天花板空間就像市中心的房地產 — HVAC 出風口、回風口、HEPA 過濾器、製程設備接口、燈具、消防噴頭全部都要搶這塊空間。原文提醒我們，HVAC 優先權最高，照明只能「見縫插針」。因此，設計階段就必須做好天花板服務的協調規劃。

重點提示：光穩定性考量

Photo Stability（光穩定性）：增加照明亮度以改善夜班工作表現是好主意，但必須評估光線對產品的影響。某些藥品（特別是生物製劑和某些小分子藥物）對光敏感，過強的照明可能導致降解。

這是一個典型的 GMP 交叉考量：改善一個面向（人員效能）時，不能忽略另一個面向（產品品質）。

重點提示：預防性維護策略

年度定期更換（Annual Replacement）：原文建議燈具可以每年定期更換，而不是等到故障再換。這是因為在潔淨室內更換燈具需要：

  • 停機或暫停生產
  • 可能需要維修人員更衣進入潔淨室
  • 更換後需要清潔和環境恢復

計劃性維護比非計劃性維護的干擾小得多。使用 LED 燈具可以將更換週期延長到數年，大幅減少維護介入次數。

練習思考

  1. Why must surface-mounted lighting be avoided in ISO 5 unidirectional airflow zones? Describe the specific mechanism by which a protruding fixture disrupts laminar flow.
  2. Your facility has a product that is light-sensitive (ICH Q1B photostability testing required). How would you design the lighting in the filling room to balance operator visibility with product protection?
7.6 Hazardous Environments 7.6 危險環境

Original Text

The selection and installation of electrical equipment within hazardous environments (due to dust or solvent vapor) should comply with applicable local codes. Classification of an area to require explosion proof electrical equipment is likely to be very rare, because of the high air change requirement and monitoring of the area; however, design should also take into consideration loss of HVAC fan rotation and reduction of room air changes (e.g., failure mode operations with regards to volatiles).

Hazardous area classification is not a GMP issue, but the class of room may affect the location of production equipment and it also may affect the selection of the electrical equipment. Some electrical equipment may suit a higher class of area in terms of cleanliness.

Electrical equipment within these areas should be kept to an absolute minimum. Any devices that can achieve their function while located in an adjacent room should be located externally and do not need to be classified.

Provisions should be made in these areas to dissipate possible static build-up on personnel, equipment, and materials. Conductive floors should be installed, if necessary.

導師解析

核心概念：防爆環境

ATEX（防爆分類）：當潔淨室中使用含溶劑的製程（如某些注射劑的配液步驟使用乙醇），或處理可燃粉塵時，該區域可能需要進行防爆分類。

但原文指出，在無菌設施中這種情況非常罕見，原因是：

  • 潔淨室的高換氣次數（每小時 20-60 次以上）快速稀釋可燃蒸氣
  • 環境監控系統持續偵測異常

然而，設計時必須考慮「如果 HVAC 風扇停止旋轉會怎樣？」— 這就是失效模式分析（Failure Mode Analysis）的範疇。

比喻說明

瓦斯爐 vs 通風廚房：在通風良好的廚房使用瓦斯爐，瓦斯洩漏的風險很低，因為空氣流通會稀釋任何洩漏。但如果抽油煙機壞了（相當於 HVAC 故障），瓦斯就可能累積到危險濃度。潔淨室的高換氣次數就是那台「超級抽油煙機」— 但你仍然需要考慮它故障時的情境。

重點提示：靜電防護

靜電累積（Static Build-up）在使用可燃溶劑或處理粉體的區域是嚴重的安全隱患。原文要求：

  • 安裝導電地板（Conductive Floors），將靜電導入地面
  • 為人員、設備、物料提供靜電消散措施

在 CDMO 環境中，如果承接含有有機溶劑的注射劑代工專案，這些防爆要求就必須納入設施設計。

7.7 Wiring 7.7 配線

Original Text

If possible, wiring and wiring accessories should be hidden within the building fabric to improve cleanliness, particularly in higher classification areas. Recessed boxes also would be appropriate in these instances. The number of penetrations through walls, ceilings, or floors for services to equipment should be minimized.

Where wiring is installed on the surface, installation should minimize the accumulation of foreign matter and allow easy and effective cleaning.

Enclosing wiring in fully sealed conduit or trunking may improve the level of cleanliness and prevent air leakage from a classified room. Trunking, which is not sealed, may appear clean but act as a reservoir for contaminants. Sealing of conduits and trunking may be necessary to reduce the risk of contamination from outside and loss of air from pressurized rooms.

Lengths of wiring to mobile equipment should be kept to a minimum and should be kept off the floor.

Where necessary, as part of the process operations, wiring and glands should withstand washing.

導師解析

核心概念：配線穿牆管理

穿牆（Wiring Penetration）是潔淨室完整性的重大威脅。每一個穿過牆壁、天花板或地板的電線通道都是潛在的：

  • 空氣洩漏點 — 破壞房間壓差
  • 污染通道 — 外部微粒或微生物可能沿著管線進入
  • 清潔死角 — 穿牆處難以徹底清潔

因此，原文強調必須最小化穿牆數量，且所有穿牆處必須密封。

重點提示：看不見的污染庫

未密封線槽的隱藏風險：原文提出一個深刻的觀察 — 未密封的線槽（Trunking）表面看起來可能很乾淨，但內部實際上是污染物的儲存庫（Reservoir for Contaminants）。灰塵、微粒甚至微生物可以在線槽內部累積，然後隨著氣流緩慢釋放到潔淨室中。

這就是為什麼 ISPE 指南要求線槽必須完全密封 — 不只是「看起來密封」，而是真正能阻止空氣和微粒流通。

比喻說明

水管漏水的比喻：想像你家的牆壁裡有一根生鏽的水管 — 表面看起來牆壁完好無損，但水管內部一直在漏水，慢慢侵蝕牆體。未密封的電線管道就是潔淨室裡的「隱形漏水管」— 外表完好，但持續讓不受控的空氣（和污染物）進出潔淨室。

實務應用

CDMO 配線最佳實務：

  • 在設計階段就規劃所有穿牆位置，預留適當的管線通道
  • 使用合格的穿牆密封系統（如 Roxtec 或同等品），每個穿牆點都要有壓力測試記錄
  • 移動設備的電纜使用天花板垂吊或捲線器，避免拖地造成清潔困難
  • 所有密封點納入定期檢查計畫，確保長期維持完整性
7.8 Door Interlocks 7.8 門互鎖

Original Text

Electrical interlocks for the doors of airlocks or changing rooms assist in maintaining pressure regimes and GMP practices. Alternatively, an audible local alarm could be generated to indicate if more than one airlock door is open at the same time. If interlocks are provided, override features should be included in case of emergency.

Additionally, provisions should include electronic access control for rooms that require restricted access for aseptic operations (e.g., ISO 5/Grade A). It is recommended that door interlocks are verified as part of facility commissioning/qualification per GEP.

導師解析

核心概念：門連鎖系統

門連鎖 / 互鎖（Door Interlock）：確保氣閘（Airlock）的兩扇門不會同時打開的電氣控制機制。這是維持潔淨室壓差級聯的關鍵防線。

運作原理：

  • 當一扇門打開時，另一扇門被電氣鎖定，無法開啟
  • 只有當第一扇門完全關閉後，第二扇門才能解鎖
  • 如果兩扇門同時打開（故障情況），系統觸發警報

比喻說明

銀行金庫的雙門設計：就像銀行金庫的入口 — 你必須先進入第一扇門，等它關閉後，第二扇門才會打開。這確保金庫不會直接暴露在外界環境中。潔淨室的氣閘互鎖設計邏輯完全相同 — 防止高潔淨度區域直接暴露在低潔淨度區域的空氣中。

重點提示：緊急覆寫功能

Override（覆寫 / 強制開啟）：原文特別強調，門互鎖系統必須包含緊急覆寫功能。這是人命安全（Life Safety）的基本要求 — 在火災、化學洩漏或其他緊急情況下，人員必須能夠快速撤離，不能被互鎖系統困住。

這是一個典型的 GMP vs 安全 的權衡：正常情況下互鎖保護產品品質，緊急情況下人命安全優先。

重點提示：電子門禁

電子門禁控制（Electronic Access Control）在 ISO 5 無菌操作區域是必要的。目的是：

  • 限制只有經過培訓和更衣認證的人員才能進入
  • 記錄進出人員和時間，提供可追溯性
  • 防止未授權人員進入可能污染無菌環境

門互鎖系統應在設施試車 / 確效（Commissioning / Qualification）階段進行驗證，確認其功能符合設計要求。

練習思考

  1. During a routine production run, an operator reports that both airlock doors opened simultaneously due to an interlock malfunction. What immediate actions do you take? How do you assess the impact on the in-process batch?
  2. Should the emergency override of door interlocks trigger an alarm and a log entry in the BMS? Why or why not?
7.9 Outlets and Miscellaneous Equipment 7.9 插座與其他設備

Original Text

Electrical components should be designed and selected to be:

  • Cleanable
  • Non-shedding
  • Ledge and crevice-free, or sealed
  • Appropriate to the classification (HVAC grade) of area

Fittings in process areas should be arranged to prevent accumulation of dust and be air tight and sealed, to ensure no foreign matter is released into the manufacturing environment. Recess mounting of fittings in these areas provides distinct benefits.

Aspirated fire detection, or systems able to detect fire within the HVAC extract systems for ISO 5/Grade A environments, may avoid installing conventional fire/smoke detection equipment within the room. Flashing lights, in place of conventional sounders, also may be beneficial. Additionally, source specific cleanroom appropriate sprinkler heads may be used for fire suppression systems.

Sealing membranes on loudspeaker systems located within ISO 5/Grade A and ISO 7/Grade B environments should be considered. A membrane in the wall between two adjoining rooms may provide acceptable voice communication between those rooms. Consideration for use of appropriate cleanable/sealed wireless communication should be given.

Insect light traps should be placed strategically outside of cleanroom areas to reduce contamination risks from flying insects.

Since sinks and drains are not permitted in aseptic processing areas (ISO 5/Grade A and ISO 7/Grade B), an electronically heated (bio-control) trap beneath sinks in ISO 8/Grade C environments could serve as an alternative to routine chemical sanitization.

導師解析

核心概念：雜項設備的 GMP 設計

潔淨室內除了照明和配電之外，還有許多「雜項」電氣設備需要符合 GMP 要求。原文列舉了幾個重要類別：

  • 消防偵測 — 吸入式偵煙（Aspirated Fire Detection）可以避免在潔淨室內安裝傳統煙霧偵測器
  • 通訊系統 — 喇叭需要加裝密封膜，或改用無線通訊
  • 蟲害防治 — 捕蟲燈（Insect Light Traps）放在潔淨室外圍
  • 排水控制 — ISO 8 區域水槽下方使用電加熱生物控制陷阱

重點提示：吸入式偵煙系統

Aspirated Fire Detection（吸入式偵煙）：這是一種將空氣從被監控區域持續吸入到遠端偵測器的系統。它的優點在於：

  • 潔淨室內無設備 — 偵測器主體安裝在技術區域，只有小型取樣管在潔淨室內
  • 高靈敏度 — 可以在極早期偵測到煙霧
  • 避免誤報 — 傳統煙霧偵測器可能被 VHP 消毒的霧氣觸發

在 ISO 5 區域，這幾乎是唯一可行的偵煙方案。

重點提示：無菌區禁止排水

ISO 5 和 ISO 7 區域不允許有水槽和排水口 — 這是 GMP 的基本原則。排水系統是微生物生長的溫床，直接威脅無菌環境。

但在 ISO 8/Grade C 區域，水槽是必要的（如手部清潔）。原文建議在水槽下方使用電加熱生物控制陷阱（Bio-control Trap） — 通過加熱來抑制排水管中的微生物生長，作為化學消毒的替代方案。

比喻說明

潔淨室是「無聲手術室」：在手術室裡，你不會安裝普通的家用對講機 — 所有通訊設備都必須防水、可消毒、不釋放微粒。潔淨室的喇叭系統也是如此 — 加裝密封膜後，聲音可以穿透，但空氣和微粒不能。現代趨勢是使用可清潔的密封式無線通訊設備，完全消除牆壁上的開孔需求。

實務應用

CDMO 設施規劃清單：

  • ISO 5 區域：吸入式偵煙 + 閃燈警報（取代蜂鳴器） + 密封式通訊
  • ISO 7 區域：嵌入式消防偵測 + 密封喇叭膜 + 無排水設計
  • ISO 8 區域：標準偵煙（含防 VHP 誤報） + 電加熱排水陷阱 + 外圍捕蟲燈
  • 所有區域：嵌入式或齊平安裝、可清潔材質、與消毒劑相容

Section Summary / 本章重點回顧

  • General Requirements / 一般要求：All electrical equipment in aseptic areas must be cleanable, ledge-free, non-shedding, sealed, and compatible with sanitization agents. ISO 5 areas require hermetic sealing and absolute minimization of installed equipment / 無菌區域所有電氣設備必須可清潔、無凸緣、不脫落、密封、與消毒劑相容。ISO 5 區域要求氣密封和最小化安裝量
  • Control System Power / 控制系統電力：UPS is essential for digital control systems (BMS, SCADA, PLC) to ensure orderly shutdown and data integrity during power loss. Staggered restart programming prevents breaker trips / UPS 對數位控制系統不可或缺，確保斷電時有序關機與數據完整性。依序重啟程式防止跳閘
  • Power Distribution / 配電系統：DP monitoring power is critical — loss of pressure monitoring during outages directly impacts product quality assessment. Power quality (harmonics, phase balance) matters for precision equipment / 差壓監控的供電至關重要。電力品質（諧波、相位平衡）影響精密設備運作
  • Lighting / 照明：Minimum 500 lux at work areas. Flush-mount (recess) fixtures mandatory in ISO 5 to avoid airflow disruption. LED preferred for reduced maintenance. Consider photo stability impact on light-sensitive products / 工作區最低 500 lux。ISO 5 區域必須使用嵌入式燈具以避免干擾氣流。LED 首選以減少維護。須考慮光穩定性影響
  • Hazardous Environments / 防爆環境：ATEX classification is rare in sterile facilities due to high air changes, but failure mode analysis (HVAC loss) is required. Static dissipation and conductive floors may be needed / 無菌設施中防爆分類較罕見，但需進行失效模式分析。可能需要靜電消散和導電地板
  • Wiring / 配線：Minimize wall/ceiling penetrations, seal all conduits. Unsealed trunking is a hidden contamination reservoir. Mobile equipment cables must be kept off the floor / 最小化穿牆數量，密封所有管線。未密封線槽是隱藏的污染庫。移動設備電纜不可拖地
  • Door Interlocks / 門連鎖：Airlock interlocks maintain pressure cascades. Emergency override is mandatory for life safety. Electronic access control required for ISO 5 areas. Verify during commissioning/qualification / 氣閘互鎖維持壓差級聯。緊急覆寫功能為強制要求。ISO 5 區域需電子門禁。試車確效時需驗證
  • Miscellaneous / 雜項設備：Aspirated fire detection for ISO 5 (avoids in-room equipment). Sealed communication membranes. Insect traps outside cleanrooms. Bio-control heated traps for ISO 8 drains / ISO 5 使用吸入式偵煙。通訊系統加密封膜。捕蟲燈設於潔淨室外。ISO 8 排水使用電加熱生物控制陷阱
ISPE Baseline Guide Vol. 3 (3rd Ed.) | p157 – p166

Learning Objectives / 本章學習目標

  • Understand the role of C&I systems in sterile manufacturing and how they impact patient safety and product quality / 理解儀控系統在無菌製造中的角色及其對病患安全與產品品質的影響
  • Identify critical environmental process parameters (CPPs) and their monitoring requirements / 辨識關鍵環境製程參數及其監測要求
  • Distinguish between active and passive control strategies for environmental parameters / 區分環境參數的主動式與被動式控制策略
  • Apply the hierarchy of Process Limits, Alert Limits, and Normal Operating Conditions / 運用製程限值、警示限值與正常操作條件的層級關係
  • Understand instrument selection criteria: accuracy, location, and calibration / 理解儀器選擇標準：精確度、安裝位置與校正
  • Evaluate HVAC control system choices: BMS/BAS vs. DCS/PLC/SCADA / 評估 HVAC 控制系統選擇：BMS/BAS 與 DCS/PLC/SCADA 的差異
  • Describe airborne particle counting configurations and monitoring considerations / 描述空氣中粒子計數系統架構與監測考量

Section Index / 本節內容索引

8.1 Introduction 8.2 CPPs – Environmental 8.2.3 Alert & Action Alarms 8.2.4 Limits Hierarchy 8.3 Instrumentation 8.4 Production Process Parameters 8.5 General Design Issues 8.6 HVAC Controls 8.6.2 Particle Counting Section Summary
8.1 Introduction — Control & Instrumentation Overview 8.1 簡介 — 控制與儀表概述

Original Text

8.1 Introduction

This chapter considers the various functions of Control and Instrumentation (C&I) systems for sterile products manufacturing facilities and focuses on those facility and environment controls which affect patient safety and product quality. The objective is to provide design guidance for cost effective systems which can be qualified.

C&I systems are used in many facility related systems. They may be deemed to affect patient safety and product quality if they control, monitor, or record a CPP, or directly affect a CQA. Components of C&I systems may also be considered critical if they come into direct physical contact with the product.

The functions described may be combined within a single C&I system or be performed by several independent systems.

Specific design advice has been given where possible, but it is stressed that each application has different priorities and operational preferences that influence the adopted solution.

Designers should also consider other relevant design criteria, such as safety, reliability, data integrity, and design for maintenance.

導師解析

核心概念：C&I 系統在無菌廠的角色

儀控系統 (C&I) 是無菌製造設施的「神經系統」。它做三件事：

  • 控制 (Control)：讓溫度、壓差、濕度等參數維持在指定範圍內
  • 監測 (Monitor)：持續或定期量測，確認參數在限值內
  • 記錄 (Record)：將數據保存以供追溯與合規查核

任何一個子系統，只要它控制、監測或記錄了一個 關鍵製程參數 (CPP) 或直接影響 關鍵品質屬性 (CQA)，就被認定為「可能影響病患安全與產品品質」。

比喻說明：無菌廠的神經系統

把無菌廠想成人體。HVAC 是呼吸系統（提供潔淨空氣），水系統是血液循環（輸送純水），而 C&I 就是神經系統——感知環境（感測器）、傳遞訊號（訊號線與網路）、做出反應（控制器調整閥門或馬達）、留下記憶（資料記錄）。

沒有神經系統，身體無法維持體溫恆定——無菌廠沒有 C&I，也無法維持潔淨室的壓差、溫度與微粒等級。

重點提示：Data Integrity 是設計標準之一

本節明確將「資料完整性 (Data Integrity)」列為設計考量。這表示在選擇或設計儀控系統時，不只要考慮「測得準」，還要確保「記得住且不可竄改」——這對 ALCOA+ 原則的落實至關重要。

8.2 Critical Process Parameters — Environmental Conditions 8.2 關鍵製程參數 — 環境條件

Original Text

8.2.1 Environmental Conditions within the Production Area

The production of sterile products requires a clean classified work environment for open, exposed processes. Processes and products vary greatly. Specific environmental parameters should be considered, specified, monitored, and recorded, as discussed in Chapter 5.

Several requirements for particulate and microbiological cleanliness, differential pressure (DP), and airflow are required in the GMPs for typical process steps and unit operations.

If manufacture of several products is considered, the design team should ensure that the design accommodates the most demanding product requirements.

8.2.2 Monitoring and Documenting

CPPs should be monitored and documented.

Monitoring means that a parameter is continuously or periodically measured to ensure it is within its defined limits. This can be accomplished with either permanently installed, portable, or disposable instruments. When determining whether to monitor a CPP continuously or periodically, it is recommended to perform a comprehensive risk assessment and develop a mitigation plan to fully define the rationale.

Documented means that the parameter value (or evidence that the value is within control limits) is recorded at some predefined frequency for future reference. The frequency should be based on a documented rationale which reflects:

  • Consequences of manufacturing outside required (process) limits
  • Probability and frequency of temporary parameter control loss
  • Duration and frequency of activities such as process interventions

An active control system is deemed to have a control loop with direct feed-back or feed-forward. A passive control system is where a condition is monitored, and management action is implemented, if needed, to rectify the deviation in conditions.

When CPPs are monitored, the monitoring regime should, where possible, be established with alert and action limits. Alert limits provide early warning of a potential deviation enabling corrective or preventative measures to be taken prior to an action limit being reached; in some conditions, alarm condition delays may be appropriate.

Table 8.1: Typical Environmental Process Parameters

Airborne particle levels (viable and non-viable) reflect the effect of achieving and maintaining the control parameters in Table 8.1. Particle levels are also influenced by internal operations (personnel).

導師解析

核心概念：主動控制 vs 被動控制

這是本節最重要的分類框架：

  • 主動控制 (Active Control)：有控制迴路、有回饋 (feedback) 或前饋 (feedforward)。例如 AHU 送風溫度控制——感測器偵測到溫度偏高，控制器自動開大冷水閥。
  • 被動控制 (Passive Control)：沒有自動迴路。靠設計本身（如固定風量比例、HEPA 過濾器）來維持條件，偏差時由人員介入。

關鍵判斷原則：被動控制系統的可靠度通常比主動系統更高（零件少、不會故障），但一旦偏差，反應速度更慢。因此本指南對被動控制的監測頻率要求可以「較低」。

重點提示：壓差控制的爭議

注意 Table 8.1 中一個關鍵建議：本指南不建議使用致動控制風門 (actuated control dampers) 來主動控制壓差。

原因：壓差對門的開關、人員進出極為敏感。用主動控制風門容易造成不同房間之間的「壓力振盪」——A 房升壓，B 房的控制器反應降壓，結果形成不穩定的來回震盪。

技術基線 (Technical Baseline)：被動式鎖定風門 + 連續監測。簡單而可靠。

比喻說明：被動 vs 主動控制

被動控制像一條設計好坡度的水溝——水自然會流向正確方向，不需要泵浦。只要定期巡檢，確認沒有堵塞即可。

主動控制像裝了泵浦的管路——能精確控制流量，但泵浦故障時水就不流了。需要更頻繁的監測和維護。

監測頻率的決策邏輯

「多久量一次？」不是憑感覺決定的。ISPE 提出三個評估因素：

  1. 偏差後果：製程限值外製造的嚴重程度（產品報廢？召回？病患風險？）
  2. 失控機率：控制系統的可靠度與複雜度
  3. 干預頻率：人員操作、門開關等可能擾動參數的活動頻率

風險越高 → 監測越頻繁。Grade A/B 區域的壓差與溫度通常需要連續監測；Grade C/D 可以較低頻率。

實務應用：CDMO 多產品設計

本節提醒：如果同一區域要製造多種產品，設計必須滿足「最嚴格的產品需求」。對 CDMO 而言，這意味著：

  • 溫度範圍取所有產品中最窄的要求
  • 壓差等級取最高分類要求
  • 監測系統要能在不同產品間切換警示限值

設計建議：預留 BMS 參數切換功能，讓操作人員依據不同產品批次快速載入對應的限值組態。

8.2.3 Alert and Action Alarms / 警示與行動警報

Original Text

8.2.3 Alert and Action Alarms

CPPs should remain within specified values. Where monitoring and documenting is necessary, the monitoring system should provide an:

  • Alert Alarm to indicate that the parameter has deviated from the normal operating range (i.e., outside the Normal Operating Conditions — a possible control problem)
  • Action Alarm to indicate that the parameter has deviated from Process Limits (i.e., may result in a product quality issue)

Alarms should latch and not self-cancel (i.e., the alarm remains active even after the condition has been corrected) until acknowledged by the user/operator. All alarm conditions should be documented and corrective actions recorded.

Where momentary parameter deviation outside specified limits is acceptable, appropriate time delay intervals can be incorporated into the alarm logic. These should be thoroughly tested, with the rationale documented as part of the system qualification.

導師解析

雙層警報架構

本節建立了 GMP 儀控系統的標準警報模型：

Action Alarm（行動警報）— 逼近製程限值
▼
Alert Alarm（警示警報）— 偏離正常操作範圍
▼
Normal Operating Conditions（正常操作條件）

Alert = 早期預警，讓你有時間採取預防措施。Action = 已接近或超出製程限值，必須立即處理。

重點提示：Alarm Latch（鎖存）原則

警報「鎖存且不自動取消」是 GMP 的核心設計要求。即使偏差條件已恢復正常，警報仍保持激活狀態，直到操作員手動確認。

為什麼？確保每一次偏差都有人看到、有人判斷、有記錄。如果警報自動消失，操作員可能永遠不知道偏差發生過——這對產品品質判定和偏差調查是致命的。

重點提示：Time Delay 的陷阱

允許短暫偏差的「時間延遲」邏輯聽起來合理（例如開門瞬間壓差短暫下降），但設定不當會隱藏真正的問題。

ISPE 要求：延遲邏輯必須經過「徹底測試」且「文件化理由」。稽核時，查核重點往往在：延遲設定依據是什麼？有沒有經過風險評估？

8.2.4 Environmental Process Limits, Facility Design Limits, and Normal Operating Conditions / 限值層級架構

Original Text

8.2.4 Environmental Process Limits, Facility Design Limits, and Normal Operating Conditions

Environmental Process Limits are the upper and lower limits demanded by the production process(es). The Facility Design Limits are used to calculate HVAC facility or utility capacity, and are based upon a number of factors, such as:

  • Operator comfort
  • Energy conservation
  • Regulatory requirements
  • Process limits
  • What is technically and practically possible

Facility Design Limits should be set to operate within Normal Operating Conditions, where the extremes of these conditions are defined by the Alert Limits.

Example: Assume that Process Limits are 22°C ± 4°C (71.6°F ± 7.2°F). The HVAC system facility is designed to provide 22°C ± 2°C (71.6°F ± 3.6°F); however, control to within 22°C ± 1°C (71.6°F ± 1.8°F) is usual. Alert Limits can be set at a lower limit of 21°C (69.8°F) and an upper limit of 23°C (71.4°F), as deviation outside these conditions indicates a situation which may require investigation.

Figure 8.1: Alert and Alarm Limits illustrates this relationship.

導師解析

比喻說明：高速公路的速限

想像高速公路限速 110 km/h（Process Limit）。車子設計巡航速度 100 km/h（Facility Design Limit）。你通常開在 95-105 km/h（Normal Operating Conditions）。儀表板在 105 km/h 時亮黃燈提醒（Alert），超過 110 km/h 時響警報（Action Alarm）。

重點：每一層都有其存在的理由，缺一不可。如果直接用 Process Limit 當 Alert Limit，就沒有預警空間了。

練習思考

  1. 如果一個產品的製程限值是 22°C ± 2°C（很窄），而 HVAC 系統在夏天外部溫度 35°C 時只能控制到 ± 1.5°C，這代表什麼問題？該如何解決？
  2. 為什麼 ISPE 強調「設施設計限值」要同時考慮操作員舒適度和節能？這和產品品質有什麼關聯？

四層限值架構——從寬到窄

這是本章最重要的設計概念，用溫度的例子一層層解析：

層與層之間的「留白」就是安全裕度。設計好的系統，各層之間有足夠空間，不會因為一點小擾動就觸發 Action Alarm。

8.3 Instrumentation / 儀器設計與選擇

Original Text

8.3.1 Physical Design

Instruments in process areas should be located to allow cleaning and sanitization of exposed surfaces and should be designed and installed to prevent accumulation of particulate matter. Computer screens and keyboards located in processing areas should be cleanable, such as by utilizing touch membrane technology.

Instruments in direct contact with the product, its components, or associated with a critical manufacturing process should be designed and installed to:

  • Prevent accumulation of any matter (including product)
  • Withstand required cleaning/sanitization processes and agents without degradation
  • Not present a contamination risk to the product or its components
  • Not be degraded (physically or in performance) by contact with the product

Many instruments have sensing elements remote from their data processing components. The use of such instruments allows isolation, separation, or remote location of the processing components. This may simplify cleaning and reduce contamination risk.

8.3.2 Performance: Accuracy

When assessing an instrument's accuracy, several factors should be considered:

  • Fitness for purpose
  • Instrument cost increases with accuracy
  • How misleading the instrument can be without threatening product quality
  • Higher accuracy instruments reduce the risk of manufacture under unsuitable conditions because of instrument drift

For each CPP, there are usually Process Limits within which a product should be produced. C&I systems should be designed to control conditions to a set point within the Process Limits, usually with a margin of safety or reserve.

An indicated value on an instrument is subject to uncertainty (i.e., subject to the instrument accuracy). For the true condition to remain within Process Limits at the indicated extremes of the Alert Limits, the instrument's accuracy should give a measurement whose uncertainty is no greater than the difference between the Process and Alert Limits. This difference defines the Instrument Permitted Limit.

Example: Process Limits are 22°C ± 2°C, Alert Limits are 22°C ± 1°C. At the extremes of the Alert Limits, the instrument should be accurate to at least ± 0.5°C to guarantee temperature remains within Process Limits.

8.3.3 Location

Instrument sensors measuring the critical process or environmental parameter(s) should be located at a point representative of the condition to be measured. Ease of calibration should also be considered.

Where separate sensors are used to control and monitor the same CPP, they should be co-located to ensure the parameter is equally measured.

8.3.4 Calibration

The calibration method and its cost should be considered when selecting any instrument. Comprehensive calibration guidance should be obtained from the suppliers before an instrument is chosen.

導師解析

儀器物理設計四原則

無菌區域的儀器不只要「量得準」，還要符合潔淨室設計原則：

  1. 可清潔 (Cleanable)：表面光滑、無死角，能承受消毒劑
  2. 不積塵 (No Accumulation)：安裝方式避免水平凹槽或縫隙
  3. 不污染 (No Contamination Risk)：與產品接觸的部分材質相容
  4. 耐腐蝕 (Durable)：不被產品或清潔劑降解

實務上，越來越多儀器採用「感測端遠端分離」設計——只有一個小探頭在潔淨室內，電子處理元件在技術夾層，大幅降低清潔難度與污染風險。

Instrument Permitted Limit（儀器允許限值）

這是一個精妙的設計概念：

儀器允許限值 = 製程限值 - 警示限值

以溫度為例：

  • 製程限值：22°C ± 2°C → 上限 24°C
  • 警示限值：22°C ± 1°C → 上限 23°C
  • 儀器允許限值：24 - 23 = 1°C
  • 因此儀器精確度至少需要 ± 0.5°C

如果用更高精確度的儀器（例如 ± 0.1°C），就有更大的「漂移裕度」，校正週期可以拉長——長遠省錢。

重點提示：精確度 vs 成本的決策

精確度越高，儀器越貴，但帶來三個好處：

  • 更大的漂移容許空間 → 校正頻率可降低
  • 降低在不適當條件下生產的風險
  • 減少偏差事件 → 減少調查和報廢成本

ISPE 建議：對關鍵支援系統 (critical support system) 的儀器選高精確度，非關鍵系統可用較低精確度。這符合「風險為基礎」的設計哲學。

重點提示：感測器共置 (Co-location)

當「控制」和「監測」同一個 CPP 使用不同感測器時，兩者必須安裝在相同位置。否則可能出現：控制感測器顯示 21.5°C（正常），但監測感測器因為在不同位置讀到 23.5°C（超標），造成混淆和調查負擔。

練習思考

  1. 一個溫度感測器安裝在回風口（較暖），另一個安裝在操作台面正上方（較冷）。哪一個更適合作為「代表性量測點」？為什麼？
  2. 如果校正成本是選擇儀器的考量之一，一支難以現場校正的高精確度感測器和一支容易校正的中等精確度感測器，你如何取捨？
8.4 Production Process Parameters / 生產製程參數

Original Text

8.4 Production Process Parameters

The number and diversity of production processes that can be used in sterile product manufacturing facilities are such that a comprehensive discussion of their parameters is not practical within the scope of this Guide.

Detailed knowledge of the production process in question and application of rigorous design and operation review methods are necessary to identify appropriate systems of control and monitoring. This can be achieved through detailed PAT (Process Analytical Technology) and application of process control to achieve proper parameters or conditions that mitigate product quality issues and avoid impact on patient safety.

導師解析

本節為何簡短？——設計哲學的暗示

本節刻意簡短，因為生產製程參數（如充填重量、壓塞位置、封蓋力矩等）因產品而異，無法一體適用。但它傳達了兩個重要訊息：

  1. PAT 是首選方法：使用即時分析技術來監測製程，而非依賴最終檢驗
  2. 必須經過嚴格的設計審查：每一個生產製程的控制與監測系統，都需要透過風險評估來量身打造

比喻說明：環境參數 vs 製程參數

如果環境參數（溫度、壓差、粒子數）是「舞台的燈光和空調」，那麼製程參數（充填量、壓塞深度、密封完整性）就是「演員的表演」。

ISPE Vol.3 主要在設計舞台——環境控制。演員的表演（製程控制）則需要配合特定劇目（產品）來設計，所以本指南只提方法論（PAT + 設計審查），不提具體參數。

實務應用：CDMO 常見的製程參數

雖然本節未列舉，以下是 CDMO 無菌充填線常見的 CPP：

  • 充填重量 (Fill Weight)：通常 ± 2-5% 範圍，取決於劑型與容器
  • 壓塞位置 (Stopper Placement)：壓塞高度與歪斜度
  • 密封完整性 (Seal Integrity)：鋁蓋壓合力矩
  • 充填速度 (Fill Speed)：影響起泡與精確度
  • 惰氣覆蓋 (Inert Gas Overlay)：殘氧量控制
8.5 General Design Issues / 一般設計議題

Original Text

8.5 General Design Issues

Computerized system lifecycle activities, such as specification, design, and verification should be scaled according to:

  • Potential for system to impact patient safety, product quality, and data integrity (risk assessment)
  • System complexity and novelty (architecture and categorization of system components)
  • Outcome of supplier assessment (supplier capability)

Refer to ISPE GAMP 5 for further details of these considerations and the scaling of lifecycle activities.

The following sections discuss cost effective separation of system functions (i.e., monitoring and control) and system choice in the context of typical supplier capabilities.

導師解析

核心概念：電腦化系統生命週期的「分級」原則

不是所有儀控系統都需要同樣嚴格的驗證。ISPE 引用 GAMP 5 的核心理念：依風險分級 (Risk-Based Approach)。

三個分級維度：

  • 影響程度：這個系統如果出錯，會影響病患安全嗎？會影響資料完整性嗎？
  • 複雜程度：是簡單的單迴路控制器，還是整合多個子系統的 SCADA？
  • 供應商可靠度：供應商有完善的品質管理系統嗎？軟體開發有遵循 SDLC 嗎？

影響高 + 複雜度高 + 供應商未經驗證 = 需要最完整的驗證文件。影響低 + 成熟簡單系統 + 知名供應商 = 可簡化驗證。

重點提示：監控與控制的分離

本節暗示了一個重要的設計策略：將「控制」和「監測」功能分離到不同系統上。例如：

  • 控制：由 BMS/BAS 負責 HVAC 迴路控制
  • 監測：由獨立的環境監測系統 (EMS) 負責記錄和警報

好處：監測系統獨立於控制系統，可作為「第二道防線」。控制系統故障時，監測系統仍能偵測到偏差。

8.6 HVAC Control System Choice / HVAC 控制系統選擇

Original Text

8.6.1 Control System Choice

Commercially available Building Management Systems/Building Automation Systems (BMS/BAS) are encouraged to be installed in all facilities to monitor critical facility control systems.

There may be some safety-critical systems that should utilize Distributed Control Systems (DCS) and Programmable Logic Controllers (PLC) with Supervisory Control and Data Acquisition (SCADA); however, these are primarily targeted at controlling processes.

HVAC may be monitored and controlled using several control system types. Those designed specifically for HVAC include conventional controllers (typically single loop controls) and, more appropriately, BMS/BAS.

When specifying systems to control HVAC, the following should be considered:

  • HVAC's industrial nature in cleanroom applications may not justify use of PLC or DCS based solutions; however, personnel safety issues may justify their use.
  • Pharmaceutical HVAC can be controlled satisfactorily using HVAC industry control systems.

Where control is needed for a few simple systems, conventional controls may provide a marginal cost advantage. This advantage is offset by the fact that conventional controls cannot be integrated readily into any future BMS/BAS demanded by site development.

As the application scale, complexity, and remote monitoring demands increase, the use of BMS/BAS rapidly becomes more cost effective.

Monitoring of critical environmental parameters can be accomplished via the Process Control System, which should be qualified. The qualification of the BMS/BAS may then become simpler.

導師解析

重點提示：ISPE 明確推薦 BMS/BAS

本節的核心訊息很清楚：HVAC 用 BMS/BAS，不需要用 DCS 或 PLC。

理由：

  • 藥廠 HVAC 的「工業本質」不需要 DCS/PLC 的高速處理能力
  • BMS/BAS 是 HVAC 產業的原生解決方案，供應商生態系統成熟
  • 隨著規模增長，BMS/BAS 的成本效益優勢越來越明顯

例外：如果涉及人員安全（如有毒氣體偵測、緊急排氣），則可能需要 PLC/DCS。

比喻說明：選車的邏輯

用 DCS 控制 HVAC，就像用 F1 賽車送小孩上學——性能遠超需求，但維護成本高昂、操作複雜。

BMS/BAS 就像家用休旅車——功能完全滿足需求，維修容易，未來要加裝導航或倒車雷達（擴充功能）也很方便。

傳統單迴路控制器就像腳踏車——短距離很好用，但無法帶全家人出門。

監測與控制分離策略

ISPE 提出一個聰明的簡化策略：

  1. 用已驗證的製程控制系統 (Process Control System) 來「監測」關鍵環境參數
  2. BMS/BAS 只負責「控制」HVAC
  3. 結果：BMS/BAS 的確認 (Qualification) 可以簡化，因為關鍵的 CPP 監測已由另一個已驗證的系統承擔

這大幅降低了 BMS/BAS 的驗證範圍與成本，同時不犧牲合規性。

8.6.2 Airborne Particle Counting / 空氣中粒子計數系統

Original Text

8.6.2 Airborne Particle Counting

The act of classification of a space environment, and of monitoring that environment "in operation", should be differentiated:

  • The method for formal classification is specified in ISO 14644-1. This standard defines the minimum number of sample locations, the minimum sample size at each location, the class limits, and the method for evaluation of data.
  • Note: In the context of sterile product manufacture, EU Annex 1 sets some class limits that are different from those found in FDA guidance and ISO 14644-1.
  • Monitoring may use similar instrumentation; in this case, specific critical or most important locations are determined from investigation and studies, and these are monitored to demonstrate the performance of critical parts of the controlled environment.

Particle counting instruments operate by taking a sample of the air and measuring the particle concentration by evaluation of scattered light in a special optical chamber. Such instruments can measure both the number and size of particles in the size range 0.1 µm to 5.0 µm.

Particle counting system configurations:

  • Single portable instruments: Located close to the environment being classified or monitored. Suitable for evaluating particles 0.1 µm to 5.0 µm. Used for both classification and monitoring.
  • Single fixed instruments with manifold: Connected to multiple sample locations via tubing arrays. Each location sampled in turn. Suitable only for 0.1 µm to 0.5 µm due to potential drop out of larger particles in transport tubing. Used for monitoring only.
  • Multiple miniature point-of-use counters: Each located close to a monitoring location, connected to a data acquisition system. Suitable for 0.1 µm to 5.0 µm. Used for monitoring only.

Major points to consider for particle monitoring systems:

  • Difficulty of correlating data from the relatively small number of sample points of a monitoring system compared to the larger number used for classification
  • Identifying the room "worst case" points and relating them to overall room conditions
  • Determination of an appropriate sampling frequency
  • Management and interpretation of potentially large amounts of data
  • Determination of alert and action levels
  • Procedures for excursion beyond alert and action levels
  • Re-evaluation of sample points if there is a change in room layout
  • Special attention to the distance between air collection point and counter: inner diameter of tubing, airflow throughput and turbulence (Reynolds numbers), particle drop-out impact, tubing material (surface roughness, electrostatic charge), geometry of flow paths (kinks, obstructions, sharp curves)

Where particle concentrations are very low, monitoring system alert and action levels may be better expressed using frequency (pattern) of seeing low counts rather than trying to discriminate between very low numbers.

2004 FDA Guidance: "Regular monitoring should be performed during each production shift. We recommend conducting nonviable particle monitoring with a remote counting system. These systems are capable of collecting more comprehensive data and are generally less invasive than portable particle counters."

2009 EU Annex 1: "For Grade A zone, particle monitoring should be undertaken for the full duration of critical processing, including equipment assembly, except where justified by contaminants in the process that would damage the particle counter or present a hazard... It is recommended that a similar system be used for Grade B zones although the sample frequency may be decreased."

導師解析

重點提示：管路設計是隱藏的關鍵

固定式歧管系統只能量 0.1-0.5 µm，因為 ≥ 0.5 µm 的大粒子在輸送管路中會「沉降」（drop out）。影響因素包括：

  • 管路內徑：太細則流速過高產生紊流
  • 管路長度：越長，大粒子損失越多
  • 管路材質：內壁粗糙度和靜電荷會吸附粒子
  • 彎頭與障礙物：銳角彎頭是粒子損失的主要原因

設計時必須計算雷諾數 (Reynolds Number)，確保管內流態在適當範圍內。

重點提示：FDA vs EU Annex 1 的差異

兩大法規對粒子監測的要求有微妙差異：

  • FDA：建議每班次監測，推薦使用遠端計數系統（侵入性低、資料更全面）
  • EU Annex 1：Grade A 區必須在整個關鍵製程期間全程監測（要求更嚴格），Grade B 可降低頻率

如果產品同時出口歐美，必須取兩者中的嚴格標準——即 Grade A 全程連續監測。

比喻說明：低計數的「頻率」表達法

粒子數極低時（例如 Grade A 區經常是 0 或 1 個粒子），單純看數字沒有意義——0 和 1 的差異不具統計意義。

ISPE 建議改用「頻率模式」：例如「每 100 次取樣中有 5 次偵測到 ≥ 1 個粒子」比「平均 0.05 個粒子/m³」更有資訊量。就像判斷一個地區是否安全，不是看「平均犯罪率 0.001」，而是看「過去一年有 3 次事件，集中在週末深夜」——模式比數字更有意義。

練習思考

  1. 你正在為一條新的充填線選擇粒子監測系統。充填線在 Grade A 隔離器內，需同時滿足 FDA 和 EU Annex 1。你會選擇哪種系統配置？為什麼？
  2. 如果歧管式系統的取樣管路從粒子計數器到最遠取樣點有 15 米，你會擔心什麼問題？如何驗證管路損失是否可接受？
  3. Room layout 變更後，為什麼必須重新評估取樣點位置？請舉一個具體例子。

分類 (Classification) vs 監測 (Monitoring)——不可混淆

這是法規稽核中常見的混淆點：

Section Summary / 本章重點摘要

Key Takeaways

Chapter 8 Summary

  1. C&I systems are the nervous system of sterile manufacturing facilities — they control, monitor, and record parameters that affect patient safety and product quality.
  2. Environmental CPPs (temperature, RH, differential pressure, particle count) can be managed through active or passive control strategies, each with different monitoring frequency requirements.
  3. Alert and Action alarms provide a two-tier warning system. Alarms must latch (not self-cancel) and any time delays must be justified and qualified.
  4. A clear hierarchy of limits (Process Limits > Facility Design Limits > Alert Limits > Normal Operating Conditions) ensures adequate safety margins at every level.
  5. Instrument selection must balance accuracy vs. cost, with the Instrument Permitted Limit defining the minimum acceptable accuracy. Sensors must be co-located when used for both control and monitoring of the same CPP.
  6. BMS/BAS is the recommended control system for HVAC in pharmaceutical facilities. DCS/PLC/SCADA should be reserved for safety-critical or complex process control applications.
  7. Airborne particle counting requires clear differentiation between classification (ISO 14644-1) and monitoring. System configuration must account for tubing losses, and both FDA and EU Annex 1 requirements must be met for global supply.

重點摘要

第八章摘要

  1. 儀控系統 (C&I) 是無菌廠的神經系統——控制、監測、記錄影響病患安全與產品品質的參數。
  2. 環境 CPP（溫度、濕度、壓差、粒子數）可透過主動或被動控制策略管理，監測頻率依策略而異。
  3. Alert 與 Action 警報構成雙層預警系統。警報必須鎖存（不自動取消），時間延遲必須有合理依據且經過確認。
  4. 四層限值架構（製程限值 > 設施設計限值 > 警示限值 > 正常操作條件）確保每一層都有足夠的安全裕度。
  5. 儀器選擇必須平衡精確度與成本，「儀器允許限值」定義了最低可接受精確度。控制與監測同一 CPP 的感測器必須共置。
  6. BMS/BAS 是藥廠 HVAC 的推薦控制系統。DCS/PLC/SCADA 應保留給安全關鍵或複雜製程控制。
  7. 空氣中粒子計數必須區分「分類」（ISO 14644-1）和「監測」。系統配置必須考慮管路損失，同時供應全球市場須滿足 FDA 和 EU Annex 1 雙重要求。

CDMO 營運關鍵行動項目

  • 確認所有環境 CPP 都有明確的四層限值架構文件
  • 審查 BMS 警報是否為鎖存式，時間延遲是否有文件化依據
  • 評估儀器精確度是否滿足「儀器允許限值」要求
  • 確認控制與監測感測器的共置狀態
  • 審查粒子監測系統是否同時滿足 FDA 與 EU Annex 1 要求
  • 確認歧管式系統的管路損失經過驗證
7a

Chapter 7a: 9a. Barrier & Isolator (9.1–9.4)

屏障與隔離器（上） | p167-p178

ISPE Baseline Guide Vol. 3 (3rd Ed.) | p167 – p178

Learning Objectives / 學習目標

  1. Understand why barrier technologies are preferred over conventional cleanrooms for aseptic processing / 理解屏障技術為何優於傳統無菌室
  2. Distinguish between oRABS, cRABS, and isolator systems with precise definitions / 精確區分 oRABS、cRABS 與隔離器之定義
  3. Compare the three technologies across cost, flexibility, contamination control, and regulatory acceptance / 比較三種技術在成本、靈活性、污染控制與法規接受度的差異
  4. Apply a risk-based framework for choosing barrier technology for new or retrofitted facilities / 運用風險評估框架為新建或改造設施選擇屏障技術
  5. Recognize the EU Annex 1 (2022) direction toward isolators and cRABS / 認知 EU Annex 1（2022）對隔離器與 cRABS 的推動方向

Section Navigation / 章節導覽

9.1 Introduction 9.2 System Definitions 9.2.1 Isolators 9.2.2 RABS 9.3 System Comparisons 9.4 Factors to Consider
9.1

Introduction / 導論

p167 – p168

English — Original Content

For new and renovated aseptic processing facilities, barrier technologies, such as isolators and RABS, are usually preferred to protect the product. They are being increasingly used for aseptic filling. Isolators can provide a higher safety level and are typically used in new facility designs. RABS are usually used to upgrade existing facilities, when existing equipment needs to have better protection.

Both technologies can be applied to batches of all sizes, from small scale filling of clinical trial materials to large, automated, high speed processing lines. They can also be applied to research and development, quality control (sterility testing), and drug formulation. When the product is hazardous, isolators or RABS, with their reduced air overspill into a room, can help to protect the operator and the surrounding environment.

People are considered the greatest source of contamination in the manufacturing of sterile products. Over the past decades, substantial progress has been made in separating the operator from the critical areas within the aseptic manufacturing suite.

Physical separation, equipment integration, and the increasing use of automation in these systems can reduce the need for personnel involvement inside critical areas. Advantages of these technologies can, however, be counteracted by poor design and ineffective operator training. Ergonomic aspects are fundamental to the design concept and should be considered in conjunction with:

  • Mechanical movement (i.e., moving machine parts)
  • Safe material and product transfers in and out of the barrier
  • Cleanability
  • Ability to decontaminate the system
  • Appropriate background environment in which the system is to be operated

These decisions should be made on a risk-based approach, depending upon the application and specific system design.

繁體中文 — 教學註解

對於新建或翻新的無菌製程設施，屏障技術（如隔離器和 RABS）通常是保護產品的首選。這些技術在無菌充填中的使用日益增加。隔離器能提供更高的安全等級，通常用於新設施設計。RABS 則通常用於升級現有設施，為既有設備提供更好的保護。

這兩種技術適用於各種批量，從小規模臨床試驗材料充填到大型自動化高速生產線。也可應用於研發、品管（無菌測試）及藥物配方。當產品具有危害性時，隔離器或 RABS 透過減少向房間溢出的空氣量，有助於保護操作人員及周圍環境。

核心概念：人是最大的污染源

在無菌產品製造中，人員被視為最大的污染來源。過去數十年來，業界在將操作人員與無菌製造套間的關鍵區域分離方面取得了重大進展。屏障技術正是實現此目標的核心手段。

物理隔離、設備整合與自動化的增加，可以減少人員在關鍵區域的參與需求。但這些技術的優勢可能被不良設計和無效的操作人員培訓所抵消。人因工程是設計概念的基礎，需與以下面向一併考量：

  • 機械運動（即移動的機器零件）
  • 物料與產品進出屏障的安全轉移
  • 可清潔性
  • 系統除污能力
  • 系統操作所處的適當背景環境

實務類比

可將屏障技術想像成廚房的「無菌廚房」概念：傳統無菌室就像開放式廚房，廚師（操作人員）在同一空間工作；RABS 像加了玻璃隔間的廚房，廚師透過手套操作；隔離器則像完全密封的自動販賣機，食物在完全隔離的環境中製備。

9.2

System Definitions / 系統定義

p168 – p172

English — Original Content

The differences between the types of isolators and RABS used in pharmaceutical aseptic processing should be understood. Isolators and RABS can be broadly classified according to the type of separation they provide and the assurance of maintaining that separation, although there may be some overlap in the degrees of separation and operator protection.

Figure 9.1 (from ISO 14644-7) illustrates increasing levels of separation assurance moving from purely aerodynamic separation (as in a unidirectional airflow hood) to complete physical separation (as in a closed isolator).

Along the continuum of assurance of maintaining separation:

  • RABS tend to utilize physical separation and air overspill all around the barrier to separate personnel from the aseptic processing critical areas.
  • Isolators tend to rely on physical separation, positive pressure differentials and mouseholes with air overspill to provide the necessary level of separation and protection.

Where hazardous materials are aseptically processed:

  • RABS requires personnel to wear PPE and rooms to be fully segregated by airlocks to avoid spreading of product throughout the facility and into the environment.
  • Isolators maintain operator protection by technical measures, such as adequate differential pressure zones and the integrity of the isolator.
繁體中文 — 教學註解

必須理解製藥無菌製程中所使用的各類隔離器與 RABS 之間的差異。隔離器與 RABS 可依據其提供的隔離類型及維持隔離的保證程度進行廣泛分類，儘管在隔離程度和操作人員保護方面可能存在一定的重疊。

隔離保證等級連續譜（Figure 9.1）

依 ISO 14644-7 所示，隔離保證等級從低到高：

氣流隔離（UAF 罩） 物理 + 氣流（RABS） 完全物理隔離（密封隔離器）

在隔離保證的連續光譜中：

  • RABS 傾向利用物理隔離及屏障周圍的空氣外溢，將人員與無菌製程關鍵區域分開。
  • 隔離器 依賴物理隔離、正壓差及帶有空氣外溢的鼠洞口，提供必要的隔離與保護等級。

危害性物料的特別考量

處理危害性物料時，RABS 需要人員穿戴 PPE 且房間需透過氣閘完全隔離。隔離器則透過技術措施（如適當的壓差區和隔離器完整性）維持操作人員保護。這是隔離器在處理高活性藥物成分（HPAPI）時特別受青睞的原因。

9.2.1 Aseptic Isolators / 無菌隔離器
English — Original Content

An aseptic isolator is described as a decontaminated unit which meets ISO 5/Grade A conditions on the inside and does not compromise these conditions over a specified period of time, by providing an uncompromised isolation of its interior from the surrounding environment.

9.2.1.1 Types of Isolators

Aseptic isolators can be either "open" or "closed", as defined in PDA TR 34, depending upon their operational state and may operate at positive or negative pressures with respect to the surrounding environment:

  • When "closed", isolators may exchange air with the surrounding environment only through microbial retentive filters.
  • When "open", isolators may transfer air directly to the surrounding environment through openings (e.g., mouseholes) that prevent the ingress of viable and non-viable particles.

1. Closed Isolators

Closed isolators are typically used for batch processes that do not require a high number of components. Material is placed inside the isolator before a decontamination cycle is performed, or material is transferred in via decontamination airlocks. Typical applications for a closed isolator are for a formulation process or for sterility testing.

2. Open Isolators

Open isolators are used in continuous process applications. Material is continuously transferred into the isolator via appropriate decontamination or sterilization devices. A differential pressure zoning concept guarantees a continuous airflow towards the surrounding environment to prevent particulate or microbiological ingress through transfer openings.

9.2.1.2 Considerations

The level of separation provided by isolators (both open and closed) allows for operating an isolator in an ISO 8/Grade C environment (Grade D or unclassified, but access controlled for sterility testing application), while providing ISO 5/Grade A conditions inside the isolator, after performing a surface decontamination.

A surface decontamination cycle is typically capable of six-log spore reduction. A surface decontamination cycle should be applied following any event when the enclosure is opened towards the surrounding environment.

The following should be considered for isolators:

  • Proper surface decontamination should be performed with a sporicidal agent (e.g., hydrogen peroxide).
  • Continuous positive pressure should be maintained inside the isolator.
  • Glove maintenance programs should ensure integrity and decontamination of gloves.
  • Transfer systems should ensure that the cleanliness of the isolator is not compromised.
  • Cleaning processes should ensure that all production remains are properly removed after a production batch, to a reproducible value allowing an efficient surface decontamination.
繁體中文 — 教學註解

關鍵定義：無菌隔離器

無菌隔離器是一個經過除污的單元，其內部符合 ISO 5/Grade A 條件，並在指定時間內透過提供與周圍環境不受損害的隔離，不會危及這些條件。

9.2.1.1 隔離器類型

無菌隔離器依操作狀態可分為「開放式」或「封閉式」（依 PDA TR 34 定義），可在相對於周圍環境的正壓或負壓下運行：

  • 「封閉式」隔離器僅透過微生物截留過濾器與周圍環境交換空氣。
  • 「開放式」隔離器透過防止可行及不可行微粒進入的開口（如鼠洞口）直接向周圍環境傳遞空氣。

9.2.1.2 隔離器注意事項

重要：背景環境降級的優勢

隔離器提供的隔離等級允許在 ISO 8/Grade C 環境中操作（無菌測試應用甚至可在 Grade D 或非分級但管控進出的環境中），同時隔離器內部在表面除污後提供 ISO 5/Grade A 條件。這是相比 RABS 的重要優勢 — RABS 需要 ISO 7/Grade B 背景。

表面除污週期通常能達到 六對數孢子降低（即 99.9999% 的殺滅率）。每當隔離器向周圍環境開放後，都應執行表面除污週期。

隔離器需考量的重點：

  • 使用殺孢子劑（如過氧化氫/VHP）進行適當的表面除污
  • 維持隔離器內部持續正壓
  • 手套維護計畫確保完整性及除污
  • 轉移系統不得危及隔離器的清潔度
  • 清潔製程確保所有生產殘留物被適當移除
9.2.2 Restricted Access Barrier Systems (RABS) / 限制進出屏障系統
English — Original Content

A RABS is described as an aseptic processing system that provides an enclosed environment to house an aseptic processing line and supply it with ISO 5/Grade A unidirectional air. RABS utilize rigid wall enclosure design to provide a physical separation of the process. This rigid wall enclosure is decontaminated with sporicidal disinfectant and interventions are done using installed barrier gloves. RABS are rarely opened, except as appropriate.

RABS design provides a physical separation of the process through rigid doors and gloves, while keeping air overspill into the surrounding (or positive differential pressure versus the surrounding) as the main method of separation. RABS can provide ISO 5/Grade A environments on the inside and can be located in ISO 7/Grade B surroundings. RABS should be decontaminated with a sporicidal agent and operated within a fully disinfected surrounding ISO 7/Grade B cleanroom.

9.2.2.1 Types of RABS

Operations Perspective:

1. Open RABS (oRABS)

An open RABS is designed to operate with doors closed at all times, except in rare predefined circumstances when the doors of the enclosure can be opened to perform specific interventions.

2. Closed RABS (cRABS)

A closed RABS remains closed at all times during operation. The only acceptable intervention would be for machinery setup.

Airflow Design Perspective:

1. Active RABS with Air Overspill into the Room

An active RABS with air overspill into the room uses an integral HEPA filtered air supply providing UAF to the critical process and air overspill into the room below the critical process. RABS are not suitable for hazardous products, as they spill air into the surrounding area.

2. Passive RABS with Air Overspill to the Surrounding

In a passive RABS, the airflow to the critical area is provided by ceiling mounted HEPA filters and the bottom of the enclosure is open to the room to provide for airflow through the system.

3. Active RABS with Air Returns Through HEPA Filters

An active RABS with air returns through HEPA filters uses an integral HEPA filtered air supply providing UAF to the critical process. It also uses air return through HEPA filters to prevent hazardous product migrating to the surrounding or microbial contamination migrating into the RABS. This type of RABS can be suitable for hazardous products, based on a risk assessment.

9.2.2.2 Considerations

A formal risk management program should be established for RABS to ensure the effectiveness of the design in relation with the process, as well as the efficiency of the applied disinfection program.

The following should be considered for RABS:

  • Gloves and gauntlets attached to the glove ports should be sterile when installed. A glove monitoring program should ensure proper disinfection procedures and intervals, as well as glove exchange intervals.
  • Written procedures should describe what is done when an open door intervention (which should be rare) is performed.
    • Open door interventions should be documented, described in batch records, and followed by a disinfection step.
    • Open door interventions may require a line clearance, which should be documented in batch records.
  • Direct and indirect product contact parts and fluid pathways should be sterilized prior to filling of each batch.
  • Product contact equipment should be subject to sterilization.
  • Sterile components and supplies should be transferred to the RABS without exposing sterile surfaces to less clean environments, such as the use of RTPs or disinfection airlocks.
  • Robust disinfection of all non-product contact surfaces within the RABS should be performed with a suitable sporicidal agent before each batch or campaign.
  • The effectiveness of the overall disinfection program should be demonstrated and routinely evaluated as part of the environmental monitoring program.
繁體中文 — 教學註解

關鍵定義：RABS（限制進出屏障系統）

RABS 是一種無菌製程系統，提供封閉環境來容納無菌製程線，並供應 ISO 5/Grade A 單向氣流。使用剛性壁封閉設計提供物理隔離，以殺孢子消毒劑除污，干預操作透過安裝的屏障手套進行。

關鍵差異：RABS 位於 ISO 7/Grade B 環境中（而非隔離器的 Grade C/D），且主要依靠空氣外溢而非正壓差來維持隔離。

9.2.2.1 RABS 類型

依操作方式分類：

依氣流設計分類：

9.2.2.2 RABS 注意事項

開門干預的嚴格管控

開門干預是 RABS 操作中的重大事件，必須：

  • 有書面程序描述何時及如何執行
  • 記錄在批次紀錄中
  • 干預後執行消毒步驟
  • 可能需要進行生產線清場（line clearance）

EU Annex 1（2022）對開門干預的要求更加嚴格，傾向於將需要頻繁開門干預的系統視為不符合 cRABS 定義。

其他 RABS 關鍵考量：

  • 手套口上的手套和護臂安裝時應為無菌狀態，需有手套監控計畫
  • 產品接觸零件及流體路徑需在每批充填前滅菌
