  • 無菌組件轉移至 RABS 時不得暴露於較低潔淨度環境（使用 RTP 或消毒氣閘）
  • 每批或每個活動前，需對 RABS 內所有非產品接觸表面進行強健的殺孢子劑消毒
  • 消毒計畫的有效性需經證實，並作為環境監控計畫的一部分定期評估
9.3

System Comparisons / 系統比較

p172 – p176

English — Original Content

In conventional aseptic filling operations, the filling equipment and gowned personnel operate together in a cleanroom environment. There is limited defined separation between the personnel and the production environment (e.g., flexible plastic curtains). The product and product contact exposure areas are locally protected in an ISO 5/Grade A environment.

Isolators and RABS utilize physical or aerodynamic methods (or both) to achieve separation between the inside of the containment and the surrounding environment. There are two primary differences between isolators and RABS:

Decontamination: Isolators are reproducibly decontaminated using an automated system (e.g., using VHP); such decontamination can be performed batch-wise. RABS are usually thoroughly manually disinfected. Alternatively, decontamination is performed by gassing or fogging processes together with the surrounding room. Typically, this cannot be performed batch-wise and manual disinfection may be used in conjunction with the room decontamination.

Pressure differentials: Isolators operate at an established pressure differential with respect to the surrounding environment, while RABS utilize air overspill without a defined pressure differential to achieve aerodynamic separation.

Table 9.1 contains points to be considered and highlights areas of differences among traditional cleanrooms, RABS, and isolator designs. Each system should be considered in terms of its intended use and the specific circumstances related to that use. All consideration points assume a proper design according to the latest standards of the respective technology. Poor design can have a negative impact (e.g., a poorly designed isolator can be less efficient than a well designed RABS).

繁體中文 — 教學註解

在傳統無菌充填操作中，充填設備與穿著無塵衣的人員在同一個無菌室環境中一起工作，人員與生產環境之間的定義隔離有限（如可撓式塑膠簾幕）。

設計品質的重要性

ISPE 特別強調：設計不良的隔離器可能不如設計良好的 RABS 有效。選擇技術類型只是第一步，後續的工程設計品質才是決定成敗的關鍵。這也是為什麼 ISPE 將本章定位為「需考慮的因素」而非簡單的「隔離器最佳」結論。

9.4

Factors to Consider When Choosing / 選擇技術的考量因素

p176 – p179

9.4.1 Personnel Involvement with the Aseptic Process / 人員參與無菌製程

English — Original Content

Isolator technology removes a major source of bio-contamination by eliminating direct operator intervention from the aseptic process, making it superior for aseptic/containment applications. RABS are superior to conventional manned cleanrooms for aseptic operation and can approach the superior separation provided by isolators if the doors remain closed.

繁體中文 — 教學註解

隔離器技術透過消除操作人員對無菌製程的直接干預，移除了生物污染的主要來源，使其在無菌/密封應用中具有優越性。RABS 在無菌操作方面優於傳統人員進入的無菌室，且若門保持關閉，可接近隔離器提供的優越隔離性。

CDMO 實務觀點

對 CDMO 而言，cRABS（門保持關閉）可接近隔離器的隔離等級，這是一個重要的設計決策點。如果現有設施無法容納隔離器，cRABS 是一個務實且法規可接受的選擇。

9.4.2 Labor Efficiency Gains / 人力效率提升

English — Original Content

Isolators eliminate a confining gown, close fitting hood, and face mask, leading to improved operator comfort and cost savings in laundry and cleanroom clothing sterilization (each operator can consume 4 to 5 gown sets per day). Isolator systems require reduced gowning according to the lower grade surrounding room and allow the same operator to serve several different functions on the same line without re-gowning, affording greater labor utilization and significantly reducing gowning costs.

In general, access to the aseptic processing area is no longer restricted by sterile gowning and de-gowning procedures, therefore permitting controlled, multiple access routes.

RABS do not offer these advantages as the operators need to wear full aseptic gowns and are largely restricted to a single location/function.

繁體中文 — 教學註解

隔離器消除了緊束的無菌衣、緊合頭套和面罩，改善操作人員舒適度，並節省洗衣和無塵衣滅菌成本（每位操作人員每天可消耗 4 至 5 套無塵衣）。隔離器系統因較低等級的周圍房間而降低穿衣要求，允許同一操作人員在同一生產線上服務多種不同功能而無需重新穿衣。

成本比較：具體數字

  • 每位操作人員每天 4-5 套無塵衣 → 隔離器環境下大幅減少
  • 操作人員可在不重新穿衣的情況下執行多項功能 → 更高的人力利用率
  • 不再受無菌穿衣/脫衣程序限制 → 允許受控的多重進入路徑

RABS 不具備這些優勢，因為操作人員需穿著完整無菌衣且通常被限制在單一位置/功能。

9.4.3 Containment of Hazardous Product / 危害產品的密封

English — Original Content

Isolators and active closed RABS with safe change HEPA filters in the air returns can be particularly useful for processing of chemically/biologically hazardous material when operated as closed systems from an operations and airflow perspective. RABS with air overspill to the room provide better separation than conventional cleanrooms but are not suitable if containment of hazardous materials is required.

繁體中文 — 教學註解

隔離器及配備安全更換 HEPA 過濾器回風的主動封閉式 RABS，在作為封閉系統操作時，特別適用於處理化學/生物危害性物料。空氣外溢至房間的 RABS 提供比傳統無菌室更好的隔離，但若需要密封危害物料則不適用。

危害品選擇決策樹

  • 非危害品 → oRABS、cRABS 或隔離器均可
  • 危害品 + 空氣外溢 RABS → 不適用
  • 危害品 + 主動封閉式 RABS（HEPA 回風 + 安全更換過濾器）→ 可行（需風險評估）
  • 危害品 + 隔離器 → 最佳選擇

9.4.4 Setup Time and Facility Start-Up / 建置時間與設施啟動

English — Original Content

Enclosing the process inside an isolator means that some early construction and pre-delivery testing can be performed offsite, prior to installation, while the surrounding environmental room is being constructed. RABS start-up periods are closer to those for conventional cleanrooms, as critical facility environmental systems are required and control systems are less complex than for isolators.

Control systems can be designed integrally and placed into operation with the isolator, potentially shortening facility start-up time, since isolators are independent units. This can be improved when using isolator air handling concepts that operate without interface to the building HVAC and exhaust.

繁體中文 — 教學註解

將製程封閉在隔離器中，意味著部分早期建造和交付前測試可在安裝前於場外執行，同時周圍環境室正在建造中。RABS 的啟動週期接近傳統無菌室，因為需要關鍵設施環境系統且控制系統比隔離器簡單。

專案時程優勢

隔離器作為獨立單元的特性帶來專案時程優勢：

  • 場外預製與測試（FAT）：可在設備供應商處完成大部分測試
  • 平行施工：隔離器預製與建築施工可同步進行
  • 獨立空調：使用不需與建築 HVAC 介面的隔離器空調概念，進一步縮短啟動時間

9.4.5 Capital Costs / 資本成本

English — Original Content

Isolator equipment cost usually is higher than conventional equipment and may offset initial capital cost savings gained by improved space utilization, compared to a conventional facility. RABS and associated processing considerations may be more expensive than conventional cleanrooms but are generally similar to isolators. Isolators may be the most cost-effective option for new construction. Individual cost analyses should be performed for RABS versus isolators. Consideration should be given to operational as well as capital costs, including the facility.

繁體中文 — 教學註解

隔離器設備成本通常高於傳統設備，相比傳統設施，其改善空間利用所節省的初始資本成本可能被抵消。RABS 及其相關製程考量可能比傳統無菌室更貴，但通常與隔離器相似。對於新建設施，隔離器可能是最具成本效益的選項。

成本分析要點

ISPE 指出需進行 RABS vs 隔離器的個別成本分析，且應同時考慮營運成本與資本成本。關鍵結論：

  • 設備成本：隔離器 > RABS ≈ 傳統設備
  • 設施總成本：隔離器 ≈ RABS（隔離器省下的空間和空調可抵消設備差價）
  • 新建設施：隔離器可能是最具成本效益的選項
  • 長期營運成本：隔離器明顯最低（約少 75%）

9.4.6 Operating Costs / 營運成本

English — Original Content

For most applications, the scaled down size of the aseptic process and associated air handling equipment, combined with the lower environmental class of the background room and reduced gowning and environmental monitoring requirements, results in significantly reduced operating costs for isolator systems. Operating costs for RABS designs are comparable to those for traditional cleanrooms, but the additional cost for maintaining and monitoring RABS gloves should also be considered.

繁體中文 — 教學註解

對大多數應用而言，隔離器系統的營運成本顯著降低，這得益於：無菌製程縮小的尺寸及相關空調設備、較低等級的背景房間、以及減少的穿衣和環境監控需求。RABS 設計的營運成本與傳統無菌室相當，但還需考慮維護和監控 RABS 手套的額外成本。

9.4.7 Maintenance Access / 維護通道

English — Original Content

Maintenance access (from outside the critical environment) is possible with both isolator and RABS designs. It should be considered at the start of the design process. Given the freestanding nature of isolators, access may be superior and gowning requirements minimal.

A suitable glove management program should be established for both isolators and RABS, as gloves may become brittle over time.

繁體中文 — 教學註解

隔離器和 RABS 設計都可以從關鍵環境外部進行維護。應在設計過程開始時就考慮此議題。鑒於隔離器的獨立式特性，其維護通道可能更優越且穿衣要求最低。

隔離器和 RABS 都應建立適當的手套管理計畫，因為手套可能隨時間變脆。手套完整性測試是兩種系統的關鍵品質要求。

9.4.8 Flexibility of the Equipment / 設備靈活性

English — Original Content

Isolator flexibility is increased by the reduced footprint of the ISO 5/Grade A area; there is also less facility area to clean between batches.

Various process equipment may be docked into isolator systems, via direct interfaces between the process equipment and isolator system.

繁體中文 — 教學註解

隔離器的靈活性因 ISO 5/Grade A 區域佔地面積縮小而增加，批次間需清潔的設施面積也較少。各種製程設備可透過製程設備與隔離器系統之間的直接介面對接至隔離器系統。

CDMO 靈活性考量

對 CDMO 而言，設備靈活性至關重要：

  • 隔離器的模組化對接能力允許快速更換製程設備
  • 較小的 Grade A 區域意味著更快的批次間轉換
  • 多產品設施中，隔離器的密封特性也有助於防止交叉污染

9.4.9 Ergonomics / 人因工程

English — Original Content

The position of the glove ports, half-suits, and interfaces with the operator should be considered, as the aseptic method may suffer if the operator is uncomfortable. Efficient layouts should be developed for both isolators and RABS. Typically, an ergonomic mockup study is performed during the design phase of the project to ensure all process steps can be performed properly.

繁體中文 — 教學註解

手套口、半身防護衣及操作人員介面的位置應仔細考量，因為如果操作人員不舒適，無菌方法可能受到影響。隔離器和 RABS 都應開發高效的佈局。

人因工程模型研究

通常在專案設計階段進行人因工程模型研究（Ergonomic Mockup Study），以確保所有製程步驟都能正確執行。這對 CDMO 尤其重要 — 操作人員需在手套口和半身防護衣的限制下完成所有干預操作，不當設計會導致：

  • 操作人員疲勞增加 → 錯誤率上升
  • 手套/半身衣損壞風險提高
  • 製程中斷頻率增加

9.4.10 Airflow within the Enclosure / 封閉體內的氣流

English — Original Content

Airflow within the enclosure should be unidirectional at the product, container, or closure exposure points wherever product is exposed and according to GMP regulations.

The purpose of the UAF is to protect the product from viable and non-viable particles.

Turbulent flow might be applied in specific cases when required by the process, for example:

  • When the system design can guarantee that no particulates generated during the process can create an out of specification result
  • In quality control applications, such as sterility testing

The airflow can help to achieve faster decontamination cycles, especially to aerate decontamination agents at the end of a cycle. Poor airflow design can result in long decontamination cycles that can impact the productivity of the facility.

The impact of the airflow on the temperature distribution inside the enclosure should also be considered.

繁體中文 — 教學註解

封閉體內的氣流在產品、容器或封蓋暴露點處應為單向，凡產品暴露處均依 GMP 法規要求。UAF 的目的是保護產品免受可行及不可行微粒的影響。

在特定情況下可使用紊流（turbulent flow），例如系統設計能保證製程中產生的微粒不會造成超標結果時，或在品管應用如無菌測試中。

氣流設計的生產力影響

氣流設計不良會導致：

  • 除污週期延長（特別是週期末端除污劑的通風排氣階段）
  • 封閉體內溫度分布不均
  • 設施生產力下降

良好的氣流設計能加速除污週期，特別是在除污劑的通風排氣階段。

9.4.11 Pressure Differential / 壓差

English — Original Content

In an open RABS, the air overspill to the surroundings generates a dynamic barrier for contamination.

Isolators should be maintained at positive pressure relative to their surroundings in order to prevent ingress of any contamination from the external environment. The differential pressure levels are typically between 15 – 50 Pa to avoid ingress of contamination through transfer openings (such as mouseholes) and other potential openings.

Higher differential pressures provide better separation (air velocity should be ≥ 0.2 m/s according to ISO 14644-4). High differential pressures also generate high airflows between isolator chambers. This should be accounted for when specifying differential pressures, as airflows might compromise the UAF inside the enclosure or have an impact on the process itself (e.g., powder dosing, vial falling).

Reverse flow might be generated at mouseholes with high air velocity. The proper design can be shown with smoke studies.

When handling hazardous materials, a differential pressure concept should be established, using multiple differential pressure zones. The concept needs to ensure that the level of contamination escaping to the surrounding area is below any critical limits. One possibility is to add a higher pressure zone at the mousehole of the critical zone.

If out of specification results occur, a risk assessment should be performed to define necessary actions. Appropriate microbial monitoring results may prevent loss of a batch.

繁體中文 — 教學註解

在開放式 RABS 中，向周圍的空氣外溢產生動態污染屏障。

隔離器應維持相對於周圍環境的正壓，以防止外部環境任何污染的進入。壓差水準通常在 15 至 50 Pa 之間，以避免污染透過傳輸開口（如鼠洞口）及其他潛在開口進入。

危害物料的多壓差區概念

處理危害物料時，應建立使用多個壓差區的壓差概念。一種可能性是在關鍵區域的鼠洞口添加較高壓力區，防止氣流從此附加區域流入關鍵區域，避免周圍環境受到污染。

壓差設計的權衡

依 ISO 14644-4，空氣速度應 ≥ 0.2 m/s。適當設計可透過煙霧測試（smoke studies）驗證。

S

Section Summary / 章節總結

English — Key Takeaways

Technology Hierarchy

Isolator — Highest Separation
↓
cRABS — Doors Always Closed
↓
oRABS — Rare Door Opening
↓
Conventional Cleanroom — Becoming Unacceptable

Key definitions to remember:

  • oRABS: Doors closed at all times except in rare predefined circumstances for specific interventions
  • cRABS: Remains closed at all times during operation; only acceptable intervention is for machinery setup
  • Isolator: Decontaminated unit meeting ISO 5/Grade A providing uncompromised isolation from surrounding environment

Two primary differences between isolator and RABS:

  1. Decontamination: Isolators use automated, reproducible VHP cycles; RABS typically use manual disinfection
  2. Pressure: Isolators maintain defined pressure differential; RABS use air overspill without defined differential

Decision factors (9.4): Personnel involvement, labor efficiency, hazardous containment, setup time, capital costs, operating costs, maintenance access, flexibility, ergonomics, airflow design, and pressure differential.

繁體中文 — 重點摘要

CDMO 設施設計決策重點

本章是 CDMO 設施設計決策的核心參考。關鍵結論：

  1. 新建設施：強烈建議隔離器 — 總體成本可能相似，但營運成本低約 75%，且法規最受認可
  2. 改造既有設施：cRABS 是務實選擇 — 若門保持關閉，可接近隔離器的隔離等級
  3. 危害品處理：隔離器為首選；主動封閉式 RABS（HEPA 回風）為替代方案
  4. 傳統無菌室：法規上日益不被接受，業界也不再視為首選

自我檢測題

  1. oRABS 和 cRABS 在操作干預方面的關鍵區別是什麼？
  2. 隔離器可在什麼等級的背景環境中操作？RABS 呢？
  3. 為什麼空氣外溢型 RABS 不適用於危害品處理？
  4. 隔離器的營運成本為何能比傳統無菌室低約 75%？列舉至少三個節省來源。
  5. 壓差設定在 15-50 Pa 的範圍內，設定較高壓差有什麼潛在風險？

與 EU Annex 1（2022）的關聯

EU GMP Annex 1（2022 修訂版）強烈推動朝向隔離器和 cRABS 的方向發展。關鍵條款包括：

  • 明確偏好屏障技術優於傳統無菌室
  • 對開門干預的嚴格限制和記錄要求
  • 強調自動化除污的可重現性
  • 要求基於風險評估的技術選擇

本章的內容與 Annex 1 高度一致，為 CDMO 的合規設計提供了實務基礎。

7b

Chapter 7b: 9b. Barrier & Isolator (9.5–9.10)

屏障與隔離器（下） | p179-p188

ISPE Baseline Guide Vol. 3 (3rd Ed.) | p179 – p188

Learning Objectives / 本章學習目標

  • Understand equipment design principles for isolator and RABS interiors, including ergonomics, transfer systems, and glove systems / 理解隔離器與RABS內部設備設計原則，包含人體工學、物料傳遞系統及手套系統
  • Master the VHP decontamination cycle development process: cleaning, bio-decontamination, aeration, and validation with biological indicators / 掌握VHP去污循環開發流程：清潔、生物去污、排氣及生物指示劑驗證
  • Apply environmental monitoring strategies specific to barrier systems / 應用屏障系統專屬的環境監測策略
  • Evaluate leak rate testing methods and acceptance criteria for isolators / 評估隔離器洩漏率測試方法與可接受標準
  • Implement preventive maintenance programs for gloves, seals, and HEPA filters / 建立手套、密封件及HEPA濾網的預防性維護計畫
  • Recognize the importance of structured operator training for barrier system operations / 認識屏障系統操作員結構化培訓的重要性
9.5 Equipment Design for Inside an Isolator or RABS 9.5 隔離器或 RABS 內部設備設計

Original Text

Equipment should be designed with the ergonomics of operating through glove ports in mind. The use of robotics or manipulators should be part of the design of isolators and RABS. This helps to minimize the potential for microbial contamination, by assuring better protection of the sterile product during aseptic processing. Considerations for equipment design inside an isolator or RABS include:

  • Format parts should be accessible via glove ports and the change should be designed as a one hand operation and tool-less, if possible.
  • Tools, such as forceps, should be used to separate the glove from the process.
  • Critical areas, where product is exposed to the surrounding, should not be covered with any parts or moving equipment, to allow proper UAF over the product.
  • Large components (e.g., stopper bowls) should be perforated to allow the airflow to penetrate as much as possible.
  • Obstructed surfaces should be avoided.
  • The interface of the equipment to the isolator should be gas tight. Penetrations (e.g., shafts and drives) should be sealed.
  • If the equipment requires shaft movements up and down through the base plate, such shafts should be protected by either a specific dynamic air barrier or bellows, to avoid ingress of contamination during operation.
  • Parts that undergo maintenance should be designed to be external to the ISO 5/Grade A environment.
  • The use of automated equipment should be considered, where feasible, to minimize human involvement within the controlled environment.
  • Half-suits may help operators to access equipment. Half-suits should be of good ergonomic design, cleanable, able to be decontaminated, and should undergo integrity testing.

For isolators and RABS that are decontaminated by gassing or fogging using sporicidal agents, the following should be considered for exposed equipment materials:

  • Chemical/corrosion resistance against decontamination agents used
  • No catalytic effect on decontamination agents
  • Potential impact on the decontamination efficiency of the surface structure of materials

The surface structure of materials can have an impact on the decontamination efficiency. Material studies should be performed to show the impact on the D-value of different surface materials. The results should be taken into consideration when validating decontamination efficiency inside an isolator.

The control system for the filling equipment should be configured to permit slow motion movement during decontamination of the isolator, to expose all the equipment surfaces to the decontamination agent.

Ergonomic design should allow access for all surfaces to be cleaned effectively, prior to gaseous surface decontamination. Before a decontamination cycle begins, the isolator should be mechanically clean (and dry, depending on the decontaminating agent). This may necessitate a manual cleaning and a drying step prior to decontamination.

導師解析

核心概念：隔離器內設備設計原則

人體工學優先（Ergonomics First）：所有設備操作都必須考慮「透過手套口操作」的限制。操作員戴著厚手套，手指靈活度有限，因此設備設計必須盡可能簡化——單手操作、免工具更換格式件是黃金標準。

UAF（單向氣流）保護：關鍵區域（產品暴露處）上方不能有遮擋物或活動設備，確保單向氣流能直接覆蓋產品，這是無菌保護的第一道防線。

D-Value（D值）：指在特定去污條件下，將微生物數量減少90%（1-log）所需的時間。不同表面材質的D值不同，粗糙表面可能使微生物更難被去污劑接觸到。

比喻說明

想像你戴著厚厚的滑雪手套在廚房做菜。你會希望所有器具都很容易拿起、刀具有大握把、瓶蓋是旋轉式而非需要指尖捏的按壓式。隔離器內的設備設計邏輯完全一樣——一切都要為「戴手套操作」而優化。

重點提示：慢動作模式

去污循環期間，充填設備的控制系統應設定為慢速運動模式（slow motion movement）。目的是讓所有設備表面都能被 VHP 接觸到。如果設備靜止不動，被遮蔽的表面（如活塞下方、傳動軸後方）可能無法被去污劑覆蓋，造成去污盲區。

練習思考

  1. 你的充填線隔離器內有哪些設備零件需要「穿越底板」（shaft movements through base plate）？目前是用氣動屏障還是波紋管（bellows）來保護？
  2. 列出你的隔離器內使用的所有材質。是否做過不同材質的 D-value 比較研究？
9.5.1 Component and Equipment Transfers 9.5.1 組件與設備轉移

Original Text

Transfer systems are used to transfer containers, product, monitoring material, and tools in and out of the enclosure. Ingress of contamination through transfer systems should be avoided. Weaknesses of transfer systems (e.g., ring of concern in RTP) should be considered. Proper manipulation and suitably trained operators can help to control risk associated with transfer systems.

Types of transfer systems include:

  • Dry heat tunnels to sterilize glass containers in-line into the ISO 5/Grade A environment
  • Electron beam (e-beam) tunnels to sterilize heat sensitive products in-line (e.g., pre-sterilized syringes in tubs)
  • RTPs designed for batch transfer of externally sterilized materials (e.g., filling pumps, stoppers, single-use assemblies)
  • Liquid transfer systems to connect bulk containers to the filling system inside an isolator
  • Transfer air locks, with the use of VHP as a surface decontamination method, to transfer heat sensitive materials, non-direct product contact parts, and bagged sterilized goods

Special consideration should be given to all interfaces for product transfer. If supply material is introduced from a lower grade area into a higher grade area by shedding an outer layer, an additional bioburden reduction step should be applied.

For isolator applications, a 6-log reduction is typically required (a minimum of 4-log can be satisfactory for very low bioburden surfaces); for RABS, a 3-log reduction is typically acceptable.

When transfers involve toxic compounds, a thorough risk assessment is required to define appropriate cleaning procedures. The efficiency of aseptic connectors should be validated during media fill.

導師解析

核心概念：物料傳遞系統

RTP（Rapid Transfer Port, 快速傳遞口）：用於批次傳入已滅菌物料（如膠塞、充填泵浦）。RTP的關鍵弱點是「ring of concern（關注環）」——兩個對接面之間的微小縫隙，是微生物可能滲入的風險區域。

Log Reduction（對數下降值）：衡量去污或滅菌效果的量化指標。6-log表示將微生物從100萬個降到1個（106 → 100）。隔離器要求6-log，RABS要求3-log，反映了兩者在密封度和風險等級上的本質差異。

比喻說明

物料傳遞系統就像太空站的氣閘門（airlock）。太空人從外太空回到太空站時，不能直接打開艙門（否則空氣全跑光）——必須先進入氣閘室、關閉外門、加壓、確認安全後才能開內門。同理，物料進入隔離器也需要一個「緩衝機制」，根據物料類型選擇適當的log reduction方法。

重點提示：傳遞方法選擇

Table 9.2 是選擇傳遞方法的決策依據。關鍵判斷邏輯：

  • 隔離器：需要 ≥6-log → 選擇乾熱隧道、高壓滅菌、VHP氣閘或e-beam
  • RABS：需要 ≥3-log → 殺孢子劑隧道或脈衝光/UV可能足夠
  • 連續生產 vs. 批次：乾熱隧道和e-beam支援連續傳遞，適合高速充填線；RTP和高壓滅菌適合批次更換
9.5.2 Glove Systems and Half-Suits 9.5.2 手套系統與半身防護衣

Original Text

The type of glove to be used depends on the application and on the replacement cost of different assemblies. Gloves can be:

  • One-piece gloves
  • Two-piece gloves with sleeves
  • Half-suits with arms and gloves (if required by the process)

Inspection, cleaning, and disinfection should be considered for gloves and half-suits mounted in both isolators and RABS. Maintenance can be difficult for a half-suit, as it has a large surface area. Care should be taken when cleaning and integrity testing half-suits.

Gloves, gloves with sleeves or half-suit system are considered the weakest part of the system and can develop leaks. Automation of the process can minimize operator interventions that necessitate the use of gloves and half-suits. The impact of any leakage requires thorough investigation and evaluation.

Occurrences of leakages can be reduced by using robust materials in conjunction with appropriate maintenance and inspection regimes. The use of a thin sterile glove liner worn by the operator, as part of a gowning regime and coupled with hand disinfection, may protect the glove from bio-contamination and reduce risk in case of damage.

Bioburden data may be collected on the non-process side of the gloves, for both isolators and RABS. All media should be removed from the glove after sampling.

Daily visual inspection and regular physical glove testing should demonstrate that the gloves retain their integrity and are, therefore, acceptable for continued use. This can significantly reduce the risk of an undetected pinhole.

The physical test is typically performed on open isolator/RABS doors before the enclosure is closed and decontaminated. Commercially available test systems typically use the pressure decay method, measuring a pressure drop inside the glove/sleeve, or the constant pressure method, measuring the leak rate as a flow. Physical test methods cannot detect holes measuring down to several micrometers and, therefore, cannot completely prevent microbiological contamination.

Studies show that a visual test by a trained operator can detect holes on white gloves with a high precision. This is a convenient method and should be performed frequently.

A preventive glove replacement program can help to avoid sudden out of specification results. How frequently gloves, sleeves, and half-suits need to be replaced depends on the frequency of use, the cleaning agents used, and the mechanical stress applied during the process.

Cleaning of Gloves

Gloves are a potential source to transport contamination from one point to another; therefore, a proper cleaning process should be applied. Cleaning has the following purposes:

  • New gloves are typically covered with a lubricant layer caused by the manufacturing process. This layer can cover contamination and prevent an efficient decontamination process. New gloves need to be cleaned thoroughly before being installed.
  • In the case of a pinhole, a high bioburden load on the outside of the glove may increase the risk of contamination on the inside; therefore, gloves need to be manually wiped and cleaned regularly on the inside and the outside.
  • As gloves, especially finger tips, are touching different surfaces inside an isolator/RABS, the risk of enabling bioburden contamination can be significant. A regular manual wipe and cleaning process needs to be applied.

導師解析

核心概念：手套完整性測試

Glove Integrity Testing（手套完整性測試）：手套是隔離器/RABS中最脆弱的環節。測試方法有兩種主流：

  • Pressure Decay Method（壓力衰減法）：將手套充氣加壓，測量一段時間內的壓力下降。壓降超過標準表示有洩漏。
  • Constant Pressure Method（恆壓法）：維持手套內恆定壓力，測量維持壓力所需的補氣流量。流量越大，洩漏越嚴重。

重要限制：物理測試無法偵測到微米級的針孔（pinhole），因此不能完全排除微生物污染風險。這就是為什麼還需要搭配目視檢查和預防性更換計畫。

重點提示：手套是「最脆弱的環節」

ISPE明確指出手套系統是整個屏障系統中最薄弱的部分。這句話的實務意義是：

  • 任何手套洩漏都需要進行徹底調查與影響評估（thorough investigation）
  • 自動化程度越高，手套使用頻率越低，風險越低
  • 操作員應配戴無菌手套內襯（sterile glove liner）作為額外保護層
  • 白色手套比深色手套更容易用目視檢查發現破洞

比喻說明

手套就像潛水衣。即使潛水衣只有一個微小的針孔，水就會慢慢滲入，最終影響潛水員的體溫和安全。同樣地，隔離器手套的任何微小洩漏都可能讓外部環境的微生物進入無菌區域。這就是為什麼需要「多重防線」：定期物理測試 + 每日目視檢查 + 預防性更換 + 無菌內襯手套。

最佳實踐建議

  • 建立預防性手套更換計畫，基於使用頻率、清潔劑類型和機械應力決定更換週期
  • 新手套安裝前必須徹底清洗，去除製造過程中的潤滑劑層
  • 定期收集手套非製程面的生物負荷數據，追蹤趨勢
  • 使用白色手套以提高目視檢查的偵測率
9.5.3–9.5.5 Background Environment, Monitoring & Classification 9.5.3–9.5.5 背景環境、監測與分級

Original Text

9.5.3 Background Environment

The classification of the background environment in which the enclosure is located should be based on a risk assessment that considers the design choice and operational characteristics of the chosen system and its associated transfer mechanisms and discharge ports (e.g., mouseholes).

  • For a globally compliant facility, the isolator background should be ISO 8/Grade C. A Grade D environment which is classified as ISO 8 "in operation" as well as "at rest" is also possible.
  • Quality control isolators providing aseptic conditions for test environments (e.g., sterility test) with no dynamically sealed openings to the surrounding room can be situated in CNC areas.
  • RABS designs require an aseptic processing environment external to the enclosure, typically ISO 7/Grade B.

9.5.4 Background Monitoring

Monitoring of cleanliness classes should be applied as specified for the relevant ISO/Grade classification. The monitoring efforts with isolators are normally significantly lower than for RABS, due to the reduced foot print and the surrounding environment being a cleaner grade for RABS as compared to isolators.

9.5.5 Enclosure Classification

The inner environment should meet ISO 5/Grade A.

導師解析

重點提示：監測成本差異

RABS的背景環境是Grade B，需要更嚴格的微粒和微生物監測，這意味著更高的日常營運成本。隔離器的背景環境只需Grade C（甚至可接受Grade D達到ISO 8 in-operation），監測工作量顯著降低。這是許多新建廠房傾向選擇隔離器的經濟因素之一。

核心概念：背景環境分級差異

隔離器與RABS在背景環境要求上的差異是兩者選擇的關鍵考量之一：

CNC（Controlled Not Classified）：品管無菌檢驗用隔離器如果沒有動態密封開口，可以放在CNC區域——有出入控制和定期清潔，但不做微粒或微生物監測。這能大幅降低QC實驗室的設施成本。

9.6 Decontamination Cycle Development (Isolators) 9.6 去污週期開發（隔離器）

Original Text

9.6.1 Cleaning and Surface Decontamination

Before any bio-decontamination is performed, an efficient cleaning needs to be applied to critical surfaces. Cleaning can either be performed manually or, if applicable, with automated WIP/CIP cycles.

The design of the enclosure and all integrated equipment needs to be compatible with cleaning processes and cleaning agents.

Cleaning validation needs to prove the efficiency of the cleaning process and its ability to avoid cross-contamination or exposure of hazardous substances to the surrounding when opening the enclosure. Removal of cleaning residuals after the cleaning process should be considered, as they may impact bio-decontamination efficiency or may be of concern to the product handled inside the isolator or RABS. Failure or incomplete cleaning can prevent exposure of hydrogen peroxide and may lead to failure of the bio-decontamination cycle.

Cycle development should be performed to establish the parameters and bio-decontamination capabilities and limits that reflect the different volumes, contours, and loading patterns within an isolator or RABS. Validation should prove that developed parameters are accurate.

The necessary level of bio-decontamination should be determined on the basis of risk assessment and analysis.

To measure the decontamination efficiency inside the isolator, biological indicators (Geobacillus stearothermophilus) are typically used to demonstrate a 6-log reduction during validation and revalidation.

In isolators, surface bio-decontamination is performed after cleaning and closing the enclosure. This is typically a fully automated process using vaporized or fogged hydrogen peroxide (VHP). After achieving the specified bio-decontamination efficiency, the bio-decontamination agent is aerated out of the isolator by either venting with HEPA filtered fresh air or by using catalytic converters to break down the hydrogen peroxide into water and oxygen.

In RABS, bio-decontamination can be performed manually with sporicidal agents via open doors. In newer RABS, automated decontamination systems using vaporized or fogged hydrogen peroxide may be used. In RABS applications, typically only a 3 to 4-log reduction is demonstrated.

The main difference between an isolator and a RABS is that a RABS is located in an ISO 7/Grade B environment and, therefore, the decontamination also needs to include the surrounding environment.

Although bio-decontamination is performed on the isolator and RABS, the indirect product contact parts (e.g., stopper tracks) should preferably be SIP or autoclaved. Where such parts cannot be sterilized in an autoclave (e.g., vibratory feeding bowls), a hydrogen peroxide decontamination system can be utilized after a thorough manual cleaning has been performed. The process should be validated and achieve a 6-log reduction of an appropriate challenge organism.

導師解析

核心概念：VHP去污循環

VHP（Vaporized Hydrogen Peroxide, 汽化過氧化氫）循環是隔離器最常用的生物去污方法。完整循環包含四個階段：

  1. 清潔（Cleaning）：手動或自動（WIP/CIP）清潔所有關鍵表面，去除殘留物質
  2. 去污（Decontamination）：密封隔離器後，注入VHP蒸氣覆蓋所有內部表面
  3. 暴露/維持（Exposure/Dwell）：維持足夠的VHP濃度和時間以達到6-log reduction
  4. 排氣（Aeration）：用HEPA過濾新鮮空氣或催化轉化器將H2O2分解為水和氧氣

核心概念：生物指示劑（BI）

Biological Indicator, BI（生物指示劑）：使用Geobacillus stearothermophilus（嗜熱脂肪芽孢桿菌）孢子作為挑戰微生物。這種孢子對VHP有高度抗性，如果能達到6-log reduction（殺死100萬個孢子中的99.9999%），就證明去污循環對一般環境微生物綽綽有餘。

BI應放置在隔離器內最難到達的位置（worst-case locations），如死角、設備下方、管路連接處等。

重點提示：清潔是去污的前提

ISPE特別強調：不完整的清潔可能導致去污循環失敗。原因包括：

  • 殘留物質（如產品、清潔劑）可能遮蔽微生物，使VHP無法接觸
  • 清潔劑殘留可能與H2O2產生化學反應，降低去污效率
  • 濕氣會影響VHP的分佈和效能

因此，去污前必須確保隔離器「機械清潔且乾燥」。

練習思考

  1. 你的隔離器VHP循環中，BI放置點有多少個？是否涵蓋了所有「最差情況位置」？
  2. 間接產品接觸件（如膠塞軌道）是否採用SIP或高壓滅菌？如果有無法高壓滅菌的零件（如振動進料碗），如何處理？
9.6.2–9.6.5 Bio-Decontamination Systems, Surface Finishes, Aeration & Airflow 9.6.2–9.6.5 生物去污系統、表面處理、通氣與氣流

Original Text

9.6.2 Bio-Decontamination Systems

There are several types of bio-decontamination systems available for use with isolators or RABS. Methods using vaporized or fogged hydrogen peroxide (H2O2) are most commonly used. Other methods such as chlorine dioxide (ClO2) or nitrogen dioxide (NO2) are available. The following criteria should be considered when selecting the bio-decontamination method:

  • Resistance of surface materials to the selected decontamination agent
  • Decontamination efficiency on all surfaces inside the enclosure
  • Integrity of the enclosure based on the Threshold Limit Value (TLV) of the decontamination agent (e.g., 0.5 ppm for H2O2, 0.1 ppm for ClO2)
  • Ability to aerate or neutralize the decontamination agent after the process

Precautions should be taken at the design stage to define load volume, configuration, and packing materials. Particular attention should be paid to areas where there is poor vapor circulation and poor accessibility for prior cleaning (e.g., masked surfaces such as beneath bottles and component packs, dead ends caused by the presence of sensors and pipework).

9.6.3 Surface Finishes

Considerations for surface finishes include:

  • Cleanability of the surfaces before and after the process
  • Guaranteeing an efficient bio-decontamination with vaporized, fogged, or gaseous decontamination agents, as cracks and crevices might shadow potential biological contamination that may not be exposed to the bio-decontaminant. Studies show different D-values of the same type spores on different surface materials.

9.6.4 Removal of the Decontaminant – Aeration

The aeration phase after the decontamination cycle is important to reduce the level of decontamination agent to acceptable levels to expose to the environment (e.g., through open mouseholes), as well as to the product. Some products are very sensitive to oxidation; in such cases it might be necessary to aerate the inside of the enclosure down to low levels (parts per billion (ppb)).

Aeration is typically achieved by diluting the inside of the enclosure with HEPA filtered air until the specified residual levels have been reached. Fresh air can be taken from the surrounding room or provided by makeup air units. Catalytic converters allow aerating of the enclosure in a circulation loop and can provide significant HVAC cost savings.

Aeration time studies should consider that decontamination agents can be adsorbed by some materials, such as gloves and other plastic materials. Packed materials (e.g., steam sterilized components packed in Tyvek paper) should also be considered, as the decontamination agent may penetrate the packaging material and aeration can be more challenging.

The aeration cycle should be performed at a positive differential pressure to the surrounding environment.

9.6.5 Airflow Modeling

Air handling systems are fundamental to the performance of decontamination processes. Air handling systems should provide even distribution of the decontamination vapor and efficient aeration.

The design of an air handling system should consider half-suits, gauntlets, wrist collars, and gloves in regard to areas likely to be shadowed from the decontaminant vapor. Frames inserted into the suit or gauntlet can ensure the garment is fully deployed. Gauntlets, wrist collars, and gloves, including fingers, should be fully extended and separated, and should not mask any surface during decontamination.

導師解析

重點提示：排氣（Aeration）的隱藏挑戰

排氣階段往往是最耗時的步驟，實務上常見的陷阱包括：

  • 材料吸附：手套和塑膠材料會吸附H2O2，然後緩慢釋放，延長排氣時間
  • 包裝材料滲透：Tyvek包裝內的已滅菌組件可能吸收VHP，排氣特別困難
  • 對氧化敏感的產品：某些生物製劑對氧化極度敏感，可能需要將殘留H2O2降至ppb級別
  • 催化轉化器：可在循環迴路中加速H2O2分解，顯著降低排氣時間和HVAC成本

比喻說明

VHP排氣就像新裝潢的房子散味。即使你打開窗戶通風（HEPA過濾空氣沖洗），油漆和木材仍會持續釋放殘餘氣體（就像手套吸附VHP後緩慢釋出）。如果你安裝空氣清淨機（催化轉化器），可以大幅加速這個過程。而且排氣時必須保持正壓——就像你不希望外面的灰塵在通風時飄進新裝潢的房間。

練習思考

  1. 你的隔離器使用哪種去污劑？排氣時間通常多長？是否使用催化轉化器？
  2. 去污循環期間，半身衣和手套的手指是否有展開機構（frames）確保蒸氣能覆蓋所有表面？
  3. 如果你的產品對氧化敏感，你會如何設定H2O2殘留的可接受限度？

核心概念：去污劑選擇與TLV

TLV（Threshold Limit Value, 閾限值）：操作員可安全暴露的去污劑最大濃度。

TLV越低的去污劑，對隔離器密封性（leak rate）的要求越嚴格，因為即使微量洩漏也可能使周圍環境濃度超標。

9.7 Environmental Monitoring 9.7 環境監測

Original Text

Environmental monitoring schedules for isolators and RABS are similar to those for a classified cleanroom. The aseptic quality of the sampling apparatus should be considered, in order to avoid false contamination of the sample. Non-invasive sampling is preferred, for example:

  • Sampling heads inside and equipment located outside the containment
  • Use of equipment exposed to the same decontamination regime as the isolator

Use of environmental monitoring equipment should be validated to ensure the results are comparable to those obtained by local sampling, because of the potential for microorganism capture in the sampling tubing. In addition, swab samples and contact plates can provide useful data.

Environmental monitoring positions should be determined during ergonomic studies for both isolators and RABS, to ensure that manipulations can be performed without compromising the integrity of the containment.

It may be possible to reduce the number of sample locations and/or frequency, depending on the level of separation of the operator from the process. This should be supported by a risk assessment.

The transfer of materials and liquids to and from the enclosure can present a significant challenge to the sterility of the system, in addition to the background challenge of the surrounding environment.

Additionally, the special requirements of glove systems should be considered, especially since a number of operators using the same gloves presents a challenge to the hygiene of the glove system.

導師解析

核心概念：屏障系統內的環境監測

Environmental Monitoring, EM（環境監測）：屏障系統內的EM有其獨特挑戰：

  • 非侵入式取樣（Non-invasive sampling）：取樣探頭放在隔離器內部，但控制設備和讀取裝置放在外部。這避免了因開啟取樣口而破壞屏障完整性的風險。
  • 取樣設備的無菌品質：取樣器具本身必須經過與隔離器相同的去污處理（VHP），否則可能引入假陽性。
  • 取樣管路中的微生物捕獲：遠端取樣設備的管路可能截留微生物，導致結果不能真實反映隔離器內部狀態。需要驗證遠端取樣結果與現場取樣的等效性。

重點提示：風險評估驅動的監測頻率

與傳統潔淨室不同，屏障系統可以根據「操作員與製程的隔離程度」來降低取樣點數量和/或頻率——但必須有風險評估支持。這是一個常見的法規審查重點：如果你的監測計畫比傳統潔淨室精簡，稽核員會要求你出示支持的風險評估文件。

比喻說明

在隔離器內做環境監測，就像在手術室的無菌區域做空氣品質檢測——你不能為了採樣而打開無菌區域的門。所以你需要用「伸進去的探針」（非侵入式取樣頭）來收集數據，同時確保探針本身是無菌的。

練習思考

  1. 你的隔離器EM取樣點是非侵入式還是需要開啟取樣口？如果是後者，是否評估過對屏障完整性的影響？
  2. 多名操作員共用同一副手套時，你的手套衛生管理程序是什麼？是否有足夠的消毒頻率？
9.8 Leak Rate 9.8 洩漏率

Original Text

The integrity of the enclosure should prevent:

  • Hazardous decontamination agents to escape during the decontamination process
  • Hazardous product escape during production
  • Ingress of contamination that could harm the product quality

During the decontamination process, the isolator needs to be kept in constant positive pressure to the surrounding environment. A potential leak in the enclosure can generate an increased concentration in the surroundings. The maximum allowable size of such a leak depends on the following parameters:

  • Differential pressure
  • Concentration inside enclosure
  • Volume of the surrounding area
  • Fresh air exchanges of the surrounding area
  • Acceptable concentration for an operator

Where hazardous products are used, similar considerations (i.e., those for decontamination agents) can be applied to determine an acceptable leak rate during production. Only airborne contamination can escape. In enclosures with UAF, only surfaces on the downstream side of the airflow and return ducts are exposed to such contamination.

The ingress of contamination can be prevented by providing a continuous positive pressure to the enclosure. Airflow around mouseholes may generate turbulence and cause inflow of air; therefore, mouseholes are usually protected by HEPA filtered airflow on the outside of the enclosure.

9.8.1 Leak Rate Test Methods

Leak rates can be determined by closing the enclosure with gas tight flaps and applying a pressure drop test or a constant pressure test. Both tests are typically performed at double operating pressure.

As for aseptic isolators that are not in contact with potent or hazardous products and for RABS applications, the only risk is the leakage of decontamination agent during decontamination. Continuous monitoring of the decontamination agent concentration in the surrounding room can be sufficient, if openings (such as doors) are position controlled and gloves are leak tested individually.

During installation, a tracer gas (such as helium or ammonia) or soap solutions can be used to identify a leak. Although these methods may be an efficient way to find a leak, they are not useful for routine operation.

導師解析

核心概念：洩漏率測試

Leak Rate Testing（洩漏率測試）驗證隔離器的密封完整性。兩種主要方法：

  • Pressure Drop Test（壓力衰減測試）：密封隔離器，加壓至操作壓力的兩倍，測量壓力下降速率。壓降速率越低，密封性越好。
  • Constant Pressure Test（恆壓測試）：維持隔離器在設定壓力，測量需要補充多少氣體來維持壓力。補氣量越少，密封性越好。

Tracer Gas（示蹤氣體）：安裝階段使用氦氣或氨氣定位洩漏點。氦氣偵測器可以精確找到微小洩漏位置，但不適合日常操作使用。

重點提示：洩漏率的三重保護目的

洩漏率測試不只是「測密封性」這麼簡單——它同時保護三個方向：

  1. 向外保護操作員：防止VHP或有害產品洩漏到操作環境（OEL/TLV考量）
  2. 向外防止產品散逸：高活性藥物（ADC、荷爾蒙等）不能外洩
  3. 向內保護產品：防止外部污染物侵入無菌環境（正壓防護）

最大可接受洩漏率取決於五個參數的組合計算，不是一個固定數值。

比喻說明

洩漏率測試就像測試游泳池是否漏水。你可以觀察水位下降速度（pressure drop test），或是量測需要補多少水才能維持水位（constant pressure test）。而在最初施工時，你會用染料（類似示蹤氣體）倒入水中來找出具體的漏點。

練習思考

  1. 你的隔離器洩漏率測試是在多少倍操作壓力下進行？測試頻率是多少？
  2. Mousehole（鼠洞口）是否配備HEPA過濾氣流保護？是否曾在煙霧測試中觀察到turbulence？
9.9 Maintenance 9.9 維護

Original Text

An adequate, condition-based, preventative maintenance program should be used to assist in sterility assurance.

Ergonomic modeling should consider the requirements of maintenance personnel who perform ongoing running adjustments to the equipment. Designs should consider the maintenance aspects of the enclosure, its support services, and also the equipment contained therein. Provision of maintenance access panels should be considered.

Maintenance should also consider:

  • Filters
  • Gaskets
  • Seals
  • Items specific to an enclosure, such as door seals, transfer port gaskets, and the attachment of glove rings to glazing panels

HEPA filters and gloves should be replaced on a regular and scheduled basis, along with other components, as part of a maintenance program.

Protocols should be developed for the calibration of sensors on an ongoing basis. Test equipment to calibrate dedicated probes (e.g., temperature and humidity sensors, pressure transducers) should be provided.

Maintenance personnel should use PPE for maintenance of critical areas where hazardous substances might be present or could not be cleaned by another method.

導師解析

重點提示：維護人員的PPE

維護人員進入可能殘留有害物質的關鍵區域時，必須使用適當的PPE（個人防護裝備）。這個要求常被忽略——生產人員有完善的更衣程序，但維護人員的防護規定往往不夠嚴謹。特別是處理高活性藥物的隔離器，維護期間的殘留暴露風險需要明確評估。

最佳實踐建議

  • 建立基於狀態的維護（condition-based maintenance）計畫，而非純粹時間驅動
  • 設計階段就應考慮維護通道面板（maintenance access panels），讓維護人員能在不影響ISO 5區域的情況下進行調整
  • 所有感測器校準必須有文件化的SOP，包含偏差處理流程
  • 維護活動應有風險評估，評估對無菌環境的潛在影響

核心概念：預防性維護計畫

Preventive Maintenance（預防性維護）對屏障系統的無菌保證至關重要。需要定期維護的關鍵項目：

9.10 Training 9.10 教育訓練

Original Text

Reliance only on the enclosure to preserve the aseptic processing environment may not be sufficient and may give a false sense of security. The selection, training, and motivation of personnel are fundamental to GMPs.

Operators should be given a thorough understanding of how to operate the control system and perform aseptic operations within the enclosure. Operators are required to have knowledge of transfer devices, decontamination systems, and their interrelationship with the overall aseptic process.

Operators should adhere to aseptic techniques in performing manipulations for any aseptic process. Failure events and how operators are to react should be considered during training.

Operator procedures should not permit inappropriate manipulation by gloves or gauntlets in the critical zone and should stress the use of sterile tools during aseptic operations. Training should consist of both theoretical and practical aspects, concluding with a formal, documented assessment and authorization to work with the system.

導師解析

核心概念：屏障系統操作員培訓

Aseptic Technique（無菌操作技術）：ISPE特別警告不要過度依賴屏障系統本身來維護無菌環境，這可能帶來「虛假的安全感（false sense of security）」。培訓內容應包含：

  • 理論培訓：屏障系統原理、去污循環、傳遞系統、環境監測概念
  • 實務操作：手套操作技巧、控制系統操作、無菌工具使用
  • 異常處理：失敗事件的辨識和應對程序（如手套破損、壓差警報、去污循環失敗）
  • 正式評核：理論 + 實務考核，通過後取得正式授權

重點提示：「不能在關鍵區域亂動手套」

ISPE明確要求操作程序不允許在關鍵區域進行不當的手套/護臂操作，並強調使用無菌工具。這意味著：

  • 即使在隔離器內，操作員也不能直接用手套觸碰產品接觸面
  • 必須使用鑷子、夾具等無菌工具進行操作
  • 操作動作應該經過設計和驗證，減少不必要的手套介入

比喻說明

就像自動駕駛汽車的駕駛——即使車輛有高度自動化系統，駕駛仍然需要接受完整培訓、了解系統原理、知道何時介入、如何應對緊急狀況。如果駕駛因為「反正車子會自己開」而放鬆警惕，反而更危險。屏障系統的操作員也是如此：系統越先進，對操作員理解系統和正確操作的要求反而越高。

練習思考

  1. 你的操作員培訓計畫是否包含失敗事件模擬（如手套洩漏警報、VHP循環中斷）？操作員的反應是否有SOP可循？
  2. 新操作員取得正式授權需要通過哪些考核項目？是否包含實務操作評估？
  3. 如何避免操作員產生「隔離器很安全所以不需要太注意無菌技術」的心態？

Section Summary / 本節重點回顧

  • Equipment Design (9.5): All equipment inside isolators/RABS must be designed for glove-port ergonomics, with emphasis on UAF protection, tool-less format changes, automated operations, and material compatibility with decontamination agents. / 隔離器/RABS內設備必須為手套口人體工學設計，強調UAF保護、免工具換型、自動化操作及材質與去污劑的相容性。
  • Transfer Systems (9.5.1): Multiple transfer methods exist with varying log reduction capabilities. Isolators require 6-log, RABS require 3-log. RTP ring of concern is a key vulnerability. / 多種傳遞方法各有不同的log reduction能力。隔離器要求6-log，RABS要求3-log。RTP關注環是關鍵弱點。
  • Glove Systems (9.5.2): Gloves are the weakest link in barrier systems. Multi-layered defense: physical testing (pressure decay/constant pressure), daily visual inspection, preventive replacement, and sterile liners. / 手套是屏障系統最脆弱環節。多層防線：物理測試、每日目視檢查、預防性更換及無菌內襯手套。
  • VHP Decontamination (9.6): Complete cycle = cleaning + decontamination + aeration. Validate with BIs (6-log for isolators). Aeration is often the longest phase due to material adsorption. / 完整循環 = 清潔 + 去污 + 排氣。用BI驗證（隔離器6-log）。排氣常因材料吸附而耗時最長。
  • Environmental Monitoring (9.7): Non-invasive sampling preferred. Monitoring frequency can be reduced based on risk assessment of operator-process separation level. / 優先採用非侵入式取樣。可基於操作員與製程隔離程度的風險評估降低監測頻率。
  • Leak Rate (9.8): Three-directional protection (operator, environment, product). Tested at double operating pressure using pressure drop or constant pressure methods. / 三向保護（操作員、環境、產品）。在雙倍操作壓力下用壓力衰減法或恆壓法測試。
  • Maintenance (9.9): Condition-based preventive maintenance for HEPA filters, gloves, seals, and gaskets. Sensor calibration protocols are essential. / 對HEPA濾網、手套、密封件和墊圈進行基於狀態的預防性維護。感測器校準程序不可或缺。
  • Training (9.10): Do not rely solely on the barrier system — operators must understand aseptic technique, failure responses, and proper tool use. Formal assessment and authorization required. / 不要僅依賴屏障系統——操作員必須理解無菌操作技術、異常應對及正確工具使用。需要正式考核與授權。
8

Chapter 8: 10. General Considerations

一般考量 | p189-p198

ISPE Baseline Guide Vol. 3 (3rd Ed.) | p189 – p198

Learning Objectives / 本章學習目標

  • Understand non-GMP regulatory considerations (environmental, health & safety) that affect sterile facility design / 理解影響無菌設施設計的非GMP法規考量（環境、健康與安全）
  • Identify key waste water management strategies and the GMP-vs-GEP conflict in recycling / 辨識廢水管理策略，以及回收再利用與GMP之間的潛在衝突
  • Recognize noise control challenges unique to sterile facilities with large HVAC systems / 認識無菌設施大型HVAC系統的噪音控制挑戰
  • Apply health & safety design principles including containment, fire prevention, and means of escape / 運用含密閉、防火與逃生路線之健康安全設計原則
  • Evaluate site selection factors critical for sterile product manufacturing / 評估無菌產品製造之廠址選擇關鍵因素
  • Understand energy conservation, security, and auditing/reporting requirements / 理解能源節約、安全防護與稽核報告要求
10.1 Introduction 10.1 簡介

Original Text

This chapter covers other considerations that may affect GMP issues outlined in this Guide. These include key non-GMP regulatory/compliance design issues, such as environmental, health and safety, that should be considered for successful facility design, and which may otherwise indirectly affect GMPs.

It is assumed that the reader of this Guide understands and applies the principles of GEP (Good Engineering Practice); it is not the intent of this section to offer GEP guidance or to list the vast array of regulations with which engineers work.

Specific country or region regulations may apply that are not covered within this chapter. Note that a facility should adhere to the legislative requirements of the country in which it is based, even if the product will be exported to another country. For example, some legislation in the country of manufacture may be more stringent than the country into which the pharmaceutical product is being imported.

This chapter generally refers to US and EU regulations and includes a brief tabulation of comparable references; Tables 10.1 and 10.2 are provided as examples, for illustrative purposes only.

教學解析

核心概念：非GMP法規也會影響GMP合規

本章的關鍵訊息：一個無菌設施可能完全符合GMP，但如果忽略了環境法規、職業安全法規或消防法規，仍然無法合法運營。設施設計必須同時滿足GMP和GEP兩個層面的要求。

更複雜的是，GEP要求有時會與GMP產生衝突（例如：廢水回收 vs. 交叉污染風險），需要在設計階段預先協調。

比喻說明：餐廳不只要衛生合格

一家餐廳即使食安評鑑滿分（= GMP合規），如果消防設備不合格、噪音擾鄰被投訴、廚餘油水直排下水道，一樣會被停業。藥廠也是如此——GMP只是合規拼圖的一塊，環安衛是另一塊不可或缺的部分。

重點提示：屬地原則（Local Legislation Prevails）

ISPE明確指出：設施必須遵守所在國的法規，即使產品出口到其他國家。這在CDMO特別重要——客戶可能來自不同國家，但廠房必須先符合當地法規。有時當地法規比目標出口國更嚴格。

10.2 Environmental – General 10.2 環境 – 一般

Original Text

10.2.1 General Discussion

The environmental impact of the processing should be considered. There is significant pressure, both statutory and voluntary, on the pharmaceutical industry to reduce the environmental load from processes, including energy usage. All areas of the product supply chain and product lifecycle should be considered, for example:

  • Processing waste
  • Environmentally friendly packaging
  • Facility energy usage
  • Emissions, such as greenhouse gases or acidic gases
  • Facility water usage
  • Non-processing waste
  • Facility and equipment disposal

Options for pre-sterilized processing system waste disposal, incineration, inactivation, or depolymerization should be considered.

Sterile processes may be completely GMP compliant, but may still not be completely within other regulations if the environmental impacts are not considered during the design process (product, process, and facility). There may also be instances where the requirements of GEP in this area conflict or contradict GMPs.

The engineering solution should consider both GEP and GMP.

10.2.2 Particulate Emissions – Air

At-source containment of solid materials is recommended as the best means of controlling particulate emissions. Where this is not possible and high airborne concentrations are unavoidable, regulations may require efficient exhaust filtration. In addition, HEPA filtration may be required before discharge to atmosphere. Permissible emission levels for pharmaceutical dusts are particularly low in most regulations.

10.2.3 Volatile Organic Compounds (VOC), Odors, and Combustion Products

Typically, sterile product facilities do not generate major amounts of these substances; however, consideration should be given for formulations of drug products which may contain organic solvents. More commonly, they can arise from cleaning, disinfection, and fumigation activities. Disposal or removal of fumigants (liquid or airborne) is a particular challenge. Storage of combustible materials may require control zones within a facility with maximum quantities per control zone.

10.2.4 Ozone Depleters

HVAC cooling systems, freeze dryers, and other process equipment may contain refrigerants that affect atmospheric ozone. Local regulations may require certified repair and service personnel. It is recommended that efforts be taken to eliminate Ozone Depleting Substances (ODS).

教學解析

核心概念：GMP vs. GEP 潛在衝突

無菌製程天生就是「高環境負擔」的：

  • 大量用水：WFI製備、清洗、滅菌都需要純水
  • 高能耗：HVAC系統24/7運轉維持潔淨度
  • 一次性耗材：Single-Use Systems的塑膠廢棄物

環保法規要求減量回收，但GMP要求防止交叉污染。設計工程師必須在兩者之間找到平衡。

重點提示：排氣管理的三層邏輯

  • 第一優先：源頭密閉（At-source containment）——在產生點就控制住
  • 第二層：高效排氣過濾（Exhaust filtration）——捕捉逃逸的顆粒
  • 第三層：HEPA過濾後排放——排入大氣前的最終防線

這個邏輯與製程污染控制策略（CCS）完全一致：源頭控制 > 過程控制 > 末端控制。

比喻說明：VOC與薰蒸劑的挑戰

無菌設施常用VHP（汽化過氧化氫）進行房間薰蒸消毒。薰蒸後，如何安全地去除殘留薰蒸劑是一個工程與環保的雙重挑戰——既要確保房間殘留量低到可以安全進入（職安要求），又要確保排放不超標（環保要求）。

實務應用：臭氧層破壞物質（ODS）淘汰

凍乾機和HVAC冷媒是無菌設施中最常見的ODS來源。現代設施應使用HFC或HFO替代冷媒。台灣依《蒙特婁議定書》已全面管制CFC，新設施必須確認所有設備冷媒符合最新環保法規。

10.3 Environmental – Waste Water 10.3 環境 – 廢水

Original Text

10.3.1 Waste Water Volumes

Waste water discharges are regulated in most countries. Design should address the control of discharges and consider the assimilative capacity of receiving waters. Use of solvents to clean process equipment increases the risk of solvent losses from the facility and, potentially, into the environment. There may be a local requirement to recycle solvent. This introduces cross-contamination issues into the processes, which could have a GMP impact and should be addressed.

Water treatment, cleaning, and washing operations can generate significant volumes of waste water from sterile product facilities. Waste water volumes can be reduced by the application of a water quality cascade. Cleaner water streams are reused in lower specification applications. Examples include WFI blow down as boiler feed water, final rinse water as first wash water, and reverse osmosis reject as irrigation water.

Treatment of biologically active waste should also be considered; due to risk to public health, these systems should be designed for high integrity and treated as GMP systems.

10.3.2 Spill Prevention

Regulatory authorities may require measures for spill prevention or containment within manufacturing and storage areas.

10.3.3 Fire Water Retention Facilities

Retention facilities (e.g., ponds, dikes) may be required to avoid storm water or surface water contamination in the event of fire.

10.3.4 Effluent Treatment

Effluent treatment may be required, depending upon projected loads and local discharge standards. Treatment steps may be chemical, biological, or combinations of both. The location of treatment facilities, in relation to facility air/HVAC intakes, should be given careful consideration.

10.3.5 Waste Water Segregation

Varying levels or types of contamination from different operations may require segregation of waste water streams within manufacturing and utilities areas. Suitable waste streams may be considered as feedstock to bio-digester plants, which generate fuel in the form of biogas.

10.3.6 Recycling/Waste Minimization

Authorities may seek the application of the principles of clean manufacturing and resource conservation. In sterile product facilities, these principles, initially, may conflict with GMP requirements. These potential conflicts should be reconciled during the design stage.

教學解析

核心概念：水質梯級利用（Water Quality Cascade）

這是無菌設施節水的核心策略——將較高品質的排放水降級再利用：

  • WFI排放水 → 鍋爐給水
  • 最終沖洗水 → 第一道清洗水
  • RO濃排水 → 灌溉用水或冷卻塔補水

但每一步降級再利用都必須評估GMP風險——特別是交叉污染的可能性。

重點提示：生物活性廢棄物需按GMP系統管理

處理含活性生物製劑（如活病毒疫苗、細胞培養液）的廢水系統，ISPE建議以GMP系統的標準來設計和驗證。這是因為洩漏可能造成公共衛生風險，系統完整性必須與製程系統同等嚴謹。

比喻說明：廢水分流如同垃圾分類

家庭垃圾分為一般垃圾、廚餘和回收物；工廠廢水同樣需要「分流」。含有機溶劑的廢水、含活性藥物成分的廢水、一般清洗廢水——各有不同的處理路徑和排放標準。混在一起不僅增加處理成本，更可能觸犯環保法規。

重點提示：廢水處理設施選址與HVAC進氣口

ISPE特別警告：廢水處理設施的位置必須遠離廠房HVAC進氣口。化學或生物處理過程產生的異味、微生物氣膠，若被HVAC系統吸入潔淨區，將直接衝擊產品品質和環境監測結果。

CDMO實務檢核

  • 你的設施是否已建立廢水分流系統？高風險廢水（含API）是否有獨立處理流程？
  • 廢水處理設施與HVAC進氣口的相對位置是否經過風險評估？
  • 溶劑回收再利用是否有交叉污染風險評估文件？
10.4 Environmental Noise 10.4 環境噪音

Original Text

10.4.1 External Noise

Due to their large air handling requirements, sterile product facilities may be a source of objectionable noise outside the building. Fans, compressors, and other utilities equipment can generate unacceptable noise levels, in terms of both volume and frequency. Check local regulations to ensure boundary noise levels do not exceed acceptable levels. Suitable attenuation techniques should be employed to comply with the appropriate levels.

10.4.2 Noise Sensitive Areas

In addition to regulatory requirements, sensitivity of the surrounding community to noise should be assessed at the site selection and early design stage. Existing and potential residential developments should be considered, and the surrounding topography should be assessed for rural sites.

10.4.3 Noise in the Working Environment

Strict standards are applied by health and safety bodies with respect to noise in the working environment. Manufacturing and utilities equipment specifications should comply with the appropriate standards, and localized attenuation implemented where needed. Processing equipment may be the major source of noise in the workplace, especially where glassware is handled.

10.4.4 Noise Reduction

If possible, noise generating equipment should be located remotely from work areas. As sound attenuation usually contains soft material, cleanable non-shedding materials may be used as noise reduction measures in the facility or in HVAC. Typical clean area finishes offer little sound absorption potential, so noise is addressed in equipment specifications (e.g., larger fans running at lower speeds in the HVAC air handler). If noise cannot be controlled in other ways, sound attenuation materials in air handling systems should provide optimum cleanability and not harbor bioburden.

教學解析

核心概念：無菌設施的噪音矛盾

無菌設施天生就是「吵」的——維持ISO 5/7/8潔淨度需要大量換氣，這意味著：

  • 大型AHU風扇持續運轉
  • 壓縮機（冷凍、壓縮空氣）24/7運作
  • 製程設備（特別是玻璃瓶/安瓿處理線）產生撞擊噪音

而潔淨室的硬質光滑表面（不鏽鋼、環氧樹脂）幾乎沒有吸音能力，反而會反射放大噪音。

重點提示：降噪材料 vs. 潔淨度的衝突

傳統吸音材料（泡棉、纖維板）會脫屑（shedding）且容易藏菌，不適合用在潔淨區。ISPE建議的解決方案是從源頭控制：

  • 使用較大尺寸的風扇以較低轉速運行（同樣風量，更低噪音）
  • 將噪音設備遠離工作區域
  • 使用可清洗、不脫屑的特殊吸音材料

比喻說明：潔淨室如同「瓷磚浴室」

想像在全貼瓷磚的浴室裡說話——聲音迴盪放大。潔淨室就是這樣。你不能像客廳一樣掛窗簾或鋪地毯來吸音，因為那些東西會脫屑污染環境。所以唯一的辦法是——讓聲源本身變安靜。

思考題

你的無菌充填線附近的噪音水準是否曾經量測？如果操作人員需要長時間在ISO 7/Grade B區域工作，工作環境噪音是否超過85 dBA（通常是需要佩戴護耳設備的門檻）？

10.5 Environmental – Solid and Concentrated Wastes 10.5 環境 – 固體與濃縮廢棄物

Original Text

10.5.1 Responsibility

Offsite disposal of some wastes from sterile facilities may be necessary. In general, facility site operators remain responsible for downstream environmental and safety hazards arising from offsite disposal. Disposal contractors should be controlled carefully and, in some instances, licensed. Disposal operations may require certification.

10.5.2 Landfill Sites

Landfill sites are subject to an increasing level of control by authorities, and their location, suitability, and management should be assessed. In some areas, even innocuous solid wastes from pharmaceutical operations are subject to strict control.

10.5.3 Shipments of Wastes

US and EU regulations apply controls for both internal and trans-border shipments of hazardous materials. These should be considered in the logistics planning of facility operation.

10.5.4 Incineration

Incineration may be essential for the disposal of toxic/potent solids or liquids, and may be located on or offsite. Onsite incineration can raise particularly sensitive environmental issues, and disposal in this manner may require an increased level of licensing and certification.

教學解析

核心概念：廢棄物的「搖籃到墳墓」責任

ISPE強調一個關鍵法律原則：即使廢棄物已交給外部處理商，產生者仍需負最終責任。這意味著：

  • 必須審慎篩選和監督廢棄物處理承包商
  • 處理商需具備適當的許可證和認證
  • 跨境運輸危險廢棄物有額外的法規要求

重點提示：Single-Use Systems的廢棄物挑戰

現代無菌設施越來越多使用一次性系統（SUS），產生大量塑膠廢棄物。這些廢棄物可能接觸過活性藥物成分，需要特殊處理（去活化或焚燒）。ISPE在10.2.1已提到「depolymerization」——這是一種將塑膠分解回單體以回收再利用的新興技術。

比喻說明：毒性廢棄物焚化如同「最後手段」

就像醫院的感染性廢棄物必須焚化處理而非丟入一般垃圾場，含有高活性藥物成分（如ADC藥物、細胞毒性藥物）的固態廢棄物也必須透過焚燒徹底銷毀。廠內設置焚化爐雖然便利，但面臨更嚴格的環保許可和社區接受度問題。

10.6 Health and Safety 10.6 健康與安全

Original Text

10.6.1 Training and Safe Behaviors

An essential element of safe behaviors is driven by attitude and a core value that safety should not be compromised. Operator safety during normal operations and mishaps also should be reviewed. Training should be evaluated for manual and material handling operations, including potential operational exposure, knowledge of universal precautions, and the use of PPE.

10.6.2 Hazardous Products

Hazardous products, which include potent and toxic products, require special design consideration. Containment considerations may conflict with cleanroom design principles, such as positive pressure cascades, and require special attention to HVAC and building design. Operator exposure limits should be established for the material being handled, and should form the basis for design of containment or isolation measures.

10.6.3 Cleaning and Disinfectant Materials

Many materials used for cleaning and disinfecting purposes are hazardous chemicals, and safe handling methods should be incorporated in the design and operating procedures. As cleaning and sanitizing dilutions should be made up fresh daily, there is potential for personnel to have frequent exposure to these chemicals.

10.6.4 Materials Handling

Mechanical handling methods help avoid unsafe lifting practices. Enhanced ergonomics in production, logistics, and maintenance should be considered. Material handling methods should be addressed in early design phases as they may affect building layout and structure.

10.6.5 Surfaces and Safe Access

Cleaning and sanitization requirements should be combined with non-slip properties when specifying floor surfaces. Dedicated access routes for the operation and maintenance of equipment should be incorporated in building layouts.

10.6.6 Fire Prevention

The requirements for fire protection (e.g., sprinklers) in clean areas may have the potential to create problems with cleaning and maintaining room pressurization if not designed properly. Sealed and concealed sprinklers which maintain a flush ceiling profile are recommended. Building and fire code regulations often drive construction with fire resistive materials, addressing flame spread and smoke generation properties of surface finishes, avoiding combustible materials, and limiting storage and use of regulated physical and health hazards.

10.6.7 Means of Escape

The requirements for exiting a facility in an emergency may conflict with GMP considerations when considering the philosophy of protecting the product in open processing. Design of sterile facilities should overcome the conflict between complex entry and exit routines to preserve air pressure cascades and fire escape routes to get people safely out of the facility. Door interlocks should be overridden when emergency exit is necessary. It is recommended that doors are fail safe and are de-energized during an emergency.

Consideration should be given to means for emergency eye wash and emergency shower availability in controlled areas that do not compromise the integrity of the area. In an ISO 7/Grade B space, the risk during cleaning is reduced since personnel are usually wearing goggles. Where eyewash is judged to be needed in highly classified space, consideration should be taken to deploy portable sterile water/saline eyewash stations.

10.6.8 Protection of Machinery

Operators should be protected from moving components in manufacturing and utility equipment. Adequate guarding, interlocking, and safe maintenance access should be provided. Equipment design should address particularly potential hand injuries and be provided with adequate means of isolation for electrical supply and other hazard sources and release of stored energy (e.g., Lock-Out/Tag-Out).

10.6.9–10.6.11

Electrical safety codes (IEEE or European equivalents) should be incorporated in facility design. Recognized standards and local requirements should be implemented for boilers, pressure vessels, and piping systems. Dust explosion and static hazards should be addressed carefully when handling solid materials in powder form, with adequate explosion venting to the atmosphere and, in some instances, explosion containing systems or process inerting.

教學解析

核心概念：密閉（Containment）vs. 正壓梯度的衝突

這是無菌設施設計中最具挑戰性的矛盾之一：

  • GMP要求：潔淨區維持正壓梯度，防止外部污染進入（保護產品）
  • 密閉要求：處理高活性/毒性產品時需要負壓，防止有害物質外洩（保護操作員）

解決方案通常是隔離器（Isolator）或RABS——在正壓潔淨室內建立一個獨立的負壓操作空間，同時保護產品和人員。

關鍵術語：職業暴露限值（OEL）

OEL（Occupational Exposure Limit）是設計密閉系統的基礎：

  • OEL > 10 μg/m³：一般通風控制可能足夠
  • OEL 1–10 μg/m³：需要局部排氣或密閉操作
  • OEL < 1 μg/m³：需要全密閉系統（隔離器）

OEL數值直接決定了設施設計的複雜度和成本。

重點提示：消防灑水器與潔淨室的衝突

標準灑水器頭突出天花板會破壞潔淨室的平整天花板設計，造成清潔死角和壓差洩漏點。ISPE推薦使用嵌入式隱藏灑水器（Sealed & Concealed Sprinklers），維持天花板平整的同時符合消防法規。

重點提示：緊急逃生 vs. 門互鎖（Interlock）

潔淨室常設有門互鎖（兩道門不能同時打開，以維持壓差）。但在緊急逃生時，所有互鎖必須可以被覆蓋（Override）。ISPE建議門採用失效安全（Fail Safe）設計——斷電時自動解鎖，確保人員可以立即撤離。

比喻說明：LOTO如同關電箱鎖門

Lock-Out/Tag-Out（LOTO）就像你在修理家裡電器前，先把總開關關掉並鎖住，貼上「維修中勿開」的標示。在藥廠，這套程序確保維修人員不會被突然啟動的機器傷害——所有能量源（電力、壓縮空氣、蒸氣）都必須被隔離和鎖定。

思考題

  1. 你的設施是否有處理高活性藥物（如ADC payload、細胞毒性藥物）？如果有，OEL是多少？密閉等級是否足夠？
  2. 潔淨區的緊急出口門是否設計為fail safe？斷電時互鎖是否自動解除？
  3. 清潔消毒人員每天配製消毒液時，是否有適當的PPE和通風措施？
10.7 Site Selection and Location 10.7 廠址選擇與位置

Original Text

10.7.1 Ambient Air Quality

Ambient air quality is a primary requirement in site selection for a sterile product facility. If the facility is located in an industrial or agricultural area, the impact of activities in those areas should be considered. Air sampling and analysis for the presence of objectionable levels of chemicals and dust may be appropriate prior to site selection.

10.7.2 Water Supply

A reliable supply of good quality water should be available for pharmaceutical facilities. Local water sources should be assessed prior to site selection, taking into account that the quality may be subject to seasonal variation. If municipal water is available, in addition to quality, the level of its pretreatment should be assessed. Excessive chlorination may cause difficulties in water treatment and purification for sterile products.

10.7.3 Environmental Sensitivity

Site selection should address the potential environmental sensitivity of the selected area. The existence of recreational areas, nature preserves, watersheds, flood plains, endangered species, etc., may require investigation.

10.7.4 Other Selection Considerations

Other considerations in the selection of sites for sterile product facilities include:

  • Climatic conditions
  • Local geographic conditions (e.g., local lakes/rivers may increase capacity requirements)
  • Suitability of the site for building foundations
  • Requirements for special structural or seismic design

Communities and industrial parks may require adherence to specific architectural standards.

10.7.5 Local Code Officials

Depending on the geographical location of the sterile product manufacturing facility, the learning curve of local officials may be quite steep. Local code officials may not have the knowledge or the experience to understand the scope of work, or how to apply the current codes, standards, and regulations to the permitting, inspection, and approval of these facilities. It helps to develop a relationship with local code officials early in the programming and conceptual design stage of the project to build trust and alignment.

教學解析

核心概念：無菌設施選址的五大關鍵因素

  1. 環境空氣品質——工業區或農業區的粉塵、化學物質影響HVAC預過濾負荷
  2. 水源品質與可靠性——季節性水質變化會影響WFI系統設計
  3. 環境敏感性——周邊是否有保護區、水源地、防洪區
  4. 氣候與地理條件——地震帶、高濕度、極端溫差都影響設施設計
  5. 基礎設施與法規環境——電力穩定性、天然氣供應、當地官員的配合度

重點提示：水源的隱藏陷阱

ISPE特別提到「過度加氯」問題。自來水公司為確保飲用水安全而大量加氯，但高氯量會：

  • 增加水處理系統（RO/EDI）的負擔
  • 縮短RO膜壽命
  • 需要額外的脫氯處理步驟

台灣的自來水餘氯量通常在0.2-1.0 ppm之間，需要在URS中明確規範進水水質。

比喻說明：廠址選擇如同選擇住家

就像選房子不能只看房屋本身——要看學區、交通、鄰居、是否在洪水區、空氣品質等。選藥廠廠址也是一樣：空氣品質決定了HVAC過濾成本，水質決定了純水系統複雜度，地理位置決定了建築結構成本。選錯地方，後續的營運成本會遠超預期。

CDMO實務經驗：與地方官員的溝通

ISPE用了很大篇幅強調與地方建管/消防/環保官員的早期溝通。這在實務中極其重要——無菌設施的設計（例如潔淨室壓差門互鎖、特殊通風系統、危險物品儲存）對不熟悉製藥業的地方官員來說可能難以理解。

建議：在概念設計階段就邀請地方官員參訪類似設施，建立互信，避免在審批階段產生不必要的延誤。

10.8 Energy Sources 10.8 能源來源

Original Text

10.8.1 Natural Gas

A nearby natural gas source is an advantage and should be assessed as a part of the initial site selection. Oil or other energy sources are normally transportable and should be easily accessible on the site.

10.8.2 Fuel Storage

Storage facilities should be specified on the basis of incoming supply usage and reliability. Storage facilities should be designed in accordance with recognized standards and provide adequate environmental protection against spillage.

10.8.3 Electrical Supplies and Characteristics

The key requirement for electrical power supplied to a sterile facility is reliability. The consequences of power failures are serious (especially if frequent or extended) and should be evaluated prior to site selection. Characteristics of the available supply should be checked. Misunderstandings can occur due to incorrect specification of voltages and frequencies. In addition to nominal values, the tolerance range for local supplies should be evaluated. Backup power supplies should be provided for critical energy sources, such as UPS for automation, backup generators, etc.

10.8.4 Energy Conservation

A level of energy conservation should be incorporated into the facility design, in anticipation of increasing regulatory requirements and economic pressure in this respect. Non-contaminating heat recovery arrangements and combined heat and power systems (also known as cogeneration) should be considered for installation in the future.

Facilities in the EU should consider workplace access to a window to the outdoors. This can be an energy saving feature, but usually is driven by operator health and safety requirements.

教學解析

核心概念：電力可靠性是無菌設施的生命線

無菌設施斷電的後果極其嚴重：

  • HVAC停止 → 潔淨室壓差消失 → 環境失控 → 整批產品可能報廢
  • 冷鏈中斷 → 溫度敏感性產品（生物製劑）可能降解
  • 自動化系統停擺 → 製程參數失去監控
  • 凍乾機斷電 → 正在凍乾的產品可能全部報廢

因此電力備援系統（UPS + 柴油發電機）是基本配置，而非可選項目。

重點提示：能源效率的永續趨勢

ISPE提到的熱回收和汽電共生（Cogeneration）在2018年出版時還是「未來考量」，但到了今天已成為許多新建藥廠的標準配置。無菌設施的HVAC系統是最大能耗來源（通常佔總能耗60-70%），熱回收系統可顯著降低營運成本。

ESG報告要求也推動了藥廠投資太陽能板、LED照明、高效馬達等節能設備。

比喻說明：電壓/頻率如同語言差異

ISPE警告「電壓和頻率的誤解」——全球不同國家使用不同的電力規格（例如台灣110V/60Hz，歐洲230V/50Hz）。這就像購買進口設備時的「語言障礙」——設備的電氣規格必須與當地供電相容，否則會造成設備損壞或性能異常。

思考題

  1. 你的設施備用發電機能支持多長時間的全負載運作？是否足以完成關鍵製程批次？
  2. UPS系統覆蓋了哪些關鍵設備？是否包含環境監測系統和BMS？
10.9 Auditing, Monitoring, and Reporting 10.9 稽核、監控與報告

Original Text

10.9.1 Freedom of Access to Information

The US and EU regulations incorporate legal requirements for freedom of access to information. These should be addressed at the design stage, and procedures developed to comply with their operational requirements.

10.9.2 Environmental Impact Statements

Both US and EU regulations require environmental impact assessments prior to proceeding with industrial developments. These requirements, and the time for processing the information and procuring permits, should be allowed for in the design schedules.

10.9.3 Emergency Planning

For regulatory reasons and good operating practice, emergency response plans should be prepared for the facility.

10.9.4 Environmental Management Systems

Most authorities require some level of management system for an environmental program. This requirement should be addressed at the design stage.

10.9.5 Emissions Register

The regulatory standards of a country may require comprehensive records for monitoring of ongoing emissions, as well as documenting and explaining deviations from accepted standards.

10.9.6 Documentation

It is good engineering practice to document both the design and the operation of a facility. Specific documentation may be required in order to comply with GEP, in addition to that required by GMP. Commissioning documents should reflect adherence to non-GMP regulations, as described in the user requirements documentation created at the start of the project.

教學解析

核心概念：環評時程對專案的影響

ISPE特別提醒：環境影響評估（EIA）需要時間。許多藥廠新建或擴建專案的時程延誤，不是因為工程問題，而是因為環評許可的審批時間被低估。在台灣，環評審查可能需要6-18個月，必須在專案規劃初期就納入時程。

重點提示：GEP文件 vs. GMP文件

設施的文件系統不僅要滿足GMP（例如確效文件、品質記錄），還需要滿足GEP要求（例如壓力容器檢驗報告、環保排放記錄、消防系統維護記錄）。ISPE建議在URS階段就將非GMP法規要求納入，確保試車文件同時反映GMP和GEP合規。

實務應用：環境管理系統（EMS）

大多數藥廠會採用ISO 14001環境管理系統。對CDMO而言，具備ISO 14001認證不僅是法規要求，更是客戶稽核時展現環境責任的重要證據。EMS應在設施設計階段就開始規劃，而非建廠完成後才補做。

CDMO實務檢核

  • 新建或擴建專案的時程是否已包含環評審查所需時間？
  • 設施的試車文件是否同時記錄了GMP和非GMP（消防、環保、職安）合規項目？
  • 是否建立了排放登記簿（Emissions Register）以持續監測和記錄？
10.10 Security 10.10 安全

Original Text

10.10.1 Controlled Substances

Where appropriate, secure storage areas should be provided for controlled narcotics and other listed dangerous substances, and should be designed to meet government standards (e.g., Drug Enforcement Agency) based on the level of security they are used for.

10.10.2 Document Storage

Consideration should be given to secure fireproof storage for hard copy manufacturing documents. Backup procedures and offsite storage may be necessary for electronically stored data. Refer to US FDA 21 CFR Part 11 and EU GMP Volume 4 (Chapter 4 and Annex 11) for more information on requirements for integrity of records maintained electronically.

10.10.3 Logical Security

In addition to providing physical security for a sterile pharmaceutical facility, logical security should also be considered. The appropriate safeguards for information and automation systems should be part of the facility design. Safeguards may include information network firewalls, use of usernames and passwords to log into computer systems, and controls for downloading and changing process recipes. Systems should provide a means to change usernames and passwords on a periodic basis. Systems should be designed to be validated in accordance with governing regulatory requirements.

10.10.4 Label Storage

Secure facilities are required for labels and printed packaging materials. In addition to internal accountability, storage of labels and printed packaging materials should be secured against external interference. Proper location, security, and environment are important considerations that may help to mitigate labeling errors.

教學解析

核心概念：實體安全（Physical Security）vs. 邏輯安全（Logical Security）

藥廠安全防護有兩個層面：

  • 實體安全：門禁系統、監視器、管制藥品保險櫃、文件防火櫃、標籤/印刷包材鎖定儲存
  • 邏輯安全：網路防火牆、使用者帳號密碼、製程配方下載權限控制、資料備份

兩者缺一不可。ISPE在2018年就已強調邏輯安全的重要性，隨著藥廠數位化和工業4.0的推進，這個議題只會越來越關鍵。

重點提示：標籤安全——防止標示錯誤的最後防線

標示錯誤（Labeling Error）是藥品召回的主要原因之一。ISPE建議標籤和印刷包材必須：

  • 儲存在專門的安全區域
  • 防止外部干擾（unauthorized access）
  • 有適當的環境控制（溫濕度，防止標籤變質）
  • 建立數量管控（發出與退回的數量核對）

重點提示：21 CFR Part 11 與 Annex 11

電子記錄和電子簽章的法規要求適用於所有電子化的品質和製程記錄。設施設計時應確保自動化系統（BMS、SCADA、MES）從一開始就符合資料完整性要求——包括審計軌跡（Audit Trail）、權限分級、定期密碼更新等。後期補做比設計階段就納入困難得多。

比喻說明：藥廠安全如同銀行金庫

管制藥品的儲存就像銀行金庫——需要專用保險櫃、門禁記錄、雙人管控。標籤儲存則像印鈔廠的紙張管理——每一張都要追蹤去向。電子資料安全則像網路銀行——防火牆、密碼、權限控制缺一不可。

思考題

  1. 你的設施的自動化系統（BMS/SCADA/MES）是否已通過21 CFR Part 11合規驗證？
  2. 管制藥品儲存區是否有雙重門禁和即時庫存記錄？
  3. 製程配方（Recipe）的修改權限是否受到嚴格控管？是否有審計軌跡？
Section Summary / 章節總結

Chapter 10 Integration Checklist / 第十章整合檢核表

Use this checklist when designing or auditing a sterile manufacturing facility:

  • Environmental impact assessment completed and timeline integrated into project schedule
  • Waste water segregation system designed with GMP risk assessment for recycling streams
  • Noise survey conducted; equipment specified with acceptable dBA levels for work areas
  • OEL established for all handled substances; containment design matched to OEL bands
  • Fire prevention systems (sealed/concealed sprinklers) compatible with cleanroom requirements
  • Emergency exit doors designed fail-safe with interlock override capability
  • Site selection criteria documented: air quality, water supply, seismic risk, power reliability
  • Backup power (UPS + generators) sized for critical systems and worst-case duration
  • Controlled substance storage meets DEA/local authority standards
  • Automation systems designed for 21 CFR Part 11 / Annex 11 compliance from day one
  • Label storage area secured with access control and inventory reconciliation procedures
9a

Chapter 9a: App 1a. HVAC Engineering (11.1–11.5)

附錄HVAC工程（上） | p199-p207

ISPE Baseline Guide Vol. 3 (3rd Ed.) | p199 – p207

Learning Objectives / 學習目標

  • Understand sources of particulate contamination from personnel and the environment / 理解人員與環境的微粒污染來源
  • Distinguish between dilution ventilation and displacement ventilation / 區分稀釋通風與置換通風的設計原理
  • Calculate Air Change Rates (ACR) based on particle generation and recovery requirements / 根據粒子產生率與恢復需求計算換氣次數
  • Apply process knowledge to inform HVAC system design decisions / 應用製程知識指導HVAC系統設計決策
  • Evaluate recovery period requirements and their relationship to ACR / 評估恢復期間需求及其與換氣次數的關係

11.1 Introduction / 導論

Original Content (ISPE)

11.1 Introduction

This Appendix contains general design information that may be useful for engineers designing an aseptic manufacturing HVAC system.

It should be read in conjunction with Chapter 5 of this Guide as the information presented supports the principles and regulatory requirements described in that chapter.

Information in more depth is available in ISPE Good Practice Guide: Heating, Ventilation, and Air Conditioning [28].

教學說明

本附錄定位

本附錄提供無菌製造HVAC系統的補充工程設計資訊，專為工程師提供實用的計算與設計參考。

關鍵定位

本附錄是第5章（HVAC主章）的技術補充，不是獨立文件。必須搭配第5章一起閱讀，才能完整理解HVAC設計要求。

更深入參考

如需更詳細的HVAC工程設計資訊，應參閱ISPE GPG: HVAC專門指南[28]，該指南涵蓋更廣泛的HVAC工程細節。

11.2 Sources of Particulate Contamination / 微粒污染來源

11.2.1 Internal Sources / 內部來源

Original Content (ISPE)

11.2.1 Internal Sources

Figure 11.1 gives an indication of particulates generated by personnel within a cleanroom.

Figure 11.1: Number of Particles Generated per Second and per Person

Figure 11.1 is but a single data point for the cleanroom designer; there have been numerous studies regarding human shedding and the impacts of proper gowning. The authors recommend reviewing current research and gowning manufacturer's data to establish the particle shedding rate to be used in calculations or modeling.

Development of a robust contamination assumption is a key step in cleanroom design.

To put this generation of particulates into perspective, the following example attempts to quantify the implications of personnel shedding on cleanroom classification.

Figure 11.2 and contamination estimates are provided to illustrate the impact of personnel to airborne contamination levels in cleanroom zones, particularly ISO 5/Grade A unidirectional airflow zones. The model considers the space immediately around an operator as the worst case within a clean zone.

Figure 11.2: Human Particle Generation — Consider the space around an operator as the worst case within a cleanroom.

教學說明

人員粒子散發

粒子產生率 (Particle Generation Rate)

人員是潔淨室中最大的污染源。粒子產生率隨活動強度變化巨大：

  • 靜止不動：約100,000粒子/分鐘
  • 頭部與手臂移動：約500,000粒子/分鐘
  • 行走：約5,000,000粒子/分鐘
  • 快速行走：約7,500,000–10,000,000粒子/分鐘

粒子散發資料的應用

圖11.1僅為單一數據點。在實際設計中應：

  • 參考多項研究數據
  • 考量防護服製造商的测試報告
  • 建立穩健的污染假設作為設計基礎
設計用粒子產生率 = f(人員數, 活動強度, 防護服類型)

比喻說明

想像人員就像在潔淨室中的「移動塑塵源」。靜止時只是慢慢漏出灰塵，但一旦動起來，就像搖動一個灰塵撲簿 — 粒子量飆升50–100倍。這就是為何無菌區內動作必須緩慢、受控。

設計重點

圖11.2以操作員周圍空間作為最差案例來建模。這是因為靠近人員處的粒子濃度最高，也是監測時最可能超標的位置。

11.2.2 External Sources / 外部來源

Original Content (ISPE)

11.2.2 External Sources

Figure 11.3 provides typical particulate counts for fresh air. It is important that these figures be taken as a range, and that local site conditions of the facility are taken into consideration, in order to optimize the filtration design.

Although a HEPA filter is capable of capturing over 99.97% of particles (both larger and smaller than 0.3 μm), it is GEP to provide the system with pre-filters to capture larger particles representing most of the mass, therefore extending the life of the final HEPA filter.

Figure 11.3: Outdoor Air — Number of Particles

While Figure 11.3 provides an approximation of outdoor contamination levels, actual outdoor particulate levels are tracked by the EPA [64] in many areas. The EPA collects data for Particulate Matters (PM) in two size ranges, PM2.5 and PM10 (particles ≤ 2.5 or 10 μm in size); the most relevant to the cleanroom designer is PM2.5, which can serve as an indication of outdoor 0.5 μm particle concentration.

With proper filtration, the percentage of outside air has little impact on cleanroom performance.

Figure 11.4: Effect of Outdoor Air Percentage of Air Supply on Room Particle Concentration

教學說明

外氣微粒與過濾策略

HEPA過濾效率

HEPA捕獲效率 ≥ 99.97%  (針對 0.3 μm MPPS粒子)

有效粒子滿透率 = 1 - 0.9997 = 0.03%

例：若外氣 = 10,000,000 粒子/m³
通過HEPA後 ≤ 3,000 粒子/m³

多級過濾策略 (Multi-Stage Filtration)

良好工程實務(GEP)要求多級過濾：

  • 粗效過濾器(G4/M5)：捕獲大粒子，保護中效過濾器
  • 中效過濾器(F7/F9)：捕獲細粒子，延長HEPA壽命
  • HEPA(H13/H14)：最終過濾，確保潔淨度

粗效過濾器捕獲大部分質量，顯著延長HEPA的使用壽命。

EPA PM2.5數據應用

美國EPA的PM2.5數據可作為外氣0.5μm粒子濃度的參考指標。在高污染地區（如工業區、主幹道旁），應增強前置過濾級數，並縮短濾網更換週期。

外氣比例影響

圖11.4的關鍵結論：在適當過濾下，外氣比例對潔淨室性能影響很小。這意味著：

  • 設計重點應放在過濾品質，而非減少外氣
  • 適當的外氣量對於通風與壓差控制仍然重要
  • 預過濾的經濟效益遠大於減少外氣的節省

11.3 HVAC Design Principles / HVAC設計原理

11.3.1 Dilution versus Displacement Designs / 稀釋與置換設計比較

Original Content (ISPE)

11.3.1 Dilution versus Displacement Designs

Cleanroom design practice recognizes that environmental conditions equal to ISO 7/Grade B (10,000 particle/ft³) can be achieved, "in operation", by turbulent airflow dilution. Higher standards "in operation", such as ISO 5/Grade A (100 particle/ft³), are achieved by a displacement system.

In a displacement design, "dirty" air is displaced by "cleaner" air (i.e., UAF).

In a dilution design, "dirty" room air is mixed continuously with "clean" air to reduce the particulate load in the room air by turbulent air mixing.

Figure 11.5: Displacement or Dilution System Designs

The type of cleanroom design shown in Figure 11.5 using dilution is known as a "mixed flow" room. Turbulent air is used to maintain background conditions with islands of higher grade environment provided by small displacement systems, e.g., UAF units.

The inherent very high ACRs (hundreds per hour), high capital costs, and operating costs associated with displacement (UAF) cleanrooms are reserved for the highest risk ISO 5/Grade A pharmaceutical aseptic cleanrooms.
