However, dilution design (turbulent airflow) also places high demands on HVAC system design, and room layout and operations should be taken into account in addition to providing adequate local UAF to protect critical areas. It is particularly important to identify areas of low air movement that may give rise to pockets of higher particle concentrations (for example, in room corners where impact of particles is low). Critical process operations should not be situated in these areas.

The use of high level return/exhaust is detrimental to acceptable airflow patterns in the room and is discouraged.

教學說明

兩種通風策略的核心差異

稀釋通風 (Dilution Ventilation)

原理：以亂流方式將乾淨空氣與房間髒空氣混合，降低整體粒子濃度。

  • 適用：ISO 7/Grade B及以下
  • 換氣次數：通常20–60 ACH
  • 成本：相對較低
  • 限制：無法達到ISO 5級別

置換通風 (Displacement Ventilation)

原理：以單向流(UAF)推送乾淨空氣，將髒空氣向下或向外推離。

  • 適用：ISO 5/Grade A 關鍵區域
  • 換氣次數：數百次/小時
  • 成本：高資本與高營運成本
  • 優勢：能達到最高潔淨級別

比喻：清水與髒水

稀釋通風：就像將乾淨水不斷倒入混濁的水池中，攤拌混合後整體變得比較乾淨。

置換通風：就像從水池一端持續注入乾淨水，將髒水從另一端推出去 — 乾淨區與髒區分明。

混合流房間 (Mixed Flow Room)

實際應用中最常見的是「混合流」設計：以亂流稀釋維持背景環境（如ISO 7），同時在關鍵位置設置單向流裝置(UAF)提供ISO 5保護。

死角區域警告

稀釋系統必須識別空氣流動不足的區域（如房間角落），這些區域可能形成高粒子濃度的「死角」。關鍵製程操作絕對不能設在這些位置。

高位回風口不建議使用 — 會破壞房間內的氣流模式。

Original Content (ISPE)

UAF Hood Contribution to Room ACR

Note that airflow from a HEPA filtered UFH can also dilute room airborne particulates, in the same manner as supply air from the HVAC system. This airflow can increase the effective room air change rate (and speed recovery) and assist dilution.

For new HVAC installations, the minimum required air change rates may be achieved using only the supply HVAC system (discounting the effect of local hoods). It is not necessary for all the room supply airflow to pass through heating or cooling coils. It is only necessary to provide HEPA filtered air of sufficient volume, so local air handlers and hoods with filters may suffice.

Room recovery may be measured with or without UAF hoods operating.

教學說明

UAF罩對房間ACR的貢獻

有效換氣次數計算

有效ACR = HVAC供氣ACR + UAF罩ACR貢獻

例：
  房間體積 = 100 m³
  HVAC供氣 = 3,000 m³/hr → 30 ACH
  UAF罩出風 = 1,500 m³/hr → +15 ACH
  有效ACR = 45 ACH

設計原則

  • 新設計應確保僅靠HVAC系統即可滿足最低ACR
  • UAF罩的貢獻視為額外安全裡益
  • 不需所有供氣都經過冷加熱盤管 — 只需HEPA過濾即可
  • 恢復測試可在UAF罩開啟或關閉狀態下進行

11.3.2 Dilution System Design / 稀釋系統設計

Original Content (ISPE)

11.3.2 Dilution System Design

The four fundamental requirements of a turbulent flow dilution cleanroom are as follows:

  1. Air supplied to the space should be significantly cleaner than the space condition to be maintained.
  2. Extract systems should be designed and located at low level to facilitate effective removal of particulate contamination, otherwise the air change calculation may be based upon the removal of clean air. This can be visualized during smoke testing.
  3. Nearly complete mixing of the clean supply and room air is required to achieve the dilution effect (i.e., adequate dilution efficiency).
  4. Volume of clean air supplied should be sufficient to offset particulate gains in the space and, hence, maintain the "in operation" condition (i.e., adequate dilution volume).

Once airflow volume (such as m³/hour) is determined to achieve adequate dilution, air change rates may be calculated.

FDA guidance [3] suggests that 20 ACH is typically acceptable for ISO 8 cleanrooms. This value, of course, is not absolute from a design point of view. To calculate the actual airflow requirement, the following should be considered:

  • Heat gains within the space
  • Exfiltration and exhaust requirements
  • Particulate gains within the space under worst case conditions to maintain classification
  • Required recovery time (from "in use" to "at rest" conditions)

Calculating air volumes to offset heat gains is a standard HVAC system design issue.

As seen in Section 11.2.1, the number of particles generated within the manufacturing area can be quite considerable, particularly if there are a number of operators or moving equipment and conveyors in the space. Therefore, at a minimum, the supply of clean air from the HVAC system should offset the instantaneous particulate gain.

The requirement of recovery time can either come from a regulatory basis (EU) or may be an operational necessity. If a facility is to operate on a shift basis, a fast recovery time may help optimize the available manufacturing time.

教學說明

稀釋系統四大基本要求

低位回風的重要性

如果回風口設在高處，可能直接抽走剛送入的乾淨空氣，而髒空氣仍留在作業區。煙霧測試可以清楚視覺化這個問題。

決定風量的四個因素

實際風量 = max(Q_thermal, Q_exhaust, Q_particle, Q_recovery)

其中：
  Q_thermal  = 抵銷熱負荷所需風量
  Q_exhaust  = 滲氣與排氣補充量
  Q_particle = 抵銷粒子產生所需風量
  Q_recovery = 滿足恢復時間所需風量

取四者最大值作為設計風量。

FDA對ISO 8的ACR建議

FDA建議ISO 8潔淨室採用20 ACH，但這不是絕對數字。實際設計必須根據上述四個因素計算，最終ACR可能高於或低於20。

恢復時間的商業價值

恢復時間不僅是法規要求（EU GMP要求15–20分鐘），更是產能優化的關鍵。在輪班作業的工廠，每次恢復省下5分鐘，每天可多出30–60分鐘的生產時間。

11.4 Calculation of Air Change Rate / 換氣次數計算

11.4.1 Particle Gain versus Air Change Rate / 粒子產生與換氣次數

Original Content (ISPE)

11.4.1 Particle Gain versus Air Change Rate

The calculation (first approximation) of supply air volume required to offset particulate gain is very simplistic but provides a good indication of minimum air change rates. It also relies on two major basic assumptions:

  • Perfect mixing of supply and room air
  • Supply air contains, essentially, zero particles of the size used as the basis of calculation (i.e., 0.5 μm)

The simplistic equation for required airflow is related to the rate of particle generation (in particles per time) divided by the desired particle concentration (in particles per unit volume), yielding volume per time.

This form of calculation is useful particularly for rooms within aseptic suites that are small, have a relative high number of people, and only small thermal heat gains to be affected, e.g., corridors, changing rooms.

If the airflow volume to the room and the room's volume are known, air change can be expressed as:

Air Changes/Hour (or ACH) = Airflow Volume/Hour ÷ Room Volume

For example, a 1000 ft³ room served by 400 ft³/minute (or cubic feet per minute (CFM)) of air supply has 24 ACH (400 × 60/1000 = 24). This airflow volume (400 CFM) may be less than is needed to satisfy room cooling requirements.

教學說明

粒子補償風量計算

基本公式 — 粒子補償風量

         G (粒子/時間)
Q = ———————————————
     C_max (粒子/體積)

其中：
  Q     = 所需供氣風量 (m³/hr 或 ft³/min)
  G     = 粒子產生率 (粒子數/hr)
  C_max = 允許最大粒子濃度 (粒子數/m³)

兩個基本假設

  1. 完美混合：供氣與房間空氣完全均勻混合
  2. 供氣零粒子：經HEPA過濾的供氣含0.5μm粒子數≈0

實際中不可能達到完美混合，因此這是「第一近似」，提供最低ACR的參考值。

ACR基本公式

ACH = Q / V

其中：
  ACH = 換氣次數 (次/小時)
  Q   = 供氣風量 (m³/hr)
  V   = 房間體積 (m³)

工作範例

已知：
  房間體積 = 1,000 ft³
  供氣風量 = 400 CFM

計算：
  Q (ft³/hr) = 400 × 60 = 24,000 ft³/hr
  ACH = 24,000 / 1,000 = 24 ACH

注意：此風量可能不足以滿足
房間冷卻需求，需與熱負荷
計算結果取大者。

適用場景

此粒子補償計算特別適合：

  • 無菌區內的小房間（走廊、更衣室）
  • 人員密度相對較高的區域
  • 熱負荷不大但粒子產生顯著的場所

11.4.2 Recovery Period versus Air Change Rates / 恢復期間與換氣次數

Original Content (ISPE)

11.4.2 Recovery Period versus Air Change Rates

If a minimum recovery period is required, this factor may be the deciding criterion for the air change rate. Figure 11.6 is a simplified model for calculating the relationship between air change rate and recovery period. Again, this model is based on the two major assumptions given above (good mixing efficiency with clean supply air).

Figure 11.6: Recovery Period versus Air Change Rates

Figure 11.6 shows, by assuming a simple exponential decay, how the recovery period changes greatly with air change rate. For example, a 100-fold recovery, from ISO 7/Grade B to ISO 5/Grade A, with 20 ACH, takes approximately 14 minutes. With 30 ACH, it takes approximately 9 minutes.

In general, it is more important to achieve target recovery than to achieve target air change rate.

教學說明

恢復時間計算

指數衰減模型

C(t) = C₀ × e^(-n × t)

其中：
  C(t) = t時刻的粒子濃度
  C₀   = 初始粒子濃度
  n    = 換氣次數 (ACH)
  t    = 時間 (小時)
  e    = 自然對數 ≈ 2.718

恢復時間公式

若需從 C₀ 恢復至 C_target：

         ln(C₀ / C_target)
t_rec = ————————————
              n

其中 ln 為自然對數

工作範例：100倍恢復

場景：從 ISO 7/Grade B 恢復至 ISO 5/Grade A
       需要100倍恢復 (粒子濃度降至1/100)

計算：
  ln(100) = 4.605

  當換氣次數 = 20 ACH：
  t = 4.605 / 20 = 0.230 hr = 13.8 min ≈ 14 min

  當換氣次數 = 30 ACH：
  t = 4.605 / 30 = 0.154 hr = 9.2 min ≈ 9 min

  當換氣次數 = 40 ACH：
  t = 4.605 / 40 = 0.115 hr = 6.9 min ≈ 7 min

  當換氣次數 = 60 ACH：
  t = 4.605 / 60 = 0.077 hr = 4.6 min ≈ 5 min

關鍵原則：恢復優先於ACR

達到目標恢復時間比達到目標換氣次數更重要。

這意味著：

  • ACR是手段，恢復時間是目的
  • 如果混合效率高，較低的ACR也能達到目標恢復
  • 如果混合效率差，即使高ACR也可能不達標

練習：計算恢復時間

場景：一個ISO 8潔淨室，在操作期間粒子濃度升至標準的10倍。HVAC系統提供25 ACH。

  1. 計算恢復到標準需要多長時間？
  2. 如果需要在5分鐘內恢復，最低ACR應為多少？

11.5 Process Knowledge / 製程知識

Original Content (ISPE)

11.5 Process Knowledge

This should be read in conjunction with Section 5.7.

Typical process and production information, required to assess the risk and impact of the operations on environmental classifications and protection systems (i.e., HVAC and UAF units) follows:

a. Product Flows:

  • At what point the product or product contact surface becomes sterile
  • How the product enters the aseptic manufacturing area
  • At what point the product is exposed to the environment
  • How the product is placed into its final container
  • Whether the product has to be transferred into its final container before it is finally sealed
  • How the product is protected until it is sealed
  • At what point the product is considered sealed in its final container
  • How the product leaves the aseptic manufacturing area

b. Container/Closure Flow:

  • What kind of washing the container/closures need
  • What type of sterilization cycle the container/closures need
  • How pre-sterilized components enter the aseptic manufacturing area
  • How the container/closures requiring sterilization enter the aseptic manufacturing area
  • Whether the container/closures need cooling in the aseptic area
  • How the container/closures are fed into the filling machine
  • How the sterile stopper bowl is protected and where it is located
  • How the container/closures are handled after filling and sealing

c. Operator Intrusion:

  • At what points in the process operators intervene with the product
  • At what points in the process operators intervene with container/closures that contact the product, and the extent, frequency, and type of intervention
  • How the container/closures and product are transferred and handled within the aseptic manufacturing area
  • How many operators are required in the preparation area
  • How many operators are required in the aseptic manufacturing area
  • Where operators stand in the aseptic area under normal operation

d. Equipment:

  • What type of washing equipment is used before the sterilization of container/closures
  • What type of sterilization equipment is used to transfer container/closures into the aseptic area
  • How pre-sterilized equipment enters the aseptic manufacturing area
  • If any accumulation of sterilized product final containers is required
  • Whether any parts of the equipment produce large particulate loads
  • Whether the equipment items that contain exposed sterilized components, or product, need regular operator intervention
  • How equipment is maintained, whether from within the aseptic area or from outside the area

e. General:

  • What other items need to enter the aseptic manufacturing area
  • How other items enter the aseptic area
  • Whether there are any storage requirements for product contact parts (machine parts, filters, etc.) within the aseptic area
  • What the cleaning/disinfection regime is for the area
  • Required hours of operation for the facility
  • Whether doors are interlocked or alarmed to maintain air pressure differential
教學說明

HVAC設計必須的製程資訊

為何製程知識對HVAC設計至關重要？

HVAC系統不是獨立設計的 — 它必須圍繞製程需求來設計。製程知識決定：

  • 需要何種級別的環境保護
  • 污染風險在哪些步驟最高
  • 需要多少人員與多少干預
  • 設備的動態空氣影響

比喻：HVAC設計像量身訂做

HVAC設計就像量身訂做西裝 — 必須先知道穿者的體型（製程需求）、活動場合（無菌操作類型）、天氣（外部環境），才能設計出合適的系統。套用標準模板往往導致過度設計或不足。

人員介入對HVAC的直接影響

11.5(c)的人員介入資訊直接影響：

  • 粒子產生率估算（人數 × 活動強度）
  • 換氣次數計算（必須抵銷粒子產生）
  • UAF保護區配置（人員介入點需額外保護）
  • 恢復時間需求（人員退出後的恢復速度）

11.5.1 Sterilizer Types / 滅菌器類型

Original Content (ISPE)

11.5.1 Sterilizer Types

This should be read in conjunction with Section 5.7.1.

The following information assists in the critical integration of tunnel sterilizer equipment with the HVAC systems.

Dynamic equipment, such as integrated depyrogenation tunnels, are complicated items that rely on finely balanced internal airflows to achieve consistent sterilizing conditions. Such equipment may draw air from or discharge air to the room in which it is located, as well as air to the area it serves. These volumes can vary considerably depending upon whether the machine is on or off, and when on, at what temperature it is operating.

These variables make the machine dynamic with respect to the rooms at the in-feed and outflow points. Changes in air volume drawn into the machine under differing operating conditions must be considered fully, and stabilizing measures taken. If not, DPs relative to the aseptic area may be lost or change dramatically, ultimately with a potential for reverse airflow.

Figure 11.7: Typical Radiant Heat Sterilizing Tunnel Airflows

Notes for Figure 11.7:

  • All air volume flow rates are shown in m³/hr.
  • Due to differing air temperatures, the air density varies, and hence volumetric quantities change throughout the machine. (Using the Ideal Gas Law, air in the cooling zone is approximately twice as dense as air in the heating zone.) An important consideration at the qualification stage is where volumetric measurements are taken for the tunnel and under what conditions the measurements are taken.

Traditional high temperature HEPA filters are limited in operation to 250°C (482°F), but many depyrogenation tunnels and ovens operate at much higher temperatures. Once a high temperature HEPA filter has been "burned in" (operated above its temperature rating), the binders in the filter media have started to break down and the filter is often incapable of passing a leak test scan. Alternative means to verify low particle levels in the hot zone are needed. Newer high temperature HEPA filters claim to be capable of higher temperatures and ongoing leak test scans.

教學說明

去熱原隧道與HVAC整合

動態設備的挑戰

去熱原隧道(Depyrogenation Tunnel)是HVAC設計中最複雜的整合點之一，因為：

  • 隧道從房間抽取空氣，也向房間排放空氣
  • 風量隨運行狀態和溫度而變化
  • 開/關機與不同溫度條件下風量差異巨大

理想氣體定律與密度變化

PV = nRT

在恒壓條件下：
  V ∝ T  (體積與溫度成正比)

加熱區 (~350°C = 623K)
冷卻區 (~25°C = 298K)

密度比 = 623/298 ≈ 2.09

意味：冷卻區空氣密度約為
加熱區的2倍，相同質量流率
下體積流率差異巨大。

壓差逆轉風險

如果未充分考慮隧道動態風量變化，可能導致：

  • 無菌區與鄰接區域之間壓差消失或逆轉
  • 產生反向氣流，將污染空氣帶入無菌區
  • 嚴重的GMP合規問題

必須針對隧道的各種運行狀態進行穩定化措施設計。

高溫HEPA過濾器限制

傳統高溫HEPA濾網耐溫上限為250°C，但許多去熱原隧道操作溫度遠高於此。一旦濾網被「燒過」：

  • 濾材黏合劑開始分解
  • 濾網無法通過洩漏測試掃描
  • 需要替代方法驗證熱區粒子水平

新型高溫HEPA濾網聲稱可耐更高溫度並支持持續洩漏測試，但應謹慎驗證。

資格確認階段的關鍵考量

對隧道進行體積流量測量時，必須記錄：

  • 測量位置（加熱區/冷卻區/進料端/出料端）
  • 測量條件（開機/關機、運行溫度）
  • 實際空氣溫度（影響密度與體積流率）

Section Summary / 章節摘要

Summary (English)

Key Takeaways: Appendix 1a (11.1–11.5)

Core Principles

  1. Personnel are the #1 contamination source — particle generation rates vary 50–100x depending on activity level. Robust contamination assumptions are essential for cleanroom design.
  2. External particles are manageable — with proper multi-stage filtration, outdoor air percentage has minimal impact on cleanroom performance.
  3. Two ventilation strategies — dilution (turbulent) for ISO 7 and below; displacement (UAF) for ISO 5/Grade A. Most facilities use a "mixed flow" approach combining both.
  4. Four factors determine airflow — thermal load, exhaust requirements, particle offset, and recovery time. The largest value governs the design.
  5. Recovery time trumps ACR — achieving target recovery is more important than hitting a specific air change number.
  6. Process knowledge drives HVAC design — product flows, container/closure flows, operator intrusions, equipment dynamics, and general operations must all inform the HVAC design.
  7. Dynamic equipment is critical — depyrogenation tunnels create variable air demands that can compromise pressure differentials if not properly stabilized.

Self-Check Questions

  1. What are the two basic assumptions underlying the simplified ACR calculation?
  2. Why is low-level return air preferred over high-level return in dilution cleanrooms?
  3. How does temperature affect volumetric flow rates in a depyrogenation tunnel?
  4. Name the four factors that determine minimum supply airflow volume.
  5. Why does ISPE say "recovery is more important than ACR"?
摘要（中文）

關鍵重點：附錄1a (11.1–11.5)

核心原則

  1. 人員是第一大污染源 — 粒子產生率隨活動強度變化50–100倍。建立穩健的污染假設是潔淨室設計的關鍵第一步。
  2. 外部粒子可管理 — 在適當多級過濾下，外氣比例對潔淨室性能影響極小。
  3. 兩種通風策略 — 稀釋通風適用ISO 7及以下；置換通風用於ISO 5/Grade A。大多數設施採用混合流設計。
  4. 四個因素決定風量 — 熱負荷、排氣需求、粒子抵銷、恢復時間，取最大值為設計基礎。
  5. 恢復時間優先於ACR — 達到目標恢復時間比达到特定換氣次數更重要。
  6. 製程知識驅動HVAC設計 — 五大類製程資訊（產品流、容器流、人員介入、設備、一般項目）缺一不可。
  7. 動態設備是關鍵 — 去熱原隧道的變動空氣需求可能破壞壓差，必須進行穩定化設計。

自我檢測問題

  1. 簡化ACR計算的兩個基本假設是什麼？
  2. 為何稀釋潔淨室偏好低位回風口而非高位？
  3. 溫度如何影響去熱原隧道的體積流率？
  4. 決定最低供氣風量的四個因素是什麼？
  5. ISPE為何說「恢復比ACR更重要」？
9b

附錄HVAC工程（下） | p208-p222

11.6 HVAC System Design / HVAC系統設計

11.6.1 Air Filtration Arrangements / 空氣過濾配置

English Original

It is common practice for aseptic manufacturing facilities to recirculate air through the AHU. This is generally good practice, as it limits the particle load on the filters, reduces the cost of conditioning outdoor air, and optimizes control. However, there are other factors to account for, including:

  • Potential for cross-contamination in multi-purpose facilities
  • Accidental recirculation of product-contaminated air affecting operators or plant maintenance staff

These factors may be overcome by the use of return air filters. However, if the logic is that these are to capture airborne contamination, they must be of the "safe change" type to protect maintenance personnel.

The environmental standards from EU Annex 1 and FDA guidance identify 0.5 µm particle size for classification. As a result of standard filter test methods, only HEPA and ULPA filters have quantified performance ratings against the most penetrating particle size, usually sizes smaller than 0.5 µm. Other filters, such as bag filters, provide some reduction against a 0.5 µm challenge, but they are not normally configured to facilitate a performance test in situ.

Therefore, when looking at sub-micron particle reduction by filtration, only properly configured filters (including HEPA and ULPA filters) should be considered as the GMP filter. ULPA filters are not commonly used, as HEPA filters can remove contaminants to acceptable levels. However, some field integrity testing practices are more reliably conducted with ULPA filters. Good engineering design dictates use of highly effective pre-filters to prolong HEPA filter life.

The location of HEPA filters within a system should be at points such that there is no chance of the air becoming re-contaminated. Hence, the use of terminal supply (ceiling) HEPA filters is recommended for classification of ISO 7/Grade B and cleaner. These also have the additional advantage of maintaining the sealed envelope of the aseptic area.

PAO / DEHS Penetration Testing

Poly Alpha Olefin (PAO) and Diethylhexyl Sebacate (DEHS) penetration tests use a high concentration of particles of a known spectrum (usually with a mass mean of 0.1 – 0.3 µm diameter). Efficiency results can then be related to specific size of airborne particle. Only filters tested by such methods have reliable data for this particle size range.

European H14 air filters can pass a penetration scan test against a standard of < 0.01% penetration, but H13 filters must be specified by the purchaser to do so.

As Figure 11.8 demonstrates, a single HEPA filter bank in normal circumstances is adequate to reduce supply particulate concentration below that of a reasonable "at rest" design classification, for example, 100 particles/ft³. However, an important consequence of using a single HEPA bank is that the supply air 0.5 µm particle count is unlikely to be near zero. This could affect the calculations of air change volume flow rate to offset particulate gains, and, in particular, recovery periods.

Another potential problem to be addressed, if only terminal HEPA filters are used, is that of uneven filter loading, that can result in reversed DPs putting environmental conditions at risk. Active room pressure controls can compensate for this issue.

中文解說

無菌製造設施通過空氣處理機組(AHU)進行空氣回圈是常見做法。這是好的工程實務，因為它可以：

  • 限制過濾器的顱粒負荷
  • 降低調節室外空氣的成本
  • 優化控制

但需考慮的風險因素包括：

  • 多產品設施中的交叉污染風險
  • 產品污染空氣意外回圈影響操作人員或維護人員

過濾器選擇重點

回風過濾器可解決上述問題，但如果其目的是捕捉空氣傳播的污染物，則必須使用安全更換型（safe change type）以保護維護人員。

關於過濾器性能：

  • EU Annex 1和FDA指南以 0.5 µm 顱粒為分級標準
  • 只有HEPA和ULPA過濾器有針對最透過顱粒尺寸的定量性能評級
  • 袋式過濾器等可提供一定過濾，但無法現場測試
  • ULPA過濾器不常用，因為HEPA已足夠；但某些現場完整性測試在ULPA上更可靠

終端HEPA過濾器位置

HEPA過濾器應安裝在空氣不會再次被污染的點。因此，對於ISO 7/Grade B及更潔淨的區域，建議使用終端供氣（天花板）HEPA過濾器。這還有維持無菌區域密封外殼的優點。

類比說明：過濾器負荷不均的風險

想像一排通道的門，如果某些門阻力較大（過濾器負荷較高），空氣會繞行造成氣流反轉，壓力階層可能被破壞。主動房間壓力控制可補償此問題。

11.6.2 HEPA Filter In Situ Testing / HEPA過濾器現場測試

English Original

The installation of HEPA filters should be tested to ensure they are performing adequately. Much has been written on in situ testing methodology, such as in ISO 14644-3, IEST recommended practices, and ISPE Good Practice Guide: HVAC. Below are considerations for pharmaceutical applications:

  • Leak testing of the HEPA filter installation should be performed using an acceptable aerosol that does not support microbiological growth. Two FDA acceptable aerosol oils are PAO and Dioctyl Phthalate (DOP, a suspected carcinogen). DEHS is another commonly used oil.
  • HEPA filters in UAF applications should be full face scan tested to assure the quality of air through the filter face is maintained downstream.
  • HEPA filters in an AHU main bank may be single point tested downstream (provided adequate distance is available for the air to mix); the overall filter efficiency is the important measure since airflow is turbulent and mixed downstream.
  • The filter and filter frame supplier/manufacturer should understand how the filters are to be tested in situ and provide confidence that the frames and seals are adequate to pass the test.
  • Upstream challenge particle counts should not be measured by damaging the filter (i.e., forming a hole) and should be of sufficient concentration to assure a reliable downstream reading. HEPA filters should be tested at their operating airflow rate.
  • Most filter leaks are due to poor seals. Particular care should be taken in designing and specifying adequate arrangements, if possible, with pre-DOP testing facilities (i.e., pressure testing of seals).
  • Wherever possible, knife edge gel seals should be used. It is essential to ensure that the gel employed does not support microbiological growth.

Special Consideration: Dry Heat Ovens / Sterilizer Tunnels

The high operating temperature exceeds the flash point of many aerosol oils and may be beyond the design specification of filter materials and filter frame; therefore, it may invalidate the vendor's performance figures. Filters which have been operated beyond specified limits may not pass leak test scans even though low particle counts are observed in the heating zone. Certain high temperature HEPA filters claim to be capable of leak testing (below the flash point temperature of the aerosol) after the filters have been operated at high temperature. Care should be taken in specifying the filters.

中文解說

HEPA過濾器安裝後必須進行現場測試以確保充分運作。藥品應用的主要考量：

洩漏測試要點

  • 使用不支持微生物生長的可接受氣溶膠（PAO、DOP或DEHS）
  • UAF應用：需全面掃描測試（full face scan）確保過濾面下游空氣品質
  • AHU主過濾器組：可單點下游測試（需足夠混合距離），因總體過濾效率是重要指標
  • HEPA過濾器應在其運行風量下測試

密封是關鍵

大多數過濾器洩漏是由於密封不良造成的。應特別注意：

  • 盡可能使用刀口膠密封（knife edge gel seal）
  • 確保使用的膠不支持微生物生長
  • 可藉由密封加壓測試作為預檢手段

乾熱烘箱/滅菌隧道特別注意

高溫操作可能超過氣溶膠油的閃燃點及過濾器材料的設計規格。在超出規定限制下運行的過濾器，即使在加熱區觀察到低顱粒計數，也可能無法通過洩漏測試。訂購時需特別#謹慎。

11.6.3 Terminal HEPA Filter Units / 終端HEPA過濾單元

English Original

Terminal HEPA filter units are of critical importance to aseptic area air quality. The following should be considered when specifying units:

  • It is desirable for the HEPA filter to be integral to the housing or fitted into the unit from the aseptic room side. Room Side Replaceable (RSR) filter packs are desirable, as they allow the filter to be removed during maintenance, while maintaining the integrity of the clean room. Other filter designs may require additional cleaning after replacement but are fully acceptable.
  • To facilitate testing there should be:
    • An arrangement to allow the measurement of upstream aerosol concentration during testing
    • An arrangement to allow the injection of the challenge media
    • An arrangement to allow filter differential pressure testing
    • An arrangement to allow easy access to the filter media for testing
  • Due to the size of the HEPA filter, the neck velocities onto a diffuser supplied with the terminal housing may be low; hence, poor diffuser performance may result. Careful performance checks are required if diffusers are being used in a turbulent airflow room application. Generally, more HEPA filters of smaller size provide better room mixing. Non-aspirating or swirl diffusers downstream of the filter provide enhanced room performance.
中文解說

終端HEPA過濾單元對無菌區域空氣品質至關重要。規格訂定時應考慮：

RSR 房間側可更換過濾器

RSR（Room Side Replaceable）過濾器組可在維護時從潔淨室側拆卸，同時維持潔淨室的完整性。其他設計在更換後可能需要額外清潔，但同樣可接受。

測試便利性要求：

  • 上游氣溶膠濃度測量設施
  • 挑戰介質注入設施
  • 過濾器壓差測試設施
  • 過濾介質的便捷進入設施

擴散器性能提示

由於HEPA過濾器尺寸較大，進入擴散器的頸部風速可能較低，導致擴散不良。一般而言，更多較小的HEPA過濾器能提供更好的房間混合。非吸入式或渦流擴散器可提升房間性能。

11.6.4 Standby Plant Considerations / 備用設備考量

English Original

An aseptic manufacturing facility must remain under positive pressure relative to the surrounding environment. Therefore, the consequences of plant failure, ranging from main electrical supply failure to fan belt failure, must be considered. An ideal method of performing this risk analysis is an FMEA tool. This allows the potential failures to be categorized by:

  • Impact of failure
  • Likelihood of the failure occurring
  • Likelihood of the failure being detected

Measures taken depend upon the risk, and consequences of loss of conditions (i.e., product value at risk). These range from:

  • Nothing (product is at risk if power fails)
  • Standby electrical supplies to maintain fans for pressure differentials only
  • Standby electrical supplies to maintain full environmental controls (including heating/cooling)
  • Full standby electrical supplies, perhaps including a UPS
  • Duplication of some items such as fans, fan belts, etc.
  • Total duplicate plant (very unusual)

A strategy of preventive maintenance is advisable, augments the above measures, and is further discussed in Section 5.10 of this Guide.

中文解說

無菌製造設施必須相對於周圍環境維持正壓。因此必須考慮設備故障的後果，從主電源故障到風扇皮帶故障皆在範圍內。

FMEA風險分析

推薦使用FMEA（故障模式與影響分析）工具，按以下三個維度分類潛在故障：

  • 故障影響程度
  • 故障發生可能性
  • 故障被檢測的可能性

備用措施由低到高的策略等級：

預防性維護策略是上述措施的重要補充。

11.7 Horizontal vs. Vertical Unidirectional Airflow (UAF) / 水平與垂直單向氣流

English Original

This should be read in conjunction with Section 5.7.3.

The following is intended to give guidance on the issues related to horizontal versus vertical UAF protection. The examples serve to demonstrate the limitations of open processing conducted in the absence of any form of barrier technology.

The items or operations to be protected are the deciding factor, particularly regarding operator intervention or other potential source of contamination. Ideally, critical activities should be located as close as possible to the face of the UAF unit and keep the operator on the downstream side or totally removed, as shown in Figure 11.10. UAF, once contaminated, may also contaminate anything downstream.

Where a large thermal load is being cooled (e.g., a trolley of vials from a hot air oven), thermal currents caused by the load may interfere with forced UAF, as illustrated in Figure 11.11. Hence, the design should ensure that forced airflow fully protects the lower items on the trolley. In such cases, the careful use of protective barriers in the form of mobile passive RABs is recommended. The walls of these systems extend up to within approximately 30 cm of the bank of ceiling HEPAs and direct a UAF down onto and around the load, protecting and separating it from the surrounding environment.

There also are potential problems with obstruction when an obstacle in a UAF creates a dead area downstream, as illustrated in Figure 11.12. In this case, even very high air change rates may not dilute the particle count adequately, and high particle values may be recorded in areas surrounding the critical point being protected. Hoods covering a larger area may be advisable.

中文解說

本節提供水平與垂直單向氣流（UAF）保護的比較指導，並示範了在無任何屏障技術條件下開放式製程的局限性。

UAF保護核心原則

  • 決定因素是被保護的物品或操作，特別是操作人員介入及其他污染源
  • 關鍵活動應盡可能靠近UAF單元的表面
  • 操作員應位於下游側或完全移除
  • UAF一旦被污染，下游的一切都可能被污染

熱負荷干擾問題

當冷卻大型熱負荷（如從熱風烘箱出來的西林瓶推車）時，熱氣流可能干擾強制UAF。設計應確保強制氣流能完全保護推車下層物品。建議使用移動式被動RABS屏障，其牆壁延伸至天花板HEPA約30 cm處，引導UAF下吹並圍繞負荷。

類比：氣流遮蔽效應

想像河流中的岩石：障礙物後方會形成渦流死區。在UAF中，障礙物後方的死區即使高換氣率也可能無法充分稀釋顱粒。覆蓋更大區域的層流罩可能是必要的。

11.8 Airflow Velocity Considerations / 氣流速度考量

English Original

This should be read in conjunction with Section 5.1.4.

Regulations and guidance (US FDA, EU Annex 1, WHO Annex 5, etc.) suggest a typically acceptable velocity of 90 ft/min (0.45 m/s) ± 20% for this displacing airflow (measured 100–150 mm below the filter face). These values should not be mistaken for a critical acceptance criterion. The origin of this value, in Federal Standard 209:1963 (replaced by ISO 14644-1), provides no scientific link to UAF performance protecting product.

FDA guidance suggests that the velocity used for a specific application should be arrived at by design. Velocities intended for UAF should be arrived at during design with justification and evaluation to ensure efficacy. Installations with velocities as low as half the recommended 0.45 m/s have been suggested (e.g., ISO 14644-4) and successfully applied in appropriate situations.

Where bluff bodies (obstructions) within the ISO 5/Grade A areas cause turbulence, this turbulence can be reduced by reducing velocity. Understanding of this principle requires some flexibility in velocity criteria for proper performance. This can be useful when filling small vials where the critical zone may be near a large flat surface (the conveyor and filler base plate). Lower velocities can also be appropriate in LP/GAAS areas where the lower velocity can reduce turbulence and possible recirculation at the interface to the ISO 5/Grade A zone.

Regulations also suggest that velocity of the flushing airflow should be measured at 100–150 mm from the filter face and at a distance proximate to the working height, or height of the critical zone. These velocity measurements should be consistent with the velocities observed at the time of airflow pattern assessment, rather than a subjective velocity standard. The velocity serves as a surrogate for repeated pattern assessment to ensure particulate control.

Regulations differ in nomenclature regarding velocity measurement at work height, with the US FDA using the word "proximate" to work height; however, elsewhere the US FDA suggests that ISO 5 conditions should be measured within 12" (about 300 mm) of the critical zone.

During design, CFD modeling is recommended to establish velocity requirements. During qualification, in situ air pattern evaluation is required to demonstrate the protection provided by the air velocity and pattern. The flushing action can be further augmented by using local exhaust ventilation to remove particles generated within the cleanroom or zone near to their source.

中文解說

氣流速度標準的歷史背景

法規建議的典型速度為 0.45 m/s ± 20%（在過濾面下方100-150 mm處測量）。但這個數值不應被誤解為關鍵接受標準：

  • 來源於1963年的Federal Standard 209，無科學依據證明與UAF保護產品的性能直接相關
  • FDA建議速度應通過設計不證來確定
  • ISO 14644-4建議低至0.45 m/s的一半也可成功應用

降低風速的場景

當ISO 5/Grade A區域內的障礙物（bluff bodies）造成索流時，可通過降低風速來減少索流。這在以下場景特別有用：

  • 填充小西林瓶時，關鍵區域靠近大型平坦表面（輸送帶及填充機底板）
  • LP/GAAS區域，較低風速可減少與ISO 5/Grade A區域交界處的索流和回流

風速測量要求

  • 在過濾面下方100-150 mm處測量
  • 在接近工作高度或關鍵區域高度處測量
  • 測量值應與氣流模式評估時觀察到的速度一致
  • 風速作為重複氣流模式評估的替代指標

設計與確認工具

設計階段推薦使用CFD（計算流體動力學）模擬來確立速度要求。確認階段需進行現場氣流模式評估。可以進一步使用局部排氣在源頭附近移除潔淨室內產生的顱粒。

11.9 Differential Pressure Control and Alerts/Alarms / 壓差控制與警報/警示

11.9.1 Differential Pressure Control / 壓差控制

English Original

This should be read in conjunction with Section 5.6.2.

There are five basic techniques of differential pressure control which are applicable to sterile product facilities. These techniques fall into the two categories of active control or passive control:

11.9.1.1 Passive Control

Fixed (Hard) Balanced: This technique relies on the balancer to adjust the supply airflows to the engineer's calculated values and then adjust the return or exhaust as needed to produce the desired pressure cascade. The supply and return or exhaust may or may not be controlled to maintain constant flow, but room adjustments are manual. This system is insensitive to opening and closing doors, is inexpensive and is easy to maintain.

11.9.1.2 Active Control

All active control systems are more complex and harder to maintain than passive control.

Fixed Offset: Utilizes a constant volume airflow control terminal to maintain supply and return/exhaust volumes. Relies on the balancer to calibrate and adjust the supply box and return/exhaust boxes to deliver the engineer's calculated flow values. Thereafter, airflow control is automatic. Insensitive to opening and closing doors; can tolerate variability in the AHU and exhaust fan systems.

Tracking Control: Utilizes a constant volume airflow control terminal to maintain supply and variable return/exhaust volume terminals. The balancer calibrates and adjusts the offset between supply and return/exhaust flow to produce the desired pressure cascade. Automatic and "self-healing" if supply or airflow drifts. Insensitive to opening and closing doors.

Direct Pressure Control: Utilizes a constant volume airflow control terminal to maintain supply and return/exhaust dampers. The system automatically adjusts return/exhaust dampers to maintain room pressurization. Sensitive to opening and closing doors, normally utilizing door switches to freeze control when a door is open. "Self-healing" regardless of changes to room airflows and leakage from/to adjoining spaces. Particularly well suited to isolator installations or other variable flow scenarios.

Master/Submaster or Tracking with Pressure Reset: Identical to tracking control, with the addition of a subloop to reset the offset value based on room pressurization. It is the most expensive but most resilient of all systems. Particularly well suited for common clean corridors and similar spaces that buffer multiple critical rooms.

中文解說

無菌製品設施有五種基本的壓差控制技術，分為被動控制與主動控制兩大類：

被動控制：固定平衡式

通過平衡儀將供氣量調整到工程師計算值，然後調整回風/排氣以產生所需壓力階層。房間調整為手動。對開關門不敏感，便宜且易於維護。

直接壓力控制的特點

此系統對開關門敏感，通常使用門開關來凍結門打開時的控制。不論房間氣流和相鄰空間洩漏如何變化，都具有自癒能力。特別適合隔離器安裝或其他變流量場景。

主/從控制：最佳選擇

追蹤控制加壓力重置是最昂貴但最具韌性的系統，特別適合作為多個關鍵房間緩衝的公共潔淨走廊。

11.9.2 Differential Pressure Alerts and Alarms / 壓差警示與警報

English Original

Alert Points: Alert points should be set based on statistical process control principles, with the alert value set to at least 3σ above and below set point to give good indication of proper operation without nuisance alarms. If Pk is calculated to be > 2.25, the alert limit may be raised to 4.5σ to further limit nuisance alarms.

Alarm Points: Alarm points should be set to the specification limit as established in regulation or in the pressurization scheme, with an allowance for instrument error subtracted from the acceptable range.

11.9.2.1 Delays and Filters

Alert/Alarm Filtering: Due to the extremely low pressures associated with space pressurization, in the order of 2.5–50 Pa (0.01–0.20" wg), signals from space pressurization instruments are often unstable, especially at the low end of the device's range. Rolling average values or time weighted rolling average values can be useful to help identify trends and limit nuisance alarms.

It is recommended to use 5 second rolling average or three readings in 5 seconds average as the input for differential pressure trending and alarming. The real time unfiltered data should be retained and only used for troubleshooting.

Reading Variability: Industry best practice is to allow a range of not less than ± 2.5 Pa (0.01" wg) for room differential pressures (± 1% of range), due to the extremely low pressures and variability of the instruments used.

Alarm Delays: Room pressurization, while a regulatory expectation for classified spaces, is not necessarily a primary or critical process parameter; however, it is an indication of a space's ability to protect itself from airborne external contaminants. Loss of target room pressurization rarely needs to be reported immediately. The delay prior to reporting pressurization alarms is usually set to a few minutes (typically less than 10 minutes) and is supported with data on the duration of door opening needed to perform the process and by study of the impact of the maximum duration of pressure loss.

Open door studies should be performed to ensure maintenance of the desired classification when the door is open, including particle counts from space to space, smoke studies of air ingress, recovery studies from upsets, and similar qualification activities.

Best practice is to observe the time associated with loss of conditions due to an HVAC failure to ensure that the pressurization alarm delay is set to a safe value, before conditions are lost.

Mechanical Filtering: Mechanical filtering of differential pressure signals is also a common solution to noisy DP signals. Devices include large volume DP reference headers or vessels, pneumatic orifices on the central reference line, or combinations of these approaches.

Door Control: The US FDA has stated that room pressurization only needs to be maintained during periods when the door is closed and that door control (when any single door to an airlock is open) is to be strictly enforced:

"For example, a positive pressure differential of at least 10-15 Pascals (Pa) should be maintained between adjacent rooms of differing classification (with doors closed). When doors are open, outward airflow should be sufficient to minimize ingress of contamination, and it is critical that the time a door can remain ajar be strictly controlled."

The difference in pressure between adjacent rooms of different classifications having an interposed airlock should not change significantly, even with door opening, as one door is always closed. Loss of pressure from class to class is indicative of an HVAC failure, not a door control failure, unless the override switch has been used to defeat the door interlock.

Best practice is to observe the necessary door open time associated with operations and ensure that the door open alarm delay is set to a value greater than the maximum necessary door open time.

中文解說

信號過濾與滾動平均

由於空間加壓的壓力極低（2.5-50 Pa），儀器信號常常不穩定。建議：

  • 使用5秒滾動平均或5秒內三次讀數平均作為趨勢及警報輸入
  • 保留即時未過濾數據僅用於故障排除
  • 允許不小於 ± 2.5 Pa 的讀數變異範圍

警報延遲

房間壓力損失很少需要立即報告。壓力警報延遲通常設定為數分鐘（通常小於10分鐘），並需以以下數據支持：

  • 製程操作門開啟持續時間
  • 壓力損失最大持續時間的影響研究
  • HVAC故障後條件喪失的時間觀察

FDA門控制要求

FDA明確表示：

  • 房間壓力只需在門關閉時維持
  • 相鄰不同級別房間之間應維持至少10-15 Pa正壓差
  • 門打開時，向外氣流應足以最小化污染侵入
  • 門開啟時間必須嚴格控制

有氣鑼的相鄰房間即使門打開，壓差也不應明顯變化，因為總有一扇門是關閉的。

門開啟研究 (Open Door Studies)

應進行門開啟研究以確保門打開時維持所需分級：

  • 空間間顱粒計數
  • 煙霧研究（低級別空間空氣侵入）
  • 門開啟擾動後的恢復研究
  • 類似的確認活動

11.10 Biological Safety or Bio-Containment (BSL) / 生物安全或生物遏制

English Original

This should be read in conjunction with Section 5.6.4.

Where products may contain pathogens, viral vectors or recombinant human DNA, biological safety requirements may modify the pressurization, filtration, and airlock schemes suggested by the desired space classification (for cleanliness). Biological safety requirements are typically designated as follows:

  • GLSP (Good Large Scale Practices, from Appendix K of the BMBL)
  • BSL-1
  • BSL-2
  • BSL-2+ or BSL-3** (not in the BMBL, commonly a BSL-2 facility with BSL-3 practices)
  • BSL-3
  • BSL-4

GLSP and BSL-1: Designs vary very little from other sterile facilities. The containment provided to ensure sterility is typically more than adequate to contain the biosafety risk. Recirculation of air is usual. HVAC arranged to facilitate gaseous decontamination and sufficient fresh air for dilution of decontamination agents and cleaning fumes are often required. Dilution of asphyxiation risks or flammable vapors may drive the quantity of fresh air required far in excess of that required for pressurization or occupancy.

BSL-2: Designs typically ensure the manufacturing room is surrounded by a ring of higher pressure spaces and may utilize bubble and sink airlocks to ensure airflow is into areas where the pathogen, vector, or DNA may become aerosolized. Recirculation is usual but sometimes limited to within the space. HVAC commonly arranged for gaseous decontamination with sufficient fresh air and exhaust.

BSL-2+/BSL-3**: Includes surrounding high-risk areas with clean spaces at higher pressure. Exhaust may be filtered. Recirculated air within the space (not to other areas) is usual, often ensuring the final filter is within the recirculated air stream. HVAC arranged for gaseous decontamination; sufficient fresh air and exhaust provided (typically about 6 ACH). While single bubble and sink airlocks are common, combinations of both or either with a cascade airlock are sometimes used.

BSL-3: Always surrounded by areas of higher pressure, even if the clean space must be at lower pressure than ambient. Airlocks always combination type, multi-stage with bubble and sink, or either with a cascade. Exhaust should be emitted remote from personnel or HEPA filtered, commonly both. Commonly 100% exhaust; at minimum, recirculation only within each room/suite. Rooms constructed nearly airtight, requiring fixed balanced HVAC, direct pressure control, or exceptionally accurate flow control. Direct pressurization control is commonly employed because no pressure reversal should be tolerated.

BSL-4: Typically isolated and remote from other facilities. Always surrounded by one or more areas of higher pressure. Airlocks always combination type, multi-stage with bubble and sink, and possibly a cascade. Exhaust HEPA filtered, commonly double HEPA filtered and exhausted remotely. 100% exhaust; rooms constructed airtight with direct pressure control.

中文解說

當產品可能含有病原體、病毒載體或重組人類DNA時，生物安全要求可能改變基於潔淨度的壓力、過濾和氣鑼方案。

生物安全等級總覽

由CDC/NIH BMBL及WHO生物安全手冊定義：

  • GLSP — 良好大規模實務
  • BSL-1 — 基本實驗室安全
  • BSL-2 — 中等風險病原
  • BSL-2+/BSL-3** — BSL-2設施+BSL-3實務
  • BSL-3 — 高風險病原
  • BSL-4 — 最高風險病原

BSL-3特別要求

  • 房間建造為近乎氣密，需要固定平衡式HVAC、直接壓力控制或高精度流量控制
  • 直接壓力控制最常用，因為絕對不能容忍壓力反轉
  • HVAC必須能進行氣體去污染處理

BSL-4：最高等級遏制

通常與其他設施隔離且遠離。排氣必須經過雙重HEPA過濾並在遠離人員處排放。房間必須氣密，使用直接壓力控制。

11.11 Other HVAC Considerations / 其他HVAC考量

English Original

Considerations for HVAC in sterile manufacture are covered in more detail in the ISPE Good Practice Guide: HVAC. Key elements include:

HEPA Bleed Through: The method of aerosol generation for testing HEPA filters may cause a false failure of the filter. A filter that was initially qualified using cold generated aerosol (DOP or PAO) may suddenly "fail" if a hot aerosol generator is used. This is due to a larger percentage of very small particles, and should not be grounds for failing the filter. The method used to initially qualify a filter should be used for ongoing qualification.

UFH Cabinets: Leaks in the casing boxes of UFH cabinets could be a source of particles generated upstream of the hood's HEPA/ULPA filters. UFH casings should be tested for leakage when the filters are first qualified.

Airflow Pattern Testing: There is an increasing expectation that airflow patterns in ISO 5/Grade A through ISO 7/Grade B areas be video recorded. Considerations include:

  • Selection of camera angles
  • Visibility of the smoke against the room background
  • Use of finer (thinner) smoke streams to better show stream lines
  • Video narrative should describe what the viewer sees, with additional pertinent data (date, personnel, air velocity at the filters, etc.)
  • Certain aerosols may be unfit for airflow pattern testing: too dense (e.g., smoke from dry ice and alcohol) or reactive with cleaning agents (titanium smoke sticks leave a catalyst residue)
  • Some of the better smoke sources may require cleaning of the room surfaces before the room can be returned to service

Airlock Design: Because of their relatively small size and the need for rapid clean up, airlocks may incorporate high air change rates at relatively low HVAC cost. Air supply and return locations should keep contaminants generated in the room away from the entry to the cleaner area. The use of local filtered hoods can add air changes and speed recovery while having a neutral effect on air balance. DPs between room classifications is measured across the airlock, since the airborne particle class of the airlock itself varies depending on which door is open. It is not necessary to have 10 Pa or more from one grade to the airlock and then another 10 Pa from the airlock to the lower grade area.

Older Facilities without Airlocks: In an existing facility there may be no airlock between areas of different air classification. Alternative means, such as bypassing-type gravity dampers in the common wall may provide sufficient airflow through the open door.

Capper (Overseal): Some regulators may require that overseal equipment be located in classified space. HVAC design may consider local exhaust at the capping station to carry away the high levels of particles generated in the overseal operation. These exhaust airflow patterns may interfere with local airflow patterns. Extensive airflow visualization (smoke) testing may be required.

中文解說

本節涵蓋無菌製造HVAC的其他重要考量：

HEPA滯留穿透 (Bleed Through)

測試HEPA過濾器的氣溶膠產生方法可能導致假失敗。用冷生成氣溶膠（DOP/PAO）合格的過濾器，改用熱生成器可能突然「失敗」，因為熱生成會產生更多極小顱粒。初始確認時使用的方法應用於持續確認。

UFH櫃體測試

UFH（單向流層流罩）櫃體外殼的洩漏可能成為HEPA/ULPA過濾器上游的顱粒源。首次確認過濾器時應對外殼進行洩漏測試。

氣流模式測試（煙霧測試）

ISO 5/Grade A至ISO 7/Grade B區域的氣流模式越來越被期望錄影。注意事項：

  • 選擇合適的攝影角度及煙霧與房間背景的可見度
  • 使用較細的煙流以更好地顯示流線
  • 錄像應含旁白描述、日期、人員、過濾器風速等數據
  • 某些氣溶膠不適合：乾冰+酒精煙霧過密；鈦煙棒留下催化劑殘留
  • 某些較好的煙霧源可能需要清潔房間表面後才能恢復使用

氣鑼設計

氣鑼由於體積小且需要快速清潔，可採用高換氣率且HVAC成本相對較低。重要原則：

  • 供氣和回風位置應使污染物遠離較潔淨區域的入口
  • 局部過濾罩可增加換氣和加速恢復
  • 壓差在氣鑼兩側測量，不需要每側都有10 Pa

壓蓋/封口機 (Capper) 考量

某些法規要求壓蓋設備位於分級空間內。HVAC設計應考慮在壓蓋站設置局部排氣以帶走封口操作產生的大量顱粒。這些排氣氣流可能干擾局部氣流模式，可能需要大量煙霧測試。

11.12 Pass-Through Boxes / 傳遞箱

11.12.1 Introduction / 介紹

English Original

Pass-through boxes differ from material airlocks in that they are never occupied by personnel, can be internally smooth and easily cleanable, are small, and therefore present relatively less risk to the surrounding cleanroom.

中文解說

傳遞箱與物料氣鑼的區別在於：

  • 不會有人員進入
  • 內部可設計為光滑、易清潔
  • 體積小
  • 對周圍潔淨室的風險相對較低

11.12.2 Basic Pass-Through Box Features / 傳遞箱基本特性

English Original

A pass-through box may be defined as a box or tunnel passing through the wall of a clean or contained enclosure or room. Basic features:

  • Fitted with doors at both ends allowing material to be placed into it from either side for withdrawal from the other side. Can be used to pass materials or to hold materials awaiting pickup.
  • Doors must be interlocked so they cannot be opened simultaneously.
  • Should be easily cleanable, especially for GMP applications.
  • Construction and hardware should be resistant to cleaning chemicals used. Windows or see-through constructions usually added.
  • Gasketed doors may be employed to minimize air transfer between spaces with differential pressurization.

Additional optional features include:

  • Timed Interlocks: Prevent door opening until a timer expires, assuring compliance with SOPs for sanitizing agent exposure or time for ventilated pass-through to dilute airborne contaminants.
  • Notification Lights and Sounders: Notify recipients that materials are ready for withdrawal.
  • Automatic Doors: Provide convenience and enforce interlocking or coordinate with automated material movement.
  • Conveyors: Provide automated material movement. Typically confined to the pass-through to avoid having a belt traverse multiple cleanliness zones.
  • Sanitizing Means: Chemical sanitizing sprays, vapors, gases or ionizing radiation (e.g., UV). If a validated log reduction in surface contaminants is expected, this may elevate the pass-through to the level of an autoclave or sanitizing chamber.
  • Gaskets:
    • Near-Airtight: Typical gaskets that minimize air exchange but do not have uniform clamping force to assure zero leakage.
    • Airtight: Mechanically or pneumatically engaged, generally employed only in the most hazardous applications (e.g., BSL-4).
  • Ventilation:
    • Passive Ventilation: Utilizes pressure relationships between rooms, airflow within rooms and opening/closing of doors as motive force. Engineered leak paths can be fitted. More commonly, pass-through boxes are near airtight which reduces passive ventilation to a minimal amount.
    • Active Ventilation: Provided to preserve pressure regimes, create bubble or sink relationships, or dilute contaminants drawn in during opening. Can be HEPA filtered supply from HVAC or adjoining spaces. May also be exhausted (with or without HEPA filter). Can be internally recirculated through a HEPA filter. Ventilated boxes can successfully bridge from unclassified to classified space with low risk.
中文解說

傳遞箱是穿過潔淨或遏制圍包體或房間牆壁的箱體或通道。

基本特性

  • 兩端装有門，可從任一側放入物料從另一側取出
  • 門必須有聯鎖，不能同時打開
  • 應易於清潔，材料耐清潔劑腐蝕
  • 通常設有觀察窗
  • 可使用墊片門減少壓差空間之間的空氣轉移

墊片類型

  • 近乎氣密：典型墊片，減少空氣交換但不能保證零洩漏
  • 氣密：機械或氣動接合，僅用於最高危險應用（如BSL-4）

通風方式

被動通風：利用房間間壓力關係和開關門作為驅動力。可設置工程化洩漏路徑，但多數傳遞箱為近乎氣密。

主動通風：用於維持壓力體制、創建泡泡/沉降壓力關係、或稀釋開門時引入的污染物。可提供HEPA過濾供氣、排氣或內部HEPA回圈。通風傳遞箱可成功實現從非分級區到分級區的低風險連接。

11.12.3 Impact on Surrounding Environments / 對周圍環境的影響

English Original

A key concern in the application of pass-throughs is the risk of contaminating a clean space by the opening of a pass-through to a less clean space. The applications and nature of the cleanliness classification of the two adjacent spaces communicating via a pass-through are quite diverse:

  • In small scale clinical biotechnology operations (including cell and gene therapies), a pass-through may transfer raw materials into an EU Grade B area from an adjacent Grade C area or transfer trash out from Grade B to Grade D.
  • In small scale aseptic filling, the product may pass from a Grade B area to a Grade D area via a pass-through box in lieu of the mousehole used in larger scale continuous manufacturing.
  • Therapeutic protein manufacturers may use a pass-through to transfer small equipment from a Grade D area or unclassified space to a Grade C area.

Table 11.1: Particle Concentration Change from Opening a Pass-Through to a Less Clean Space

The difference in classification between adjoining spaces is a key issue. The direction of travel for materials through a pass-through box may also be a concern. Since materials leaving a clean area present less contamination risk to the room they enter (neglecting EHS concerns), the risk of compromising space classification varies with the direction of travel.

Table 11.2: Particle Concentration Change Risk Depending on Direction of Travel

Table 11.2: Risk by Direction of Travel

中文解說

傳遞箱應用的關鍵風險是打開通向較不潔淨空間的門時污染潔淨空間。

典型應用場景

  • 細胞/基因治療：從Grade C通過傳遞箱將原料送入Grade B，或從Grade B送出廢棄物到Grade D
  • 小規模無菌填充：產品從Grade B通過傳遞箱到Grade D（替代大規模連續製造的鼠洞）
  • 蛋白質製造商：從Grade D或非分級區通過傳遞箱將小型設備送入Grade C

顱粒濃度變化風險

相鄰空間的分級差異是關鍵問題。例如：

  • Grade A與Grade B之間：2 log差異
  • Grade A與U/C之間：5 log差異

物料移動方向也影響風險：

  • 進入（從較不潔淨側）：風險較高
  • （從潔淨側）：風險較低，因為離開潔淨區的物料對目標房間污染風險較低

類比：傳遞箱如空氣鑼門

傳遞箱相當於一個微型氣鑼：聯鎖門確保始終只有一側打開，限制了空氣交換。但與人員氣鑼不同，傳遞箱體積小且不會有人員進入帶入污染。

11.12.4 Recommendations / 建議

English Original

Where a room pressure cascade is from cleaner to less clean adjacent spaces, and there is low risk of particulate contamination or a short recovery time, passively ventilated pass-throughs are fully appropriate for bridging 1–2 log differences in particle concentration.

Actively ventilated boxes may be used to handle more robust particle concentration differences and provide lower risk. Where containment is required and the room pressure cascade is from the contained space, actively ventilated pass-throughs are recommended; the need to effectively contain toxic materials justifies their use.

中文解說

實務思考題

1. 在您的設施中，傳遞箱連接了哪些不同級別的空間？顱粒濃度差異是多少log？

2. 您的傳遞箱是被動通風還是主動通風？是否與風險等級相符？

3. 對於需要遏制的產品（如病毒載體），您的傳遞箱是否有主動通風來防止有害氣溶膠洩漏？

Section Summary / 章節總結

Key Takeaways (English)

11.6 HVAC System Design

  • Recirculated air systems need "safe change" return air filters for multi-purpose facilities
  • Only HEPA/ULPA filters have quantified sub-micron performance ratings; terminal ceiling HEPA filters recommended for ISO 7/Grade B and cleaner
  • HEPA in situ testing: use PAO/DOP/DEHS aerosol; knife edge gel seals preferred; special care for high-temperature applications
  • RSR terminal HEPA units maintain cleanroom integrity during maintenance
  • Use FMEA to assess standby plant requirements; preventive maintenance is essential

11.7–11.8 UAF and Airflow Velocity

  • Critical activities should be close to UAF face; operator on downstream side or removed
  • Thermal currents and obstructions create dead zones; mobile passive RABs recommended
  • 0.45 m/s ± 20% is a design guideline, not a scientific acceptance criterion
  • Lower velocities can reduce turbulence near obstructions; CFD modeling recommended during design

11.9 DP Control and Alarms

  • Five DP control techniques: Fixed Balanced (passive), Fixed Offset, Tracking, Direct Pressure, Master/Submaster
  • Alerts at ≥3σ; alarms at specification limits minus instrument error
  • Use 5-second rolling averages; allow ±2.5 Pa reading variability
  • Alarm delays typically <10 minutes; supported by open door studies

11.10–11.12 BSL, Other HVAC, Pass-Throughs

  • BSL requirements progressively increase from GLSP to BSL-4: pressure, filtration, exhaust, and airlock complexity all escalate
  • HEPA bleed through, UFH casing leaks, and smoke study methodology are critical HVAC considerations
  • Pass-through boxes: interlocked doors, optional timed interlocks, active/passive ventilation based on log difference and containment needs
重點整理（中文）

11.6 HVAC系統設計

  • 多產品設施的回風系統需要「安全更換型」回風過濾器
  • 只有HEPA/ULPA過濾器有針對亞微米顱粒的定量性能評級；ISO 7/Grade B及更潔淨區域應使用終端天花板HEPA
  • HEPA現場測試：使用PAO/DOP/DEHS；優先刀口膠密封；高溫應用需特別注意
  • RSR終端HEPA單元在維護時維持潔淨室完整性
  • 使用FMEA評估備用設備需求；預防性維護不可或缺

11.7-11.8 單向氣流與風速

  • 關鍵活動應靠近UAF表面；操作員在下游側或移除
  • 熱氣流和障礙物會產生死區；推薦移動式被動RABS
  • 0.45 m/s ± 20%是設計指南而非科學接受標準
  • 障礙物附近可降低風速減少索流；設計階段推薦CFD模擬

11.9 壓差控制與警報

  • 五種壓差控制技術：固定平衡（被動）、固定偏移、追蹤、直接壓力、主/從控制
  • 警示設≥3σ；警報設於規格限值減去儀器誤差
  • 使用5秒滾動平均；允許±2.5 Pa讀數變異
  • 警報延遲通常<10分鐘；需門開啟研究支持

11.10-11.12 生物安全、其他HVAC、傳遞箱

  • BSL要求從GLSP到BSL-4逐步增加：壓力、過濾、排氣、氣鑼複雜度全面升級
  • HEPA滯留穿透、UFH外殼洩漏、煙霧研究方法學是關鍵HVAC考量
  • 傳遞箱：聯鎖門、可選定時聯鎖、根據log差異和遏制需求選擇主動/被動通風

Chapter 10: App 2–3. References & Glossary

參考資料與術語 | p223-p244

ISPE Baseline Guide Vol. 3 (3rd Ed.) | p223 – p226

Learning Objectives / 學習目標

  • Understand the full scope of regulatory, standards, and industry references underpinning sterile facility design
  • Identify which references are mandatory regulatory requirements vs. voluntary industry guidance
  • Recognize the key ISO, ICH, FDA, and EU GMP documents that drive cleanroom and aseptic processing decisions

Reference Overview / 參考資料總覽

Complete Reference List

This appendix compiles all 71 references cited throughout the ISPE Baseline Guide Volume 3. These references span regulatory guidelines, international standards, pharmacopoeial chapters, ISPE guides, PDA technical reports, and published scientific literature. They represent the complete knowledge foundation for designing, building, and operating sterile product manufacturing facilities.

參考資料導讀

本附錄收錄了 ISPE 第三卷全書引用的 71 份參考文獻。這些文獻涵蓋法規指引、國際標準、藥典章節、ISPE 指南、PDA 技術報告及學術文獻，構成無菌製造設施設計、建造與營運的完整知識基礎。

對於 CDMO 從業者而言，不需要逐一熟讀全部 71 份文獻，但應根據職責範圍掌握核心文件。以下分類整理有助於快速定位重點。

Regulatory & GMP References / 法規類參考文獻

Regulatory Guidelines (Refs 1-3, 9-10, 17-18, 43, 62-63, 71)

  1. EudraLex Volume 4 – Annex 1: Manufacture of Sterile Medicinal Products, ec.europa.eu
  2. Pharmaceutical cGMPs for the 21st Century – A Risk-Based Approach: Final Report, September 2004, US FDA
  3. FDA Guidance for Industry: Sterile Drug Products Produced by Aseptic Processing – Current Good Manufacturing Practice, September 2004, US FDA

PIC/S & WHO

  1. PIC/S Guide: PE 009-13, Guide to Good Manufacturing Practices for Medicinal Products, 1 January 2017, PIC/S
  2. WHO GMP Guidelines, World Health Organization (WHO)

Validation & Qualification

  1. FDA Guidance for Industry: Process Validation – General Principles and Practices, January 2011, US FDA
  2. EudraLex Volume 4 – Annex 15: Qualification and Validation, 30 March 2015

Electronic Records & Documentation

  1. 21 CFR Part 11 – Electronic Records; Electronic Signatures, US FDA
  1. EudraLex Volume 4, Chapter 4: Documentation, January 2011
  2. EudraLex Volume 4, Annex 11: Computerized Systems, June 2011

法規文獻解讀

EU GMP Annex 1（Ref 1）是全球無菌製造最重要的法規文件。2022年修訂版大幅強化了污染控制策略（CCS）、無菌製程模擬（APS）及環境監測要求。所有 CDMO 從業者必讀。

FDA 無菌製程指引（Ref 3）是美國市場的核心法規依據，雖然發布於 2004 年，但至今仍為 FDA 查廠的主要參考標準。與 Annex 1 搭配閱讀可建立完整的全球法規視角。

PIC/S PE 009（Ref 9）是全球超過 50 個會員國採用的 GMP 指引框架，對於出口多國市場的 CDMO 尤為重要。

21 CFR Part 11（Ref 43）及 Annex 11（Ref 63）是電子紀錄與電子簽章的法規基礎，在數位化轉型中越來越重要。

Must-Read Regulatory Documents / 法規必讀清單

  • Ref 1 – EU GMP Annex 1 (2022 Rev.)：無菌製造的全球黃金標準，2023年8月生效
  • Ref 3 – FDA Aseptic Processing：美國市場查廠核心依據
  • Ref 17 – FDA Process Validation：製程驗證生命週期方法論
  • Ref 18 – Annex 15：歐盟確效與驗證要求
  • Ref 9 – PIC/S PE 009：多國市場 GMP 基準

ICH Guidelines / ICH 指引

ICH Harmonised Guidelines (Refs 6-7, 11-13)

  1. ICH Q7/Q7A: Good Manufacturing Practice Guide for Active Pharmaceutical Ingredients, Step 4, 10 November 2000
  2. ICH Q11: Development and Manufacture of Drug Substances (chemical entities and biotechnological/biological entities), Step 4, 1 May 2012
  1. ICH Q8(R2): Pharmaceutical Development, Step 5, August 2009
  2. ICH Q9: Quality Risk Management, Step 4, 9 November 2005
  3. ICH Q10: Pharmaceutical Quality System, Step 4, 4 June 2008

ICH 指引體系說明

ICH Q8/Q9/Q10 構成品質管理的「鐵三角」：

  • Q8 藥學開發：設計空間（Design Space）概念，為設施設計提供科學基礎
  • Q9 品質風險管理：FMEA、FTA 等工具的應用框架，直接影響設施風險評估
  • Q10 藥品品質系統：管理審查、CAPA、變更管制的系統性框架

Q7（Ref 6）針對 API 製造，與本指南的終產品無菌設施設計互補。Q11（Ref 7）則涵蓋藥物物質的開發與製造。

  1. ISO 14644-3:2005 – Part 3: Test methods
  1. ISO 14644-13:2017 – Part 13: Cleaning of surfaces to achieve defined levels of cleanliness
  1. ISO 14644-2:2015 – Part 2: Monitoring to provide evidence of cleanroom performance

Other ISO Standards

  1. ISO 8573-1:2010 Compressed Air – Part 1: Contaminants and purity classes

ISO 標準體系解說

ISO 14644 系列是潔淨室設計與驗證的國際標準基礎，本指南引用了該系列的 7 個部分：

  • Part 1（Ref 4）：空氣潔淨度分級 — 定義 ISO Class 5/7/8 等級別，是設施設計的起點
  • Part 2（Ref 42）：潔淨室性能監測 — 確認持續符合等級要求
  • Part 3（Ref 31）：測試方法 — 粒子計數、風速測量等驗證方法
  • Part 4（Ref 29）：設計、建造與啟動 — 設施工程實務
  • Part 7（Ref 20）：隔離裝置 — 隔離器、手套箱等分隔設備
  • Part 13（Ref 36）：表面清潔 — 達到定義潔淨度的清潔方法

ISO 13408（Ref 5）是無菌加工的專門標準，與 ISO 14644 互補，涵蓋無菌製程的一般要求。

ISO 8573（Ref 49）定義壓縮空氣品質等級，對製程氣體系統設計至關重要。

Section Summary / 本節摘要

Summary

The 71 references in this appendix represent the complete regulatory, standards, and scientific knowledge base for sterile product manufacturing facility design. They span:

  • 8 regulatory guidelines from FDA, EU, PIC/S, and WHO
  • 5 ICH harmonised guidelines (Q7-Q11)
  • 8 ISO standards covering cleanrooms, aseptic processing, and compressed air
  • 6 USP chapters on sterilization, inspection, and packaging
  • 14 ISPE guides across Baseline, GPG, and GAMP series
  • 3 PDA technical reports on sterilization, isolators, and process simulation
  • 27 additional references from engineering standards bodies, scientific journals, and regulatory agencies

Together, these documents provide the technical and regulatory foundation for every chapter in this guide, from facility layout and HVAC design to water systems, automation, and commissioning.

摘要

本附錄收錄的 71 份參考文獻構成無菌產品製造設施設計的完整知識體系。從法規要求（EU GMP Annex 1、FDA 指引）到技術標準（ISO 14644 系列）、從品質管理（ICH Q8-Q10）到工程實務（ISPE/ASHRAE/ASME），涵蓋了設施設計所需的所有面向。

CDMO Reading Priorities / CDMO 從業者閱讀優先順序

Tier 1 — 必讀（Must Read）：

  • EU GMP Annex 1（Ref 1）— 全球無菌製造法規基準
  • FDA Aseptic Processing（Ref 3）— 美國市場查廠依據
  • ISO 14644-1（Ref 4）— 潔淨室分級標準
  • ICH Q9（Ref 12）— 品質風險管理

Tier 2 — 應讀（Should Read）：

  • PIC/S PE 009（Ref 9）— 多國市場 GMP 要求
  • FDA Process Validation（Ref 17）— 製程驗證方法論
  • ISPE HVAC GPG（Ref 28）— HVAC 設計實務
  • ISPE Vol. 5 C&Q（Ref 34）— 試車與確效
  • GAMP 5（Ref 52）— 電腦化系統驗證

Tier 3 — 參考閱讀（Reference as Needed）：

  • ISO 14644 其他部分（Refs 20, 29, 31, 36, 42）— 依專案需求查閱
  • USP 章節（Refs 22-24, 27）— 滅菌與檢查相關
  • PDA TR1/TR22/TR34（Refs 26, 54, 69）— 深入技術細節
  • ASME BPE（Ref 21）— 設備工程規範
